Huwa allathee ja'ala a **l** shshamsa diyaan wa **a** lqamara nooran waqaddarahu manazila lita'lamoo 'adada a **l** ssineena wa **a** lhisaba ma khalaqa Allahu thalika illa bi **a** lhaqqi yufassilu alayati liqawmin ya'lamoon **a**

# 1370

Inna fee ikhtilafi allayli wa **al** nnahari wama khalaqa Allahu fee a **l** ssamawati wa **a** lardi laayatin liqawmin yattaqoon **a**

# 1371

Inna allatheena la yarjoona liqaana waradoo bi **a** lhayati a **l** ddunya wa **i** tmaannoo biha wa **a** llatheena hum 'an ayatina ghafiloon **a**

# 1372

Olaika mawahumu a **l** nnaru bima kanoo yaksiboon **a**

# 1373

Inna allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo a **l** ssalihati yahdeehim rabbuhum bieemanihim tajree min tahtihimu alanharu fee jannati a **l** nna'eem **i**

# 1374

Da'wahum feeha subhanaka allahumma watahiyyatuhum feeha salamun waakhiru da'wahum ani alhamdu lillahi rabbi al'alameen **a**

# 1375

Walaw yu'ajjilu Allahu li **l** nnasi a **l** shsharra isti'jalahum bi **a** lkhayri laqudiya ilayhim ajaluhum fanatharu allatheena la yarjoona liqaana fee tughyanihim ya'mahoon **a**

# 1376

Waitha massa alinsana a **l** ddurru da'ana lijanbihi aw qa'idan aw qaiman falamma kashafna 'anhu durrahu marra kaan lam yad'una iladurrin massahu kathalika zuyyina lilmusrifeena ma kanoo ya'maloon **a**

# 1377

Walaqad ahlakna alquroona min qablikum lamma _th_ alamoo wajaathum rusuluhum bi **a** lbayyinati wama kanoo liyuminoo kathalika najzee alqawma almujrimeen **a**

# 1378

Thumma ja'anakum khalaifa fee alardi min ba'dihim linan _th_ ura kayfa ta'maloon **a**

# 1379

Waitha tutla 'alayhim ayatuna bayyinatin qala allatheena la yarjoona liqaana iti biquranin ghayri hatha aw baddilhu qul ma yakoonu lee an obaddilahu min tilqai nafsee in attabi'u illa ma yooha ilayya innee akhafu in 'asaytu rabbee 'athaba yawmin 'a _th_ eem **in**

# 1380

Qul law shaa Allahu ma talawtuhu 'alaykum wala adrakum bihi faqad labithtu feekum 'umuran min qablihi afala ta'qiloon **a**

# 1381

Faman a _th_ lamu mimmani iftara 'ala Allahi kathiban aw kaththaba biayatihi innahu la yuflihu almujrimoon **a**

# 1382

Waya'budoona min dooni Allahi ma la yadurruhum wala yanfa'uhum wayaqooloona haolai shufa'aona 'inda Allahi qul atunabbioona Allaha bima la ya'lamu fee a **l** ssamawati wala fee alardi subhanahu wata'ala 'amma yushrikoon **a**

# 1383

Wama kana a **l** nnasu illa ommatan wahidatan fa **i** khtalafoo walawla kalimatun sabaqat min rabbika laqudiya baynahum feema feehi yakhtalifoon **a**

# 1384

Wayaqooloona lawla onzila 'alayhi ayatun min rabbihi faqul innama alghaybu lillahi fa **i** nta _th_ iroo innee ma'akum mina almunta _th_ ireen **a**

# 1385

Waitha athaqna a **l** nnasa rahmatan min ba'di darraa massathum itha lahum makrun fee ayatina quli Allahu asra'u makran inna rusulana yaktuboona ma tamkuroon **a**

# 1386

Huwa allathee yusayyirukum fee albarri wa **a** lbahri hatta itha kuntum fee alfulki wajarayna bihim bireehin tayyibatin wafarihoo biha jaatha reehun 'asifun wajaahumu almawju min kulli makanin wa _th_ annoo annahum oheeta bihim da'awoo Allaha mukhliseena lahu a **l** ddeena lain anjaytana min hathihi lanakoonanna mina a **l** shshakireen **a**

# 1387

Falamma anjahum itha hum yabghoona fee alardi bighayri alhaqqi ya ayyuha a **l** nnasu innama baghyukum 'ala anfusikum mata'a alhayati a **l** ddunya thumma ilayna marji'ukum fanunabbiokum bima kuntum ta'maloon **a**

# 1388

Innama mathalu alhayati a **l** ddunya kamain anzanahu mina a **l** ssamai fa **i** khtalata bihi nabatu alardi mimma yakulu a **l** nnasu wa **a** lan'amu hatta itha akhathati alardu zukhrufaha wa **i** zzayyanat wa _th_ anna ahluha annahum qadiroona 'alayha ataha amruna laylan aw naharan faja'anahahaseedan kaan lam taghna bi **a** lamsi kathalika nufassilu alayati liqawmin yatafakkaroon **a**

# 1389

Wa **A** llahu yad'oo ila dari a **l** ssalami wayahdee man yashao ilasiratin mustaqeem **in**

# 1390

Lillatheena ahsanoo alhusna waziyadatun wala yarhaqu wujoohahum qatarun walathillatun olaika ashabu aljannati hum feeha khalidoon **a**

# 1391

Wa **a** llatheena kasaboo a **l** ssayyiati jazao sayyiatin bimithliha watarhaquhum thillatun ma lahum mina Allahi min 'asimin kaannama oghshiyat wujoohuhum qita'an mina allayli mu _th_ liman olaika ashabu a **l** nnari hum feeha khalidoon **a**

# 1392

Wayawma nahshuruhum jamee'an thumma naqoolu lillatheena ashrakoo makanakum antum washurakaokum fazayyana baynahum waqala shurakaohum ma kuntum iyyana ta'budoon **a**

# 1393

Fakafa bi **A** llahi shaheedan baynana wabaynakum in kunna 'an 'ibadatikum laghafileen **a**

# 1394

Hunalika tabloo kullu nafsin ma aslafat waruddoo ila Allahi mawlahumu alhaqqi wadalla 'anhum ma kanoo yaftaroon **a**

# 1395

Qul man yarzuqukum mina a **l** ssamai wa **a** lardi amman yamliku a **l** ssam'a wa **a** labsara waman yukhriju alhayya mina almayyiti wayukhriju almayyita mina alhayyi waman yudabbiru alamra fasayaqooloona Allahu faqul afala tattaqoon **a**

# 1396

Fathalikumu Allahu rabbukumu alhaqqu famatha ba'da alhaqqi illa a **l** ddalalu faanna tusrafoon **a**

# 1397

Kathalika haqqat kalimatu rabbika 'ala allatheena fasaqoo annahum la yuminoon **a**

# 1398

Qul hal min shurakaikum man yabdao alkhalqa thumma yu'eeduhu quli Allahu yabdao alkhalqa thumma yu'eeduhu faanna tufakoon **a**

# 1399

Qul hal min shurakaikum man yahdee ila alhaqqi quli Allahu yahdee lilhaqqi afaman yahdee ila alhaqqi ahaqqu an yuttaba'a amman la yahiddee illa an yuhda fama lakum kayfa tahkumoon **a**

# 1400

Wama yattabi'u aktharuhum illa _th_ annan inna a **l** _thth_ anna la yughnee mina alhaqqi shayan inna Allaha 'aleemun bima yaf'aloon **a**

# 1401

Wama kana hatha alquranu an yuftara min dooni Allahi walakin tasdeeqa allathee bayna yadayhi watafseela alkitabi la rayba feehi min rabbi al'alameen **a**

# 1402

Am yaqooloona iftarahu qul fatoo bisooratin mithlihi wa **o** d'oo mani istata'tum min dooni Allahi in kuntum sadiqeen **a**

# 1403

Bal kaththaboo bima lam yuheetoo bi'ilmihi walamma yatihim taweeluhu kathalika kaththaba allatheena min qablihim fa **o** n _th_ ur kayfa kana 'aqibatu a **l** _thth_ alimeen **a**

# 1404

Waminhum man yuminu bihi waminhum man la yuminu bihi warabbuka a'lamu bi **a** lmufsideen **a**

# 1405

Wain kaththabooka faqul lee 'amalee walakum 'amalukum antum bareeoona mimma a'malu waana bareeon mimma ta'maloon **a**

# 1406

Waminhum man yastami'oona ilayka afaanta tusmi'u a **l** ssumma walaw kanoo la ya'qiloon **a**

# 1407

Waminhum man yan _th_ uru ilayka afaanta tahdee al'umya walaw kanoo la yubsiroon **a**

# 1408

Inna Allaha la ya _th_ limu a **l** nnasa shayan walakinna a **l** nnasa anfusahum ya _th_ limoon **a**

# 1409

Wayawma yahshuruhum kaan lam yalbathoo illa sa'atan mina a **l** nnahari yata'arafoona baynahum qad khasira allatheena kaththaboo biliqai Allahi wama kanoo muhtadeen **a**

# 1410

Waimma nuriyannaka ba'da allathee na'iduhum aw natawaffayannaka failayna marji'uhum thumma Allahu shaheedun 'ala ma yaf'aloon **a**

# 1411

Walikulli ommatin rasoolun faitha jaa rasooluhum qudiya baynahum bi **a** lqisti wahum la yu _th_ lamoon **a**

# 1412

Wayaqooloona mata hatha alwa'du in kuntum sadiqeen **a**

# 1413

Qul la amliku linafsee darran wala naf'an illa ma shaa Allahu likulli ommatin ajalun itha jaa ajaluhum fala yastakhiroona sa'atan wala yastaqdimoon **a**

# 1414

Qul araaytum in atakum 'athabuhu bayatan aw naharan matha yasta'jilu minhu almujrimoon **a**

# 1415

Athumma itha ma waqa'a amantum bihi alana waqad kuntum bihi tasta'jiloon **a**

# 1416

Thumma qeela lillatheena _th_ alamoo thooqoo 'athaba alkhuldi hal tujzawna illa bima kuntum taksiboon **a**

# 1417

Wayastanbioonaka ahaqqun huwa qul ee warabbee innahu lahaqqun wama antum bimu'jizeen **a**

# 1418

Walaw anna likulli nafsin _th_ alamat ma fee alardi la **i** ftadat bihi waasarroo a **l** nnadamata lamma raawoo al'athaba waqudiya baynahum bi **a** lqisti wahum la yu _th_ lamoon **a**

# 1419

Ala inna lillahi ma fee a **l** ssamawati wa **a** lardi ala inna wa'da Allahi haqqun walakinna aktharahum la ya'lamoon **a**

# 1420

Huwa yuhyee wayumeetu wailayhi turja'oon **a**

# 1421

Ya ayyuha a **l** nnasu qad jaatkum maw'i _th_ atun min rabbikum washifaon lima fee a **l** ssudoori wahudan warahmatun lilmumineen **a**

# 1422

Qul bifadli Allahi wabirahmatihi fabithalika falyafrahoo huwa khayrun mimma yajma'oon **a**

# 1423

Qul araaytum ma anzala Allahu lakum min rizqin faja'atum minhu haraman wahalalan qul allahu athina lakum am 'ala Allahi taftaroon **a**

# 1424

Wama _th_ annu allatheena yaftaroona 'ala Allahi alkathiba yawma alqiyamati inna Allaha lathoo fadlin 'ala a **l** nnasi walakinna aktharahum la yashkuroon **a**

# 1425

Wama takoonu fee shanin wama tatloo minhu min quranin wala ta'maloona min 'amalin illa kunna 'alaykum shuhoodan ith tufeedoona feehi wama ya'zubu 'an rabbika min mithqali tharratin fee alardi wala fee a **l** ssamai wala asghara min thalika wala akbara illa fee kitabin mubeen **un**

# 1426

Ala inna awliyaa Allahi la khawfun 'alayhim wala hum yahzanoon **a**

# 1427

Allatheena amanoo wakanoo yattaqoon **a**

# 1428

Lahumu albushra fee alhayati a **l** ddunya wafee alakhirati la tabdeela likalimati Allahi thalika huwa alfawzu al'a _th_ eem **u**

# 1429

Wala yahzunka qawluhum inna al'izzata lillahi jamee'an huwa a **l** ssamee'u al'aleem **u**

# 1430

Ala inna lillahi man fee a **l** ssamawati waman fee alardi wama yattabi'u allatheena yad'oona min dooni Allahi shurakaa in yattabi'oona illa a **l** _thth_ anna wain hum illa yakhrusoon **a**

# 1431

Huwa allathee ja'ala lakumu allayla litaskunoo feehi wa **al** nnahara mubsiran inna fee thalika laayatin liqawmin yasma'oon **a**

# 1432

Qaloo ittakhatha Allahu waladan subhanahu huwa alghaniyyu lahu ma fee a **l** ssamawati wama fee alardi in 'indakum min sultanin bihatha ataqooloona 'ala Allahi ma la ta'lamoon **a**

# 1433

Qul inna allatheena yaftaroona 'ala Allahi alkathiba la yuflihoon **a**

# 1434

Mata'un fee a **l** ddunya thumma ilayna marji'uhum thumma nutheequhumu al'athaba a **l** shshadeeda bima kanoo yakfuroon **a**

# 1435

Wa **o** tlu 'alayhim nabaa noohin ith qala liqawmihi ya qawmi in kana kabura 'alaykum maqamee watathkeeree biayati Allahi fa'ala Allahi tawakkatu faajmi'oo amrakum washurakaakum thumma la yakun amrukum 'alaykum ghummatan thumma iqdoo ilayya wala tun _th_ iroon **i**

# 1436

Fain tawallaytum fama saatukum min ajrin in ajriya illa 'ala Allahi waomirtu an akoona mina almuslimeen **a**

# 1437

Fakaththaboohu fanajjaynahu waman ma'ahu fee alfulki waja'anahum khalaifa waaghraqna allatheena kaththaboo biayatina fa **o** n _th_ ur kayfa kana 'aqibatu almunthareen **a**

# 1438

Thumma ba'athna min ba'dihi rusulan ila qawmihim fajaoohum bi **a** lbayyinati fama kanoo liyuminoo bima kaththaboo bihi min qablu kathalika natba'u 'ala quloobi almu'tadeen **a**

# 1439

Thumma ba'athna min ba'dihim moosa waharoona ila fir'awna wamalaihi biayatina fa **i** stakbaroo wakanoo qawman mujrimeen **a**

# 1440

Falamma jaahumu alhaqqu min 'indina qaloo inna hatha lasihrun mubeen **un**

# 1441

Qala moosa ataqooloona lilhaqqi lamma jaakum asihrun hatha wala yuflihu a **l** ssahiroon **a**

# 1442

Qaloo ajitana litalfitana 'amma wajadna 'alayhi abaana watakoona lakuma alkibriyao fee alardi wama nahnu lakuma bimumineen **a**

# 1443

Waqala fir'awnu itoonee bikulli sahirin 'aleem **in**

# 1444

Falamma jaa a **l** ssaharatu qala lahum moosa alqoo ma antum mulqoon **a**

# 1445

Falamma alqaw qala moosa ma jitum bihi a **l** ssihru inna Allaha sayubtiluhu inna Allaha la yuslihu 'amala almufsideen **a**

# 1446

Wayuhiqqu Allahu alhaqqa bikalimatihi walaw kariha almujrimoon **a**

# 1447

Famaamana limoosa illathurriyyatun min qawmihi 'ala khawfin min fir'awna wamalaihim an yaftinahum wainna fir'awna la'alin fee alardi wainnahu lamina almusrifeen **a**

# 1448

Waqala moosa ya qawmi in kuntum amantum bi **A** llahi fa'alayhi tawakkaloo in kuntum muslimeen **a**

# 1449

Faqaloo 'ala Allahi tawakkana rabbana la taj'ana fitnatan lilqawmi a **l** _thth_ alimeen **a**

# 1450

Wanajjina birahmatika mina alqawmi alkafireen **a**

# 1451

Waawhayna ila moosa waakheehi an tabawwaa liqawmikuma bimisra buyootan wa **i** j'aloo buyootakum qiblatan waaqeemoo a **l** ssalata wabashshiri almumineen **a**

# 1452

Waqala moosa rabbana innaka atayta fir'awna wamalaahu zeenatan waamwalan fee alhayati a **l** ddunya rabbana liyudilloo 'an sabeelika rabbana itmis 'ala amwalihim wa **o** shdud 'ala quloobihim fala yuminoo hatta yarawoo al'athaba alaleem **a**

# 1453

Qala qad ojeebat da'watukuma fa **i** staqeema wala tattabi'anni sabeela allatheena la ya'lamoon **a**

# 1454

Wajawazna bibanee israeela albahra faatba'ahum fir'awnu wajunooduhu baghyan wa'adwan hatta itha adrakahu algharaqu qala amantu annahu la ilaha illa allathee amanat bihi banoo israeela waana mina almuslimeen **a**

# 1455

Alana waqad 'asayta qablu wakunta mina almufsideen **a**

# 1456

Fa **a** lyawma nunajjeeka bibadanika litakoona liman khalfaka ayatan wainna katheeran mina a **l** nnasi 'an ayatina laghafiloon **a**

# 1457

Walaqad bawwana banee israeela mubawwaa sidqin warazaqnahum mina a **l** ttayyibati fama ikhtalafoo hatta jaahumu al'ilmu inna rabbaka yaqdee baynahum yawma alqiyamati feema kanoo feehi yakhtalifoon **a**

# 1458

Fain kunta fee shakkin mimma anzanna ilayka fa **i** sali allatheena yaqraoona alkitaba min qablika laqad jaaka alhaqqu min rabbika fala takoonanna mina almumtareen **a**

# 1459

Wala takoonanna mina allatheena kaththaboo biayati Allahi fatakoona mina alkhasireen **a**

# 1460

Inna allatheena haqqat 'alayhim kalimatu rabbika la yuminoon **a**

# 1461

Walaw jaathum kullu ayatin hatta yarawoo al'athaba alaleem **a**

# 1462

Falawla kanat qaryatun amanat fanafa'aha eemanuha illa qawma yoonusa lammaamanoo kashafna 'anhum 'athaba alkhizyi fee alhayati a **l** ddunya wamatta'nahum ilaheen **in**

# 1463

Walaw shaa rabbuka laamana man fee alardi kulluhum jamee'an afaanta tukrihu a **l** nnasa hatta yakoonoo mumineen **a**

# 1464

Wama kana linafsin an tumina illa biithni Allahi wayaj'alu a **l** rrijsa 'ala allatheena la ya'qiloon **a**

# 1465

Quli on _th_ uroo matha fee a **l** ssamawati wa **a** lardi wama tughnee alayatu wa **al** nnuthuru 'an qawmin la yuminoon **a**

# 1466

Fahal yanta _th_ iroona illa mithla ayyami allatheena khalaw min qablihim qul fa **i** nta _th_ iroo innee ma'akum mina almunta _th_ ireen **a**

# 1467

Thumma nunajjee rusulana wa **a** llatheena amanoo kathalika haqqan 'alayna nunjee almumineen **a**

# 1468

Qul ya ayyuha a **l** nnasu in kuntum fee shakkin min deenee fala a'budu allatheena ta'budoona min dooni Allahi walakin a'budu Allaha allathee yatawaffakum waomirtu an akoona mina almumineen **a**

# 1469

Waan aqim wajhaka li **l** ddeeni haneefan wala takoonanna mina almushrikeen **a**

# 1470

Wala tad'u min dooni Allahi ma la yanfa'uka wala yadurruka fain fa'ata fainnaka ithan mina a **l** _thth_ alimeen **a**

# 1471

Wain yamsaska Allahu bidurrin fala kashifa lahu illa huwa wain yuridka bikhayrin fala radda lifadlihi yuseebu bihi man yashao min 'ibadihi wahuwa alghafooru a **l** rraheem **u**

# 1472

Qul ya ayyuha a **l** nnasu qad jaakumu alhaqqu min rabbikum famani ihtada fainnama yahtadee linafsihi waman dalla fainnama yadillu 'alayha wama ana 'alaykum biwakeel **in**

# 1473

Wa **i** ttabi' ma yooha ilayka wa **i** sbir hatta yahkuma Allahu wahuwa khayru alhakimeen **a**

# 1474

Aliflamra kitabun ohkimat ayatuhu thumma fussilat min ladun hakeemin khabeer **in**

# 1475

Alla ta'budoo illa Allaha innanee lakum minhu natheerun wabasheer **un**

# 1476

Waani istaghfiroo rabbakum thumma tooboo ilayhi yumatti'kum mata'an hasanan ila ajalin musamman wayuti kulla thee fadlin fadlahu wain tawallaw fainee akhafu 'alaykum 'athaba yawmin kabeer **in**

# 1477

Ila Allahi marji'ukum wahuwa 'ala kulli shayin qadeer **un**

# 1478

Ala innahum yathnoona sudoorahum liyastakhfoo minhu alaheena yastaghshoona thiyabahum ya'lamu ma yusirroona wama yu'linoona innahu 'aleemun bithati a **l** ssudoor **i**

# 1479

Wama min dabbatin fee alardi illa 'ala Allahi rizquha waya'lamu mustaqarraha wamustawda'aha kullun fee kitabin mubeen **in**

# 1480

Wahuwa allathee khalaqa a **l** ssamawati wa **a** larda fee sittati ayyamin wakana 'arshuhu 'ala almai liyabluwakum ayyukum ahsanu 'amalan walain qulta innakum mab'oothoona min ba'di almawti layaqoolanna allatheena kafaroo in hatha illa sihrun mubeen **un**

# 1481

Walain akhkharna 'anhumu al'athaba ila ommatin ma'doodatin layaqoolunna ma yahbisuhu ala yawma yateehim laysa masroofan 'anhum wahaqa bihim ma kanoo bihi yastahzioon **a**

# 1482

Walain athaqna alinsana minna rahmatan thumma naza'naha minhu innahu layaoosun kafoor **un**

# 1483

Walain athaqnahu na'maa ba'da darraa massathu layaqoolanna thahaba a **l** ssayyiatu 'annee innahu lafarihun fakhoor **un**

# 1484

Illa allatheena sabaroo wa'amiloo a **l** ssalihati olaika lahum maghfiratun waajrun kabeer **un**

# 1485

Fala'allaka tarikun ba'da ma yooha ilayka wadaiqun bihi sadruka an yaqooloo lawla onzila 'alayhi kanzun aw jaa ma'ahu malakun innama anta natheerun wa **A** llahu 'ala kulli shayin wakeel **un**

# 1486

Am yaqooloona iftarahu qul fatoo bi'ashri suwarin mithlihi muftarayatin wa **o** d'oo mani istata'tum min dooni Allahi in kuntum sadiqeen **a**

# 1487

Fai llam yastajeeboo lakum fa **i** 'lamoo annama onzila bi'ilmi Allahi waan la ilaha illa huwa fahal antum muslimoon **a**

# 1488

Man kana yureedu alhayata a **l** ddunya wazeenataha nuwaffi ilayhim a'malahum feeha wahum feeha la yubkhasoon **a**

# 1489

Olaika allatheena laysa lahum fee alakhirati illa a **l** nnaru wahabita masana'oo feeha wabatilun ma kanoo ya'maloon **a**

# 1490

Afaman kana 'ala bayyinatin min rabbihi wayatloohu shahidun minhu wamin qablihi kitabu moosa imaman warahmatan olaika yuminoona bihi waman yakfur bihi mina alahzabi fa **al** nnaru maw'iduhu fala taku fee miryatin minhu innahu alhaqqu min rabbika walakinna akthara a **l** nnasi la yuminoon **a**

# 1491

Waman a _th_ lamu mimmani iftara 'ala Allahi kathiban olaika yu'radoona 'ala rabbihim wayaqoolu alashhadu haolai allatheena kathaboo 'ala rabbihim ala la'natu Allahi 'ala a **l** _thth_ alimeen **a**

# 1492

Allatheena yasuddoona 'an sabeeli Allahi wayabghoonaha 'iwajan wahum bi **a** lakhirati hum kafiroon **a**

# 1493

Olaika lam yakoonoo mu'jizeena fee alardi wama kana lahum min dooni Allahi min awliyaa yuda'afu lahumu al'athabu ma kanoo yastatee'oona a **l** ssam'a wama kanoo yubsiroon **a**

# 1494

Olaika allatheena khasiroo anfusahum wadalla 'anhum ma kanoo yaftaroon **a**

# 1495

La jarama annahum fee alakhirati humu alakhsaroon **a**

# 1496

Inna allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo a **l** salihati waakhbatoo ila rabbihim olaika ashabu aljannati hum feeha khalidoon **a**

# 1497

Mathalu alfareeqayni ka **a** la'ma wa **a** lasammi wa **a** lbaseeri wa **al** ssamee'i hal yastawiyani mathalan afala tathakkaroon **a**

# 1498

Walaqad arsana noohan ila qawmihi innee lakum natheerun mubeen **un**

# 1499

An la ta'budoo illa Allaha innee akhafu 'alaykum 'athaba yawmin aleem **in**

# 1500

Faqala almalao allatheena kafaroo min qawmihi ma naraka illa basharan mithlana wama naraka ittaba'aka illa allatheena hum arathiluna badiya a **l** rrayi wama nara lakum 'alayna min fadlin bal na _th_ unnukum kathibeen **a**

# 1501

Qala ya qawmi araaytum in kuntu 'ala bayyinatin min rabbee waatanee rahmatan min 'indihi fa'ummiyat 'alaykum anulzimukumooha waantum laha karihoon **a**

# 1502

Waya qawmi la asalukum 'alayhi malan in ajriya illa 'ala Allahi wama ana bitaridi allatheena amanoo innahum mulaqoo rabbihim walakinnee arakum qawman tajhaloon **a**

# 1503

Waya qawmi man yansurunee mina Allahi in taradtuhum afala tathakkaroon **a**

# 1504

Wala aqoolu lakum 'indee khazainu Allahi wala a'lamu alghayba wala aqoolu innee malakun wala aqoolu lillatheena tazdaree a'yunukum lan yutiyahumu Allahu khayran Allahu a'lamu bima fee anfusihim innee ithan lamina a **l** _thth_ alimeen **a**

# 1505

Qaloo ya noohu qad jadatana faaktharta jidalana fatina bima ta'iduna in kunta mina a **l** ssadiqeen **a**

# 1506

Qala innama yateekum bihi Allahu in shaa wama antum bimu'jizeen **a**

# 1507

Wala yanfa'ukum nushee in aradtu an ansaha lakum in kana Allahu yureedu an yughwiyakum huwa rabbukum wailayhi turja'oon **a**

# 1508

Am yaqooloona iftarahu qul ini iftaraytuhu fa'alayya ijramee waana bareeon mimma tujrimoon **a**

# 1509

Waoohiya ila noohin annahu lan yumina min qawmika illa man qad amana fala tabtais bima kanoo yaf'aloon **a**

# 1510

Wa **i** sna'i alfulka bia'yunina wawahyina wala tukhatibnee fee allatheena _th_ alamoo innahum mughraqoon **a**

# 1511

Wayasna'u alfulka wakullama marra 'alayhi malaon min qawmihi sakhiroo minhu qala in taskharoo minna fainna naskharu minkum kama taskharoon **a**

# 1512

Fasawfa ta'lamoona man yateehi 'athabun yukhzeehi wayahillu 'alayhi 'athabun muqeem **un**

# 1513

Hatta itha jaa amruna wafara a **l** ttannooru qulna ihmil feeha min kullin zawjayni ithnayni waahlaka illa man sabaqa 'alayhi alqawlu waman amana wamaamana ma'ahu illa qaleel **un**

# 1514

Waqala irkaboo feeha bismi Allahi majraha wamursaha inna rabbee laghafoorun raheem **un**

# 1515

Wahiya tajree bihim fee mawjin ka **a** ljibali wanada noohunu ibnahu wakana fee ma'zilin ya bunayya irkab ma'ana wala takun ma'a alkafireen **a**

# 1516

Qala saawee ila jabalin ya'simunee mina almai qala la 'asima alyawma min amri Allahi illa man rahima wahala baynahuma almawju fakana mina almughraqeen **a**

# 1517

Waqeela ya ardu ibla'ee maaki waya samao aqli'ee wagheeda almao waqudiya alamru wa **i** stawat 'ala aljoodiyyi waqeela bu'dan lilqawmi a **l** _thth_ alimeen **a**

# 1518

Wanada noohun rabbahu faqala rabbi inna ibnee min ahlee wainna wa'daka alhaqqu waanta ahkamu alhakimeen **a**

# 1519

Qala ya noohu innahu laysa min ahlika innahu 'amalun ghayru salihin fala tasani ma laysa laka bihi 'ilmun innee a'i _th_ uka an takoona mina aljahileen **a**

# 1520

Qala rabbi innee a'oothu bika an asalaka ma laysa lee bihi 'ilmun wailla taghfir lee watarhamnee akun mina alkhasireen **a**

# 1521

Qeela ya noohu ihbit bisalamin minna wabarakatin 'alayka wa'ala omamin mimman ma'aka waomamun sanumatti'uhum thumma yamassuhum minna 'athabun aleem **un**

# 1522

Tilka min anbai alghaybi nooheeha ilayka ma kunta ta'lamuha anta wala qawmuka min qabli hatha fa **i** sbir inna al'aqibata lilmuttaqeen **a**

# 1523

Waila 'adin akhahum hoodan qala ya qawmi o'budoo Allaha ma lakum min ilahin ghayruhu in antum illa muftaroon **a**

# 1524

Ya qawmi la asalukum 'alayhi ajran in ajriya illa 'ala allathee fataranee afala ta'qiloon **a**

# 1525

Waya qawmi istaghfiroo rabbakum thumma tooboo ilayhi yursili a **l** ssamaa 'alaykum midraran wayazidkum quwwatan ila quwwatikum wala tatawallaw mujrimeen **a**

# 1526

Qaloo ya hoodu ma jitana bibayyinatin wama nahnu bitarikee alihatina 'an qawlika wama nahnu laka bimumineen **a**

# 1527

In naqoolu illa i'taraka ba'du alihatina bisooin qala innee oshhidu Allaha wa **i** shhadoo annee bareeon mimma tushrikoon **a**

# 1528

Min doonihi fakeedoonee jamee'an thumma la tun _th_ iroon **i**

# 1529

Innee tawakkatu 'ala Allahi rabbee warabbikum ma min dabbatin illa huwa akhithun binasiyatiha inna rabbee 'alasiratin mustaqeem **in**

# 1530

Fain tawallaw faqad ablaghtukum ma orsiltu bihi ilaykum wayastakhlifu rabbee qawman ghayrakum wala tadurroonahu shayan inna rabbee 'ala kulli shayin hafee _th_ **un**

# 1531

Walamma jaa amruna najjayna hoodan wa **a** llatheena amanoo ma'ahu birahmatin minna wanajjaynahum min 'athabin ghalee _th_ **in**

# 1532

Watilka 'adun jahadoo biayati rabbihim wa'asaw rusulahu wa **i** ttaba'oo amra kulli jabbarin 'aneed **in**

# 1533

Waotbi'oo fee hathihi a **l** ddunya la'natan wayawma alqiyamati ala inna 'adan kafaroo rabbahum ala bu'dan li'adin qawmi hood **in**

# 1534

Waila thamooda akhahum salihan qala ya qawmi o'budoo Allaha ma lakum min ilahin ghayruhu huwa anshaakum mina alardi wa **i** sta'marakum feeha fa **i** staghfiroohu thumma tooboo ilayhi inna rabbee qareebun mujeeb **un**

# 1535

Qaloo yasalihu qad kunta feena marjuwwan qabla hatha atanhana an na'buda ma ya'budu abaona wainnana lafee shakkin mimma tad'oona ilayhi mureeb **un**

# 1536

Qala ya qawmi araaytum in kuntu 'ala bayyinatin min rabbee waatanee minhu rahmatan faman yansurunee mina Allahi in 'asaytuhu fama tazeedoonanee ghayra takhseer **in**

# 1537

Waya qawmi hathihi naqatu Allahi lakum ayatan fatharooha takul fee ardi Allahi wala tamassooha bisooin fayakhuthakum 'athabun qareeb **un**

# 1538

Fa'aqarooha faqala tamatta'oo fee darikum thalathata ayyamin thalika wa'dun ghayru makthoob **in**

# 1539

Falamma jaa amruna najjaynasalihan wa **a** llatheena amanoo ma'ahu birahmatin minna wamin khizyi yawmiithin inna rabbaka huwa alqawiyyu al'azeez **u**

# 1540

Waakhatha allatheena _th_ alamoo a **l** ssayhatu faasbahoo fee diyarihim jathimeen **a**

# 1541

Kaan lam yaghnaw feeha ala inna thamooda kafaroo rabbahum ala bu'dan lithamood **a**

# 1542

Walaqad jaat rusuluna ibraheema bi **a** lbushra qaloo salaman qala salamun fama labitha an jaa bi'ijlin haneeth **in**

# 1543

Falamma raa aydiyahum la tasilu ilayhi nakirahum waawjasa minhum kheefatan qaloo la takhaf inna orsilna ila qawmi loot **in**

# 1544

Wa **i** mraatuhu qaimatun fadahikat fabashsharnaha biishaqa wamin warai ishaqa ya'qoob **a**

# 1545

Qalat ya waylata aalidu waana 'ajoozun wahatha ba'lee shaykhan inna hatha lashayon 'ajeeb **un**

# 1546

Qaloo ata'jabeena min amri Allahi rahmatu Allahi wabarakatuhu 'alaykum ahla albayti innahu hameedun majeed **un**

# 1547

Falammathahaba 'an ibraheema a **l** rraw'u wajaathu albushra yujadiluna fee qawmi loot **in**

# 1548

Inna ibraheema lahaleemun awwahun muneeb **un**

# 1549

Ya ibraheemu a'rid 'an hatha innahu qad jaa amru rabbika wainnahum ateehim 'athabun ghayru mardood **in**

# 1550

Walamma jaat rusuluna lootan seea bihim wadaqa bihim thar'an waqala hatha yawmun 'aseeb **un**

# 1551

Wajaahu qawmuhu yuhra'oona ilayhi wamin qablu kanoo ya'maloona a **l** ssayyiati qala ya qawmi haolai banatee hunna atharu lakum fa **i** ttaqoo Allaha wala tukhzooni fee dayfee alaysa minkum rajulun rasheed **un**

# 1552

Qaloo laqad 'alimta ma lana fee banatika min haqqin wainnaka lata'lamu ma nureed **u**

# 1553

Qala law anna lee bikum quwwatan aw awee ila ruknin shadeed **in**

# 1554

Qaloo ya lootu inna rusulu rabbika lan yasiloo ilayka faasri biahlika biqit'in mina allayli wala yatafit minkum ahadun illa imraataka innahu museebuha ma asabahum inna maw'idahumu a **l** ssubhu alaysa a **l** ssubhu biqareeb **in**

# 1555

Falamma jaa amruna ja'ana 'aliyaha safilaha waamtarna 'alayhahijaratan min sijjeelin mandood **in**

# 1556

Musawwamatan 'inda rabbika wama hiya mina a **l** _thth_ alimeena biba'eed **in**

# 1557

Waila madyana akhahum shu'ayban qala ya qawmi o'budoo Allaha ma lakum min ilahin ghayruhu wala tanqusoo almikyala wa **a** lmeezana innee arakum bikhayrin wainnee akhafu 'alaykum 'athaba yawmin muheet **in**

# 1558

Waya qawmi awfoo almikyala wa **a** lmeezana bi **a** lqisti wala tabkhasoo a **l** nnasa ashyaahum wala ta'thaw fee alardi mufsideen **a**

# 1559

Baqiyyatu Allahi khayrun lakum in kuntum mumineena wama ana 'alaykum bihafee _th_ **in**

# 1560

Qaloo ya shu'aybu asalatuka tamuruka an natruka ma ya'budu abaona aw an naf'ala fee amwalina ma nashao innaka laanta alhaleemu a **l** rrasheed **u**

# 1561

Qala ya qawmi araaytum in kuntu 'ala bayyinatin min rabbee warazaqanee minhu rizqan hasanan wama oreedu an okhalifakum ila ma anhakum 'anhu in oreedu illa alislaha ma istata'tu wama tawfeeqee illa bi **A** llahi 'alayhi tawakkatu wailayhi oneeb **u**

# 1562

Waya qawmi la yajrimannakum shiqaqee an yuseebakum mithlu ma asaba qawma noohin aw qawma hoodin aw qawma salihin wama qawmu lootin minkum biba'eed **in**

# 1563

Wa **i** staghfiroo rabbakum thumma tooboo ilayhi inna rabbee raheemun wadood **un**

# 1564

Qaloo ya shu'aybu ma nafqahu katheeran mimma taqoolu wainna lanaraka feenada'eefan walawla rahtuka larajamnaka wama anta 'alayna bi'azeez **in**

# 1565

Qala ya qawmi arahtee a'azzu 'alaykum mina Allahi wa **i** ttakhathtumoohu waraakum _th_ ihriyyan inna rabbee bima ta'maloona muheet **un**

# 1566

Waya qawmi i'maloo 'ala makanatikum innee 'amilun sawfa ta'lamoona man yateehi 'athabun yukhzeehi waman huwa kathibun wa **i** rtaqiboo inne ma'akum raqeeb **un**

# 1567

Walamma jaa amruna najjayna shu'ayban wa **a** llatheena amanoo ma'ahu birahmatin minna waakhathati allatheena _th_ alamoo a **l** ssayhatu faasbahoo fee diyarihim jathimeen **a**

# 1568

Kaan lam yaghnaw feeha ala bu'dan limadyana kama ba'idat thamood **u**

# 1569

Walaqad arsana moosa biayatina wasultanin mubeen **in**

# 1570

Ila fir'awna wamalaihi fa **i** ttaba'oo amra fir'awna wama amru fir'awna birasheed **in**

# 1571

Yaqdumu qawmahu yawma alqiyamati faawradahumu a **l** nnara wabisa alwirdu almawrood **u**

# 1572

Waotbi'oo fee hathihi la'natan wayawma alqiyamati bisa a **l** rrifdu almarfood **u**

# 1573

Thalika min anbai alqura naqussuhu 'alayka minha qaimun wahaseed **un**

# 1574

Wama _th_ alamnahum walakin _th_ alamoo anfusahum fama aghnat 'anhum alihatuhumu allatee yad'oona min dooni Allahi min shayin lamma jaa amru rabbika wama zadoohum ghayra tatbeeb **in**

# 1575

Wakathalika akhthu rabbika itha akhatha alqura wahiya _th_ alimatun inna akhthahu aleemun shadeed **un**

# 1576

Inna fee thalika laayatan liman khafa 'athaba alakhirati thalika yawmun majmoo'un lahu a **l** nnasu wathalika yawmun mashhoodun

# 1577

Wama nuakhkhiruhu illa liajalin ma'dood **in**

# 1578

Yawma yati la takallamu nafsun illa biithnihi faminhum shaqiyyun wasa'eed **in**

# 1579

Faamma allatheena shaqoo fafee a **l** nnari lahum feeha zafeerun washaheeq **un**

# 1580

Khalideena feeha ma damati a **l** ssamawatu wa **a** lardu illa ma shaa rabbuka inna rabbaka fa''alun lima yureed **u**

# 1581

Waamma allatheena su'idoo fafee aljannati khalideena feeha ma damati a **l** ssamawatu wa **a** lardu illa ma shaa rabbuka 'ataan ghayra majthooth **in**

# 1582

Fala taku fee miryatin mimma ya'budu haolai ma ya'budoona illa kama ya'budu abaohum min qablu wainna lamuwaffoohum naseebahum ghayra manqoos **in**

# 1583

Walaqad atayna moosa alkitaba fa **i** khtulifa feehi walawla kalimatun sabaqat min rabbika laqudiya baynahum wainnahum lafee shakkin minhu mureeb **un**

# 1584

Wainna kullan lamma layuwaffiyannahum rabbuka a'malahum innahu bima ya'maloona khabeer **un**

# 1585

Fa **i** staqim kama omirta waman taba ma'aka wala tatghaw innahu bima ta'maloona baseer **un**

# 1586

Wala tarkanoo ila allatheena _th_ alamoo fatamassakumu a **l** nnaru wama lakum min dooni Allahi min awliyaa thumma la tunsaroon **a**

# 1587

Waaqimi a **l** ssalata tarafayi a **l** nnahari wazulafan mina allayli inna alhasanati yuthhibna a **l** ssayyiati thalika thikra li **l** ththakireen **a**

# 1588

Wa **i** sbir fainna Allaha la yudee'u ajra almuhsineen **a**

# 1589

Falawla kana mina alqurooni min qablikum oloo baqiyyatin yanhawna 'ani alfasadi fee alardi illa qaleelan mimman anjayna minhum wa **i** ttaba'a allatheena _th_ alamoo ma otrifoo feehi wakanoo mujrimeen **a**

# 1590

Wama kana rabbuka liyuhlika alqura bi _th_ ulmin waahluha muslihoon **a**

# 1591

Walaw shaa rabbuka laja'ala a **l** nnasa ommatan wahidatan wala yazaloona mukhtalifeen **a**

# 1592

Illa man rahima rabbuka walithalika khalaqahum watammat kalimatu rabbika laamlaanna jahannama mina aljinnati wa **al** nnasi ajma'een **a**

# 1593

Wakullan naqussu 'alayka min anbai a **l** rrusuli ma nuthabbitu bihi fuadaka wajaaka fee hathihi alhaqqu wamaw'i _th_ atun wathikra lilmumineen **a**

# 1594

Waqul lillatheena la yuminoona i'maloo 'ala makanatikum inna 'amiloon **a**

# 1595

Wa **i** nta _th_ iroo inna munta _th_ iroon **a**

# 1596

Walillahi ghaybu a **l** ssamawati wa **a** lardi wailayhi yurja'u alamru kulluhu fa **o** 'budhu watawakkal 'alayhi wama rabbuka bighafilin 'amma ta'maloon **a**

# 1597

Aliflamra tilka ayatu alkitabi almubeen **u**

# 1598

Inna anzanahu quranan 'arabiyyan la'allakum ta'qiloon **a**

# 1599

Nahnu naqussu 'alayka ahsana alqasasi bima awhayna ilayka hatha alqurana wain kunta min qablihi lamina alghafileen **a**

# 1600

Ith qala yoosufu liabeehi ya abati innee raaytu ahada 'ashara kawkaban wa **al** shshamsa wa **a** lqamara raaytuhum lee sajideen **a**

# 1601

Qala ya bunayya la taqsus ruyaka 'ala ikhwatika fayakeedoo laka kaydan inna a **l** shshaytana lilinsani 'aduwwun mubeen **un**

# 1602

Wakathalika yajtabeeka rabbuka wayu'allimuka min taweeli alahadeethi wayutimmu ni'matahu 'alayka wa'alaali ya'qooba kama atammaha 'ala abawayka min qablu ibraheema waishaqa inna rabbaka 'aleemun hakeem **un**

# 1603

Laqad kana fee yoosufa waikhwatihi ayatun li **l** ssaileen **a**

# 1604

Ith qaloo layoosufu waakhoohu ahabbu ila abeena minna wanahnu 'usbatun inna abana lafee dalalin mubeen **in**

# 1605

Oqtuloo yoosufa awi itrahoohu ardan yakhlu lakum wajhu abeekum watakoonoo min ba'dihi qawman saliheen **a**

# 1606

Qala qailun minhum la taqtuloo yoosufa waalqoohu fee ghayabati aljubbi yataqithu ba'du a **l** ssayyarati in kuntum fa'ileen **a**

# 1607

Qaloo ya abana ma laka la tamanna 'ala yoosufa wainna lahu lanasihoon **a**

# 1608

Arsilhu ma'ana ghadan yarta' wayal'ab wainna lahu lahafi _th_ oon **a**

# 1609

Qala innee layahzununee an thathhaboo bihi waakhafu an yakulahu a **l** ththibu waantum 'anhu ghafiloon **a**

# 1610

Qaloo lain akalahu a **l** ththibu wanahnu 'usbatun inna ithan lakhasiroon **a**

# 1611

Falammathahaboo bihi waajma'oo an yaj'aloohu fee ghayabati aljubbi waawhayna ilayhi latunabiannahum biamrihim hatha wahum la yash'uroon **a**

# 1612

Wajaoo abahum 'ishaan yabkoon **a**

# 1613

Qaloo ya abana innathahabna nastabiqu watarakna yoosufa 'inda mata'ina faakalahu a **l** ththibu wama anta bimuminin lana walaw kunnasadiqeen **a**

# 1614

Wajaoo 'ala qameesihi bidamin kathibin qala bal sawwalat lakum anfusukum amran fasabrun jameelun wa **A** llahu almusta'anu 'ala ma tasifoon **a**

# 1615

Wajaat sayyaratun faarsaloo waridahum faadla dalwahu qala ya bushra hatha ghulamun waasarroohu bida'atan wa **A** llahu 'aleemun bima ya'maloon **a**

# 1616

Washarawhu bithamanin bakhsin darahima ma'doodatin wakanoo feehi mina a **l** zzahideen **a**

# 1617

Waqala allathee ishtarahu min misra li **i** mraatihi akrimee mathwahu 'asa an yanfa'ana aw nattakhithahu waladan wakathalika makkanna liyoosufa fee alardi walinu'allimahu min taweeli alahadeethi wa **A** llahu ghalibun 'ala amrihi walakinna akthara a **l** nnasi la ya'lamoon **a**

# 1618

Walamma balagha ashuddahu ataynahu hukman wa'ilman wakathalika najzee almuhsineen **a**

# 1619

Warawadathu allatee huwa fee baytiha 'an nafsihi waghallaqati alabwaba waqalat hayta laka qala ma'atha Allahi innahu rabbee ahsana mathwaya innahu la yuflihu a **l** _thth_ alimoon **a**

# 1620

Walaqad hammat bihi wahamma biha lawla an raa burhana rabbihi kathalika linasrifa 'anhu a **l** ssooa wa **a** lfahshaa innahu min 'ibadina almukhlaseen **a**

# 1621

Wa **i** stabaqa albaba waqaddat qameesahu min duburin waalfaya sayyidaha lada albabi qalat ma jazao man arada biahlika sooan illa an yusjana aw 'athabun aleem **un**

# 1622

Qala hiya rawadatnee 'an nafsee washahida shahidun min ahliha in kana qameesuhu qudda min qubulin fasadaqat wahuwa mina alkathibeen **a**

# 1623

Wain kana qameesuhu qudda min duburin fakathabat wahuwa mina a **l** ssadiqeen **a**

# 1624

Falamma raa qameesahu qudda min duburin qala innahu min kaydikunna inna kaydakunna 'a _th_ eem **un**

# 1625

Yoosufu a'rid 'an hatha wa **i** staghfiree lithanbiki innaki kunti mina alkhatieen **a**

# 1626

Waqala niswatun fee almadeenati imraatu al'azeezi turawidu fataha 'an nafsihi qad shaghafahahubban inna lanaraha fee dalalin mubeen **in**

# 1627

Falamma sami'at bimakrihinna arsalat ilayhinna waa'tadat lahunna muttakaan waatat kulla wahidatin minhunna sikkeenan waqalati okhruj 'alayhinna falamma raaynahu akbarnahu waqatta'na aydiyahunna waqulna hasha lillahi ma hatha basharan in hatha illa malakun kareem **un**

# 1628

Qalat fathalikunna allathee lumtunnanee feehi walaqad rawadtuhu 'an nafsihi fa **i** st'sama walain lam yaf'al maamuruhu layusjananna walayakoonan mina a **l** ssaghireen **a**

# 1629

Qala rabbi a **l** ssijnu ahabbu ilayya mimma yad'oonanee ilayhi wailla tasrif 'annee kaydahunna asbu ilayhinna waakun mina aljahileen **a**

# 1630

Fa **i** stajaba lahu rabbuhu fasarafa 'anhu kaydahunna innahu huwa a **l** ssamee'u al'aleem **u**

# 1631

Thumma bada lahum min ba'di ma raawoo alayati layasjununnahu hattaheen **in**

# 1632

Wadakhala ma'ahu a **l** ssijna fatayani qala ahaduhuma innee aranee a'siru khamran waqala alakharu innee aranee ahmilu fawqa rasee khubzan takulu a **l** ttayru minhu nabbina bitaweelihi inna naraka mina almuhsineen **a**

# 1633

Qala la yateekumata'amun turzaqanihi illa nabbatukuma bitaweelihi qabla an yatiyakumathalikuma mimma 'allamanee rabbee innee taraktu millata qawmin la yuminoona bi **A** llahi wahum bi **a** lakhirati hum kafiroon **a**

# 1634

Wa **i** ttaba'tu millata abaee ibraheema waishaqa waya'qooba ma kana lana an nushrika bi **A** llahi min shayin thalika min fadli Allahi 'alayna wa'ala a **l** nnasi walakinna akthara a **l** nnasi la yashkuroon **a**

# 1635

Yasahibayi a **l** ssijni aarbabun mutafarriqoona khayrun ami Allahu alwahidu alqahhar **u**

# 1636

Ma ta'budoona min doonihi illa asmaan sammaytumooha antum waabaokum ma anzala Allahu biha min sultanin ini alhukmu illa lillahi amara alla ta'budoo illa iyyahu thalika a **l** ddeenu alqayyimu walakinna akthara a **l** nnasi la ya'lamoon **a**

# 1637

Yasahibayi a **l** ssijni amma ahadukuma fayasqee rabbahu khamran waamma alakharu fayuslabu fatakulu a **l** ttayru min rasihi qudiya alamru allathee feehi tastaftiyan **i**

# 1638

Waqala lillathee _th_ anna annahu najin minhuma othkurnee 'inda rabbika faansahu a **l** shshaytanu thikra rabbihi falabitha fee a **l** ssijni bid'a sineen **a**

# 1639

Waqala almaliku innee ara sab'a baqaratin simanin yakuluhunna sab'un 'ijafun wasab'a sunbulatin khudrin waokhara yabisatin ya ayyuha almalao aftoonee fee ruyaya in kuntum li **l** rruya ta'buroon **a**

# 1640

Qaloo adghathu ahlamin wama nahnu bitaweeli alahlami bi'alimeen **a**

# 1641

Waqala allathee naja minhuma wa **i** ddakara ba'da ommatin ana onabbiokum bitaweelihi faarsiloon **i**

# 1642

Yoosufu ayyuha a **l** ssiddeequ aftina fee sab'i baqaratin simanin yakuluhunna sab'un 'ijafun wasab'i sunbulatin khudrin waokhara yabisatin la'allee arji'u ila a **l** nnasi la'allahum ya'lamoon **a**

# 1643

Qala tazra'oona sab'a sineena daaban famahasadtum fatharoohu fee sunbulihi illa qaleelan mimma takuloon **a**

# 1644

Thumma yatee min ba'di thalika sab'un shidadun yakulna ma qaddamtum lahunna illa qaleelan mimma tuhsinoon **a**

# 1645

Thumma yatee min ba'di thalika 'amun feehi yughathu a **l** nnasu wafeehi ya'siroon **a**

# 1646

Waqala almaliku itoonee bihi falamma jaahu a **l** rrasoolu qala irji' ila rabbika fa **i** salhu ma balu a **l** nniswati allatee qatta'na aydiyahunna inna rabbee bikaydihinna 'aleem **un**

# 1647

Qala ma khatbukunna ith rawadtunna yoosufa 'an nafsihi qulna hasha lillahi ma 'alimna 'alayhi min sooin qalati imraatu al'azeezi alana hashasa alhaqqu ana rawadtuhu 'an nafsihi wainnahu lamina a **l** ssadiqeen **a**

# 1648

Thalika liya'lama annee lam akhunhu bi **a** lghaybi waanna Allaha la yahdee kayda alkhaineen **a**

# 1649

Wama obarrio nafsee inna a **l** nnafsa laammaratun bi **al** ssooi illa ma rahima rabbee inna rabbee ghafoorun raheem **un**

# 1650

Waqala almaliku itoonee bihi astakhlishu linafsee falamma kallamahu qala innaka alyawma ladayna makeenun ameen **un**

# 1651

Qala ij'anee 'ala khazaini alardi innee hafee _th_ un 'aleem **un**

# 1652

Wakathalika makanna liyoosufa fee alardi yatabawwao minhahaythu yashao nuseebu birahmatina man nashao wala nudee'u ajra almuhsineen **a**

# 1653

Walaajru alakhirati khayrun lillatheena amanoo wakanoo yattaqoon **a**

# 1654

Wajaa ikhwatu yoosufa fadakhaloo 'alayhi fa'arafahum wahum lahu munkiroon **a**

# 1655

Walamma jahhazahum bijahazihim qala itoonee biakhin lakum min abeekum ala tarawna annee oofee alkayla waana khayru almunzileen **a**

# 1656

Fain lam tatoonee bihi fala kayla lakum 'indee wala taqraboon **i**

# 1657

Qaloo sanurawidu 'anhu abahu wainna lafa'iloon **a**

# 1658

Waqala lifityanihi ij'aloo bida'atahum fee rihalihim la'allahum ya'rifoonaha itha inqalaboo ila ahlihim la'allahum yarji'oon **a**

# 1659

Falamma raja'oo ila abeehim qaloo ya abana muni'a minna alkaylu faarsil ma'ana akhana naktal wainna lahu lahafi _th_ oon **a**

# 1660

Qala hal amanukum 'alayhi illa kama amintukum 'ala akheehi min qablu fa **A** llahu khayrun hafi _th_ an wahuwa arhamu a **l** rrahimeen **a**

# 1661

Walamma fatahoo mata'ahum wajadoo bida'atahum ruddat ilayhim qaloo ya abana ma nabghee hathihi bida'atuna ruddat ilayna wanameeru ahlana wanahfa _th_ u akhana wanazdadu kayla ba'eerin thalika kaylun yaseer **un**

# 1662

Qala lan orsilahu ma'akum hatta tutooni mawthiqan mina Allahi latatunnanee bihi illa an yuhata bikum falammaatawhu mawthiqahum qala Allahu 'ala ma naqoolu wakeel **un**

# 1663

Waqala ya baniyya la tadkhuloo min babin wahidin wa **o** dkhuloo min abwabin mutafarriqatin wama oghnee 'ankum mina Allahi min shayin ini alhukmu illa lillahi 'alayhi tawakkatu wa'alayhi falyatawakkali almutawakkiloon **a**

# 1664

Walamma dakhaloo min haythu amarahum aboohum ma kana yughnee 'anhum mina Allahi min shayin illahajatan fee nafsi ya'qooba qadaha wainnahu lathoo 'ilmin lima 'allamnahu walakinna akthara a **l** nnasi la ya'lamoon **a**

# 1665

Walamma dakhaloo 'ala yoosufa awa ilayhi akhahu qala innee ana akhooka fala tabtais bima kanoo ya'maloon **a**

# 1666

Falamma jahhazahum bijahazihim ja'ala a **l** ssiqayata fee rahli akheehi thumma aththana muaththinun ayyatuha al'eeru innakum lasariqoon **a**

# 1667

Qaloo waaqbaloo 'alayhim matha tafqidoon **a**

# 1668

Qaloo nafqidu suwa'a almaliki waliman jaa bihi himlu ba'eerin waana bihi za'eem **un**

# 1669

Qaloo ta **A** llahi laqad 'alimtum ma jina linufsida fee alardi wama kunna sariqeen **a**

# 1670

Qaloo fama jazaohu in kuntum kathibeen **a**

# 1671

Qaloo jazaohu man wujida fee rahlihi fahuwa jazaohu kathalika najzee a **l** _thth_ alimeen **a**

# 1672

Fabadaa biaw'iyatihim qabla wi'ai akheehi thumma istakhrajaha min wi'ai akheehi kathalika kidna liyoosufa ma kana liyakhutha akhahu fee deeni almaliki illa an yashaa Allahu narfa'u darajatin man nashao wafawqa kulli thee 'ilmin 'aleem **un**

# 1673

Qaloo in yasriq faqad saraqa akhun lahu min qablu faasarraha yoosufu fee nafsihi walam yubdiha lahum qala antum sharrun makanan wa **A** llahu a'lamu bima tasifoon **a**

# 1674

Qaloo ya ayyuha al'azeezu inna lahu aban shaykhan kabeeran fakhuth ahadana makanahu inna naraka mina almuhsineen **a**

# 1675

Qala ma'atha Allahi an nakhutha illa man wajadna mata'ana 'indahu inna ithan la _th_ alimoon **a**

# 1676

Falamma istayasoo minhu khalasoo najiyyan qala kabeeruhum alam ta'lamoo anna abakum qad akhatha 'alaykum mawthiqan mina Allahi wamin qablu ma farrattum fee yoosufa falan abraha alarda hatta yathana lee abee aw yahkuma Allahu lee wahuwa khayru alhakimeen **a**

# 1677

Irji'oo ila abeekum faqooloo ya abana inna ibnaka saraqa wama shahidna illa bima 'alimna wama kunna lilghaybi hafi _th_ een **a**

# 1678

Wa **i** sali alqaryata allatee kunna feeha wa **a** l'eera allatee aqbana feeha wainna lasadiqoon **a**

# 1679

Qala bal sawwalat lakum anfusukum amran fasabrun jameelun 'asa Allahu an yatiyanee bihim jamee'an innahu huwa al'aleemu alhakeem **u**

# 1680

Watawalla 'anhum waqala ya asafa 'ala yoosufa wa **i** byaddat 'aynahu mina alhuzni fahuwa ka _th_ eem **un**

# 1681

Qaloo ta **A** llahi taftao tathkuru yoosufa hatta takoona haradan aw takoona mina alhalikeen **a**

# 1682

Qala innama ashkoo baththee wahuznee ila Allahi waa'lamu mina Allahi ma la ta'lamoon **a**

# 1683

Ya baniyya ithhaboo fatahassasoo min yoosufa waakheehi wala tayasoo min rawhi Allahi innahu la yayasu min rawhi Allahi illa alqawmu alkafiroon **a**

# 1684

Falamma dakhaloo 'alayhi qaloo ya ayyuha al'azeezu massana waahlana a **l** ddurru wajina bibida'atin muzjatin faawfi lana alkayla watasaddaq 'alayna inna Allaha yajzee almutasaddiqeen **a**

# 1685

Qala hal 'alimtum ma fa'atum biyoosufa waakheehi ith antum jahiloon **a**

# 1686

Qaloo ainnaka laanta yoosufa qala ana yoosufu wahatha akhee qad manna Allahu 'alayna innahu man yattaqi wayasbir fainna Allaha la yudee'u ajra almuhsineen **a**

# 1687

Qaloo ta **A** llahi laqad atharaka Allahu 'alayna wain kunna lakhatieen **a**

# 1688

Qala la tathreeba 'alaykumu alyawma yaghfiru Allahu lakum wahuwa arhamu a **l** rrahimeen **a**

# 1689

Ithhaboo biqameesee hatha faalqoohu 'ala wajhi abee yati baseeran watoonee biahlikum ajma'een **a**

# 1690

Walamma fasalati al'eeru qala aboohum innee laajidu reeha yoosufa lawla an tufannidoon **i**

# 1691

Qaloo ta **A** llahi innaka lafee dalalika alqadeem **i**

# 1692

Falamma an jaa albasheeru alqahu 'ala wajhihi fa **i** rtadda baseeran qala alam aqul lakum innee a'lamu mina Allahi ma la ta'lamoon **a**

# 1693

Qaloo ya abana istaghfir lanathunoobana inna kunna khatieen **a**

# 1694

Qala sawfa astaghfiru lakum rabbee innahu huwa alghafooru a **l** rraheem **u**

# 1695

Falamma dakhaloo 'ala yoosufa awa ilayhi abawayhi waqala odkhuloo misra in shaa Allahu amineen **a**

# 1696

Warafa'a abawayhi 'ala al'arshi wakharroo lahu sujjadan waqala ya abati hatha taweelu ruyaya min qablu qad ja'alaha rabbee haqqan waqad ahsana bee ith akhrajanee mina a **l** ssijni wajaa bikum mina albadwi min ba'di an nazagha a **l** shshaytanu baynee wabayna ikhwatee inna rabbee lateefun lima yashao innahu huwa al'aleemu alhakeem **u**

# 1697

Rabbi qad ataytanee mina almulki wa'allamtanee min taweeli alahadeethi fatira a **l** ssamawati wa **a** lardi anta waliyyee fee a **l** ddunya wa **a** lakhirati tawaffanee musliman waalhiqnee bi **al** ssaliheen **a**

# 1698

Thalika min anbai alghaybi nooheehi ilayka wama kunta ladayhim ith ajma'oo amrahum wahum yamkuroon **a**

# 1699

Wama aktharu a **l** nnasi walaw harasta bimumineen **a**

# 1700

Wama tasaluhum 'alayhi min ajrin in huwa illathikrun lil'alameen **a**

# 1701

Wakaayyin min ayatin fee a **l** ssamawati wa **a** lardi yamurroona 'alayha wahum 'anha mu'ridoon **a**

# 1702

Wama yuminu aktharuhum bi **A** llahi illa wahum mushrikoon **a**

# 1703

Afaaminoo an tatiyahum ghashiyatun min 'athabi Allahi aw tatiyahumu a **l** ssa'atu baghtatan wahum la yash'uroon **a**

# 1704

Qul hathihi sabeelee ad'oo ila Allahi 'ala baseeratin ana wamani ittaba'anee wasubhana Allahi wama ana mina almushrikeen **a**

# 1705

Wama arsana min qablika illa rijalan noohee ilayhim min ahli alqura afalam yaseeroo fee alardi fayan _th_ uroo kayfa kana 'aqibatu allatheena min qablihim waladaru alakhirati khayrun lillatheena ittaqaw afala ta'qiloon **a**

# 1706

Hatta itha istayasa a **l** rrusulu wa _th_ annoo annahum qad kuthiboo jaahum nasruna fanujjiya man nashao wala yuraddu basuna 'ani alqawmi almujrimeen **a**

# 1707

Laqad kana fee qasasihim 'ibratun liolee alalbabi ma kana hadeethan yuftara walakin tasdeeqa allathee bayna yadayhi watafseela kulli shayin wahudan warahmatan liqawmin yuminoon **a**

# 1708

Aliflammeemra tilka ayatu alkitabi wa **a** llathee onzila ilayka min rabbika alhaqqu walakinna akthara a **l** nnasi la yuminoon **a**

# 1709

Allahu allathee rafa'a a **l** ssamawati bighayri 'amadin tarawnaha thumma istawa 'ala al'arshi wasakhkhara a **l** shshamsa wa **a** lqamara kullun yajree liajalin musamman yudabbiru alamra yufassilu alayati la'allakum biliqai rabbikum tooqinoon **a**

# 1710

Wahuwa allathee madda alarda waja'ala feeha rawasiya waanharan wamin kulli a **l** ththamarati ja'ala feeha zawjayni ithnayni yughshee allayla a **l** nnahara inna fee thalika laayatin liqawmin yatafakkaroon **a**

# 1711

Wafee alardi qita'un mutajawiratun wajannatun min a'nabin wazar'un wanakheelun sinwanun waghayru sinwanin yusqa bimain wahidin wanufaddilu ba'daha 'ala ba'din fee alokuli inna fee thalika laayatin liqawmin ya'qiloon **a**

# 1712

Wain ta'jab fa'ajabun qawluhum aitha kunna turaban ainna lafee khalqin jadeedin olaika allatheena kafaroo birabbihim waolaika alaghlalu fee a'naqihim waolaika ashabu a **l** nnari hum feeha khalidoon **a**

# 1713

Wayasta'jiloonaka bi **al** ssayyiati qabla alhasanati waqad khalat min qablihimu almathulatu wainna rabbaka lathoo maghfiratin li **l** nnasi 'ala _th_ ulmihim wainna rabbaka lashadeedu al'iqab **i**

# 1714

Wayaqoolu allatheena kafaroo lawla onzila 'alayhi ayatun min rabbihi innama anta munthirun walikulli qawmin had **in**

# 1715

Allahu ya'lamu ma tahmilu kullu ontha wama tagheedu alarhamu wama tazdadu wakullu shayin 'indahu bimiqdar **in**

# 1716

'alimu alghaybi wa **al** shshahadati alkabeeru almuta'al **i**

# 1717

Sawaon minkum man asarra alqawla waman jahara bihi waman huwa mustakhfin bi **a** llayli wasaribun bi **al** nnahar **i**

# 1718

Lahu mu'aqqibatun min bayni yadayhi wamin khalfihi yahfa _th_ oonahu min amri Allahi inna Allaha la yughayyiru ma biqawmin hatta yughayyiroo ma bianfusihim waitha arada Allahu biqawmin sooan fala maradda lahu wama lahum min doonihi min wal **in**

# 1719

Huwa allathee yureekumu albarqa khawfan watama'an wayunshio a **l** ssahaba a **l** ththiqal **a**

# 1720

Wayusabbihu a **l** rra'du bihamdihi wa **a** lmalaikatu min kheefatihi wayursilu a **l** ssawa'iqa fayuseebu biha man yashao wahum yujadiloona fee Allahi wahuwa shadeedu almihal **i**

# 1721

Lahu da'watu alhaqqi wa **a** llatheena yad'oona min doonihi la yastajeeboona lahum bishayin illa kabasiti kaffayhi ila almai liyablugha fahu wama huwa bibalighihi wama du'ao alkafireena illa fee dalal **in**

# 1722

Walillahi yasjudu man fee a **l** ssamawati wa **a** lardi taw'an wakarhan wa _th_ ilaluhum bi **a** lghuduwwi wa **a** lasal **i**

# 1723

Qul man rabbu a **l** ssamawati wa **a** lardi quli Allahu qul afa **i** ttakhathtum min doonihi awliyaa la yamlikoona lianfusihim naf'an waladarran qul hal yastawee ala'ma wa **a** lbaseeru am hal tastawee a **l** _thth_ ulumatu wa **al** nnooru am ja'aloo lillahi shurakaa khalaqoo kakhalqihi fatashabaha alkhalqu 'alayhim quli Allahu khaliqu kulli shayin wahuwa alwahidu alqahhar **u**

# 1724

Anzala mina a **l** ssamai maan fasalat awdiyatun biqadariha fa **i** htamala a **l** ssaylu zabadan rabiyan wamimma yooqidoona 'alayhi fee a **l** nnari ibtighaa hilyatin aw mata'in zabadun mithluhu kathalika yadribu Allahu alhaqqa wa **a** lbatila faamma a **l** zzabadu fayathhabu jufaan waamma ma yanfa'u a **l** nnasa fayamkuthu fee alardi kathalika yadribu Allahu alamthal **a**

# 1725

Lillatheena istajaboo lirabbihimu alhusna wa **a** llatheena lam yastajeeboo lahu law anna lahum ma fee alardi jamee'an wamithlahu ma'ahu la **i** ftadaw bihi olaika lahum sooo alhisabi wamawahum jahannamu wabisa almihad **u**

# 1726

Afaman ya'lamu annama onzila ilayka min rabbika alhaqqu kaman huwa a'ma innama yatathakkaru oloo alalbab **i**

# 1727

Allatheena yoofoona bi'ahdi Allahi wala yanqudoona almeethaq **a**

# 1728

Wa **a** llatheena yasiloona ma amara Allahu bihi an yoosala wayakhshawna rabbahum wayakhafoona sooa alhisab **i**

# 1729

Wa **a** llatheena sabaroo ibtighaa wajhi rabbihim waaqamoo a **l** ssalata waanfaqoo mimma razaqnahum sirran wa'alaniyatan wayadraoona bi **a** lhasanati a **l** ssayyiata olaika lahum 'uqba a **l** ddar **i**

# 1730

Jannatu 'adnin yadkhuloonaha waman salaha min abaihim waazwajihim wathurriyyatihim wa **a** lmalaikatu yadkhuloona 'alayhim min kulli bab **in**

# 1731

Salamun 'alaykum bimasabartum fani'ma 'uqba a **l** ddar **i**

# 1732

Wa **a** llatheena yanqudoona 'ahda Allahi min ba'di meethaqihi wayaqta'oona ma amara Allahu bihi an yoosala wayufsidoona fee alardi olaika lahumu alla'natu walahum sooo a **l** ddar **i**

# 1733

Allahu yabsutu a **l** rrizqa liman yashao wayaqdiru wafarihoo bi **a** lhayati a **l** ddunya wama alhayatu a **l** ddunya fee alakhirati illa mata' **un**

# 1734

Wayaqoolu allatheena kafaroo lawla onzila 'alayhi ayatun min rabbihi qul inna Allaha yudillu man yashao wayahdee ilayhi man anab **a**

# 1735

Allatheena amanoo watatmainnu quloobuhum bithikri Allahi ala bithikri Allahi tatmainnu alquloob **u**

# 1736

Allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo a **l** ssalihati tooba lahum wahusnu maab **in**

# 1737

Kathalika arsanaka fee ommatin qad khalat min qabliha omamun litatluwa 'alayhimu allathee awhayna ilayka wahum yakfuroona bi **al** rrahmani qul huwa rabbee la ilaha illa huwa 'alayhi tawakkatu wailayhi matab **i**

# 1738

Walaw anna quranan suyyirat bihi aljibalu aw qutti'at bihi alardu aw kullima bihi almawta bal lillahi alamru jamee'an afalam yayasi allatheena amanoo an law yashao Allahu lahada a **l** nnasa jamee'an wala yazalu allatheena kafaroo tuseebuhum bimasana'oo qari'atun aw tahullu qareeban min darihim hatta yatiya wa'du Allahi inna Allaha la yukhlifu almee'ad **a**

# 1739

Walaqadi istuhzia birusulin min qablika faamlaytu lillatheena kafaroo thumma akhathtuhum fakayfa kana 'iqab **i**

# 1740

Afaman huwa qaimun 'ala kulli nafsin bima kasabat waja'aloo lillahi shurakaa qul sammoohum am tunabbioonahu bima la ya'lamu fee alardi am bi _th_ ahirin mina alqawli bal zuyyina lillatheena kafaroo makruhum wasuddoo 'ani a **l** ssabeeli waman yudlili Allahu fama lahu min had **in**

# 1741

Lahum 'athabun fee alhayati a **l** ddunya wala'athabu alakhirati ashaqqu wama lahum mina Allahi min waq **in**

# 1742

Mathalu aljannati allatee wu'ida almuttaqoona tajree min tahtiha alanharu okuluha daimun wa _th_ illuha tilka 'uqba allatheena ittaqaw wa'uqba alkafireena a **l** nnar **u**

# 1743

Wa **a** llatheena ataynahumu alkitaba yafrahoona bima onzila ilayka wamina alahzabi man yunkiru ba'dahu qul innama omirtu an a'buda Allaha wala oshrika bihi ilayhi ad'oo wailayhi maab **i**

# 1744

Wakathalika anzanahu hukman 'arabiyyan walaini ittaba'ta ahwaahum ba'da ma jaaka mina al'ilmi ma laka mina Allahi min waliyyin wala waq **in**

# 1745

Walaqad arsana rusulan min qablika waja'ana lahum azwajan wathurriyyatan wama kana lirasoolin an yatiya biayatin illa biithni Allahi likulli ajalin kitab **un**

# 1746

Yamhoo Allahu ma yashao wayuthbitu wa'indahu ommu alkitab **i**

# 1747

Wain ma nuriyannaka ba'da allathee na'iduhum aw natawaffayannaka fainnama 'alayka albalaghu wa'alayna alhisab **u**

# 1748

Awalam yaraw anna natee alarda nanqusuha min atrafiha wa **A** llahu yahkumu la mu'aqqiba lihukmihi wahuwa saree'u alhisab **i**

# 1749

Waqad makara allatheena min qablihim falillahi almakru jamee'an ya'lamu ma taksibu kullu nafsin wasaya'lamu alkuffaru liman 'uqba a **l** ddar **i**

# 1750

Wayaqoolu allatheena kafaroo lasta mursalan qul kafa bi **A** llahi shaheedan baynee wabaynakum waman 'indahu 'ilmu alkitab **i**

# 1751

Aliflamra kitabun anzanahu ilayka litukhrija a **l** nnasa mina a **l** _thth_ ulumati ila a **l** nnoori biithni rabbihim ilasirati al'azeezi alhameed **i**

# 1752

Allahi allathee lahu ma fee a **l** ssamawati wama fee alardi wawaylun lilkafireena min 'athabin shadeed **in**

# 1753

Allatheena yastahibboona alhayata a **l** ddunya 'ala alakhirati wayasuddoona 'an sabeeli Allahi wayabghoonaha 'iwajan olaika fee dalalin ba'eed **in**

# 1754

Wama arsana min rasoolin illa bilisani qawmihi liyubayyina lahum fayudillu Allahu man yashao wayahdee man yashao wahuwa al'azeezu alhakeem **u**

# 1755

Walaqad arsana moosa biayatina an akhrij qawmaka mina a **l** _thth_ ulumati ila a **l** nnoori wathakkirhum biayyami Allahi inna fee thalika laayatin likulli sabbarin shakoor **in**

# 1756

Waith qala moosa liqawmihi othkuroo ni'mata Allahi 'alaykum ith anjakum min ali fir'awna yasoomoonakum sooa al'athabi wayuthabbihoona abnaakum wayastahyoona nisaakum wafee thalikum balaon min rabbikum 'a _th_ eem **un**

# 1757

Waith taaththana rabbukum lain shakartum laazeedannakum walain kafartum inna 'athabee lashadeed **un**

# 1758

Waqala moosa in takfuroo antum waman fee alardi jamee'an fainna Allaha laghaniyyun hameed **un**

# 1759

Alam yatikum nabao allatheena min qablikum qawmi noohin wa'adin wathamooda wa **a** llatheena min ba'dihim la ya'lamuhum illa Allahu jaathum rusuluhum bi **a** lbayyinati faraddoo aydiyahum fee afwahihim waqaloo inna kafarna bima orsiltum bihi wainna lafee shakkin mimma tad'oonana ilayhi mureeb **un**

# 1760

Qalat rusuluhum afee Allahi shakkun fatiri a **l** ssamawati wa **a** lardi yad'ookum liyaghfira lakum min thunoobikum wayuakhkhirakum ila ajalin musamman qaloo in antum illa basharun mithluna tureedoona an tasuddoona 'amma kana ya'budu abaona fatoona bisultanin mubeen **in**

# 1761

Qalat lahum rusuluhum in nahnu illa basharun mithlukum walakinna Allaha yamunnu 'ala man yashao min 'ibadihi wama kana lana an natiyakum bisultanin illa biithni Allahi wa'ala Allahi falyatawakkali almuminoon **a**

# 1762

Wama lana alla natawakkala 'ala Allahi waqad hadana subulana walanasbiranna 'ala maathaytumoona wa'ala Allahi falyatawakkali almutawakkiloon **a**

# 1763

Waqala allatheena kafaroo lirusulihim lanukhrijannakum min ardina aw lata'oodunna fee millatina faawha ilayhim rabbuhum lanuhlikanna a **l** _thth_ alimeen **a**

# 1764

Walanuskinannakumu alarda min ba'dihim thalika liman khafa maqamee wakhafa wa'eed **i**

# 1765

Wa **i** staftahoo wakhaba kullu jabbarin 'aneed **in**

# 1766

Min waraihi jahannamu wayusqa min main sadeed **in**

# 1767

Yatajarra'uhu wala yakadu yuseeghuhu wayateehi almawtu min kulli makanin wama huwa bimayyitin wamin waraihi 'athabun ghalee _th_ **un**

# 1768

Mathalu allatheena kafaroo birabbihim a'maluhum karamadin ishtaddat bihi a **l** rreehu fee yawmin 'asifin la yaqdiroona mimma kasaboo 'ala shayin thalika huwa a **l** ddalalu alba'eed **u**

# 1769

Alam tara anna Allaha khalaqa a **l** ssamawati wa **a** larda bi **a** lhaqqi in yasha yuthhibkum wayati bikhalqin jadeed **in**

# 1770

Wamathalika 'ala Allahi bi'azeez **in**

# 1771

Wabarazoo lillahi jamee'an faqala a **l** ddu'afao lillatheena istakbaroo inna kunna lakum taba'an fahal antum mughnoona 'anna min 'athabi Allahi min shayin qaloo law hadana Allahu lahadaynakum sawaon 'alayna ajazi'na am sabarna ma lana min mahees **in**

# 1772

Waqala a **l** shshaytanu lamma qudiya alamru inna Allaha wa'adakum wa'da alhaqqi wawa'adtukum faakhlaftukum wama kana liya 'alaykum min sultanin illa an da'awtukum fa **i** stajabtum lee fala taloomoonee waloomoo anfusakum ma ana bimusrikhikum wama antum bimusrikhiyya innee kafartu bima ashraktumooni min qablu inna a **l** _thth_ alimeena lahum 'athabun aleem **un**

# 1773

Waodkhila allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo a **l** ssalihati jannatin tajree min tahtiha alanharu khalideena feeha biithni rabbihim tahiyyatuhum feeha salam **un**

# 1774

Alam tara kayfa daraba Allahu mathalan kalimatan tayyibatan kashajaratin tayyibatin asluha thabitun wafar'uha fee a **l** ssama **i**

# 1775

Tutee okulaha kulla heenin biithni rabbiha wayadribu Allahu alamthala li **l** nnasi la'allahum yatathakkaroon **a**

# 1776

Wamathalu kalimatin khabeethatin kashajaratin khabeethatin ijtuththat min fawqi alardi ma laha min qarar **in**

# 1777

Yuthabbitu Allahu allatheena amanoo bi **a** lqawli a **l** ththabiti fee alhayati a **l** ddunya wafee alakhirati wayudillu Allahu a **l** _thth_ alimeena wayaf'alu Allahu ma yasha **o**

# 1778

Alam tara ila allatheena baddaloo ni'mata Allahi kufran waahalloo qawmahum dara albawar **i**

# 1779

Jahannama yaslawnaha wabisa alqarar **u**

# 1780

Waja'aloo lillahi andadan liyudilloo 'an sabeelihi qul tamatta'oo fainna maseerakum ila a **l** nnar **i**

# 1781

Qul li'ibadiya allatheena amanoo yuqeemoo a **l** ssalata wayunfiqoo mimma razaqnahum sirran wa'alaniyatan min qabli an yatiya yawmun la bay'un feehi wala khilal **un**

# 1782

Allahu allathee khalaqa a **l** ssamawati wa **a** larda waanzala mina a **l** ssamai maan faakhraja bihi mina a **l** ththamarati rizqan lakum wasakhkhara lakumu alfulka litajriya fee albahri biamrihi wasakhkhara lakumu alanhar **a**

# 1783

Wasakhkhara lakumu a **l** shshamsa wa **a** lqamara daibayni wasakhkhara lakumu allayla wa **al** nnahar **a**

# 1784

Waatakum min kulli ma saatumoohu wain ta'uddoo ni'mata Allahi la tuhsooha inna alinsana la _th_ aloomun kaffar **un**

# 1785

Waith qala ibraheemu rabbi ij'al hatha albalada aminan wa **o** jnubnee wabaniyya an na'buda alasnam **a**

# 1786

Rabbi innahunna adlana katheeran mina a **l** nnasi faman tabi'anee fainnahu minnee waman 'asanee fainnaka ghafoorun raheem **un**

# 1787

Rabbana innee askantu min thurriyyatee biwadin ghayri thee zar'in 'inda baytika almuharrami rabbana liyuqeemoo a **l** ssalata fa **i** j'al afidatan mina a **l** nnasi tahwee ilayhim wa **o** rzuqhum mina a **l** ththamarati la'allahum yashkuroon **a**

# 1788

Rabbana innaka ta'lamu ma nukhfee wama nu'linu wama yakhfa 'ala Allahi min shayin fee alardi wala fee a **l** ssama **i**

# 1789

Alhamdu lillahi allathee wahaba lee 'ala alkibari isma'eela waishaqa inna rabbee lasamee'u a **l** ddu'a **i**

# 1790

Rabbi ij'anee muqeema a **l** ssalati wamin thurriyyatee rabbana wtaqabbal du'a **i**

# 1791

Rabbana ighfir lee waliwalidayya walilmumineena yawma yaqoomu alhisab **u**

# 1792

Wala tahsabanna Allaha ghafilan 'amma ya'malu a **l** _thth_ alimoona innama yuakhkhiruhum liyawmin tashkhasu feehi alabsar **u**

# 1793

Muhti'eena muqni'ee ruoosihim la yartaddu ilayhim tarfuhum waafidatuhum hawa **on**

# 1794

Waanthiri a **l** nnasa yawma yateehimu al'athabu fayaqoolu allatheena _th_ alamoo rabbana akhkhirna ila ajalin qareebin nujib da'wataka wanattabi'i a **l** rrusula awalam takoonoo aqsamtum min qablu ma lakum min zawal **in**

# 1795

Wasakantum fee masakini allatheena _th_ alamoo anfusahum watabayyana lakum kayfa fa'ana bihim wadarabna lakumu alamthal **a**

# 1796

Waqad makaroo makrahum wa'inda Allahi makruhum wain kana makruhum litazoola minhu aljibal **u**

# 1797

Fala tahsabanna Allaha mukhlifa wa'dihi rusulahu inna Allaha 'azeezun thoo intiqam **in**

# 1798

Yawma tubaddalu alardu ghayra alardi wa **al** ssamawatu wabarazoo lillahi alwahidi alqahhar **i**

# 1799

Watara almujrimeena yawmaithin muqarraneena fee alasfad **i**

# 1800

Sarabeeluhum min qatranin wataghsha wujoohahumu a **l** nnar **u**

# 1801

Liyajziya Allahu kulla nafsin ma kasabat inna Allaha saree'u alhisab **i**

# 1802

Hatha balaghun li **l** nnasi waliyuntharoo bihi waliya'lamoo annama huwa ilahun wahidun waliyaththakkara oloo alalbab **i**

# 1803

Aliflamra tilka ayatu alkitabi waquranin mubeen **in**

# 1804

Rubama yawaddu allatheena kafaroo law kanoo muslimeen **a**

# 1805

Tharhum yakuloo wayatamatta'oo wayulhihimu alamalu fasawfa ya'lamoon **a**

# 1806

Wama ahlakna min qaryatin illa walaha kitabun ma'loom **un**

# 1807

Ma tasbiqu min ommatin ajalaha wama yastakhiroon **a**

# 1808

Waqaloo ya ayyuha allathee nuzzila 'alayhi a **l** ththikru innaka lamajnoon **un**

# 1809

Law ma tateena bi **a** lmalaikati in kunta mina a **l** ssadiqeen **a**

# 1810

Ma nunazzilu almalaikata illa bi **a** lhaqqi wama kanoo ithan mun _th_ areen **a**

# 1811

Inna nahnu nazzana a **l** ththikra wainna lahu lahafi _th_ oon **a**

# 1812

Walaqad arsana min qablika fee shiya'i alawwaleen **a**

# 1813

Wama yateehim min rasoolin illa kanoo bihi yastahzioon **a**

# 1814

Kathalika naslukuhu fee quloobi almujrimeen **a**

# 1815

La yuminoona bihi waqad khalat sunnatu alawwaleen **a**

# 1816

Walaw fatahna 'alayhim baban mina a **l** ssamai fa _th_ alloo feehi ya'rujoon **a**

# 1817

Laqaloo innama sukkirat absaruna bal nahnu qawmun mashooroon **a**

# 1818

Walaqad ja'ana fee a **l** ssamai buroojan wazayyannaha li **l** nna _th_ ireen **a**

# 1819

Wahafi _th_ naha min kulli shaytanin rajeem **in**

# 1820

Illa mani istaraqa a **l** ssam'a faatba'ahu shihabun mubeen **un**

# 1821

Wa **a** larda madadnaha waalqayna feeha rawasiya waanbatna feeha min kulli shayin mawzoon **in**

# 1822

Waja'ana lakum feeha ma'ayisha waman lastum lahu biraziqeen **a**

# 1823

Wain min shayin illa 'indana khazainuhu wama nunazziluhu illa biqadarin ma'loom **in**

# 1824

Waarsana a **l** rriyaha lawaqiha faanzana mina a **l** ssamai maan faasqaynakumoohu wama antum lahu bikhazineen **a**

# 1825

Wainna lanahnu nuhyee wanumeetu wanahnu alwarithoon **a**

# 1826

Walaqad 'alimna almustaqdimeena minkum walaqad 'alimna almustakhireen **a**

# 1827

Wainna rabbaka huwa yahshuruhum innahu hakeemun 'aleem **un**

# 1828

Walaqad khalaqna alinsana min sasalin min hamain masnoon **in**

# 1829

Wa **a** ljanna khalaqnahu min qablu min nari a **l** ssamoom **i**

# 1830

Waith qala rabbuka lilmalaikati innee khaliqun basharan min sasalin min hamain masnoon **in**

# 1831

Faitha sawwaytuhu wanafakhtu feehi min roohee faqa'oo lahu sajideen **a**

# 1832

Fasajada almalaikatu kulluhum ajma'oon **a**

# 1833

Illa ibleesa aba an yakoona ma'a a **l** ssajideen **a**

# 1834

Qala ya ibleesu ma laka alla takoona ma'a a **l** ssajideen **a**

# 1835

Qala lam akun liasjuda libasharin khalaqtahu min sasalin min hamain masnoon **in**

# 1836

Qala fa **o** khruj minha fainnaka rajeem **un**

# 1837

Wainna 'alayka alla'nata ila yawmi a **l** ddeen **i**

# 1838

Qala rabbi faan _th_ irnee ila yawmi yub'athoon **a**

# 1839

Qala fainnaka mina almun _th_ areen **a**

# 1840

Ila yawmi alwaqti alma'loom **i**

# 1841

Qala rabbi bima aghwaytanee laozayyinanna lahum fee alardi walaoghwiyannahum ajma'een **a**

# 1842

Illa 'ibadaka minhumu almukhlaseen **a**

# 1843

Qala hathasiratun 'alayya mustaqeem **un**

# 1844

Inna 'ibadee laysa laka 'alayhim sultanun illa mani ittaba'aka mina alghaween **a**

# 1845

Wainna jahannama lamaw'iduhum ajma'een **a**

# 1846

Laha sab'atu abwabin likulli babin minhum juzon maqsoom **un**

# 1847

Inna almuttaqeena fee jannatin wa'uyoon **in**

# 1848

Odkhulooha bisalamin amineen **a**

# 1849

Wanaza'na ma fee sudoorihim min ghillin ikhwanan 'ala sururin mutaqabileen **a**

# 1850

La yamassuhum feeha nasabun wama hum minha bimukhrajeen **a**

# 1851

Nabbi 'ibadee annee ana alghafooru a **l** rraheem **u**

# 1852

Wa anna 'athabee huwa al'athabu alaleem **u**

# 1853

Wanabbihum 'an dayfi ibraheem **a**

# 1854

Ith dakhaloo 'alayhi faqaloo salaman qala inna minkum wajiloon **a**

# 1855

Qaloo la tawjal inna nubashshiruka bighulamin 'aleem **in**

# 1856

Qala abashshartumoonee 'ala an massaniya alkibaru fabima tubashshiroon **i**

# 1857

Qaloo bashsharnaka bi **a** lhaqqi fala takun mina alqaniteen **a**

# 1858

Qala waman yaqnatu min rahmati rabbihi illa a **l** ddalloon **a**

# 1859

Qala fama khatbukum ayyuha almursaloon **a**

# 1860

Qaloo inna orsilna ila qawmin mujrimeen **a**

# 1861

Illaala lootin inna lamunajjoohum ajma'een **a**

# 1862

Illa imraatahu qaddarna innaha lamina alghabireen **a**

# 1863

Falamma jaa ala lootin almursaloon **a**

# 1864

Qala innakum qawmun munkaroon **a**

# 1865

Qaloo bal jinaka bima kanoo feehi yamtaroon **a**

# 1866

Waataynaka bi **a** lhaqqi wainna lasadiqoon **a**

# 1867

Faasri biahlika biqit'in mina allayli wa **i** ttabi' adbarahum wala yatafit minkum ahadun wa **i** mdoo haythu tumaroon **a**

# 1868

Waqadayna ilayhi thalika alamra anna dabira haolai maqtoo'un musbiheen **a**

# 1869

Wajaa ahlu almadeenati yastabshiroon **a**

# 1870

Qala inna haolai dayfee fala tafdahoon **i**

# 1871

Wa **i** ttaqoo Allaha wala tukhzoon **i**

# 1872

Qaloo awalam nanhaka 'ani al'alameen **a**

# 1873

Qala haolai banatee in kuntum fa'ileen **a**

# 1874

La'amruka innahum lafee sakratihim ya'mahoona

# 1875

Faakhathathumu a **l** ssayhatu mushriqeen **a**

# 1876

Faja'ana 'aliyaha safilaha waamtarna 'alayhim hijaratan min sijjeel **in**

# 1877

Inna fee thalika laayatin lilmutawassimeen **a**

# 1878

Wainnaha labisabeelin muqeem **in**

# 1879

Inna fee thalika laayatan lilmumineen **a**

# 1880

Wain kana ashabu alaykati la _th_ alimeen **a**

# 1881

Fa **i** ntaqamna minhum wainnahuma labiimamin mubeen **in**

# 1882

Walaqad kaththaba ashabu alhijri almursaleen **a**

# 1883

Waataynahum ayatina fakanoo 'anha mu'rideen **a**

# 1884

Wakanoo yanhitoona mina aljibali buyootan amineen **a**

# 1885

Faakhathathumu a **l** ssayhatu musbiheen **a**

# 1886

Fama aghna 'anhum ma kanoo yaksiboon **a**

# 1887

Wama khalaqna a **l** ssamawati wa **a** larda wama baynahuma illa bi **a** lhaqqi wainna a **l** ssa'ata laatiyatun fa **i** sfahi a **l** ssafha aljameel **a**

# 1888

Inna rabbaka huwa alkhallaqu al'aleem **u**

# 1889

Walaqad ataynaka sab'an mina almathanee wa **a** lqurana al'a _th_ eem **a**

# 1890

La tamuddanna 'aynayka ila ma matta'na bihi azwajan minhum wala tahzan 'alayhim wa **i** khfid janahaka lilmumineen **a**

# 1891

Waqul innee ana a **l** nnatheeru almubeen **u**

# 1892

Kama anzana 'ala almuqtasimeen **a**

# 1893

Allatheena ja'aloo alqurana 'ideen **a**

# 1894

Fawarabbika lanasalannahum ajma'een **a**

# 1895

'amma kanoo ya'maloon **a**

# 1896

Fa **i** sda' bima tumaru waa'rid 'ani almushrikeen **a**

# 1897

Inna kafaynaka almustahzieen **a**

# 1898

Allatheena yaj'aloona ma'a Allahi ilahan akhara fasawfa ya'lamoon **a**

# 1899

Walaqad na'lamu annaka yadeequ sadruka bima yaqooloon **a**

# 1900

Fasabbih bihamdi rabbika wakun mina a **l** ssajideen **a**

# 1901

Wa **o** 'bud rabbaka hatta yatiyaka alyaqeen **u**

# 1902

Ata amru Allahi fala tasta'jiloohu subhanahu wata'ala 'amma yushrikoon **a**

# 1903

Yunazzilu almalaikata bi **al** rroohi min amrihi 'ala man yashao min 'ibadihi an anthiroo annahu la ilaha illa ana fa **i** ttaqoon **i**

# 1904

Khalaqa a **l** ssamawati wa **a** larda bi **a** lhaqqi ta'ala 'amma yushrikoon **a**

# 1905

Khalaqa alinsana min nutfatin faitha huwa khaseemun mubeen **un**

# 1906

Wa **a** lan'ama khalaqaha lakum feeha difon wamanafi'u waminha takuloon **a**

# 1907

Walakum feeha jamalun heena tureehoona waheena tasrahoon **a**

# 1908

Watahmilu athqalakum ila baladin lam takoonoo baligheehi illa bishiqqi alanfusi inna rabbakum laraoofun raheem **un**

# 1909

Wa **a** lkhayla wa **a** lbighala wa **a** lhameera litarkabooha wazeenatan wayakhluqu ma la ta'lamoon **a**

# 1910

Wa'ala Allahi qasdu a **l** ssabeeli waminha jairun walaw shaa lahadakum ajma'een **a**

# 1911

Huwa allathee anzala mina a **l** ssamai maan lakum minhu sharabun waminhu shajarun feehi tuseemoon **a**

# 1912

Yunbitu lakum bihi a **l** zzar'a wa **al** zzaytoona wa **al** nnakheela wa **a** la'naba wamin kulli a **l** ththamarati inna fee thalika laayatan liqawmin yatafakkaroon **a**

# 1913

Wasakhkhara lakumu allayla wa **al** nnahara wa **al** shshamsa wa **a** lqamara wa **al** nnujoomu musakhkharatun biamrihi inna fee thalika laayatin liqawmin ya'qiloon **a**

# 1914

Wamatharaa lakum fee alardi mukhtalifan alwanuhu inna fee thalika laayatan liqawmin yaththakkaroon **a**

# 1915

Wahuwa allathee sakhkhara albahra litakuloo minhu lahman tariyyan watastakhrijoo minhu hilyatan talbasoonaha watara alfulka mawakhira feehi walitabtaghoo min fadlihi wala'allakum tashkuroon **a**

# 1916

Waalqa fee alardi rawasiya an tameeda bikum waanharan wasubulan la'allakum tahtadoon **a**

# 1917

Wa'alamatin wabi **al** nnajmi hum yahtadoon **a**

# 1918

Afaman yakhluqu kaman la yakhluqu afala tathakkaroon **a**

# 1919

Wain ta'uddoo ni'mata Allahi la tuhsooha inna Allaha laghafoorun raheem **un**

# 1920

Wa **A** llahu ya'lamu ma tusirroona wama tu'linoon **a**

# 1921

Wa **a** llatheena yad'oona min dooni Allahi la yakhluqoona shayan wahum yukhlaqoon **a**

# 1922

Amwatun ghayru ahyain wama yash'uroona ayyana yub'athoon **a**

# 1923

Ilahukum ilahun wahidun fa **a** llatheena la yuminoona bi **a** lakhirati quloobuhum munkiratun wahum mustakbiroon **a**

# 1924

La jarama anna Allaha ya'lamu ma yusirroona wama yu'linoona innahu la yuhibbu almustakbireen **a**

# 1925

Waitha qeela lahum matha anzala rabbukum qaloo asateeru alawwaleen **a**

# 1926

Liyahmiloo awzarahum kamilatan yawma alqiyamati wamin awzari allatheena yudilloonahum bighayri 'ilmin ala saa ma yaziroon **a**

# 1927

Qad makara allatheena min qablihim faata Allahu bunyanahum mina alqawa'idi fakharra 'alayhimu a **l** ssaqfu min fawqihim waatahumu al'athabu min haythu la yash'uroon **a**

# 1928

Thumma yawma alqiyamati yukhzeehim wayaqoolu ayna shurakaiya allatheena kuntum tushaqqoona feehim qala allatheena ootoo al'ilma inna alkhizya alyawma wa **al** ssooa 'ala alkafireen **a**

# 1929

Allatheena tatawaffahumu almalaikatu _th_ alimee anfusihim faalqawoo a **l** ssalama ma kunna na'malu min sooin bala inna Allaha 'aleemun bima kuntum ta'maloon **a**

# 1930

Fa **o** dkhuloo abwaba jahannama khalideena feeha falabisa mathwa almutakabbireen **a**

# 1931

Waqeela lillatheena ittaqaw matha anzala rabbukum qaloo khayran lillatheena ahsanoo fee hathihi a **l** ddunyahasanatun waladaru alakhirati khayrun walani'ma daru almuttaqeen **a**

# 1932

Jannatu 'adnin yadkhuloonaha tajree min tahtiha alanharu lahum feeha ma yashaoona kathalika yajzee Allahu almuttaqeen **a**

# 1933

Allatheena tatawaffahumu almalaikatu tayyibeena yaqooloona salamun 'alaykumu odkhuloo aljannata bima kuntum ta'maloon **a**

# 1934

Hal yan _th_ uroona illa an tatiyahumu almalaikatu aw yatiya amru rabbika kathalika fa'ala allatheena min qablihim wama _th_ alamahumu Allahu walakin kanoo anfusahum ya _th_ limoon **a**

# 1935

Faasabahum sayyiatu ma 'amiloo wahaqa bihim ma kanoo bihi yastahzioon **a**

# 1936

Waqala allatheena ashrakoo law shaa Allahu ma 'abadna min doonihi min shayin nahnu walaabaona walaharramna min doonihi min shayin kathalika fa'ala allatheena min qablihim fahal 'ala a **l** rrusuli illa albalaghu almubeen **u**

# 1937

Walaqad ba'athna fee kulli ommatin rasoolan ani o'budoo Allaha wa **i** jtaniboo a **l** ttaghoota faminhum man hada Allahu waminhum man haqqat 'alayhi a **l** ddalalatu faseeroo fee alardi fa **o** n _th_ uroo kayfa kana 'aqibatu almukaththibeen **a**

# 1938

In tahris 'ala hudahum fainna Allaha la yahdee man yudillu wama lahum min nasireen **a**

# 1939

Waaqsamoo bi **A** llahi jahda aymanihim la yab'athu Allahu man yamootu bala wa'dan 'alayhi haqqan walakinna akthara a **l** nnasi la ya'lamoon **a**

# 1940

Liyubayyina lahumu allathee yakhtalifoona feehi waliya'lama allatheena kafaroo annahum kanoo kathibeen **a**

# 1941

Innama qawluna lishayin itha aradnahu an naqoola lahu kun fayakoon **u**

# 1942

Wa **a** llatheena hajaroo fee Allahi min ba'di ma _th_ ulimoo lanubawwiannahum fee a **l** ddunyahasanatan walaajru alakhirati akbaru law kanoo ya'lamoon **a**

# 1943

Allatheena sabaroo wa'ala rabbihim yatawakkaloon **a**

# 1944

Wama arsana min qablika illa rijalan noohee ilayhim fa **i** saloo ahla a **l** ththikri in kuntum la ta'lamoon **a**

# 1945

Bi **a** lbayyinati wa **al** zzuburi waanzana ilayka a **l** ththikra litubayyina li **l** nnasi ma nuzzila ilayhim wala'allahum yatafakkaroon **a**

# 1946

Afaamina allatheena makaroo a **l** ssayyiati an yakhsifa Allahu bihimu alarda aw yatiyahumu al'athabu min haythu la yash'uroon **a**

# 1947

Aw yakhuthahum fee taqallubihim fama hum bimu'jizeen **a**

# 1948

Aw yakhuthahum 'ala takhawwufin fainna rabbakum laraoofun raheem **un**

# 1949

Awa lam yaraw ila ma khalaqa Allahu min shayin yatafayyao _th_ ilaluhu 'ani alyameeni wa **al** shshamaili sujjadan lillahi wahum dakhiroon **a**

# 1950

Walillahi yasjudu ma fee a **l** ssamawati wama fee alardi min dabbatin wa **a** lmalaikatu wahum la yastakbiroon **a**

# 1951

Yakhafoona rabbahum min fawqihim wayaf'aloona ma yumaroon **a**

# 1952

Waqala Allahu la tattakhithoo ilahayni ithnayni innama huwa ilahun wahidun faiyyaya fa **i** rhaboon **i**

# 1953

Walahu ma fee a **l** ssamawati wa **a** lardi walahu a **l** ddeenu wasiban afaghayra Allahi tattaqoon **a**

# 1954

Wama bikum min ni'matin famina Allahi thumma itha massakumu a **l** ddurru failayhi tajaroon **a**

# 1955

Thumma itha kashafa a **l** ddurra 'ankum itha fareequn minkum birabbihim yushrikoon **a**

# 1956

Liyakfuroo bimaataynahum fatamatta'oo fasawfa ta'lamoon **a**

# 1957

Wayaj'aloona lima la ya'lamoona naseeban mimma razaqnahum ta **A** llahi latusalunna 'amma kuntum taftaroon **a**

# 1958

Wayaj'aloona lillahi albanati subhanahu walahum ma yashtahoon **a**

# 1959

Waitha bushshira ahaduhum bi **a** lontha _th_ alla wajhuhu muswaddan wahuwa ka _th_ eem **un**

# 1960

Yatawara mina alqawmi min sooi ma bushshira bihi ayumsikuhu 'ala hoonin am yadussuhu fee a **l** tturabi ala saa ma yahkumoon **a**

# 1961

Lillatheena la yuminoona bi **a** lakhirati mathalu a **l** ssawi walillahi almathalu ala'la wahuwa al'azeezu alhakeem **u**

# 1962

Walaw yuakhithu Allahu a **l** nnasa bi _th_ ulmihim ma taraka 'alayha min dabbatin walakin yuakhkhiruhum ila ajalin musamman faitha jaa ajaluhum la yastakhiroona sa'atan wala yastaqdimoon **a**

# 1963

Wayaj'aloona lillahi ma yakrahoona watasifu asinatuhumu alkathiba anna lahumu alhusna la jarama anna lahumu a **l** nnara waannahum mufratoon **a**

# 1964

Ta **A** llahi laqad arsana ila omamin min qablika fazayyana lahumu a **l** shshaytanu a'malahum fahuwa waliyyuhumu alyawma walahum 'athabun aleem **un**

# 1965

Wama anzana 'alayka alkitaba illa litubayyina lahumu allathee ikhtalafoo feehi wahudan warahmatan liqawmin yuminoon **a**

# 1966

Wa **A** llahu anzala mina a **l** ssamai maan faahya bihi alarda ba'da mawtiha inna fee thalika laayatan liqawmin yasma'oon **a**

# 1967

Wainna lakum fee alan'ami la'ibratan nusqeekum mimma fee butoonihi min bayni farthin wadamin labanan khalisan saighan li **l** shsharibeen **a**

# 1968

Wamin thamarati a **l** nnakheeli wa **a** la'nabi tattakhithoona minhu sakaran warizqan hasanan inna fee thalika laayatan liqawmin ya'qiloon **a**

# 1969

Waawha rabbuka ila a **l** nnahli ani ittakhithee mina aljibali buyootan wamina a **l** shshajari wamimma ya'rishoon **a**

# 1970

Thumma kulee min kulli a **l** ththamarati fa **o** slukee subula rabbiki thululan yakhruju min butooniha sharabun mukhtalifun alwanuhu feehi shifaon li **l** nnasi inna fee thalika laayatan liqawmin yatafakkaroon **a**

# 1971

Wa **A** llahu khalaqakum thumma yatawaffakum waminkum man yuraddu ila arthali al'umuri likay la ya'lama ba'da 'ilmin shayan inna Allaha 'aleemun qadeer **un**

# 1972

Wa **A** llahu faddala ba'dakum 'ala ba'din fee a **l** rrizqi fama allatheena fuddiloo biraddee rizqihim 'ala ma malakat aymanuhum fahum feehi sawaon afabini'mati Allahi yajhadoon **a**

# 1973

Wa **A** llahu ja'ala lakum min anfusikum azwajan waja'ala lakum min azwajikum baneena wahafadatan warazaqakum mina a **l** ttayyibati afabi **a** lbatili yuminoona wabini'mati Allahi hum yakfuroon **a**

# 1974

Waya'budoona min dooni Allahi ma la yamliku lahum rizqan mina a **l** ssamawati wa **a** lardi shayan wala yastatee'oon **a**

# 1975

Fala tadriboo lillahi alamthala inna Allaha ya'lamu waantum la ta'lamoon **a**

# 1976

Daraba Allahu mathalan 'abdan mamlookan la yaqdiru 'ala shayin waman razaqnahu minna rizqan hasanan fahuwa yunfiqu minhu sirran wajahran hal yastawoona alhamdu lillahi bal aktharuhum la ya'lamoon **a**

# 1977
