Wadaraba Allahu mathalan rajulayni ahaduhuma abkamu la yaqdiru 'ala shayin wahuwa kallun 'ala mawlahu aynama yuwajjihhu la yati bikhayrin hal yastawee huwa waman yamuru bi **a** l'adli wahuwa 'alasiratin mustaqeem **in**

# 1978

Walillahi ghaybu a **l** ssamawati wa **a** lardi wama amru a **l** ssa'ati illa kalamhi albasari aw huwa aqrabu inna Allaha 'ala kulli shayin qadeer **un**

# 1979

Wa **A** llahu akhrajakum min butooni ommahatikum la ta'lamoona shayan waja'ala lakumu a **l** ssam'a wa **a** labsara wa **a** lafidata la'allakum tashkuroon **a**

# 1980

Alam yaraw ila a **l** ttayri musakhkharatin fee jawwi a **l** ssamai ma yumsikuhunna illa Allahu inna fee thalika laayatin liqawmin yuminoon **a**

# 1981

Wa **A** llahu ja'ala lakum min buyootikum sakanan waja'ala lakum min juloodi alan'ami buyootan tastakhiffoonaha yawma _th_ a'nikum wayawma iqamatikum wamin aswafiha waawbariha waash'ariha athathan wamata'an ilaheen **in**

# 1982

Wa **A** llahu ja'ala lakum mimma khalaqa _th_ ilalan waja'ala lakum mina aljibali aknanan waja'ala lakum sarabeela taqeekumu alharra wasarabeela taqeekum basakum kathalika yutimmu ni'matahu 'alaykum la'allakum tuslimoon **a**

# 1983

Fain tawallaw fainnama 'alayka albalaghu almubeen **u**

# 1984

Ya'rifoona ni'mata Allahi thumma yunkiroonaha waaktharuhumu alkafiroon **a**

# 1985

Wayawma nab'athu min kulli ommatin shaheedan thumma la yuthanu lillatheena kafaroo wala hum yusta'taboon **a**

# 1986

Waitha raa allatheena _th_ alamoo al'athaba fala yukhaffafu 'anhum wala hum yun _th_ aroon **a**

# 1987

Waitha raa allatheena ashrakoo shurakaahum qaloo rabbana haolai shurakaona allatheena kunna nad'oo min doonika faalqaw ilayhimu alqawla innakum lakathiboon **a**

# 1988

Waalqaw ila Allahi yawmaithin a **l** ssalama wadalla 'anhum ma kanoo yaftaroon **a**

# 1989

Allatheena kafaroo wasaddoo 'an sabeeli Allahi zidnahum 'athaban fawqa al'athabi bima kanoo yufsidoon **a**

# 1990

Wayawma nab'athu fee kulli ommatin shaheedan 'alayhim min anfusihim wajina bika shaheedan 'ala haolai wanazzana 'alayka alkitaba tibyanan likulli shayin wahudan warahmatan wabushra lilmuslimeen **a**

# 1991

Inna Allaha yamuru bi **a** l'adli wa **a** lihsani waeetai thee alqurba wayanha 'ani alfahshai wa **a** lmunkari wa **a** lbaghyi ya'i _th_ ukum la'allakum tathakkaroon **a**

# 1992

Waawfoo bi'ahdi Allahi itha 'ahadtum wala tanqudoo alaymana ba'da tawkeediha waqad ja'atumu Allaha 'alaykum kafeelan inna Allaha ya'lamu ma taf'aloon **a**

# 1993

Wala takoonoo ka **a** llatee naqadat ghazlaha min ba'di quwwatin ankathan tattakhithoona aymanakum dakhalan baynakum an takoona ommatun hiya arba min ommatin innama yablookumu Allahu bihi walayubayyinanna lakum yawma alqiyamati ma kuntum feehi takhtalifoon **a**

# 1994

Walaw shaa Allahu laja'alakum ommatan wahidatan walakin yudillu man yashao wayahdee man yashao walatusalunna 'amma kuntum ta'maloon **a**

# 1995

Wala tattakhithoo aymanakum dakhalan baynakum fatazilla qadamun ba'da thubootiha watathooqoo a **l** ssooa bimasadadtum 'an sabeeli Allahi walakum 'athabun 'a _th_ eem **un**

# 1996

Wala tashtaroo bi'ahdi Allahi thamanan qaleelan innama 'inda Allahi huwa khayrun lakum in kuntum ta'lamoon **a**

# 1997

Ma 'indakum yanfadu wama 'inda Allahi baqin walanajziyanna allatheena sabaroo ajrahum biahsani ma kanoo ya'maloon **a**

# 1998

Man 'amila salihan min thakarin aw ontha wahuwa muminun falanuhyiyannahu hayatan tayyibatan walanajziyannahum ajrahum biahsani ma kanoo ya'maloon **a**

# 1999

Faitha qarata alqurana fa **i** sta'ith bi **A** llahi mina a **l** shshaytani a **l** rrajeem **i**

# 2000

Innahu laysa lahu sultanun 'ala allatheena amanoo wa'ala rabbihim yatawakkaloon **a**

# 2001

Innama sultanuhu 'ala allatheena yatawallawnahu wa **a** llatheena hum bihi mushrikoon **a**

# 2002

Waitha baddanaayatan makana ayatin wa **A** llahu a'lamu bima yunazzilu qaloo innama anta muftarin bal aktharuhum la ya'lamoon **a**

# 2003

Qul nazzalahu roohu alqudusi min rabbika bi **a** lhaqqi liyuthabbita allatheena amanoo wahudan wabushra lilmuslimeen **a**

# 2004

Walaqad na'lamu annahum yaqooloona innama yu'allimuhu basharun lisanu allathee yulhidoona ilayhi a'jamiyyun wahatha lisanun 'arabiyyun mubeen **un**

# 2005

Inna allatheena la yuminoona biayati Allahi la yahdeehimu Allahu walahum 'athabun aleem **un**

# 2006

Innama yaftaree alkathiba allatheena la yuminoona biayati Allahi waolaika humu alkathiboon **a**

# 2007

Man kafara bi **A** llahi min ba'di eemanihi illa man okriha waqalbuhu mutmainnun bi **a** leemani walakin man sharaha bi **a** lkufri sadran fa'alayhim ghadabun mina Allahi walahum 'athabun 'a _th_ eem **un**

# 2008

Thalika biannahumu istahabboo alhayata a **l** ddunya 'ala alakhirati waanna Allaha la yahdee alqawma alkafireen **a**

# 2009

Olaika allatheena taba'a Allahu 'ala quloobihim wasam'ihim waabsarihim waolaika humu alghafiloon **a**

# 2010

La jarama annahum fee alakhirati humu alkhasiroon **a**

# 2011

Thumma inna rabbaka lillatheena hajaroo min ba'di ma futinoo thumma jahadoo wasabaroo inna rabbaka min ba'diha laghafoorun raheem **un**

# 2012

Yawma tatee kullu nafsin tujadilu 'an nafsiha watuwaffa kullu nafsin ma 'amilat wahum la yu _th_ lamoon **a**

# 2013

Wadaraba Allahu mathalan qaryatan kanat aminatan mutmainnatan yateeha rizquha raghadan min kulli makanin fakafarat bian'umi Allahi faathaqaha Allahu libasa aljoo'i wa **a** lkhawfi bima kanoo yasna'oon **a**

# 2014

Walaqad jaahum rasoolun minhum fakaththaboohu faakhathahumu al'athabu wahum _th_ alimoon **a**

# 2015

Fakuloo mimma razaqakumu Allahu halalan tayyiban wa **o** shkuroo ni'mata Allahi in kuntum iyyahu ta'budoon **a**

# 2016

Innamaharrama 'alaykumu almaytata wa **al** ddama walahma alkhinzeeri wama ohilla lighayri Allahi bihi famani idturra ghayra baghin wala 'adin fainna Allaha ghafoorun raheem **un**

# 2017

Wala taqooloo lima tasifu asinatukumu alkathiba hathahalalun wahathaharamun litaftaroo 'ala Allahi alkathiba inna allatheena yaftaroona 'ala Allahi alkathiba la yuflihoon **a**

# 2018

Mata'un qaleelun walahum 'athabun aleem **un**

# 2019

Wa'ala allatheena hadoo harramna ma qasasna 'alayka min qablu wama _th_ alamnahum walakin kanoo anfusahum ya _th_ limoon **a**

# 2020

Thumma inna rabbaka lillatheena 'amiloo a **l** ssooa bijahalatin thumma taboo min ba'di thalika waaslahoo inna rabbaka min ba'diha laghafoorun raheem **un**

# 2021

Inna ibraheema kana ommatan qanitan lillahi haneefan walam yaku mina almushrikeen **a**

# 2022

Shakiran lian'umihi ijtabahu wahadahu ilasiratin mustaqeem **in**

# 2023

Waataynahu fee a **l** ddunyahasanatan wainnahu fee alakhirati lamina a **l** ssaliheen **a**

# 2024

Thumma awhayna ilayka ani ittabi' millata ibraheema haneefan wama kana mina almushrikeen **a**

# 2025

Innama ju'ila a **l** ssabtu 'ala allatheena ikhtalafoo feehi wainna rabbaka layahkumu baynahum yawma alqiyamati feema kanoo feehi yakhtalifoon **a**

# 2026

Od'u ila sabeeli rabbika bi **a** lhikmati wa **a** lmaw'i _th_ ati alhasanati wajadilhum bi **a** llatee hiya ahsanu inna rabbaka huwa a'lamu biman dalla 'an sabeelihi wahuwa a'lamu bi **a** lmuhtadeen **a**

# 2027

Wain 'aqabtum fa'aqiboo bimithli ma 'ooqibtum bihi walain sabartum lahuwa khayrun li **l** ssabireen **a**

# 2028

Wa **i** sbir wamasabruka illa bi **A** llahi wala tahzan 'alayhim wala taku fee dayqin mimma yamkuroon **a**

# 2029

Inna Allaha ma'a allatheena ittaqaw wa **a** llatheena hum muhsinoon **a**

# 2030

Subhana allathee asra bi'abdihi laylan mina almasjidi alharami ila almasjidi alaqsa allathee baraknahawlahu linuriyahu min ayatina innahu huwa a **l** ssamee'u albaseer **u**

# 2031

Waatayna moosa alkitaba waja'anahu hudan libanee israeela alla tattakhithoo min doonee wakeela **n**

# 2032

Thurriyyata man hamana ma'a noohin innahu kana 'abdan shakoora **n**

# 2033

Waqadayna ila banee israeela fee alkitabi latufsidunna fee alardi marratayni walata'lunna 'uluwwan kabeera **n**

# 2034

Faitha jaa wa'du oolahuma ba'athna 'alaykum 'ibadan lana olee basin shadeedin fajasoo khilala a **l** ddiyari wakana wa'dan maf'oola **n**

# 2035

Thumma radadna lakumu alkarrata 'alayhim waamdadnakum biamwalin wabaneena waja'anakum akthara nafeera **n**

# 2036

In ahsantum ahsantum lianfusikum wain asatum falaha faitha jaa wa'du alakhirati liyasoooo wujoohakum waliyadkhuloo almasjida kama dakhaloohu awwala marratin waliyutabbiroo ma 'alaw tatbeera **n**

# 2037

'asa rabbukum an yarhamakum wain 'udtum 'udna waja'ana jahannama lilkafireena haseera **n**

# 2038

Inna hatha alqurana yahdee lillatee hiya aqwamu wayubashshiru almumineena allatheena ya'maloona a **l** ssalihati anna lahum ajran kabeera **n**

# 2039

Waanna allatheena la yuminoona bi **a** lakhirati a'tadna lahum 'athaban aleema **n**

# 2040

Wayad'u alinsanu bi **al** shsharri du'aahu bi **a** lkhayri wakana alinsanu 'ajoola **n**

# 2041

Waja'ana allayla wa **al** nnahara ayatayni famahawnaayata allayli waja'anaayata a **l** nnahari mubsiratan litabtaghoo fadlan min rabbikum walita'lamoo 'adada a **l** ssineena wa **a** lhisaba wakulla shayin fassanahu tafseela **n**

# 2042

Wakulla insanin azamnahu tairahu fee 'unuqihi wanukhriju lahu yawma alqiyamati kitaban yalqahu manshoora **n**

# 2043

Iqra kitabaka kafa binafsika alyawma 'alayka haseeba **n**

# 2044

Mani ihtada fainnama yahtadee linafsihi waman dalla fainnama yadillu 'alayha wala taziru waziratun wizra okhra wama kunna mu'aththibeena hatta nab'atha rasoola **n**

# 2045

Waitha aradna an nuhlika qaryatan amarna mutrafeeha fafasaqoo feeha fahaqqa 'alayha alqawlu fadammarnaha tadmeera **n**

# 2046

Wakam ahlakna mina alqurooni min ba'di noohin wakafa birabbika bithunoobi 'ibadihi khabeeran baseera **n**

# 2047

Man kana yureedu al'ajilata 'ajjana lahu feeha ma nashao liman nureedu thumma ja'ana lahu jahannama yaslaha mathmooman madhoora **n**

# 2048

Waman arada alakhirata wasa'a laha sa'yaha wahuwa muminun faolaika kana sa'yuhum mashkoora **n**

# 2049

Kullan numiddu haolai wahaolai min 'atai rabbika wama kana 'atao rabbika mah _th_ oora **n**

# 2050

On _th_ ur kayfa faddana ba'dahum 'ala ba'din walalakhiratu akbaru darajatin waakbaru tafdeela **n**

# 2051

La taj'al ma'a Allahi ilahan akhara fataq'uda mathmooman makhthoola **n**

# 2052

Waqada rabbuka alla ta'budoo illa iyyahu wabi **a** lwalidayni ihsanan imma yablughanna 'indaka alkibara ahaduhuma aw kilahuma fala taqul lahuma offin wala tanharhuma waqul lahuma qawlan kareema **n**

# 2053

Wa **i** khfid lahuma janaha a **l** ththulli mina a **l** rrahmati waqul rabbi irhamhuma kama rabbayanee sagheera **n**

# 2054

Rabbukum a'lamu bima fee nufoosikum in takoonoo saliheena fainnahu kana lilawwabeena ghafoora **n**

# 2055

Waati tha alqurbahaqqahu wa **a** lmiskeena wa **i** bna a **l** ssabeeli wala tubaththir tabtheera **n**

# 2056

Inna almubaththireena kanoo ikhwana a **l** shshayateeni wakana a **l** shshaytanu lirabbihi kafoora **n**

# 2057

Waimma tu'ridanna 'anhumu ibtighaa rahmatin min rabbika tarjooha faqul lahum qawlan maysoora **n**

# 2058

Wala taj'al yadaka maghloolatan ila 'unuqika wala tabsutha kulla albasti fataq'uda malooman mahsoora **n**

# 2059

Inna rabbaka yabsutu a **l** rrizqa liman yashao wayaqdiru innahu kana bi'ibadihi khabeeran baseera **n**

# 2060

Wala taqtuloo awladakum khashyata imlaqin nahnu narzuquhum waiyyakum inna qatlahum kana khitan kabeera **n**

# 2061

Wala taqraboo a **l** zzina innahu kana fahishatan wasaa sabeela **n**

# 2062

Wala taqtuloo a **l** nnafsa allatee harrama Allahu illa bi **a** lhaqqi waman qutila ma _th_ looman faqad ja'ana liwaliyyihi sultanan fala yusrif fee alqatli innahu kana mansoora **n**

# 2063

Wala taqraboo mala alyateemi illa bi **a** llatee hiya ahsanu hatta yablugha ashuddahu waawfoo bi **a** l'ahdi inna al'ahda kana masoola **n**

# 2064

Waawfoo alkayla itha kiltum wazinoo bi **a** lqistasi almustaqeemi thalika khayrun waahsanu taweela **n**

# 2065

Wala taqfu ma laysa laka bihi 'ilmun inna a **l** ssam'a wa **a** lbasara wa **a** lfuada kullu olaika kana 'anhu masoola **n**

# 2066

Wala tamshi fee alardi marahan innaka lan takhriqa alarda walan tablugha aljibala toola **n**

# 2067

Kullu thalika kana sayyiohu 'inda rabbika makrooha **n**

# 2068

Thalika mimma awha ilayka rabbuka mina alhikmati wala taj'al ma'a Allahi ilahan akhara fatulqa fee jahannama malooman madhoora **n**

# 2069

Afaasfakum rabbukum bi **a** lbaneena wa **i** ttakhatha mina almalaikati inathan innakum lataqooloona qawlan 'a _th_ eema **n**

# 2070

Walaqad sarrafna fee hatha alqurani liyaththakkaroo wama yazeeduhum illa nufoora **n**

# 2071

Qul law kana ma'ahu alihatun kama yaqooloona ithan la **i** btaghaw ilathee al'arshi sabeela **n**

# 2072

Subhanahu wata'ala 'amma yaqooloona 'uluwwan kabeera **n**

# 2073

Tusabbihu lahu a **l** ssamawatu a **l** ssab'u wa **a** lardu waman feehinna wain min shayin illa yusabbihu bihamdihi walakin la tafqahoona tasbeehahum innahu kana haleeman ghafoora **n**

# 2074

Waitha qarata alqurana ja'ana baynaka wabayna allatheena la yuminoona bi **a** lakhirati hijaban mastoora **n**

# 2075

Waja'ana 'ala quloobihim akinnatan an yafqahoohu wafee athanihim waqran waithathakarta rabbaka fee alqurani wahdahu wallaw 'ala adbarihim nufoora **n**

# 2076

Nahnu a'lamu bima yastami'oona bihi ith yastami'oona ilayka waith hum najwa ith yaqoolu a **l** _thth_ alimoona in tattabi'oona illa rajulan mashoora **n**

# 2077

On _th_ ur kayfa daraboo laka alamthala fadalloo fala yastatee'oona sabeela **n**

# 2078

Waqaloo aitha kunna 'i _th_ aman warufatan ainna lamab'oothoona khalqan jadeeda **n**

# 2079

Qul koonoo hijaratan aw hadeeda **n**

# 2080

Aw khalqan mimma yakburu fee sudoorikum fasayaqooloona man yu'eeduna quli allathee fatarakum awwala marratin fasayunghidoona ilayka ruoosahum wayaqooloona mata huwa qul 'asa an yakoona qareeba **n**

# 2081

Yawma yad'ookum fatastajeeboona bihamdihi wata _th_ unnoona in labithtum illa qaleela **n**

# 2082

Waqul li'ibadee yaqooloo allatee hiya ahsanu inna a **l** shshaytana yanzaghu baynahum inna a **l** shshaytana kana lilinsani 'aduwwan mubeena **n**

# 2083

Rabbukum a'lamu bikum in yasha yarhamkum aw in yasha yu'aththibkum wama arsanaka 'alayhim wakeela **n**

# 2084

Warabbuka a'lamu biman fee a **l** ssamawati wa **a** lardi walaqad faddana ba'da a **l** nnabiyyeena 'ala ba'din waatayna dawooda zaboora **n**

# 2085

Quli od'u allatheena za'amtum min doonihi fala yamlikoona kashfa a **l** ddurri 'ankum wala tahweela **n**

# 2086

Olaika allatheena yad'oona yabtaghoona ila rabbihimu alwaseelata ayyuhum aqrabu wayarjoona rahmatahu wayakhafoona 'athabahu inna 'athaba rabbika kana mahthoora **n**

# 2087

Wain min qaryatin illa nahnu muhlikooha qabla yawmi alqiyamati aw mu'aththibooha 'athaban shadeedan kana thalika fee alkitabi mastoora **n**

# 2088

Wama mana'ana an nursila bi **a** layati illa an kaththaba biha alawwaloona waatayna thamooda a **l** nnaqata mubsiratan fa _th_ alamoo biha wama nursilu bi **a** layati illa takhweefa **n**

# 2089

Waith qulna laka inna rabbaka ahata bi **al** nnasi wama ja'ana a **l** rruya allatee araynaka illa fitnatan li **l** nnasi wa **al** shshajarata almal'oonata fee alqurani wanukhawwifuhum fama yazeeduhum illatughyanan kabeera **n**

# 2090

Waith qulna lilmalaikati osjudoo liadama fasajadoo illa ibleesa qala aasjudu liman khalaqta teena **n**

# 2091

Qala araaytaka hatha allathee karramta 'alayya lain akhkhartani ila yawmi alqiyamati laahtanikanna thurriyyatahu illa qaleela **n**

# 2092

Qala ithhab faman tabi'aka minhum fainna jahannama jazaokum jazaan mawfoora **n**

# 2093

Wa **i** stafziz mani istata'ta minhum bisawtika waajlib 'alayhim bikhaylika warajlika washarikhum fee alamwali wa **a** lawladi wa'idhum wama ya'iduhumu a **l** shshaytanu illa ghuroora **n**

# 2094

Inna 'ibadee laysa laka 'alayhim sultanun wakafa birabbika wakeela **n**

# 2095

Rabbukumu allathee yuzjee lakumu alfulka fee albahri litabtaghoo min fadlihi innahu kana bikum raheema **n**

# 2096

Waitha massakumu a **l** ddurru fee albahri dalla man tad'oona illa iyyahu falamma najjakum ila albarri a'radtum wakana alinsanu kafoora **n**

# 2097

Afaamintum an yakhsifa bikum janiba albarri aw yursila 'alaykum hasiban thumma la tajidoo lakum wakeela **n**

# 2098

Am amintum an yu'eedakum feehi taratan okhra fayursila 'alaykum qasifan mina a **l** rreehi fayughriqakum bima kafartum thumma la tajidoo lakum 'alayna bihi tabee'a **n**

# 2099

Walaqad karramna banee adama wahamanahum fee albarri wa **a** lbahri warazaqnahum mina a **l** ttayyibati wafaddanahum 'ala katheerin mimman khalaqna tafdeela **n**

# 2100

Yawma nad'oo kulla onasin biimamihim faman ootiya kitabahu biyameenihi faolaika yaqraoona kitabahum wala yu _th_ lamoona fateela **n**

# 2101

Waman kana fee hathihi a'ma fahuwa fee alakhirati a'ma waadallu sabeela **n**

# 2102

Wain kadoo layaftinoonaka 'ani allathee awhayna ilayka litaftariya 'alayna ghayrahu waithan la **i** ttakhathooka khaleela **n**

# 2103

Walawla an thabbatnaka laqad kidta tarkanu ilayhim shayan qaleela **n**

# 2104

Ithan laathaqnaka di'fa alhayati wadi'fa almamati thumma la tajidu laka 'alayna naseera **n**

# 2105

Wain kadoo layastafizzoonaka mina alardi liyukhrijooka minha waithan la yalbathoona khilafaka illa qaleela **n**

# 2106

Sunnata man qad arsana qablaka min rusulina wala tajidu lisunnatina tahweela **n**

# 2107

Aqimi a **l** ssalata lidulooki a **l** shshamsi ila ghasaqi allayli waqurana alfajri inna qurana alfajri kana mashhooda **n**

# 2108

Wamina allayli fatahajjad bihi nafilatan laka 'asa an yab'athaka rabbuka maqaman mahmooda **n**

# 2109

Waqul rabbi adkhilnee mudkhala sidqin waakhrijnee mukhraja sidqin wa **i** j'al lee min ladunka sultanan naseera **n**

# 2110

Waqul jaa alhaqqu wazahaqa albatilu inna albatila kana zahooqa **n**

# 2111

Wanunazzilu mina alqurani ma huwa shifaon warahmatun lilmumineena wala yazeedu a **l** _thth_ alimeena illa khasara **n**

# 2112

Waitha an'amna 'ala alinsani a'rada wanaa bijanibihi waitha massahu a **l** shsharru kana yaoosa **n**

# 2113

Qul kullun ya'malu 'ala shakilatihi farabbukum a'lamu biman huwa ahda sabeela **n**

# 2114

Wayasaloonaka 'ani a **l** rroohi quli a **l** rroohu min amri rabbee wama ooteetum mina al'ilmi illa qaleela **n**

# 2115

Walain shina lanathhabanna bi **a** llathee awhayna ilayka thumma la tajidu laka bihi 'alayna wakeela **n**

# 2116

Illa rahmatan min rabbika inna fadlahu kana 'alayka kabeera **n**

# 2117

Qul laini ijtama'ati alinsu wa **a** ljinnu 'ala an yatoo bimithli hatha alqurani la yatoona bimithlihi walaw kana ba'duhum liba'din _th_ aheera **n**

# 2118

Walaqad sarrafna li **l** nnasi fee hatha alqurani min kulli mathalin faaba aktharu a **l** nnasi illa kufoora **n**

# 2119

Waqaloo lan numina laka hatta tafjura lana mina alardi yanboo'a **n**

# 2120

Aw takoona laka jannatun min nakheelin wa'inabin fatufajjira alanhara khilalaha tafjeera **n**

# 2121

Aw tusqita a **l** ssamaa kama za'amta 'alayna kisafan aw tatiya bi **A** llahi wa **a** lmalaikati qabeela **n**

# 2122

Aw yakoona laka baytun min zukhrufin aw tarqa fee a **l** ssamai walan numina liruqiyyika hatta tunazzila 'alayna kitaban naqraohu qul subhana rabbee hal kuntu illa basharan rasoola **n**

# 2123

Wama mana'a a **l** nnasa an yuminoo ith jaahumu alhuda illa an qaloo aba'atha Allahu basharan rasoola **n**

# 2124

Qul law kana fee alardi malaikatun yamshoona mutmainneena lanazzana 'alayhim mina a **l** ssamai malakan rasoola **n**

# 2125

Qul kafa bi **A** llahi shaheedan baynee wabaynakum innahu kana bi'ibadihi khabeeran baseera **n**

# 2126

Waman yahdi Allahu fahuwa almuhtadi waman yudlil falan tajida lahum awliyaa min doonihi wanahshuruhum yawma alqiyamati 'ala wujoohihim 'umyan wabukman wasumman mawahum jahannamu kullama khabat zidnahum sa'eera **n**

# 2127

Thalika jazaohum biannahum kafaroo biayatina waqaloo aitha kunna 'i _th_ aman warufatan ainna lamab'oothoona khalqan jadeeda **n**

# 2128

Awalam yaraw anna Allaha allathee khalaqa a **l** ssamawati wa **a** larda qadirun 'ala an yakhluqa mithlahum waja'ala lahum ajalan la rayba feehi faaba a **l** _thth_ alimoona illa kufoora **n**

# 2129

Qul law antum tamlikoona khazaina rahmati rabbee ithan laamsaktum khashyata alinfaqi wakana alinsanu qatoora **n**

# 2130

Walaqad atayna moosa tis'a ayatin bayyinatin fa **i** sal banee israeela ith jaahum faqala lahu fir'awnu innee laa _th_ unnuka ya moosa mashoora **n**

# 2131

Qala laqad 'alimta ma anzala haolai illa rabbu a **l** ssamawati wa **a** lardi basaira wainnee laa _th_ unnuka ya fir'awnu mathboora **n**

# 2132

Faarada an yastafizzahum mina alardi faaghraqnahu waman ma'ahu jamee'a **n**

# 2133

Waqulna min ba'dihi libanee israeela oskunoo alarda faitha jaa wa'du alakhirati jina bikum lafeefa **n**

# 2134

Wabi **a** lhaqqi anzanahu wabi **a** lhaqqi nazala wama arsanaka illa mubashshiran wanatheera **n**

# 2135

Waquranan faraqnahu litaqraahu 'ala a **l** nnasi 'ala mukthin wanazzanahu tanzeela **n**

# 2136

Qul aminoo bihi aw la tuminoo inna allatheena ootoo al'ilma min qablihi itha yutla 'alayhim yakhirroona lilathqani sujjada **n**

# 2137

Wayaqooloona subhana rabbina in kana wa'du rabbina lamaf'oola **n**

# 2138

Wayakhirroona lilathqani yabkoona wayazeeduhum khushoo'a **n**

# 2139

Quli od'oo Allaha awi od'oo a **l** rrahmana ayyan ma tad'oo falahu alasmao alhusna wala tajhar bisalatika wala tukhafit biha wa **i** btaghi bayna thalika sabeela **n**

# 2140

Waquli alhamdu lillahi allathee lam yattakhith waladan walam yakun lahu shareekun fee almulki walam yakun lahu waliyyun mina a **l** ththulli wakabbirhu takbeera **n**

# 2141

Alhamdu lillahi allathee anzala 'ala 'abdihi alkitaba walam yaj'al lahu 'iwaja **n**

# 2142

Qayyiman liyunthira basan shadeedan min ladunhu wayubashshira almumineena allatheena ya'maloona a **l** ssalihati anna lahum ajran hasana **n**

# 2143

Makitheena feehi abada **n**

# 2144

Wayunthira allatheena qaloo ittakhatha Allahu walada **n**

# 2145

Ma lahum bihi min 'ilmin wala liabaihim kaburat kalimatan takhruju min afwahihim in yaqooloona illa kathiba **n**

# 2146

Fala'allaka bakhi'un nafsaka 'alaatharihim in lam yuminoo bihatha alhadeethi asafa **n**

# 2147

Inna ja'ana ma 'ala alardi zeenatan laha linabluwahum ayyuhum ahsanu 'amala **n**

# 2148

Wainna laja'iloona ma 'alayhasa'eedan juruza **n**

# 2149

Am hasibta anna ashaba alkahfi wa **al** rraqeemi kanoo min ayatina 'ajaba **n**

# 2150

Ith awa alfityatu ila alkahfi faqaloo rabbanaatina min ladunka rahmatan wahayyi lana min amrina rashada **n**

# 2151

Fadarabna 'alaathanihim fee alkahfi sineena 'adada **n**

# 2152

Thumma ba'athnahum lina'lama ayyu alhizbayni ahsa lima labithoo amada **n**

# 2153

Nahnu naqussu 'alayka nabaahum bi **a** lhaqqi innahum fityatun amanoo birabbihim wazidnahum huda **n**

# 2154

Warabatna 'ala quloobihim ith qamoo faqaloo rabbuna rabbu a **l** ssamawati wa **a** lardi lan nad'uwa min doonihi ilahan laqad qulna ithan shatata **n**

# 2155

Haolai qawmuna ittakhathoo min doonihi alihatan lawla yatoona 'alayhim bisultanin bayyinin faman a _th_ lamu mimmani iftara 'ala Allahi kathiba **n**

# 2156

Waithi i'tazatumoohum wama ya'budoona illa Allaha fawoo ila alkahfi yanshur lakum rabbukum min rahmatihi wayuhayyi lakum min amrikum mirfaqa **n**

# 2157

Watara a **l** shshamsa ithatala'at tazawaru 'an kahfihim thata alyameeni waitha gharabat taqriduhum thata a **l** shshimali wahum fee fajwatin minhu thalika min ayati Allahi man yahdi Allahu fahuwa almuhtadi waman yudlil falan tajida lahu waliyyan murshida **n**

# 2158

Watahsabuhum ayqa _th_ an wahum ruqoodun wanuqallibuhum thata alyameeni wathata a **l** shshimali wakalbuhum basitun thira'ayhi bi **a** lwaseedi lawi ittala'ta 'alayhim lawallayta minhum firaran walamulita minhum ru'ba **n**

# 2159

Wakathalika ba'athnahum liyatasaaloo baynahum qala qailun minhum kam labithtum qaloo labithna yawman aw ba'da yawmin qaloo rabbukum a'lamu bima labithtum fa **i** b'athoo ahadakum biwariqikum hathihi ila almadeenati falyan _th_ ur ayyuha azkata'aman falyatikum birizqin minhu walyatalattaf wala yush'iranna bikum ahada **n**

# 2160

Innahum in ya _th_ haroo 'alaykum yarjumookum aw yu'eedookum fee millatihim walan tuflihoo ithan abada **n**

# 2161

Wakathalika a'tharna 'alayhim liya'lamoo anna wa'da Allahi haqqun waanna a **l** sa'ata la rayba feeha ith yatanaza'oona baynahum amrahum faqaloo ibnoo 'alayhim bunyanan rabbuhum a'lamu bihim qala allatheena ghalaboo 'ala amrihim lanattakhithanna 'alayhim masjida **n**

# 2162

Sayaqooloona thalathatun rabi'uhum kalbuhum wayaqooloona khamsatun sadisuhum kalbuhum rajman bi **a** lghaybi wayaqooloona sab'atun wathaminuhum kalbuhum qul rabbee a'lamu bi'iddatihim ma ya'lamuhum illa qaleelun fala tumari feehim illa miraan _th_ ahiran wala tastafti feehim minhum ahada **n**

# 2163

Wala taqoolanna lishayin innee fa'ilun thalika ghada **n**

# 2164

Illa an yashaa Allahu wa **o** thkur rabbaka itha naseeta waqul 'asa an yahdiyani rabbee liaqraba min hatha rashada **n**

# 2165

Walabithoo fee kahfihim thalatha miatin sineena wa **i** zdadoo tis'a **n**

# 2166

Quli Allahu a'lamu bima labithoo lahu ghaybu a **l** ssamawati wa **a** lardi absir bihi waasmi' ma lahum min doonihi min waliyyin wala yushriku fee hukmihi ahada **n**

# 2167

Wa **o** tlu ma oohiya ilayka min kitabi rabbika la mubaddila likalimatihi walan tajida min doonihi multahada **n**

# 2168

Wa **i** sbir nafsaka ma'a allatheena yad'oona rabbahum bi **a** lghadati wa **a** l'ashiyyi yureedoona wajhahu wala ta'du 'aynaka 'anhum tureedu zeenata alhayati a **l** ddunya wala tuti' man aghfana qalbahu 'an thikrina wa **i** ttaba'a hawahu wakana amruhu furuta **n**

# 2169

Waquli alhaqqu min rabbikum faman shaa falyumin waman shaa falyakfur inna a'tadna li **l** _thth_ alimeena naran ahata bihim suradiquha wain yastagheethoo yughathoo bimain ka **a** lmuhli yashwee alwujooha bisa a **l** shsharabu wasaat murtafaqa **n**

# 2170

Inna allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo a **l** ssalihati inna la nudee'u ajra man ahsana 'amala **n**

# 2171

Olaika lahum jannatu 'adnin tajree min tahtihimu alanharu yuhallawna feeha min asawira min thahabin way **a** lbasoona thiyaban khudran min sundusin waistabraqin muttakieena feeha 'ala alaraiki ni'ma a **l** ththawabu wahasunat murtafaqa **n**

# 2172

Wa **i** drib lahum mathalan rajulayni ja'ana liahadihima jannatayni min a'nabin wahafafnahuma binakhlin waja'ana baynahuma zar'a **n**

# 2173

Kilta aljannatayni atat okulaha walam ta _th_ lim minhu shayan wafajjarna khilalahuma nahara **n**

# 2174

Wakana lahu thamarun faqala lisahibihi wahuwa yuhawiruhu ana aktharu minka malan waa'azzu nafara **n**

# 2175

Wadakhala jannatahu wahuwa _th_ alimun linafsihi qala ma a _th_ unnu an tabeeda hathihi abada **n**

# 2176

Wama a _th_ unnu a **l** ssa'ata qaimatan walain rudidtu ila rabbee laajidanna khayran minha munqalaba **n**

# 2177

Qala lahu sahibuhu wahuwa yuhawiruhu akafarta bi **a** llathee khalaqaka min turabin thumma min nutfatin thumma sawwaka rajula **n**

# 2178

Lakinna huwa Allahu rabbee wala oshriku birabbee ahada **n**

# 2179

Walawla ith dakhata jannataka qulta ma shaa Allahu la quwwata illa bi **A** llahi in tarani ana aqalla minka malan wawalada **n**

# 2180

Fa'asa rabbee an yutiyani khayran min jannatika wayursila 'alayhahusbanan mina a **l** ssamai fatusbiha sa'eedan zalaqa **n**

# 2181

Aw yusbiha maoha ghawran falan tastatee'a lahu talaba **n**

# 2182

Waoheeta bithamarihi faasbaha yuqallibu kaffayhi 'ala ma anfaqa feeha wahiya khawiyatun 'ala 'urooshiha wayaqoolu ya laytanee lam oshrik birabbee ahada **n**

# 2183

Walam takun lahu fiatun yansuroonahu min dooni Allahi wama kana muntasira **n**

# 2184

Hunalika alwalayatu lillahi alhaqqi huwa khayrun thawaban wakhayrun 'uqba **n**

# 2185

Wa **i** drib lahum mathala alhayati a **l** ddunya kamain anzanahu mina a **l** ssamai fa **i** khtalata bihi nabatu alardi faasbaha hasheeman tathroohu a **l** rriyahu wakana Allahu 'ala kulli shayin muqtadira **n**

# 2186

Almalu wa **a** lbanoona zeenatu alhayati a **l** ddunya wa **a** lbaqiyatu a **l** ssalihatu khayrun 'inda rabbika thawaban wakhayrun amala **n**

# 2187

Wayawma nusayyiru aljibala watara alarda barizatan wahasharnahum falam nughadir minhum ahada **n**

# 2188

Wa'uridoo 'ala rabbika saffan laqad jitumoona kama khalaqnakum awwala marratin bal za'amtum allan naj'ala lakum maw'ida **n**

# 2189

Wawudi'a alkitabu fatara almujrimeena mushfiqeena mimma feehi wayaqooloona ya waylatana ma lihatha alkitabi la yughadiru sagheeratan wala kabeeratan illa ahsaha wawajadoo ma 'amiloo hadiran wala ya _th_ limu rabbuka ahada **n**

# 2190

Waith qulna lilmalaikati osjudoo liadama fasajadoo illa ibleesa kana mina aljinni fafasaqa 'an amri rabbihi afatattakhithoonahu wathurriyyatahu awliyaa min doonee wahum lakum 'aduwwun bisa li **l** _thth_ alimeena badala **n**

# 2191

Ma ashhadtuhum khalqa a **l** ssamawati wa **a** lardi wala khalqa anfusihim wama kuntu muttakhitha almudilleena 'aduda **n**

# 2192

Wayawma yaqoolu nadoo shurakaiya allatheena za'amtum fada'awhum falam yastajeeboo lahum waja'ana baynahum mawbiqa **n**

# 2193

Waraa almujrimoona a **l** nnara fa _th_ annoo annahum muwaqi'ooha walam yajidoo 'anha masrifa **n**

# 2194

Walaqad sarrafna fee hatha alqurani li **l** nnasi min kulli mathalin wakana alinsanu akthara shayin jadala **n**

# 2195

Wama mana'a a **l** nnasa an yuminoo ith jaahumu alhuda wayastaghfiroo rabbahum illa an tatiyahum sunnatu alawwaleena aw yatiyahumu al'athabu qubula **n**

# 2196

Wama nursilu almursaleena illa mubashshireena wamunthireena wayujadilu allatheena kafaroo bi **a** lbatili liyudhidoo bihi alhaqqa wa **i** ttakhathoo ayatee wama onthiroo huzuwa **n**

# 2197

Waman a _th_ lamu mimman thukkira biayati rabbihi faa'rada 'anha wanasiya ma qaddamat yadahu inna ja'ana 'ala quloobihim akinnatan an yafqahoohu wafee athanihim waqran wain tad'uhum ila alhuda falan yahtadoo ithan abada **n**

# 2198

Warabbuka alghafooru thoo a **l** rrahmati law yuakhithuhum bima kasaboo la'ajjala lahumu al'athaba bal lahum maw'idun lan yajidoo min doonihi mawila **n**

# 2199

Watilka alqura ahlaknahum lamma _th_ alamoo waja'ana limahlikihim maw'ida **n**

# 2200

Waith qala moosa lifatahu la abrahu hatta ablugha majma'a albahrayni aw amdiya huquba **n**

# 2201

Falamma balagha majma'a baynihima nasiyahootahuma fa **i** ttakhatha sabeelahu fee albahri saraba **n**

# 2202

Falamma jawaza qala lifatahu atina ghadaana laqad laqeena min safarina hatha nasaba **n**

# 2203

Qala araayta ith awayna ila a **l** ssakhrati fainnee naseetu alhoota wama ansaneehu illa a **l** shshaytanu an athkurahu wa **i** ttakhatha sabeelahu fee albahri 'ajaba **n**

# 2204

Qala thalika ma kunna nabghi fa **i** rtadda 'alaatharihima qasasa **n**

# 2205

Fawajada 'abdan min 'ibadinaataynahu rahmatan min 'indina wa'allamnahu min ladunna 'ilma **n**

# 2206

Qala lahu moosa hal attabi'uka 'ala an tu'allimani mimma 'ullimta rushda **n**

# 2207

Qala innaka lan tastatee'a ma'iya sabra **n**

# 2208

Wakayfa tasbiru 'ala ma lam tuhit bihi khubra **n**

# 2209

Qala satajidunee in shaa Allahu sabiran wala a'see laka amra **n**

# 2210

Qala faini ittaba'tanee fala tasanee 'an shayin hatta ohditha laka minhu thikra **n**

# 2211

Fa **i** ntalaqahatta itha rakiba fee a **l** ssafeenati kharaqaha qala akharaqtaha litughriqa ahlaha laqad jita shayan imra **n**

# 2212

Qala alam aqul innaka lan tastatee'a ma'iya sabra **n**

# 2213

Qala la tuakhithnee bima naseetu wala turhiqnee min amree 'usra **n**

# 2214

Fa **i** ntalaqahatta itha laqiya ghulaman faqatalahu qala aqatata nafsan zakiyyatan bighayri nafsin laqad jita shayan nukra **n**

# 2215

Qala alam aqul laka innaka lan tastatee'a ma'iya sabra **n**

# 2216

Qala in saatuka 'an shayin ba'daha fala tusahibnee qad balaghta min ladunnee 'uthra **n**

# 2217

Fa **i** ntalaqahatta itha ataya ahla qaryatin istat'ama ahlaha faabaw an yudayyifoohuma fawajada feeha jidaran yureedu an yanqadda faaqamahu qala law shita la **i** ttakhathta 'alayhi ajra **n**

# 2218

Qala hatha firaqu baynee wabaynika saonabbioka bitaweeli ma lam tastati' 'alayhi sabra **n**

# 2219

Amma a **l** ssafeenatu fakanat limasakeena ya'maloona fee albahri faaradtu an a'eebaha wakana waraahum malikun yakhuthu kulla safeenatin ghasba **n**

# 2220

Waamma alghulamu fakana abawahu muminayni fakhasheena an yurhiqahumatughyanan wakufra **n**

# 2221

Faaradna an yubdilahuma rabbuhuma khayran minhu zakatan waaqraba ruhma **n**

# 2222

Waamma aljidaru fakana lighulamayni yateemayni fee almadeenati wakana tahtahu kanzun lahuma wakana aboohumasalihan faarada rabbuka an yablugha ashuddahuma wayastakhrija kanzahuma rahmatan min rabbika wama fa'atuhu 'an amree thalika taweelu ma lam tasti' 'alayhi sabra **n**

# 2223

Wayasaloonaka 'an thee alqarnayni qul saatloo 'alaykum minhu thikra **n**

# 2224

Inna makkanna lahu fee alardi waataynahu min kulli shayin sababa **n**

# 2225

Faatba'a sababa **n**

# 2226

Hatta itha balagha maghriba a **l** shshamsi wajadaha taghrubu fee 'aynin hamiatin wawajada 'indaha qawman qulna yatha alqarnayni imma an tu'aththiba waimma an tattakhitha feehim husna **n**

# 2227

Qala amma man _th_ alama fasawfa nu'aththibuhu thumma yuraddu ila rabbihi fayu'aththibuhu 'athaban nukra **n**

# 2228

Waamma man amana wa'amila salihan falahu jazaan alhusna wasanaqoolu lahu min amrina yusra **n**

# 2229

Thumma atba'a sababa **n**

# 2230

Hatta itha balagha matli'a a **l** shshamsi wajadaha tatlu'u 'ala qawmin lam naj'al lahum min dooniha sitra **n**

# 2231

Kathalika waqad ahatna bima ladayhi khubra **n**

# 2232

Thumma atba'a sababa **n**

# 2233

Hatta itha balagha bayna a **l** ssaddayni wajada min doonihima qawman la yakadoona yafqahoona qawla **n**

# 2234

Qaloo yatha alqarnayni inna yajooja wamajooja mufsidoona fee alardi fahal naj'alu laka kharjan 'ala an taj'ala baynana wabaynahum sadda **n**

# 2235

Qala ma makkannee feehi rabbee khayrun faa'eenoonee biquwwatin aj'al baynakum wabaynahum radma **n**

# 2236

Atoonee zubara alhadeedi hatta itha sawa bayna a **l** sadafayni qala onfukhoo hatta itha ja'alahu naran qala atoonee ofrigh 'alayhi qitra **n**

# 2237

Fama ista'oo an ya _th_ haroohu wama istata'oo lahu naqba **n**

# 2238

Qala hatha rahmatun min rabbee faitha jaa wa'du rabbee ja'alahu dakkaa wakana wa'du rabbee haqqa **n**

# 2239

Watarakna ba'dahum yawmaithin yamooju fee ba'din wanufikha fee a **l** ssoori fajama'nahum jam'a **n**

# 2240

Wa'aradna jahannama yawmaithin lilkafireena 'arda **n**

# 2241

Allatheena kanat a'yunuhum fee ghitain 'an thikree wakanoo la yastatee'oona sam'a **n**

# 2242

Afahasiba allatheena kafaroo an yattakhithoo 'ibadee min doonee awliyaa inna a'tadna jahannama lilkafireena nuzula **n**

# 2243

Qul hal nunabbiokum bi **a** lakhsareena a'mala **n**

# 2244

Allatheena dalla sa'yuhum fee alhayati a **l** ddunya wahum yahsaboona annahum yuhsinoona sun'a **n**

# 2245

Olaika allatheena kafaroo biayati rabbihim waliqaihi fahabitat a'maluhum fala nuqeemu lahum yawma alqiyamati wazna **n**

# 2246

Thalika jazaohum jahannamu bima kafaroo wa **i** ttakhathoo ayatee warusulee huzuwa **n**

# 2247

Inna allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo a **l** ssalihati kanat lahum jannatu alfirdawsi nuzula **n**

# 2248

Khalideena feeha la yabghoona 'anhahiwala **n**

# 2249

# 2250

# 2453

Wayasaloonaka 'ani aljibali faqul yansifuha rabbee nasfa **n**

# 2454

Fayatharuha qa'an safsafa **n**

# 2455

La tara feeha 'iwajan wala amta **n**

# 2456

Yawmaithin yattabi'oona a **l** dda'iya la 'iwaja lahu wakhasha'ati alaswatu li **l** rrahmani fala tasma'u illa hamsa **n**

# 2457

Yawmaithin la tanfa'u a **l** shshafa'atu illa man athina lahu a **l** rrahmanu waradiya lahu qawla **n**

# 2458

Ya'lamu ma bayna aydeehim wama khalfahum wala yuheetoona bihi 'ilma **n**

# 2459

Wa'anati alwujoohu lilhayyi alqayyoomi waqad khaba man hamala _th_ ulma **n**

# 2460

Waman ya'mal mina a **l** ssalihati wahuwa muminun fala yakhafu _th_ ulman wala hadma **n**

# 2461

Wakathalika anzanahu quranan 'arabiyyan wasarrafna feehi mina alwa'eedi la'allahum yattaqoona aw yuhdithu lahum thikra **n**

# 2462

Fata'ala Allahu almaliku alhaqqu wala ta'jal bi **a** lqurani min qabli an yuqda ilayka wahyuhu waqul rabbi zidnee 'ilma **n**

# 2463

Walaqad 'ahidna ilaadama min qablu fanasiya walam najid lahu 'azma **n**

# 2464

Waith qulna lilmalaikati osjudoo liadama fasajadoo illa ibleesa aba

# 2465

Faqulna yaadamu inna hatha 'aduwwun laka walizawjika fala yukhrijannakuma mina aljannati fatashqa

# 2466

Inna laka alla tajoo'a feeha wala ta'ra

# 2467

Waannaka la ta _th_ mao feeha wala tadha

# 2468

Fawaswasa ilayhi a **l** shshaytanu qala yaadamu hal adulluka 'ala shajarati alkhuldi wamulkin la yabla

# 2469

Faakala minha fabadat lahuma sawatuhuma watafiqa yakhsifani 'alayhima min waraqi aljannati wa'asaadamu rabbahu faghawa

# 2470

Thumma ijtabahu rabbuhu fataba 'alayhi wahada

# 2471

Qala ihbita minha jamee'an ba'dukum liba'din 'aduwwun faimma yatiyannakum minnee hudan famani ittaba'a hudaya fala yadillu wala yashqa

# 2472

Waman a'rada 'an thikree fainna lahu ma'eeshatan danka **n** wanahshuruhu yawma alqiyamati a'ma **n**

# 2473

Qala rabbi lima hashartanee a'ma waqad kuntu baseera **n**

# 2474

Qala kathalika atatka ayatuna fanaseetaha wakathalika alyawma tunsa

# 2475

Wakathalika najzee man asrafa walam yumin biayati rabbihi wala'athabu alakhirati ashaddu waabqa

# 2476

Afalam yahdi lahum kam ahlakna qablahum mina alqurooni yamshoona fee masakinihim inna fee thalika laayatin liolee a **l** nnuha

# 2477

Walawla kalimatun sabaqat min rabbika lakana lizaman waajalun musamma **n**

# 2478

Fa **i** sbir 'ala ma yaqooloona wasabbih bihamdi rabbika qabla tuloo'i a **l** shshamsi waqabla ghuroobiha wamin anai allayli fasabbih waatrafa a **l** nnahari la'allaka tarda

# 2479

Wala tamuddanna 'aynayka ila ma matta'na bihi azwajan minhum zahrata alhayati a **l** ddunya linaftinahum feehi warizqu rabbika khayrun waabqa

# 2480

Wamur ahlaka bi **al** ssalati wa **i** stabir 'alayha la nasaluka rizqan nahnu narzuquka wa **a** l'aqibatu li **l** ttaqwa

# 2481

Waqaloo lawla yateena biayatin min rabbihi awalam tatihim bayyinatu ma fee a **l** ssuhufi aloola

# 2482

Walaw anna ahlaknahum bi'athabin min qablihi laqaloo rabbana lawla arsata ilayna rasoolan fanattabi'a ayatika min qabli an nathilla wanakhza

# 2483

Qul kullun mutarabbisun fatarabbasoo fasata'lamoona man ashabu a **l** ssirati a **l** ssawiyyi wamani ihtada

# 2484

Iqtaraba li **l** nnasi hisabuhum wahum fee ghaflatin mu'ridoon **a**

# 2485

Ma yateehim min thikrin min rabbihim muhdathin illa istama'oohu wahum yal'aboon **a**

# 2486

Lahiyatan quloobuhum waasarroo a **l** nnajwa allatheena _th_ alamoo hal hatha illa basharun mithlukum afatatoona a **l** ssihra waantum tubsiroon **a**

# 2487

Qala rabbee ya'lamu alqawla fee a **l** ssamai wa **a** lardi wahuwa a **l** ssamee'u al'aleem **u**

# 2488

Bal qaloo adghathu ahlamin bali iftarahu bal huwa sha'irun falyatina biayatin kama orsila alawwaloon **a**

# 2489

Maamanat qablahum min qaryatin ahlaknaha afahum yuminoon **a**

# 2490

Wama arsana qablaka illa rijalan noohee ilayhim fa **i** saloo ahla a **l** ththikri in kuntum la ta'lamoon **a**

# 2491

Wama ja'anahum jasadan la yakuloona a **l** tta'ama wama kanoo khalideen **a**

# 2492

Thumma sadaqnahumu alwa'da faanjaynahum waman nashao waahlakna almusrifeen **a**

# 2493

Laqad anzana ilaykum kitaban feehi thikrukum afala ta'qiloon **a**

# 2494

Wakam qasamna min qaryatin kanat _th_ alimatan waanshana ba'daha qawman akhareen **a**

# 2495

Falamma ahassoo basana itha hum minha yarkudoon **a**

# 2496

La tarkudoo wa **i** rji'oo ila ma otriftum feehi wamasakinikum la'allakum tusaloon **a**

# 2497

Qaloo ya waylana inna kunna _th_ alimeen **a**

# 2498

Fama zalat tilka da'wahum hatta ja'anahum haseedan khamideen **a**

# 2499

Wama khalaqna a **l** ssamaa wa **a** larda wama baynahuma la'ibeen **a**

# 2500

Law aradna an nattakhitha lahwan la **i** ttakhathnahu min ladunna in kunna fa'ileen **a**

# 2501

Bal naqthifu bi **a** lhaqqi 'ala albatili fayadmaghuhu faitha huwa zahiqun walakumu alwaylu mimma tasifoon **a**

# 2502

Walahu man fee a **l** ssamawati wa **a** lardi waman 'indahu la yastakbiroona 'an 'ibadatihi wala yastahsiroon **a**

# 2503

Yusabbihoona allayla wa **al** nnahara la yafturoon **a**

# 2504

Ami ittakhathoo alihatan mina alardi hum yunshiroon **a**

# 2505

Law kana feehimaalihatun illa Allahu lafasadata fasubhana Allahi rabbi al'arshi 'amma yasifoon **a**

# 2506

La yusalu 'amma yaf'alu wahum yusaloon **a**

# 2507

Ami ittakhathoo min doonihi alihatan qul hatoo burhanakum hathathikru man ma'iya wathikru man qablee bal aktharuhum la ya'lamoona alhaqqa fahum mu'ridoon **a**

# 2508

Wama arsana min qablika min rasoolin illa noohee ilayhi annahu la ilaha illa ana fa **o** 'budoon **i**

# 2509

Waqaloo ittakhatha a **l** rrahmanu waladan subhanahu bal 'ibadun mukramoon **a**

# 2510

La yasbiqoonahu bi **a** lqawli wahum biamrihi ya'maloon **a**

# 2511

Ya'lamu ma bayna aydeehim wama khalfahum wala yashfa'oona illa limani irtada wahum min khashyatihi mushfiqoon **a**

# 2512

Waman yaqul minhum innee ilahun min doonihi fathalika najzeehi jahannama kathalika najzee a **l** _thth_ alimeen **a**

# 2513

Awalam yara allatheena kafaroo anna a **l** ssamawati wa **a** larda kanata ratqan fafataqnahuma waja'ana mina almai kulla shayin hayyin afala yuminoon **a**

# 2514

Waja'ana fee alardi rawasiya an tameeda bihim waja'ana feeha fijajan subulan la'allahum yahtadoon **a**

# 2515

Waja'ana a **l** ssamaa saqfan mahfoo _th_ an wahum 'an ayatiha mu'ridoon **a**

# 2516

Wahuwa allathee khalaqa allayla wa **al** nnahara wa **al** shshamsa wa **a** lqamara kullun fee falakin yasbahoon **a**

# 2517

Wama ja'ana libasharin min qablika alkhulda afain mitta fahumu alkhalidoon **a**

# 2518

Kullu nafsin thaiqatu almawti wanablookum bi **al** shsharri wa **a** lkhayri fitnatan wailayna turja'oon **a**

# 2519

Waitha raaka allatheena kafaroo in yattakhithoonaka illa huzuwan ahatha allathee yathkuru alihatakum wahum bithikri a **l** rrahmani hum kafiroon **a**

# 2520

Khuliqa alinsanu min 'ajalin saoreekum ayatee fala tasta'jiloon **a**

# 2521

Wayaqooloona mata hatha alwa'du in kuntum sadiqeen **a**

# 2522

Law ya'lamu allatheena kafaroo heena la yakuffoona 'an wujoohihimu a **l** nnara wala 'an _th_ uhoorihim wala hum yunsaroon **a**

# 2523

Bal tateehim baghtatan fatabhatuhum fala yastatee'oona raddaha wala hum yun _th_ aroon **a**

# 2524

Walaqadi istuhzia birusulin min qablika fahaqa bi **a** llatheena sakhiroo minhum ma kanoo bihi yastahzioon **a**

# 2525

Qul man yaklaokum bi **a** llayli wa **al** nnahari mina a **l** rrahmani bal hum 'an thikri rabbihim mu'ridoon **a**

# 2526

Am lahum alihatun tamna'uhum min doonina la yastatee'oona nasra anfusihim wala hum minna yushaboon **a**

# 2527

Bal matta'na haolai waabaahum hattatala 'alayhimu al'umuru afala yarawna anna natee alarda nanqusuha min atrafiha afahumu alghaliboon **a**

# 2528

Qul innama onthirukum bi **a** lwahyi wala yasma'u a **l** ssummu a **l** ddu'aa itha ma yuntharoon **a**

# 2529

Walain massathum nafhatun min 'athabi rabbika layaqoolunna ya waylana inna kunna _th_ alimeen **a**

# 2530

Wanada'u almawazeena alqista liyawmi alqiyamati fala tu _th_ lamu nafsun shayan wain kana mithqala habbatin min khardalin atayna biha wakafa binahasibeen **a**

# 2531

Walaqad atayna moosa waharoona alfurqana wadiyaan wathikran lilmuttaqeen **a**

# 2532

Allatheena yakhshawna rabbahum bi **a** lghaybi wahum mina a **l** ssa'ati mushfiqoon **a**

# 2533

Wahathathikrun mubarakun anzanahu afaantum lahu munkiroon **a**

# 2534

Walaqad atayna ibraheema rushdahu min qablu wakunna bihi 'alimeen **a**

# 2535

Ith qala liabeehi waqawmihi ma hathihi a **l** ttamatheelu allatee antum laha 'akifoon **a**

# 2536

Qaloo wajadnaabaana laha 'abideen **a**

# 2537

Qala laqad kuntum antum waabaokum fee dalalin mubeen **in**

# 2538

Qaloo ajitana bi **a** lhaqqi am anta mina alla'ibeen **a**

# 2539

Qala bal rabbukum rabbu a **l** ssamawati wa **a** lardi allathee fatarahunna waana 'alathalikum mina a **l** shshahideen **a**

# 2540

Wata **A** llahi laakeedanna asnamakum ba'da an tuwalloo mudbireen **a**

# 2541

Faja'alahum juthathan illa kabeeran lahum la'allahum ilayhi yarji'oon **a**

# 2542

Qaloo man fa'ala hatha bialihatina innahu lamina a **l** _thth_ alimeen **a**

# 2543

Qaloo sami'na fatan yathkuruhum yuqalu lahu ibraheem **u**

# 2544

Qaloo fatoo bihi 'ala a'yuni a **l** nnasi la'allahum yashhadoon **a**

# 2545

Qaloo aanta fa'ata hatha bialihatina ya ibraheem **u**

# 2546

Qala bal fa'alahu kabeeruhum hatha fa **i** saloohum in kanoo yantiqoon **a**

# 2547

Faraja'oo ila anfusihim faqaloo innakum antumu a **l** _thth_ alimoon **a**

# 2548

Thumma nukisoo 'ala ruoosihim laqad 'alimta ma haolai yantiqoon **a**

# 2549

Qala afata'budoona min dooni Allahi ma la yanfa'ukum shayan wala yadurrukum

# 2550

Offin lakum walima ta'budoona min dooni Allahi afala ta'qiloon **a**

# 2551

Qaloo harriqoohu wa **o** nsuroo alihatakum in kuntum fa'ileen **a**

# 2552

Qulna ya naru koonee bardan wasalaman 'ala ibraheem **a**

# 2553

Waaradoo bihi kaydan faja'anahumu alakhsareen **a**

# 2554

Wanajjaynahu walootan ila alardi allatee barakna feeha lil'alameen **a**

# 2555

Wawahabna lahu ishaqa waya'qooba nafilatan wakullan ja'anasaliheen **a**

# 2556

Waja'anahum aimmatan yahdoona biamrina waawhayna ilayhim fi'la alkhayrati waiqama a **l** ssalati waeetaa a **l** zzakati wakanoo lana 'abideen **a**

# 2557

Walootan ataynahu hukman wa'ilman wanajjaynahu mina alqaryati allatee kanat ta'malu alkhabaitha innahum kanoo qawma sawin fasiqeen **a**

# 2558

Waadkhanahu fee rahmatina innahu mina a **l** ssaliheen **a**

# 2559

Wanoohan ith nada min qablu fa **i** stajabna lahu fanajjaynahu waahlahu mina alkarbi al'a _th_ eem **i**

# 2560

Wanasarnahu mina alqawmi allatheena kaththaboo biayatina innahum kanoo qawma sawin faaghraqnahum ajma'een **a**

# 2561

Wadawooda wasulaymana ith yahkumani fee alharthi ith nafashat feehi ghanamu alqawmi wakunna lihukmihim shahideen **a**

# 2562

Fafahhamnaha sulaymana wakullan ataynahukman wa'ilman wasakhkharna ma'a dawooda aljibala yusabbihna wa **al** ttayra wakunna fa'ileen **a**

# 2563

Wa'allamnahu san'ata laboosin lakum lituhsinakum min basikum fahal antum shakiroon **a**

# 2564

Walisulaymana a **l** rreeha 'asifatan tajree biamrihi ila alardi allatee barakna feeha wakunna bikulli shayin 'alimeen **a**

# 2565

Wamina a **l** shshayateeni man yaghoosoona lahu waya'maloona 'amalan doona thalika wakunna lahum hafi _th_ een **a**

# 2566

Waayyooba ith nada rabbahu annee massaniya a **l** ddurru waanta arhamu a **l** rrahimeen **a**

# 2567

Fa **i** stajabna lahu fakashafna ma bihi min durrin waataynahu ahlahu wamithlahum ma'ahum rahmatan min 'indina wathikra lil'abideen **a**

# 2568

Waisma'eela waidreesa watha alkifli kullun mina a **l** ssabireen **a**

# 2569

Waadkhanahum fee rahmatina innahum mina a **l** ssaliheen **a**

# 2570

Watha a **l** nnooni iththahaba mughadiban fa _th_ anna an lan naqdira 'alayhi fanada fee a **l** _thth_ ulumati an la ilaha illa anta subhanaka innee kuntu mina a **l** _thth_ alimeen **a**

# 2571

Fa **i** stajabna lahu wanajjaynahu mina alghammi wakathalika nunjee almumineen **a**

# 2572

Wazakariyya ith nada rabbahu rabbi la tatharnee fardan waanta khayru alwaritheen **a**

# 2573

Fa **i** stajabna lahu wawahabna lahu yahya waaslahna lahu zawjahu innahum kanoo yusari'oona fee alkhayrati wayad'oonana raghaban warahaban wakanoo lana khashi'een **a**

# 2574

Wa **a** llatee ahsanat farjaha fanafakhna feeha min roohina waja'anaha wa **i** bnahaayatan lil'alameen **a**

# 2575

Inna hathihi ommatukum ommatan wahidatan waana rabbukum fao'budoon **i**

# 2576

Wataqatta'oo amrahum baynahum kullun ilayna raji'oon **a**

# 2577

Faman ya'mal mina a **l** ssalihati wahuwa muminun fala kufrana lisa'yihi wainna lahu katiboon **a**

# 2578

Waharamun 'ala qaryatin ahlaknaha annahum la yarji'oon **a**

# 2579

Hatta itha futihat yajooju wamajooju wahum min kulli hadabin yansiloon **a**

# 2580

Wa **i** qtaraba alwa'du alhaqqu faitha hiya shakhisatun absaru allatheena kafaroo ya waylana qad kunna fee ghaflatin min hatha bal kunna _th_ alimeen **a**

# 2581

Innakum wama ta'budoona min dooni Allahi hasabu jahannama antum laha waridoon **a**

# 2582

Law kana haolai alihatan ma waradooha wakullun feeha khalidoon **a**

# 2583

Lahum feeha zafeerun wahum feeha la yasma'oon **a**

# 2584

Inna allatheena sabaqat lahum minna alhusna olaika 'anha mub'adoon **a**

# 2585

La yasma'oona haseesaha wahum fee ma ishtahat anfusuhum khalidoon **a**

# 2586

La yahzunuhumu alfaza'u alakbaru watatalaqqahumu almalaikatu hatha yawmukumu allathee kuntum too'adoon **a**

# 2587

Yawma natwee a **l** ssamaa katayyi a **l** ssijlli lilkutubi kama badana awwala khalqin nu'eeduhu wa'dan 'alayna inna kunna fa'ileen **a**

# 2588

Walaqad katabna fee a **l** zzaboori min ba'di a **l** ththikri anna alarda yarithuha 'ibadiya a **l** ssalihoon **a**

# 2589

Inna fee hatha labalaghan liqawmin 'abideen **a**

# 2590

Wama arsanaka illa rahmatan lil'alameen **a**

# 2591

Qul innama yooha ilayya annama ilahukum ilahun wahidun fahal antum muslimoon **a**

# 2592

Fain tawallaw faqul athantukum 'ala sawain wain adree aqareebun am ba'eedun ma too'adoon **a**

# 2593

Innahu ya'lamu aljahra mina alqawli waya'lamu ma taktumoon **a**

# 2594

Wain adree la'allahu fitnatun lakum wamata'un ilaheen **in**

# 2595

Qala rabbi ohkum bi **a** lhaqqi warabbuna a **l** rrahmanu almusta'anu 'ala ma tasifoon **a**

# 2596

Ya ayyuha a **l** nnasu ittaqoo rabbakum inna zazalata a **l** ssa'ati shayon 'a _th_ eem **un**

# 2597

Yawma tarawnaha tathhalu kullu murdi'atin 'amma arda'at watada'u kullu thati hamlin hamlaha watara a **l** nnasa sukara wama hum bisukara walakinna 'athaba Allahi shadeed **un**

# 2598

Wamina a **l** nnasi man yujadilu fee Allahi bighayri 'ilmin wayattabi'u kulla shaytanin mareed **in**

# 2599

Kutiba 'alayhi annahu man tawallahu faannahu yudilluhu wayahdeehi ila 'athabi a **l** ssa'eer **i**

# 2600

Ya ayyuha a **l** nnasu in kuntum fee raybin mina alba'thi fainna khalaqnakum min turabin thumma min nutfatin thumma min 'alaqatin thumma min mudghatin mukhallaqatin waghayri mukhallaqatin linubayyina lakum wanuqirru fee alarhami ma nashao ila ajalin musamman thumma nukhrijukum tiflan thumma litablughoo ashuddakum waminkum man yutawaffa waminkum man yuraddu ila arthali al'umuri likayla ya'lama min ba'di 'ilmin shayan watara alarda hamidatan faitha anzana 'alayha almaa ihtazzat warabat waanbatat min kulli zawjin baheej **in**

# 2601

Thalika bianna Allaha huwa alhaqqu waannahu yuhyee almawta waannahu 'ala kulli shayin qadeer **un**

# 2602

Waanna a **l** ssa'ata atiyatun la rayba feeha waanna Allaha yab'athu man fee alquboor **i**

# 2603

Wamina a **l** nnasi man yujadilu fee Allahi bighayri 'ilmin wala hudan wala kitabin muneer **in**

# 2604

Thaniya 'itfihi liyudilla 'an sabeeli Allahi lahu fee a **l** ddunya khizyun wanutheequhu yawma alqiyamati 'athaba alhareeq **i**

# 2605

Thalika bima qaddamat yadaka waanna Allaha laysa bi _th_ allamin lil'abeed **i**

# 2606

Wamina a **l** nnasi man ya'budu Allaha 'alaharfin fain asabahu khayrun itmaanna bihi wain asabathu fitnatun inqalaba 'ala wajhihi khasira a **l** ddunya wa **a** lakhirata thalika huwa alkhusranu almubeen **u**

# 2607

Yad'oo min dooni Allahi ma la yadurruhu wama la yanfa'uhu thalika huwa a **l** ddalalu alba'eed **u**

# 2608

Yad'oo laman darruhu aqrabu min naf'ihi labisa almawla walabisa al'asheer **u**

# 2609

Inna Allaha yudkhilu allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo a **l** ssalihati jannatin tajree min tahtiha alanharu inna Allaha yaf'alu ma yureed **u**

# 2610

Man kana ya _th_ unnu an lan yansurahu Allahu fee a **l** ddunya wa **a** lakhirati falyamdud bisababin ila a **l** ssamai thumma liyaqta' falyan _th_ ur hal yuthhibanna kayduhu ma yaghee _th_ **u**

# 2611

Wakathalika anzanahu ayatin bayyinatin waanna Allaha yahdee man yureed **u**

# 2612

Inna allatheena amanoo wa **a** llatheena hadoo wa **al** ssabieena wa **al** nnasara wa **a** lmajoosa wa **a** llatheena ashrakoo inna Allaha yafsilu baynahum yawma alqiyamati inna Allaha 'ala kulli shayin shaheed **un**

# 2613

Alam tara anna Allaha yasjudu lahu man fee a **l** ssamawati waman fee alardi wa **al** shshamsu wa **a** lqamaru wa **al** nnujoomu wa **a** ljibalu wa **al** shshajaru wa **al** ddawabbu wakatheerun mina a **l** nnasi wakatheerun haqqa 'alayhi al'athabu waman yuhini Allahu fama lahu min mukrimin inna Allaha yaf'alu ma yasha **o**

# 2614

Hathani khasmani ikhtasamoo fee rabbihim fa **a** llatheena kafaroo qutti'at lahum thiyabun min narin yusabbu min fawqi ruoosihimu alhameem **u**

# 2615

Yusharu bihi ma fee butoonihim wa **a** ljulood **u**

# 2616

Walahum maqami'u min hadeed **in**

# 2617

Kullama aradoo an yakhrujoo minha min ghammin o'eedoo feeha wathooqoo 'athaba alhareeq **i**

# 2618

Inna Allaha yudkhilu allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo a **l** ssalihati jannatin tajree min tahtiha alanharu yuhallawna feeha min asawira min thahabin waluluan walibasuhum feehahareer **un**

# 2619

Wahudoo ila a **l** ttayyibi mina alqawli wahudoo ilasirati alhameed **i**

# 2620

Inna allatheena kafaroo wayasuddoona 'an sabeeli Allahi wa **a** lmasjidi alharami allathee ja'anahu li **l** nnasi sawaan al'akifu feehi wa **a** lbadi waman yurid feehi biilhadin bi _th_ ulmin nuthiqhu min 'athabin aleem **in**

# 2621

Waith bawwana liibraheema makana albayti an la tushrik bee shayan watahhir baytiya li **l** ttaifeena wa **a** lqaimeena wa **al** rrukka'i a **l** ssujood **i**

# 2622

Waaththin fee a **l** nnasi bi **a** lhajji yatooka rijalan wa'ala kulli damirin yateena min kulli fajjin 'ameeq **in**

# 2623

Liyashhadoo manafi'a lahum wayathkuroo isma Allahi fee ayyamin ma'loomatin 'ala ma razaqahum min baheemati alan'ami fakuloo minha waat'imoo albaisa alfaqeer **a**

# 2624

Thumma lyaqdoo tafathahum walyoofoo nuthoorahum walyattawwafoo bi **a** lbayti al'ateeq **i**

# 2625

Thalika waman yu'a _thth_ im hurumati Allahi fahuwa khayrun lahu 'inda rabbihi waohillat lakumu alan'amu illa ma yutla 'alaykum fa **i** jtaniboo a **l** rrijsa mina alawthani wa **i** jtaniboo qawla a **l** zzoor **i**

# 2626

Hunafaa lillahi ghayra mushrikeena bihi waman yushrik bi **A** llahi fakaannama kharra mina a **l** ssamai fatakhtafuhu a **l** ttayru aw tahwee bihi a **l** rreehu fee makanin saheeq **in**

# 2627

Thalika waman yu'a _thth_ im sha'aira Allahi fainnaha min taqwa alquloob **i**

# 2628

Lakum feeha manafi'u ila ajalin musamman thumma mahilluha ila albayti al'ateeq **i**

# 2629

Walikulli ommatin ja'ana mansakan liyathkuroo isma Allahi 'ala ma razaqahum min baheemati alan'ami failahukum ilahun wahidun falahu aslimoo wabashshiri almukhbiteen **a**

# 2630

Allatheena ithathukira Allahu wajilat quloobuhum wa **al** ssabireena 'ala ma asabahum wa **a** lmuqeemee a **l** ssalati wamimma razaqnahum yunfiqoon **a**

# 2631

Wa **a** lbudna ja'anaha lakum min sha'airi Allahi lakum feeha khayrun fa **o** thkuroo isma Allahi 'alayhasawaffa faitha wajabat junoobuha fakuloo minha waat'imoo alqani'a wa **a** lmu'tarra kathalika sakhkharnaha lakum la'allakum tashkuroon **a**

# 2632

Lan yanala Allaha luhoomuha wala dimaoha walakin yanaluhu a **l** ttaqwa minkum kathalika sakhkharaha lakum litukabbiroo Allaha 'ala ma hadakum wabashshiri almuhsineen **a**

# 2633

Inna Allaha yudafi'u 'ani allatheena amanoo inna Allaha la yuhibbu kulla khawwanin kafoor **in**

# 2634

Othina lillatheena yuqataloona biannahum _th_ ulimoo wainna Allaha 'ala nasrihim laqadeer **un**

# 2635

Allatheena okhrijoo min diyarihim bighayri haqqin illa an yaqooloo rabbuna Allahu walawla daf'u Allahi a **l** nnasa ba'dahum biba'din lahuddimat sawami'u wabiya'un wasalawatun wamasajidu yuthkaru feeha ismu Allahi katheeran walayansuranna Allahu man yansuruhu inna Allaha laqawiyyun 'azeez **un**

# 2636

Allatheena in makkannahum fee alardi aqamoo a **l** ssalata waatawoo a **l** zzakata waamaroo bi **a** lma'roofi wanahaw 'ani almunkari walillahi 'aqibatu alomoor **i**

# 2637

Wain yukaththibooka faqad kaththabat qablahum qawmu noohin wa'adun wathamood **u**

# 2638

Waqawmu ibraheema waqawmu loot **in**

# 2639

Waashabu madyana wakuththiba moosa faamlaytu lilkafireena thumma akhathtuhum fakayfa kana nakeer **i**

# 2640

Fakaayyin min qaryatin ahlaknaha wahiya _th_ alimatun fahiya khawiyatun 'ala 'urooshiha wabirin mu'attalatin waqasrin masheed **in**

# 2641

Afalam yaseeroo fee alardi fatakoona lahum quloobun ya'qiloona biha aw athanun yasma'oona biha fainnaha la ta'ma alabsaru walakin ta'ma alquloobu allatee fee a **l** ssudoor **i**

# 2642

Wayasta'jiloonaka bi **a** l'athabi walan yukhlifa Allahu wa'dahu wainna yawman 'inda rabbika kaalfi sanatin mimma ta'uddoon **a**

# 2643

Wakaayyin min qaryatin amlaytu laha wahiya _th_ alimatun thumma akhathtuha wailayya almaseer **u**

# 2644

Qul ya ayyuha a **l** nnasu innama ana lakum natheerun mubeen **un**

# 2645

Fa **a** llatheena amanoo wa'amiloo a **l** ssalihati lahum maghfiratun warizqun kareem **un**

# 2646

Wa **a** llatheena sa'aw fee ayatina mu'ajizeena olaika ashabu aljaheem **i**

# 2647

Wama arsana min qablika min rasoolin wala nabiyyin illa itha tamanna alqa a **l** shshaytanu fee omniyyatihi fayansakhu Allahu ma yulqee a **l** shshaytanu thumma yuhkimu Allahu ayatihi wa **A** llahu 'aleemun hakeem **un**

# 2648

Liyaj'ala ma yulqee a **l** shshaytanu fitnatan lillatheena fee quloobihim maradun wa **a** lqasiyati quloobuhum wainna a **l** _thth_ alimeena lafee shiqaqin ba'eed **in**

# 2649

Waliya'lama allatheena ootoo al'ilma annahu alhaqqu min rabbika fayuminoo bihi fatukhbita lahu quloobuhum wainna Allaha lahadi allatheena amanoo ilasiratin mustaqeem **in**

# 2650

Wala yazalu allatheena kafaroo fee miryatin minhu hatta tatiyahumu a **l** ssa'atu baghtatan aw yatiyahum 'athabu yawmin 'aqeem **in**

# 2651

Almulku yawmaithin lillahi yahkumu baynahum fa **a** llatheena amanoo wa'amiloo a **l** ssalihati fee jannati a **l** nna'eem **i**

# 2652

Wa **a** llatheena kafaroo wakaththaboo biayatina faolaika lahum 'athabun muheen **un**

# 2653

Wa **a** llatheena hajaroo fee sabeeli Allahi thumma qutiloo aw matoo layarzuqannahumu Allahu rizqan hasanan wainna Allaha lahuwa khayru a **l** rraziqeen **a**

# 2654

Layudkhilannahum mudkhalan yardawnahu wainna Allaha la'aleemun haleem **un**

# 2655

Thalika waman 'aqaba bimithli ma 'ooqiba bihi thumma bughiya 'alayhi layansurannahu Allahu inna Allaha la'afuwwun ghafoor **un**

# 2656

Thalika bianna Allaha yooliju allayla fee a **l** nnahari wayooliju a **l** nnahara fee allayli waanna Allaha samee'un baseer **un**

# 2657

Thalika bianna Allaha huwa alhaqqu waanna ma yad'oona min doonihi huwa albatilu waanna Allaha huwa al'aliyyu alkabeer **u**

# 2658

Alam tara anna Allaha anzala mina a **l** ssamai maan fatusbihu alardu mukhdarratan inna Allaha lateefun khabeer **un**

# 2659

Lahu ma fee a **l** ssamawati wama fee alardi wainna Allaha lahuwa alghaniyyu alhameed **u**

# 2660

Alam tara anna Allaha sakhkhara lakum ma fee alardi wa **a** lfulka tajree fee albahri biamrihi wayumsiku a **l** ssamaa an taqa'a 'ala alardi illa biithnihi inna Allaha bi **al** nnasi laraoofun raheem **un**

# 2661

Wahuwa allathee ahyakum thumma yumeetukum thumma yuhyeekum inna alinsana lakafoor **un**

# 2662

Likulli ommatin ja'ana mansakan hum nasikoohu fala yunazi'unnaka fee alamri wa **o** d'u ila rabbika innaka la'ala hudan mustaqeem **in**

# 2663

Wain jadalooka faquli Allahu a'lamu bima ta'maloon **a**

# 2664

Allahu yahkumu baynakum yawma alqiyamati feema kuntum feehi takhtalifoon **a**

# 2665

Alam ta'lam anna Allaha ya'lamu ma fee a **l** ssamai wa **a** lardi inna thalika fee kitabin inna thalika 'ala Allahi yaseer **un**

# 2666

Waya'budoona min dooni Allahi ma lam yunazzil bihi sultanan wama laysa lahum bihi 'ilmun wama li **l** _thth_ alimeena min naseer **in**

# 2667

Waitha tutla 'alayhim ayatuna bayyinatin ta'rifu fee wujoohi allatheena kafaroo almunkara yakadoona yastoona bi **a** llatheena yatloona 'alayhim ayatina qul afaonabbiokum bisharrin min thalikum a **l** nnaru wa'adaha Allahu allatheena kafaroo wabisa almaseer **u**

# 2668

Ya ayyuha a **l** nnasu duriba mathalun fa **i** stami'oo lahu inna allatheena tad'oona min dooni Allahi lan yakhluqoo thubaban walawi ijtama'oo lahu wain yaslubuhumu a **l** ththubabu shayan la yastanqithoohu minhu da'ufa a **l** ttalibu wa **a** lmatloob **u**

# 2669

Ma qadaroo Allaha haqqa qadrihi inna Allaha laqawiyyun 'azeez **un**

# 2670

Allahu yastafee mina almalaikati rusulan wamina a **l** nnasi inna Allaha samee'un baseer **un**

# 2671

Ya'lamu ma bayna aydeehim wama khalfahum waila Allahi turja'u alomoor **u**

# 2672

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo irka'oo wa **o** sjudoo wa **o** 'budoo rabbakum wa **i** f'aloo alkhayra la'allakum tuflihoon **a**

# 2673

Wajahidoo fee Allahi haqqa jihadihi huwa ijtabakum wama ja'ala 'alaykum fee a **l** ddeeni min harajin millata abeekum ibraheema huwa sammakumu almuslimeena min qablu wafee hatha liyakoona a **l** rrasoolu shaheedan 'alaykum watakoonoo shuhadaa 'ala a **l** nnasi faaqeemoo a **l** ssalata waatoo a **l** zzakata wa **i** 'tasimoo bi **A** llahi huwa mawlakum fani'ma almawla wani'ma a **l** nnaseer **u**

# 2674

Qad aflaha almuminoon **a**

# 2675

Allatheena hum fee salatihim khashi'oon **a**

# 2676

Wa **a** llatheena hum 'ani allaghwi mu'ridoon **a**

# 2677

Wa **a** llatheena hum li **l** zzakati fa'iloon **a**

# 2678

Wa **a** llatheena hum lifuroojihim hafi _th_ oon **a**

# 2679

Illa 'ala azwajihim aw ma malakat aymanuhum fainnahum ghayru maloomeen **a**

# 2680

Famani ibtagha waraa thalika faolaika humu al'adoon **a**

# 2681

Wa **a** llatheena hum liamanatihim wa'ahdihim ra'oon **a**

# 2682

Wa **a** llatheena hum 'alasalawatihim yuhafi _th_ oon **a**

# 2683

Olaika humu alwarithoon **a**

# 2684

Allatheena yarithoona alfirdawsa hum feeha khalidoon **a**

# 2685

Walaqad khalaqna alinsana min sulalatin min teen **in**

# 2686

Thumma ja'anahu nutfatan fee qararin makeen **in**

# 2687

Thumma khalaqna a **l** nnutfata 'alaqatan fakhalaqna al'alaqata mudghatan fakhalaqna almudghata 'i _th_ aman fakasawna al'i _th_ ama lahman thumma anshanahu khalqan akhara fatabaraka Allahu ahsanu alkhaliqeen **a**

# 2688

Thumma innakum ba'da thalika lamayyitoon **a**

# 2689

Thumma innakum yawma alqiyamati tub'athoon **a**

# 2690

Walaqad khalaqna fawqakum sab'a taraiqa wama kunna 'ani alkhalqi ghafileen **a**

# 2691

Waanzana mina a **l** ssamai maan biqadarin faaskannahu fee alardi wainna 'alathahabin bihi laqadiroon **a**

# 2692

Faanshana lakum bihi jannatin min nakheelin waa'nabin lakum feeha fawakihu katheeratun waminha takuloon **a**

# 2693

Washajaratan takhruju min toori saynaa tanbutu bi **al** dduhni wasibghin lilakileen **a**

# 2694

Wainna lakum fee alan'ami la'ibratan nusqeekum mimma fee butooniha walakum feeha manafi'u katheeratun waminha takuloon **a**

# 2695

Wa'alayha wa'ala alfulki tuhmaloon **a**

# 2696

Walaqad arsana noohan ila qawmihi faqala ya qawmi o'budoo Allaha ma lakum min ilahin ghayruhu afala tattaqoon **a**

# 2697

Faqala almalao allatheena kafaroo min qawmihi ma hatha illa basharun mithlukum yureedu an yatafaddala 'alaykum walaw shaa Allahu laanzala malaikatan ma sami'na bihatha fee abaina alawwaleen **a**

# 2698

In huwa illa rajulun bihi jinnatun fatarabbasoo bihi hattaheen **in**

# 2699

Qala rabbi onsurnee bima kaththaboon **i**

# 2700

Faawhayna ilayhi ani isna'i alfulka bia'yunina wawahyina faitha jaa amruna wafara a **l** ttannooru fa **o** sluk feeha min kullin zawjayni ithnayni waahlaka illa man sabaqa 'alayhi alqawlu minhum wala tukhatibnee fee allatheena _th_ alamoo innahum mughraqoon **a**

# 2701

Faitha istawayta anta waman ma'aka 'ala alfulki faquli alhamdu lillahi allathee najjana mina alqawmi a **l** _thth_ alimeen **a**

# 2702

Waqul rabbi anzilnee munzalan mubarakan waanta khayru almunzileen **a**

# 2703

Inna fee thalika laayatin wain kunna lamubtaleen **a**

# 2704

Thumma anshana min ba'dihim qarnan akhareen **a**

# 2705

Faarsana feehim rasoolan minhum ani o'budoo Allaha ma lakum min ilahin ghayruhu afala tattaqoon **a**

# 2706

Waqala almalao min qawmihi allatheena kafaroo wakaththaboo biliqai alakhirati waatrafnahum fee alhayati a **l** ddunya ma hatha illa basharun mithlukum yakulu mimma takuloona minhu wayashrabu mimma tashraboon **a**

# 2707

Walain ata'tum basharan mithlakum innakum ithan lakhasiroon **a**

# 2708

Aya'idukum annakum itha mittum wakuntum turaban wa'i _th_ aman annakum mukhrajoon **a**

# 2709

Hayhata hayhata lima too'adoon **a**

# 2710

In hiya illahayatuna a **l** ddunya namootu wanahya wama nahnu bimab'ootheen **a**

# 2711

In huwa illa rajulun iftara 'ala Allahi kathiban wama nahnu lahu bimumineen **a**

# 2712

Qala rabbi onsurnee bima kaththaboon **i**

# 2713

Qala 'amma qaleelin layusbihunna nadimeen **a**

# 2714

Faakhathathumu a **l** ssayhatu bi **a** lhaqqi faja'anahum ghuthaan fabu'dan lilqawmi a **l** _thth_ alimeen **a**

# 2715

Thumma anshana min ba'dihim quroonan akhareen **a**

# 2716

Ma tasbiqu min ommatin ajalaha wama yastakhiroon **a**

# 2717

Thumma arsana rusulana tatra kulla ma jaa ommatan rasooluha kaththaboohu faatba'na ba'dahum ba'dan waja'anahum ahadeetha fabu'dan liqawmin la yuminoon **a**

# 2718

Thumma arsana moosa waakhahu haroona biayatina wasultanin mubeen **in**

# 2719

Ila fir'awna wamalaihi fa **i** stakbaroo wakanoo qawman 'aleen **a**

# 2720

Faqaloo anuminu libasharayni mithlina waqawmuhuma lana 'abidoon **a**

# 2721

Fakaththaboohuma fakanoo mina almuhlakeen **a**

# 2722

Walaqad atayna moosa alkitaba la'allahum yahtadoon **a**

# 2723

Waja'ana ibna maryama waommahu ayatan waawaynahuma ila rabwatin thati qararin wama'een **in**

# 2724

Ya ayyuha a **l** rrusulu kuloo mina a **l** ttayyibati wa **i** 'maloo salihan innee bima ta'maloona 'aleem **un**

# 2725

Wainna hathihi ommatukum ommatan wahidatan waana rabbukum fa **i** ttaqoon **i**

# 2726

Fataqatta'oo amrahum baynahum zuburan kullu hizbin bima ladayhim farihoon **a**

# 2727

Fatharhum fee ghamratihim hattaheen **in**

# 2728

Ayahsaboona annama numidduhum bihi min malin wabaneen **a**

# 2729

Nusari'u lahum fee alkhayrati bal la yash'uroon **a**

# 2730

Inna allatheena hum min khashyati rabbihim mushfiqoon **a**

# 2731

Wa **a** llatheena hum biayati rabbihim yuminoon **a**

# 2732

Wa **a** llatheena hum birabbihim la yushrikoon **a**

# 2733

Wa **a** llatheena yutoona maataw waquloobuhum wajilatun annahum ila rabbihim raji'oon **a**

# 2734

Olaika yusari'oona fee alkhayrati wahum laha sabiqoon **a**

# 2735

Wala nukallifu nafsan illa wus'aha waladayna kitabun yantiqu bi **a** lhaqqi wahum la yu _th_ lamoon **a**

# 2736

Bal quloobuhum fee ghamratin min hatha walahum a'malun min dooni thalika hum laha 'amiloon **a**

# 2737

Hatta itha akhathna mutrafeehim bi **a** l'athabi itha hum yajaroon **a**

# 2738

La tajaroo alyawma innakum minna la tunsaroon **a**

# 2739

Qad kanat ayatee tutla 'alaykum fakuntum 'ala a'qabikum tankisoon **a**

# 2740

Mustakbireena bihi samiran tahjuroon **a**

# 2741

Afalam yaddabbaroo alqawla am jaahum ma lam yati abaahumu alawwaleen **a**

# 2742

Am lam ya'rifoo rasoolahum fahum lahu munkiroon **a**

# 2743

Am yaqooloona bihi jinnatun bal jaahum bi **a** lhaqqi waaktharuhum lilhaqqi karihoon **a**

# 2744

Walawi ittaba'a alhaqqu ahwaahum lafasadati a **l** ssamawatu wa **a** lardu waman feehinna bal ataynahum bithikrihim fahum 'an thikrihim mu'ridoon **a**

# 2745

Am tasaluhum kharjan fakharaju rabbika khayrun wahuwa khayru a **l** rraziqeen **a**

# 2746

Wainnaka latad'oohum ilasiratin mustaqeem **in**

# 2747

Wainna allatheena la yuminoona bi **a** lakhirati 'ani a **l** ssirati lanakiboon **a**

# 2748

Walaw rahimnahum wakashafna ma bihim min durrin lalajjoo fee tughyanihim ya'mahoon **a**

# 2749

Walaqad akhathnahum bi **a** l'athabi fama istakanoo lirabbihim wama yatadarra'oon **a**

# 2750

Hatta itha fatahna 'alayhim baban tha 'athabin shadeedin itha hum feehi mublisoon **a**

# 2751

Wahuwa allathee anshaa lakumu a **l** ssam'a wa **a** labsara wa **a** lafidata qaleelan ma tashkuroon **a**

# 2752

Wahuwa allathee tharaakum fee alardi wailayhi tuhsharoon **a**

# 2753

Wahuwa allathee yuhyee wayumeetu walahu ikhtilafu allayli wa **al** nnahari afala ta'qiloon **a**

# 2754

# 2755

Qaloo aitha mitna wakunna turaban wa'i _th_ aman ainna lamab'oothoon **a**

# 2756

Laqad wu'idna nahnu waabaona hatha min qablu in hatha illa asateeru alawwaleen **a**

# 2757

# 2758

Sayaqooloona lillahi qul afala tathakkaroon **a**

# 2759

# 2760

Sayaqooloona lillahi qul afala tattaqoon **a**

# 2761

Qul man biyadihi malakootu kulli shayin wahuwa yujeeru wala yujaru 'alayhi in kuntum ta'lamoon **a**

# 2762

Sayaqooloona lillahi qul faanna tusharoon **a**

# 2763

Bal ataynahum bi **a** lhaqqi wainnahum lakathiboon **a**

# 2764

Ma ittakhatha Allahu min waladin wama kana ma'ahu min ilahin ithan lathahaba kullu ilahin bima khalaqa wala'ala ba'duhum 'ala ba'din subhana Allahi 'amma yasifoon **a**

# 2765

'alimi alghaybi wa **al** shshahadati fata'ala 'amma yushrikoon **a**

# 2766

Qul rabbi imma turiyannee ma yoo'adoon **a**

# 2767

Rabbi fala taj'anee fee alqawmi a **l** _thth_ alimeen **a**

# 2768

Wainna 'ala an nuriyaka ma na'iduhum laqadiroon **a**

# 2769

Idfa' bi **a** llatee hiya ahsanu a **l** ssayyiata nahnu a'lamu bima yasifoon **a**

# 2770

Waqul rabbi a'oothu bika min hamazati a **l** shshayateen **i**

# 2771

Waa'oothu bika rabbi an yahduroon **i**

# 2772

Hatta itha jaa ahadahumu almawtu qala rabbi irji'oon **i**

# 2773

# 2774

Faitha nufikha fee a **l** ssoori fala ansaba baynahum yawmaithin wala yatasaaloon **a**

# 2775

Faman thaqulat mawazeenuhu faolaika humu almuflihoon **a**

# 2776

# 2777

# 2778

Alam takun ayatee tutla 'alaykum fakuntum biha tukaththiboon **a**

# 2779

# 2780

# 2781

# 2782

# 2783

Fa **i** ttakhathtumoohum sikhriyyan hatta ansawkum thikree wakuntum minhum tadhakoon **a**

# 2784

# 2785

# 2786

# 2787

# 2788
