# 2789

Fata'ala Allahu almaliku alhaqqu la ilaha illa huwa rabbu al'arshi alkareem **i**

# 2790

Waman yad'u ma'a Allahi ilahan akhara la burhana lahu bihi fainnamahisabuhu 'inda rabbihi innahu la yuflihu alkafiroon **a**

# 2791

Waqul rabbi ighfir wa **i** rham waanta khayru a **l** rrahimeen **a**

# 2792

Sooratun anzanaha wafaradnaha waanzana feehaayatin bayyinatin la'allakum tathakkaroon **a**

# 2793

A **l** zzaniyatu wa **al** zzanee fa **i** jlidoo kulla wahidin minhuma miata jadatin wala takhuthkum bihima rafatun fee deeni Allahi in kuntum tuminoona bi **A** llahi wa **a** lyawmi alakhiri walyashhad 'athabahumataifatun mina almumineen **a**

# 2794

A **l** zzanee la yankihu illa zaniyatan aw mushrikatan wa **al** zzaniyatu la yankihuha illa zanin aw mushrikun wahurrima thalika 'ala almumineen **a**

# 2795

Wa **a** llatheena yarmoona almuhsanati thumma lam yatoo biarba'ati shuhadaa fa **i** jlidoohum thamaneena jadatan wala taqbaloo lahum shahadatan abadan waolaika humu alfasiqoon **a**

# 2796

Illa allatheena taboo min ba'di thalika waaslahoo fainna Allaha ghafoorun raheem **un**

# 2797

Wa **a** llatheena yarmoona azwajahum walam yakun lahum shuhadao illa anfusuhum fashahadatu ahadihim arba'u shahadatin bi **A** llahi innahu lamina a **l** ssadiqeen **a**

# 2798

Wa **a** lkhamisatu anna la'nata Allahi 'alayhi in kana mina alkathibeen **a**

# 2799

Wayadrao 'anha al'athaba an tashhada arba'a shahadatin bi **A** llahi innahu lamina alkathibeen **a**

# 2800

Wa **a** lkhamisata anna ghadaba Allahi 'alayha in kana mina a **l** ssadiqeen **a**

# 2801

Walawla fadlu Allahi 'alaykum warahmatuhu waanna Allaha tawwabun hakeem **un**

# 2802

Inna allatheena jaoo bi **a** lifki 'usbatun minkum la tahsaboohu sharran lakum bal huwa khayrun lakum likulli imriin minhum ma iktasaba mina alithmi wa **a** llathee tawalla kibrahu minhum lahu 'athabun 'a _th_ eem **un**

# 2803

Lawla ith sami'tumoohu _th_ anna almuminoona wa **a** lmuminatu bianfusihim khayran waqaloo hatha ifkun mubeen **un**

# 2804

Lawla jaoo 'alayhi biarba'ati shuhadaa faith lam yatoo bi **al** shshuhadai faolaika 'inda Allahi humu alkathiboon **a**

# 2805

Walawla fadlu Allahi 'alaykum warahmatuhu fee a **l** ddunya wa **a** lakhirati lamassakum fee ma afadtum feehi 'athabun 'a _th_ eem **un**

# 2806

Ith talaqqawnahu biasinatikum wataqooloona biafwahikum ma laysa lakum bihi 'ilmun watahsaboonahu hayyinan wahuwa 'inda Allahi 'a _th_ eem **un**

# 2807

Walawla ith sami'tumoohu qultum ma yakoonu lana an natakallama bihatha subhanaka hatha buhtanun 'a _th_ eem **un**

# 2808

Ya'i _th_ ukumu Allahu an ta'oodoo limithlihi abadan in kuntum mumineen **a**

# 2809

Wayubayyinu Allahu lakumu alayati wa **A** llahu 'aleemun hakeem **un**

# 2810

Inna allatheena yuhibboona an tashee'a alfahishatu fee allatheena amanoo lahum 'athabun aleemun fee a **l** ddunya wa **a** lakhirati wa **A** llahu ya'lamu waantum la ta'lamoon **a**

# 2811

Walawla fadlu Allahi 'alaykum warahmatuhu waanna Allaha raoofun raheem **un**

# 2812

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la tattabi'oo khutuwati a **l** shshaytani waman yattabi' khutuwati a **l** shshaytani fainnahu yamuru bi **a** lfahshai wa **a** lmunkari walawla fadlu Allahi 'alaykum warahmatuhu ma zaka minkum min ahadin abadan walakinna Allaha yuzakkee man yashao wa **A** llahu samee'un 'aleem **un**

# 2813

Wala yatali oloo alfadli minkum wa **al** ssa'ati an yutoo olee alqurba wa **a** lmasakeena wa **a** lmuhajireena fee sabeeli Allahi walya'foo walyasfahoo ala tuhibboona an yaghfira Allahu lakum wa **A** llahu ghafoorun raheem **un**

# 2814

Inna allatheena yarmoona almuhsanati alghafilati almuminati lu'inoo fee a **l** ddunya wa **a** lakhirati walahum 'athabun 'a _th_ eem **un**

# 2815

Yawma tashhadu 'alayhim asinatuhum waaydeehim waarjuluhum bima kanoo ya'maloon **a**

# 2816

Yawmaithin yuwaffeehimu Allahu deenahumu alhaqqa waya'lamoona anna Allaha huwa alhaqqu almubeen **u**

# 2817

Alkhabeethatu lilkhabeetheena wa **a** lkhabeethoona lilkhabeethati wa **al** ttayyibatu li **l** ttayyibeena wa **al** ttayyiboona li **l** ttayyibati olaika mubarraoona mimma yaqooloona lahum maghfiratun warizqun kareem **un**

# 2818

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la tadkhuloo buyootan ghayra buyootikum hatta tastanisoo watusallimoo 'ala ahlihathalikum khayrun lakum la'allakum tathakkaroon **a**

# 2819

Fain lam tajidoo feeha ahadan fala tadkhuloohahatta yuthana lakum wain qeela lakumu irji'oo fa **i** rji'oo huwa azka lakum wa **A** llahu bima ta'maloona 'aleem **un**

# 2820

Laysa 'alaykum junahun an tadkhuloo buyootan ghayra maskoonatin feeha mata'un lakum wa **A** llahu ya'lamu ma tubdoona wama taktumoon **a**

# 2821

Qul lilmumineena yaghuddoo min absarihum wayahfa _th_ oo furoojahum thalika azka lahum inna Allaha khabeerun bima yasna'oon **a**

# 2822

Waqul lilmuminati yaghdudna min absarihinna wayahfa _th_ na furoojahunna wala yubdeena zeenatahunna illa ma _th_ ahara minha walyadribna bikhumurihinna 'ala juyoobihinna wala yubdeena zeenatahunna illa libu'oolatihinna aw abaihinna aw abai bu'oolatihinna aw abnaihinna aw abnai bu'oolatihinna aw ikhwanihinna aw banee ikhwanihinna aw banee akhawatihinna aw nisaihinna aw ma malakat aymanuhunna awi a **l** ttabi'eena ghayri olee alirbati mina a **l** rrijali awi a **l** ttifli allatheena lam ya _th_ haroo 'ala 'awrati a **l** nnisai wala yadribna biarjulihinna liyu'lama ma yukhfeena min zeenatihinna watooboo ila Allahi jamee'an ayyuha almuminoona la'allakum tuflihoon **a**

# 2823

Waankihoo alayama minkum wa **al** ssaliheena min 'ibadikum waimaikum in yakoonoo fuqaraa yughnihimu Allahu min fadlihi wa **A** llahu wasi'un 'aleem **un**

# 2824

Walyasta'fifi allatheena la yajidoona nikahan hatta yughniyahumu Allahu min fadlihi wa **a** llatheena yabtaghoona alkitaba mimma malakat aymanukum fakatiboohum in 'alimtum feehim khayran waatoohum min mali Allahi allathee atakum wala tukrihoo fatayatikum 'ala albighai in aradna tahassunan litabtaghoo 'arada alhayati a **l** ddunya waman yukrihhunna fainna Allaha min ba'di ikrahihinna ghafoorun raheem **un**

# 2825

Walaqad anzana ilaykum ayatin mubayyinatin wamathalan mina allatheena khalaw min qablikum wamaw'i _th_ atan lilmuttaqeen **a**

# 2826

Allahu nooru a **l** ssamawati wa **a** lardi mathalu noorihi kamishkatin feeha misbahun almisbahu fee zujajatin a **l** zzujajatu kaannaha kawkabun durriyyun yooqadu min shajaratin mubarakatin zaytoonatin la sharqiyyatin wala gharbiyyatin yakadu zaytuha yudeeo walaw lam tamsashu narun noorun 'ala noorin yahdee Allahu linoorihi man yashao wayadribu Allahu alamthala li **l** nnasi wa **A** llahu bikulli shayin 'aleem **un**

# 2827

Fee buyootin athina Allahu an turfa'a wayuthkara feeha ismuhu yusabbihu lahu feeha bi **a** lghuduwwi wa **a** lasal **i**

# 2828

Rijalun la tulheehim tijaratun wala bay'un 'an thikri Allahi waiqami a **l** ssalati waeetai a **l** zzakati yakhafoona yawman tataqallabu feehi alquloobu wa **a** labsar **u**

# 2829

Liyajziyahumu Allahu ahsana ma 'amiloo wayazeedahum min fadlihi wa **A** llahu yarzuqu man yashao bighayri hisab **in**

# 2830

Wa **a** llatheena kafaroo a'maluhum kasarabin biqee'atin yahsabuhu a **l** _thth_ amanu maan hatta itha jaahu lam yajidhu shayan wawajada Allaha 'indahu fawaffahu hisabahu wa **A** llahu saree'u alhisab **i**

# 2831

Aw ka _th_ ulumatin fee bahrin lujjiyyin yaghshahu mawjun min fawqihi mawjun min fawqihi sahabun _th_ ulumatun ba'duha fawqa ba'din itha akhraja yadahu lam yakad yaraha waman lam yaj'ali Allahu lahu nooran fama lahu min noor **in**

# 2832

Alam tara anna Allaha yusabbihu lahu man fee a **l** ssamawati wa **a** lardi wa **al** ttayru saffatin kullun qad 'alima salatahu watasbeehahu wa **A** llahu 'aleemun bima yaf'aloon **a**

# 2833

Walillahi mulku a **l** ssamawati wa **a** lardi waila Allahi almaseer **u**

# 2834

Alam tara anna Allaha yuzjee sahaban thumma yuallifu baynahu thumma yaj'aluhu rukaman fatara alwadqa yakhruju min khilalihi wayunazzilu mina a **l** ssamai min jibalin feeha min baradin fayuseebu bihi man yashao wayasrifuhu 'an man yashao yakadu sana barqihi yathhabu bi **a** labsar **i**

# 2835

Yuqallibu Allahu allayla wa **al** nnahara inna fee thalika la'ibratan liolee alabsar **i**

# 2836

Wa **A** llahu khalaqa kulla dabbatin min main faminhum man yamshee 'ala batnihi waminhum man yamshee 'ala rijlayni waminhum man yamshee 'ala arba'in yakhluqu Allahu ma yashao inna Allaha 'ala kulli shayin qadeer **un**

# 2837

Laqad anzanaayatin mubayyinatin wa **A** llahu yahdee man yashao ilasiratin mustaqeem **in**

# 2838

Wayaqooloona amanna bi **A** llahi wabi **al** rrasooli waata'na thumma yatawalla fareequn minhum min ba'di thalika wama olaika bi **a** lmumineen **a**

# 2839

Waitha du'oo ila Allahi warasoolihi liyahkuma baynahum itha fareequn minhum mu'ridoon **a**

# 2840

Wain yakun lahumu alhaqqu yatoo ilayhi muth'ineen **a**

# 2841

Afee quloobihim maradun ami irtaboo am yakhafoona an yaheefa Allahu 'alayhim warasooluhu bal olaika humu a **l** _thth_ alimoon **a**

# 2842

Innama kana qawla almumineena itha du'oo ila Allahi warasoolihi liyahkuma baynahum an yaqooloo sami'na waata'na waolaika humu almuflihoon **a**

# 2843

Waman yuti'i Allaha warasoolahu wayakhsha Allaha wayattaqhi faolaika humu alfaizoon **a**

# 2844

Waaqsamoo bi **A** llahi jahda aymanihim lain amartahum layakhrujunna qul la tuqsimoo ta'atun ma'roofatun inna Allaha khabeerun bima ta'maloon **a**

# 2845

Qul atee'oo Allaha waatee'oo a **l** rrasoola fain tawallaw fainnama 'alayhi mahummila wa'alaykum mahummiltum wain tutee'oohu tahtadoo wama 'ala a **l** rrasooli illa albalaghu almubeen **a**

# 2846

Wa'ada Allahu allatheena amanoo minkum wa'amiloo a **l** ssalihati layastakhlifannahum fee alardi kama istakhlafa allatheena min qablihim walayumakkinanna lahum deenahumu allathee irtada lahum walayubaddilannahum min ba'di khawfihim amnan ya'budoonanee la yushrikoona bee shayan waman kafara ba'da thalika faolaika humu alfasiqoon **a**

# 2847

Waaqeemoo a **l** ssalata waatoo a **l** zzakata waatee'oo a **l** rrasoola la'allakum turhamoon **a**

# 2848

La tahsabanna allatheena kafaroo mu'jizeena fee alardi wamawahumu a **l** nnaru walabisa almaseer **u**

# 2849

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo liyastathinkumu allatheena malakat aymanukum wa **a** llatheena lam yablughoo alhuluma minkum thalatha marratin min qabli salati alfajri waheena tada'oona thiyabakum mina a **l** _thth_ aheerati wamin ba'di salati al'ishai thalathu 'awratin lakum laysa 'alaykum wala 'alayhim junahun ba'dahunna tawwafoona 'alaykum ba'dukum 'ala ba'din kathalika yubayyinu Allahu lakumu alayati wa **A** llahu 'aleemun hakeem **un**

# 2850

Waitha balagha alatfalu minkumu alhuluma falyastathinoo kama istathana allatheena min qablihim kathalika yubayyinu Allahu lakum ayatihi wa **A** llahu 'aleemun hakeem **un**

# 2851

Wa **a** lqawa'idu mina a **l** nnisai allatee la yarjoona nikahan falaysa 'alayhinna junahun an yada'na thiyabahunna ghayra mutabarrijatin bizeenatin waan yasta'fifna khayrun lahunna wa **A** llahu samee'un 'aleem **un**

# 2852

Laysa 'ala ala'maharajun wala 'ala ala'raji harajun wala 'ala almareedi harajun wala 'ala anfusikum an takuloo min buyootikum aw buyooti abaikum aw buyooti ommahatikum aw buyooti ikhwanikum aw buyooti akhawatikum aw buyooti a'mamikum aw buyooti 'ammatikum aw buyooti akhwalikum aw buyooti khalatikum aw ma malaktum mafatihahu aw sadeeqikum laysa 'alaykum junahun an takuloo jamee'an aw ashtatan faitha dakhatum buyootan fasallimoo 'ala anfusikum tahiyyatan min 'indi Allahi mubarakatan tayyibatan kathalika yubayyinu Allahu lakumu alayati la'allakum ta'qiloon **a**

# 2853

Innama almuminoona allatheena amanoo bi **A** llahi warasoolihi waitha kanoo ma'ahu 'ala amrin jami'in lam yathhaboo hatta yastathinoohu inna allatheena yastathinoonaka olaika allatheena yuminoona bi **A** llahi warasoolihi faitha istathanooka liba'di shanihim fathan liman shita minhum wa **i** staghfir lahumu Allaha inna Allaha ghafoorun raheem **un**

# 2854

La taj'aloo du'aa a **l** rrasooli baynakum kadu'ai ba'dikum ba'dan qad ya'lamu Allahu allatheena yatasallaloona minkum liwathan falyahthari allatheena yukhalifoona 'an amrihi an tuseebahum fitnatun aw yuseebahum 'athabun aleem **un**

# 2855

Ala inna lillahi ma fee a **l** ssamawati wa **a** lardi qad ya'lamu ma antum 'alayhi wayawma yurja'oona ilayhi fayunabbiohum bima 'amiloo wa **A** llahu bikulli shayin 'aleem **un**

# 2856

Tabaraka allathee nazzala alfurqana 'ala 'abdihi liyakoona lil'alameena natheera **n**

# 2857

Allathee lahu mulku a **l** ssamawati wa **a** lardi walam yattakhith waladan walam yakun lahu shareekun fee almulki wakhalaqa kulla shayin faqaddarahu taqdeera **n**

# 2858

Wa **i** ttakhathoo min doonihi alihatan la yakhluqoona shayan wahum yukhlaqoona wala yamlikoona lianfusihim darran wala naf'an wala yamlikoona mawtan walahayatan wala nushoora **n**

# 2859

Waqala allatheena kafaroo in hatha illa ifkun iftarahu waa'anahu 'alayhi qawmun akharoona faqad jaoo _th_ ulman wazoora **n**

# 2860

Waqaloo asateeru alawwaleena iktatabaha fahiya tumla 'alayhi bukratan waaseela **n**

# 2861

Qul anzalahu allathee ya'lamu a **l** ssirra fee a **l** ssamawati wa **a** lardi innahu kana ghafooran raheema **n**

# 2862

Waqaloo mali hatha a **l** rrasooli yakulu a **l** tta'ama wayamshee fee alaswaqi lawla onzila ilayhi malakun fayakoona ma'ahu natheera **n**

# 2863

Aw yulqa ilayhi kanzun aw takoonu lahu jannatun yakulu minha waqala a **l** _thth_ alimoona in tattabi'oona illa rajulan mashoora **n**

# 2864

On _th_ ur kayfa daraboo laka alamthala fadalloo fala yastatee'oona sabeela **n**

# 2865

Tabaraka allathee in shaa ja'ala laka khayran min thalika jannatin tajree min tahtiha alanharu wayaj'al laka qusoora **n**

# 2866

Bal kaththaboo bi **al** ssa'ati waa'tadna liman kaththaba bi **al** ssa'ati sa'eera **n**

# 2867

Itha raathum min makanin ba'eedin sami'oo laha taghayyu _th_ an wazafeera **n**

# 2868

Waitha olqoo minha makanan dayyiqan muqarraneena da'aw hunalika thuboora **n**

# 2869

La tad'oo alyawma thubooran wahidan wa **o** d'oo thubooran katheera **n**

# 2870

Qul athalika khayrun am jannatu alkhuldi allatee wu'ida almuttaqoona kanat lahum jazaan wamaseera **n**

# 2871

Lahum feeha ma yashaoona khalideena kana 'ala rabbika wa'dan masoola **n**

# 2872

Wayawma yahshuruhum wama ya'budoona min dooni Allahi fayaqoolu aantum adlatum 'ibadee haolai am hum dalloo a **l** ssabeel **a**

# 2873

Qaloo subhanaka ma kana yanbaghee lana an nattakhitha min doonika min awliyaa walakin matta'tahum waabaahum hatta nasoo a **l** ththikra wakanoo qawman boora **n**

# 2874

Faqad kaththabookum bima taqooloona fama tastatee'oona sarfan wala nasran waman ya _th_ lim minkum nuthiqhu 'athaban kabeera **n**

# 2875

Wama arsana qablaka mina almursaleena illa innahum layakuloona a **l** tta'ama wayamshoona fee alaswaqi waja'ana ba'dakum liba'din fitnatan atasbiroona wakana rabbuka baseera **n**

# 2876

Waqala allatheena la yarjoona liqaana lawla onzila 'alayna almalaikatu aw nara rabbana laqadi istakbaroo fee anfusihim wa'ataw 'utuwwan kabeera **n**

# 2877

Yawma yarawna almalaikata la bushra yawmaithin lilmujrimeena wayaqooloona hijran mahjoora **n**

# 2878

Waqadimna ila ma 'amiloo min 'amalin faja'anahu habaan manthoora **n**

# 2879

Ashabu aljannati yawmaithin khayrun mustaqarran waahsanu maqeela **n**

# 2880

Wayawma tashaqqaqu a **l** ssamao bi **a** lghamami wanuzzila almalaikatu tanzeela **n**

# 2881

Almulku yawmaithin alhaqqu li **l** rrahmani wakana yawman 'ala alkafireena 'aseera **n**

# 2882

Wayawma ya'addu a **l** _thth_ alimu 'ala yadayhi yaqoolu ya laytanee ittakhathtu ma'a a **l** rrasooli sabeela **n**

# 2883

Ya waylata laytanee lam attakhith fulanan khaleela **n**

# 2884

Laqad adallanee 'ani a **l** ththikri ba'da ith jaanee wakana a **l** shshaytanu lilinsani khathoola **n**

# 2885

Waqala a **l** rrasoolu ya rabbi inna qawmee ittakhathoo hatha alqurana mahjoora **n**

# 2886

Wakathalika ja'ana likulli nabiyyin 'aduwwan mina almujrimeena wakafa birabbika hadiyan wanaseera **n**

# 2887

Waqala allatheena kafaroo lawla nuzzila 'alayhi alquranu jumlatan wahidatan kathalika linuthabbita bihi fuadaka warattanahu tarteela **n**

# 2888

Wala yatoonaka bimathalin illa jinaka bi **a** lhaqqi waahsana tafseera **n**

# 2889

Allatheena yuhsharoona 'ala wujoohihim ila jahannama olaika sharrun makanan waadallu sabeela **n**

# 2890

Walaqad atayna moosa alkitaba waja'ana ma'ahu akhahu haroona wazeera **n**

# 2891

Faqulna ithhaba ila alqawmi allatheena kaththaboo biayatina fadammarnahum tadmeera **n**

# 2892

Waqawma noohin lamma kaththaboo a **l** rrusula aghraqnahum waja'anahum li **l** nnasi ayatan waa'tadna li **l** _thth_ alimeena 'athaban aleema **n**

# 2893

Wa'adan wathamooda waashaba a **l** rrassi waquroonan bayna thalika katheera **n**

# 2894

Wakullan darabna lahu alamthala wakullan tabbarna tatbeera **n**

# 2895

Walaqad ataw 'ala alqaryati allatee omtirat matara a **l** ssawi afalam yakoonoo yarawnaha bal kanoo la yarjoona nushoora **n**

# 2896

Waitha raawka in yattakhithoonaka illa huzuwan ahatha allathee ba'atha Allahu rasoola **n**

# 2897

In kada layudilluna 'an alihatina lawla an sabarna 'alayha wasawfa ya'lamoona heena yarawna al'athaba man adallu sabeela **n**

# 2898

Araayta mani ittakhatha ilahahu hawahu afaanta takoonu 'alayhi wakeela **n**

# 2899

Am tahsabu anna aktharahum yasma'oona aw ya'qiloona in hum illa ka **a** lan'ami bal hum adallu sabeela **n**

# 2900

Alam tara ila rabbika kayfa madda a **l** _thth_ illa walaw shaa laja'alahu sakinan thumma ja'ana a **l** shshamsa 'alayhi daleela **n**

# 2901

Thumma qabadnahu ilayna qabdan yaseera **n**

# 2902

Wahuwa allathee ja'ala lakumu allayla libasan wa **al** nnawma subatan waja'ala a **l** nnahara nushoora **n**

# 2903

Wahuwa allathee arsala a **l** rriyaha bushran bayna yaday rahmatihi waanzana mina a **l** ssamai maan tahoora **n**

# 2904

Linuhyiya bihi badatan maytan wanusqiyahu mimma khalaqna an'aman waanasiyya katheera **n**

# 2905

Walaqad sarrafnahu baynahum liyaththakkaroo faaba aktharu a **l** nnasi illa kufoora **n**

# 2906

Walaw shina laba'athna fee kulli qaryatin natheera **n**

# 2907

Fala tuti'i alkafireena wajahidhum bihi jihadan kabeera **n**

# 2908

Wahuwa allathee maraja albahrayni hatha 'athbun furatun wahatha milhun ojajun waja'ala baynahuma barzakhan wahijran mahjoora **n**

# 2909

Wahuwa allathee khalaqa mina almai basharan faja'alahu nasaban wasihran wakana rabbuka qadeera **n**

# 2910

Waya'budoona min dooni Allahi ma la yanfa'uhum wala yadurruhum wakana alkafiru 'ala rabbihi _th_ aheera **n**

# 2911

Wama arsanaka illa mubashshiran wanatheera **n**

# 2912

Qul ma asalukum 'alayhi min ajrin illa man shaa an yattakhitha ila rabbihi sabeela **n**

# 2913

Watawakkal 'ala alhayyi allathee la yamootu wasabbih bihamdihi wakafa bihi bithunoobi 'ibadihi khabeera **n**

# 2914

Allathee khalaqa a **l** ssamawati wa **a** larda wama baynahuma fee sittati ayyamin thumma istawa 'ala al'arshi a **l** rrahmanu fa **i** sal bihi khabeera **n**

# 2915

Waitha qeela lahumu osjudoo li **l** rrahmani qaloo wama a **l** rrahmanu anasjudu lima tamuruna wazadahum nufoora **n**

# 2916

Tabaraka allathee ja'ala fee a **l** ssamai buroojan waja'ala feeha sirajan waqamaran muneera **n**

# 2917

Wahuwa allathee ja'ala allayla wa **al** nnahara khilfatan liman arada an yaththakkara aw arada shukoora **n**

# 2918

Wa'ibadu a **l** rrahmani allatheena yamshoona 'ala alardi hawnan waitha khatabahumu aljahiloona qaloo salama **n**

# 2919

Wa **a** llatheena yabeetoona lirabbihim sujjadan waqiyama **n**

# 2920

Wa **a** llatheena yaqooloona rabbana isrif 'anna 'athaba jahannama inna 'athabaha kana gharama **n**

# 2921

Innaha saat mustaqarran wamuqama **n**

# 2922

Wa **a** llatheena itha anfaqoo lam yusrifoo walam yaqturoo wakana bayna thalika qawama **n**

# 2923

Wa **a** llatheena la yad'oona ma'a Allahi ilahan akhara wala yaqtuloona a **l** nnafsa allatee harrama Allahu illa bi **a** lhaqqi wala yaznoona waman yaf'al thalika yalqa athama **n**

# 2924

Yuda'af lahu al'athabu yawma alqiyamati wayakhlud feehi muhana **n**

# 2925

Illa man taba waamana wa'amila 'amalan salihan faolaika yubaddilu Allahu sayyiatihim hasanatin wakana Allahu ghafooran raheema **n**

# 2926

Waman taba wa'amila salihan fainnahu yatoobu ila Allahi mataba **n**

# 2927

# 2928

# 2929

# 2930

# 2931

Illa man _th_ alama thumma baddala husnan ba'da sooin fainnee ghafoorun raheem **un**

# 3171

Waadkhil yadaka fee jaybika takhruj baydaa min ghayri sooin fee tis'i ayatin ila fir'awna waqawmihi innahum kanoo qawman fasiqeen **a**

# 3172

Falamma jaathum ayatuna mubsiratan qaloo hatha sihrun mubeen **un**

# 3173

Wajahadoo biha wa **i** stayqanatha anfusuhum _th_ ulman wa'uluwwan fa **o** n _th_ ur kayfa kana 'aqibatu almufsideen **a**

# 3174

Walaqad atayna dawooda wasulaymana 'ilman waqala alhamdu lillahi allathee faddalana 'ala katheerin min 'ibadihi almumineen **a**

# 3175

Wawaritha sulaymanu dawooda waqala ya ayyuha a **l** nnasu 'ullimna mantiqa a **l** ttayri waooteena min kulli shayin inna hatha lahuwa alfadlu almubeen **u**

# 3176

Wahushira lisulaymana junooduhu mina aljinni wa **a** linsi wa **al** ttayri fahum yooza'oon **a**

# 3177

Hatta itha ataw 'ala wadi a **l** nnamli qalat namlatun ya ayyuha a **l** nnamlu odkhuloo masakinakum la yahtimannakum sulaymanu wajunooduhu wahum la yash'uroon **a**

# 3178

Fatabassama dahikan min qawliha waqala rabbi awzi'nee an ashkura ni'mataka allatee an'amta 'alayya wa'ala walidayya waan a'mala salihan tardahu waadkhilnee birahmatika fee 'ibadika a **l** ssaliheen **a**

# 3179

Watafaqqada a **l** ttayra faqala ma liya la ara alhudhuda am kana mina alghaibeen **a**

# 3180

Lao'aththibannahu 'athaban shadeedan aw laathbahannahu aw layatiyannee bisultanin mubeen **in**

# 3181

Famakatha ghayra ba'eedin faqala ahattu bima lam tuhit bihi wajituka min sabain binabain yaqeen **in**

# 3182

Innee wajadtu imraatan tamlikuhum waootiyat min kulli shayin walaha 'arshun 'a _th_ eem **un**

# 3183

Wajadtuha waqawmaha yasjudoona li **l** shshamsi min dooni Allahi wazayyana lahumu a **l** shshaytanu a'malahum fasaddahum 'ani a **l** ssabeeli fahum la yahtadoon **a**

# 3184

Alla yasjudoo lillahi allathee yukhriju alkhabaa fee a **l** ssamawati wa **a** lardi waya'lamu ma tukhfoona wama tu'linoon **a**

# 3185

Allahu la ilaha illa huwa rabbu al'arshi al'a _th_ eem **i**

# 3186

Qala sanan _th_ uru asadaqta am kunta mina alkathibeen **a**

# 3187

Ithhab bikitabee hatha faalqih ilayhim thumma tawalla 'anhum fa **o** n _th_ ur matha yarji'oon **a**

# 3188

Qalat ya ayyuha almalao innee olqiya ilayya kitabun kareem **un**

# 3189

Innahu min sulaymana wainnahu bismi Allahi a **l** rrahmani a **l** rraheem **i**

# 3190

Alla ta'loo 'alayya watoonee muslimeen **a**

# 3191

Qalat ya ayyuha almalao aftoonee fee amree ma kuntu qati'atan amran hatta tashhadoon **a**

# 3192

Qaloo nahnu oloo quwwatin waoloo basin shadeedin wa **a** lamru ilayki fa **o** n _th_ uree matha tamureen **a**

# 3193

Qalat inna almulooka itha dakhaloo qaryatan afsadooha waja'aloo a'izzata ahliha athillatan wakathalika yaf'aloon **a**

# 3194

Wainnee mursilatun ilayhim bihadiyyatin fana _th_ iratun bima yarji'u almursaloon **a**

# 3195

Falamma jaa sulaymana qala atumiddoonani bimalin famaataniya Allahu khayrun mimmaatakum bal antum bihadiyyatikum tafrahoon **a**

# 3196

Irji' ilayhim falanatiyannahum bijunoodin la qibala lahum biha walanukhrijannahum minha athillatan wahum saghiroon **a**

# 3197

Qala ya ayyuha almalao ayyukum yateenee bi'arshiha qabla an yatoonee muslimeen **a**

# 3198

Qala 'ifreetun mina aljinni anaateeka bihi qabla an taqooma min maqamika wainne 'alayhi laqawiyyun ameen **un**

# 3199

Qala allathee 'indahu 'ilmun mina alkitabi anaateeka bihi qabla an yartadda ilayka tarfuka falamma raahu mustaqirran 'indahu qala hatha min fadli rabbee liyabluwanee aashkuru am akfuru waman shakara fainnama yashkuru linafsihi waman kafara fainna rabbee ghaniyyun kareem **un**

# 3200

Qala nakkiroo laha 'arshaha nan _th_ ur atahtadee am takoonu mina allatheena la yahtadoon **a**

# 3201

Falamma jaat qeela ahakatha 'arshuki qalat kaannahu huwa waooteena al'ilma min qabliha wakunna muslimeen **a**

# 3202

Wasaddaha ma kanat ta'budu min dooni Allahi innaha kanat min qawmin kafireen **a**

# 3203

Qeela laha odkhulee a **l** ssarha falamma raathu hasibathu lujjatan wakashafat 'an saqayha qala innahu sarhun mumarradun min qawareera qalat rabbi innee _th_ alamtu nafsee waaslamtu ma'a sulaymana lillahi rabbi al'alameen **a**

# 3204

Walaqad arsana ila thamooda akhahum salihan ani o'budoo Allaha faitha hum fareeqani yakhtasimoon **a**

# 3205

Qala ya qawmi lima tasta'jiloona bi **al** ssayyiati qabla alhasanati lawla tastaghfiroona Allaha la'allakum turhamoon **a**

# 3206

Qaloo ittayyarna bika wabiman ma'aka qala tairukum 'inda Allahi bal antum qawmun tuftanoon **a**

# 3207

Wakana fee almadeenati tis'atu rahtin yufsidoona fee alardi wala yuslihoon **a**

# 3208

Qaloo taqasamoo bi **A** llahi lanubayyitannahu waahlahu thumma lanaqoolanna liwaliyyihi ma shahidna mahlika ahlihi wainna lasadiqoon **a**

# 3209

Wamakaroo makran wamakarna makran wahum la yash'uroon **a**

# 3210

Fa **o** n _th_ ur kayfa kana 'aqibatu makrihim anna dammarnahum waqawmahum ajma'een **a**

# 3211

Fatilka buyootuhum khawiyatan bima _th_ alamoo inna fee thalika laayatan liqawmin ya'lamoon **a**

# 3212

Waanjayna allatheena amanoo wakanoo yattaqoon **a**

# 3213

Walootan ith qala liqawmihi atatoona alfahishata waantum tubsiroon **a**

# 3214

Ainnakum latatoona a **l** rrijala shahwatan min dooni a **l** nnisai bal antum qawmun tajhaloon **a**

# 3215

Fama kana jawaba qawmihi illa an qaloo akhrijoo ala lootin min qaryatikum innahum onasun yatatahharoon **a**

# 3216

Faanjaynahu waahlahu illa imraatahu qaddarnaha mina alghabireen **a**

# 3217

Waamtarna 'alayhim mataran fasaa mataru almunthareen **a**

# 3218

Quli alhamdu lillahi wasalamun 'ala 'ibadihi allatheena istafaallahu khayrun amma yushrikoon **a**

# 3219

Amman khalaqa a **l** ssamawati wa **a** larda waanzala lakum mina a **l** ssamai maan faanbatna bihi hadaiqa thata bahjatin ma kana lakum an tunbitoo shajaraha ailahun ma'a Allahi bal hum qawmun ya'diloon **a**

# 3220

Amman ja'ala alarda qararan waja'ala khilalaha anharan waja'ala laha rawasiya waja'ala bayna albahrayni hajizan ailahun ma'a Allahi bal aktharuhum la ya'lamoon **a**

# 3221

Amman yujeebu almudtarra itha da'ahu wayakshifu a **l** ssooa wayaj'alukum khulafaa alardi ailahun ma'a Allahi qaleelan ma tathakkaroon **a**

# 3222

Amman yahdeekum fee _th_ ulumati albarri wa **a** lbahri waman yursilu a **l** rriyaha bushran bayna yaday rahmatihi ailahun ma'a Allahi ta'ala Allahu 'amma yushrikoon **a**

# 3223

Amman yabdao alkhalqa thumma yu'eeduhu waman yarzuqukum mina a **l** ssamai wa **a** lardi ailahun ma'a Allahi qul hatoo burhanakum in kuntum sadiqeen **a**

# 3224

Qul la ya'lamu man fee a **l** ssamawati wa **a** lardi alghayba illa Allahu wama yash'uroona ayyana yub'athoon **a**

# 3225

Bali iddaraka 'ilmuhum fee alakhirati bal hum fee shakkin minha bal hum minha 'amoon **a**

# 3226

Waqala allatheena kafaroo aitha kunna turaban waabaona ainna lamukhrajoon **a**

# 3227

Laqad wu'idna hatha nahnu waabaona min qablu in hatha illa asateeru alawwaleen **a**

# 3228

Qul seeroo fee alardi fa **o** n _th_ uroo kayfa kana 'aqibatu almujrimeen **a**

# 3229

Wala tahzan 'alayhim wala takun fee dayqin mimma yamkuroon **a**

# 3230

Wayaqooloona mata hatha alwa'du in kuntum sadiqeen **a**

# 3231

Qul 'asa an yakoona radifa lakum ba'du allathee tasta'jiloon **a**

# 3232

Wainna rabbaka lathoo fadlin 'ala a **l** nnasi walakinna aktharahum la yashkuroon **a**

# 3233

Wainna rabbaka laya'lamu ma tukinnu sudooruhum wama yu'linoon **a**

# 3234

Wama min ghaibatin fee a **l** ssamai wa **a** lardi illa fee kitabin mubeen **in**

# 3235

Inna hatha alqurana yaqussu 'ala banee israeela akthara allathee hum feehi yakhtalifoon **a**

# 3236

Wainnahu lahudan warahmatun lilmumineen **a**

# 3237

Inna rabbaka yaqdee baynahum bihukmihi wahuwa al'azeezu al'aleem **u**

# 3238

Fatawakkal 'ala Allahi innaka 'ala alhaqqi almubeen **i**

# 3239

Innaka la tusmi'u almawta wala tusmi'u a **l** ssumma a **l** ddu'aa itha wallaw mudbireen **a**

# 3240

Wama anta bihadee al'umyi 'an dalalatihim in tusmi'u illa man yuminu biayatina fahum muslimoon **a**

# 3241

Waitha waqa'a alqawlu 'alayhim akhrajna lahum dabbatan mina alardi tukallimuhum anna a **l** nnasa kanoo biayatina la yooqinoon **a**

# 3242

Wayawma nahshuru min kulli ommatin fawjan mimman yukaththibu biayatina fahum yooza'oon **a**

# 3243

Hatta itha jaoo qala akaththabtum biayatee walam tuheetoo biha 'ilman ammatha kuntum ta'maloon **a**

# 3244

Wawaqa'a alqawlu 'alayhim bima _th_ alamoo fahum la yantiqoon **a**

# 3245

Alam yaraw anna ja'ana allayla liyaskunoo feehi wa **al** nnahara mubsiran inna fee thalika laayatin liqawmin yuminoon **a**

# 3246

Wayawma yunfakhu fee a **l** ssoori fafazi'a man fee a **l** ssamawati waman fee alardi illa man shaa Allahu wakullun atawhu dakhireen **a**

# 3247

Watara aljibala tahsabuha jamidatan wahiya tamurru marra a **l** ssahabi sun'a Allahi allathee atqana kulla shayin innahu khabeerun bima taf'aloon **a**

# 3248

Man jaa bi **a** lhasanati falahu khayrun minha wahum min faza'in yawmaithin aminoon **a**

# 3249

Waman jaa bi **al** ssayyiati fakubbat wujoohuhum fee a **l** nnari hal tujzawna illa ma kuntum ta'maloon **a**

# 3250

Innama omirtu an a'buda rabba hathihi albadati allathee harramaha walahu kullu shayin waomirtu an akoona mina almuslimeen **a**

# 3251

Waan atluwa alqurana famani ihtada fainnama yahtadee linafsihi waman dalla faqul innama ana mina almunthireen **a**

# 3252

Waquli alhamdu lillahi sayureekum ayatihi fata'rifoonaha wama rabbuka bighafilin 'amma ta'maloon **a**

# 3253

Taseenmeem

# 3254

Tilka ayatu alkitabi almubeen **i**

# 3255

Natloo 'alayka min nabai moosa wafir'awna bi **a** lhaqqi liqawmin yuminoon **a**

# 3256

Inna fir'awna 'ala fee alardi waja'ala ahlaha shiya'an yastad'ifu taifatan minhum yuthabbihu abnaahum wayastahyee nisaahum innahu kana mina almufsideen **a**

# 3257

Wanureedu an namunna 'ala allatheena istud'ifoo fee alardi wanaj'alahum aimmatan wanaj'alahumu alwaritheen **a**

# 3258

Wanumakkina lahum fee alardi wanuriya fir'awna wahamana wajunoodahuma minhum ma kanoo yahtharoon **a**

# 3259

Waawhayna ila ommi moosa an ardi'eehi faitha khifti 'alayhi faalqeehi fee alyammi wala takhafee wala tahzanee inna raddoohu ilayki waja'iloohu mina almursaleen **a**

# 3260

Fa **i** ltaqatahu alu fir'awna liyakoona lahum 'aduwwan wahazanan inna fir'awna wahamana wajunoodahuma kanoo khatieen **a**

# 3261

Waqalati imraatu fir'awna qurratu 'aynin lee walaka la taqtuloohu 'asa an yanfa'ana aw nattakhithahu waladan wahum la yash'uroon **a**

# 3262

Waasbaha fuadu ommi moosa farighan in kadat latubdee bihi lawla an rabatna 'ala qalbiha litakoona mina almumineen **a**

# 3263

Waqalat liokhtihi qusseehi fabasurat bihi 'an junubin wahum la yash'uroon **a**

# 3264

Waharramna 'alayhi almaradi'a min qablu faqalat hal adullukum 'ala ahli baytin yakfuloonahu lakum wahum lahu nasihoon **a**

# 3265

Faradadnahu ila ommihi kay taqarra 'aynuha wala tahzana walita'lama anna wa'da Allahi haqqun walakinna aktharahum la ya'lamoon **a**

# 3266

Walamma balagha ashuddahu wa **i** stawaataynahu hukman wa'ilman wakathalika najzee almuhsineen **a**

# 3267

Wadakhala almadeenata 'alaheeni ghaflatin min ahliha fawajada feeha rajulayni yaqtatilani hatha min shee'atihi wahatha min 'aduwwihi fa **i** staghathahu allathee min shee'atihi 'ala allathee min 'aduwwihi fawakazahu moosa faqada 'alayhi qala hatha min 'amali a **l** shshaytani innahu 'aduwwun mudillun mubeen **un**

# 3268

Qala rabbi innee _th_ alamtu nafsee fa **i** ghfir lee faghafara lahu innahu huwa alghafooru a **l** rraheem **u**

# 3269

Qala rabbi bima an'amta 'alayya falan akoona _th_ aheeran lilmujrimeen **a**

# 3270

Faasbaha fee almadeenati khaifan yataraqqabu faitha allathee istansarahu bi **a** lamsi yastasrikhuhu qala lahu moosa innaka laghawiyyun mubeen **un**

# 3271

Falamma an arada an yabtisha bi **a** llathee huwa 'aduwwun lahuma qala ya moosa atureedu an taqtulanee kama qatata nafsan bi **a** lamsi in tureedu illa an takoona jabbaran fee alardi wama tureedu an takoona mina almusliheen **a**

# 3272

Wajaa rajulun min aqsa almadeenati yas'a qala ya moosa inna almalaa yatamiroona bika liyaqtulooka fa **o** khruj innee laka mina a **l** nnasiheen **a**

# 3273

Fakharaja minha khaifan yataraqqabu qala rabbi najjinee mina alqawmi a **l** _thth_ alimeen **a**

# 3274

Walamma tawajjaha tilqaa madyana qala 'asa rabbee an yahdiyanee sawaa a **l** ssabeel **i**

# 3275

Walamma warada maa madyana wajada 'alayhi ommatan mina a **l** nnasi yasqoona wawajada min doonihimu imraatayni tathoodani qala ma khatbukuma qalata la nasqee hatta yusdira a **l** rri'ao waaboona shaykhun kabeer **un**

# 3276

Fasaqa lahuma thumma tawalla ila a **l** _thth_ illi faqala rabbi innee lima anzata ilayya min khayrin faqeer **un**

# 3277

Fajaathu ihdahuma tamshee 'ala istihyain qalat inna abee yad'ooka liyajziyaka ajra ma saqayta lana falamma jaahu waqassa 'alayhi alqasasa qala la takhaf najawta mina alqawmi a **l** _thth_ alimeen **a**

# 3278

Qalat ihdahuma ya abati istajirhu inna khayra mani istajarta alqawiyyu alameen **u**

# 3279

Qala innee oreedu an onkihaka ihda ibnatayya hatayni 'ala an tajuranee thamaniya hijajin fain atmamta 'ashran famin 'indika wama oreedu an ashuqqa 'alayka satajidunee in shaa Allahu mina a **l** ssaliheen **a**

# 3280

Qala thalika baynee wabaynaka ayyama alajalayni qadaytu fala 'udwana 'alayya wa **A** llahu 'ala ma naqoolu wakeel **un**

# 3281

Falamma qada moosaalajala wasara biahlihi anasa min janibi a **l** ttoori naran qala liahlihi omkuthoo innee anastu naran la'allee ateekum minha bikhabarin aw jathwatin mina a **l** nnari la'allakum tastaloon **a**

# 3282

Falamma ataha noodiya min shatii alwadi alaymani fee albuq'ati almubarakati mina a **l** shshajarati an ya moosa innee ana Allahu rabbu al'alameen **a**

# 3283

Waan alqi 'asaka falamma raaha tahtazzu kaannaha jannun walla mudbiran walam yu'aqqib ya moosa aqbil wala takhaf innaka mina alamineen **a**

# 3284

Osluk yadaka fee jaybika takhruj baydaa min ghayri sooin wa **o** dmum ilayka janahaka mina a **l** rrahbi fathanika burhanani min rabbika ila fir'awna wamalaihi innahum kanoo qawman fasiqeen **a**

# 3285

Qala rabbi innee qatatu minhum nafsan faakhafu an yaqtuloon **i**

# 3286

Waakhee haroonu huwa afsahu minnee lisanan faarsilhu ma'iya ridan yusaddiqunee innee akhafu an yukaththiboon **i**

# 3287

Qala sanashuddu 'adudaka biakheeka wanaj'alu lakuma sultanan fala yasiloona ilaykuma biayatina antuma wamani ittaba'akuma alghaliboon **a**

# 3288

Falamma jaahum moosa biayatina bayyinatin qaloo ma hatha illa sihrun muftaran wama sami'na bihatha fee abaina alawwaleen **a**

# 3289

Waqala moosa rabbee a'lamu biman jaa bi **a** lhuda min 'indihi waman takoonu lahu 'aqibatu a **l** ddari innahu la yuflihu a **l** _thth_ alimoon **a**

# 3290

Waqala fir'awnu ya ayyuha almalao ma 'alimtu lakum min ilahin ghayree faawqid lee ya hamanu 'ala a **l** tteeni fa **i** j'al lee sarhan la'allee attali'u ila ilahi moosa wainnee laa _th_ unnuhu mina alkathibeen **a**

# 3291

Wa **i** stakbara huwa wajunooduhu fee alardi bighayri alhaqqi wa _th_ annoo annahum ilayna la yurja'oon **a**

# 3292

Faakhathnahu wajunoodahu fanabathnahum fee alyammi fa **o** n _th_ ur kayfa kana 'aqibatu a **l** _thth_ alimeen **a**

# 3293

Waja'anahum aimmatan yad'oona ila a **l** nnari wayawma alqiyamati la yunsaroon **a**

# 3294

Waatba'nahum fee hathihi a **l** ddunya la'natan wayawma alqiyamati hum mina almaqbooheen **a**

# 3295

Walaqad atayna moosa alkitaba min ba'di ma ahlakna alquroona aloola basaira li **l** nnasi wahudan warahmatan la'allahum yatathakkaroon **a**

# 3296

Wama kunta bijanibi algharbiyyi ith qadayna ila moosa alamra wama kunta mina a **l** shshahideen **a**

# 3297

Walakinna anshana quroonan fatatawala 'alayhimu al'umuru wama kunta thawiyan fee ahli madyana tatloo 'alayhim ayatina walakinna kunna mursileen **a**

# 3298

Wama kunta bijanibi a **l** ttoori ith nadayna walakin rahmatan min rabbika litunthira qawman ma atahum min natheerin min qablika la'allahum yatathakkaroon **a**

# 3299

Walawla an tuseebahum museebatun bima qaddamat aydeehim fayaqooloo rabbana lawla arsata ilayna rasoolan fanattabi'a ayatika wanakoona mina almumineen **a**

# 3300

Falamma jaahumu alhaqqu min 'indina qaloo lawla ootiya mithla ma ootiya moosa awalam yakfuroo bima ootiya moosa min qablu qaloo sihrani ta _th_ ahara waqaloo inna bikullin kafiroon **a**

# 3301

Qul fatoo bikitabin min 'indi Allahi huwa ahda minhuma attabi'hu in kuntum sadiqeen **a**

# 3302

Fain lam yastajeeboo laka fa **i** 'lam annama yattabi'oona ahwaahum waman adallu mimmani ittaba'a hawahu bighayri hudan mina Allahi inna Allaha la yahdee alqawma a **l** _thth_ alimeen **a**

# 3303

Walaqad wassana lahumu alqawla la'allahum yatathakkaroon **a**

# 3304

Allatheena ataynahumu alkitaba min qablihi hum bihi yuminoon **a**

# 3305

Waitha yutla 'alayhim qaloo amanna bihi innahu alhaqqu min rabbina inna kunna min qablihi muslimeen **a**

# 3306

Olaika yutawna ajrahum marratayni bimasabaroo wayadraoona bi **a** lhasanati a **l** ssayyiata wamimma razaqnahum yunfiqoon **a**

# 3307

Waitha sami'oo allaghwa a'radoo 'anhu waqaloo lana a'maluna walakum a'malukum salamun 'alaykum la nabtaghee aljahileen **a**

# 3308

Innaka la tahdee man ahbabta walakinna Allaha yahdee man yashao wahuwa a'lamu bi **a** lmuhtadeen **a**

# 3309

Waqaloo in nattabi'i alhuda ma'aka nutakhattaf min ardina awalam numakkin lahum haraman aminan yujba ilayhi thamaratu kulli shayin rizqan min ladunna walakinna aktharahum la ya'lamoon **a**

# 3310

Wakam ahlakna min qaryatin batirat ma'eeshataha fatilka masakinuhum lam tuskan min ba'dihim illa qaleelan wakunna nahnu alwaritheen **a**

# 3311

Wama kana rabbuka muhlika alqurahatta yab'atha fee ommiha rasoolan yatloo 'alayhim ayatina wama kunna muhlikee alqura illa waahluha _th_ alimoon **a**

# 3312

Wama ooteetum min shayin famata'u alhayati a **l** ddunya wazeenatuha wama 'inda Allahi khayrun waabqa afala ta'qiloon **a**

# 3313

Afaman wa'adnahu wa'dan hasanan fahuwa laqeehi kaman matta'nahu mata'a alhayati a **l** ddunya thumma huwa yawma alqiyamati mina almuhdareen **a**

# 3314

Wayawma yunadeehim fayaqoolu ayna shurakaiya allatheena kuntum taz'umoon **a**

# 3315

Qala allatheena haqqa 'alayhimu alqawlu rabbana haolai allatheena aghwayna aghwaynahum kama ghawayna tabarrana ilayka ma kanoo iyyana ya'budoon **a**

# 3316

Waqeela od'oo shurakaakum fada'awhum falam yastajeeboo lahum waraawoo al'athaba law annahum kanoo yahtadoon **a**

# 3317

Wayawma yunadeehim fayaqoolu matha ajabtumu almursaleen **a**

# 3318

Fa'amiyat 'alayhimu alanbao yawmaithin fahum la yatasaaloon **a**

# 3319

Faamma man taba waamana wa'amila salihan fa'asa an yakoona mina almufliheen **a**

# 3320

Warabbuka yakhluqu ma yashao wayakhtaru ma kana lahumu alkhiyaratu subhana Allahi wata'ala 'amma yushrikoon **a**

# 3321

Warabbuka ya'lamu ma tukinnu sudooruhum wama yu'linoon **a**

# 3322

Wahuwa Allahu la ilaha illa huwa lahu alhamdu fee aloola wa **a** lakhirati walahu alhukmu wailayhi turja'oon **a**

# 3323

Qul araaytum in ja'ala Allahu 'alaykumu allayla sarmadan ila yawmi alqiyamati man ilahun ghayru Allahi yateekum bidiyain afala tasma'oon **a**

# 3324

Qul araaytum in ja'ala Allahu 'alaykumu a **l** nnahara sarmadan ila yawmi alqiyamati man ilahun ghayru Allahi yateekum bilaylin taskunoona feehi afala tubsiroon **a**

# 3325

Wamin rahmatihi ja'ala lakumu allayla wa **al** nnahara litaskunoo feehi walitabtaghoo min fadlihi wala'allakum tashkuroon **a**

# 3326

Wayawma yunadeehim fayaqoolu ayna shurakaiya allatheena kuntum taz'umoon **a**

# 3327

Wanaza'na min kulli ommatin shaheedan faqulna hatoo burhanakum fa'alimoo anna alhaqqa lillahi wadalla 'anhum ma kanoo yaftaroon **a**

# 3328

Inna qaroona kana min qawmi moosa fabagha 'alayhim waataynahu mina alkunoozi ma inna mafatihahu latanooo bi **a** l'usbati olee alquwwati ith qala lahu qawmuhu la tafrah inna Allaha la yuhibbu alfariheen **a**

# 3329

Wa **i** btaghi feemaataka Allahu a **l** ddara alakhirata wala tansa naseebaka mina a **l** ddunya waahsin kama ahsana Allahu ilayka wala tabghi alfasada fee alardi inna Allaha la yuhibbu almufsideen **a**

# 3330

Qala innama ooteetuhu 'ala 'ilmin 'indee awalam ya'lam anna Allaha qad ahlaka min qablihi mina alqurooni man huwa ashaddu minhu quwwatan waaktharu jam'an wala yusalu 'an thunoobihimu almujrimoon **a**

# 3331

Fakharaja 'ala qawmihi fee zeenatihi qala allatheena yureedoona alhayata a **l** ddunya ya layta lana mithla ma ootiya qaroonu innahu lathoo ha _thth_ in 'a _th_ eem **in**

# 3332

Waqala allatheena ootoo al'ilma waylakum thawabu Allahi khayrun liman amana wa'amila salihan wala yulaqqaha illa a **l** ssabiroon **a**

# 3333

Fakhasafna bihi wabidarihi alarda fama kana lahu min fiatin yansuroonahu min dooni Allahi wama kana mina almuntasireen **a**

# 3334

Waasbaha allatheena tamannaw makanahu bi **a** lamsi yaqooloona waykaanna Allaha yabsutu a **l** rrizqa liman yashao min 'ibadihi wayaqdiru lawla an manna Allahu 'alayna lakhasafa bina waykaannahu la yuflihu alkafiroon **a**

# 3335

Tilka a **l** ddaru alakhiratu naj'aluha lillatheena la yureedoona 'uluwwan fee alardi wala fasadan wa **a** l'aqibatu lilmuttaqeen **a**

# 3336

Man jaa bi **a** lhasanati falahu khayrun minha waman jaa bi **al** ssayyiati fala yujza allatheena 'amiloo a **l** ssayyiati illa ma kanoo ya'maloon **a**

# 3337

Inna allathee farada 'alayka alqurana laradduka ila ma'adin qul rabbee a'lamu man jaa bi **a** lhuda waman huwa fee dalalin mubeen **in**

# 3338

Wama kunta tarjoo an yulqa ilayka alkitabu illa rahmatan min rabbika fala takoonanna _th_ aheeran lilkafireen **a**

# 3339

Wala yasuddunnaka 'an ayati Allahi ba'da ith onzilat ilayka wa **o** d'u ila rabbika wala takoonanna mina almushrikeen **a**

# 3340

Wala tad'u ma'a Allahi ilahan akhara la ilaha illa huwa kullu shayin halikun illa wajhahu lahu alhukmu wailayhi turja'oon **a**

# 3341

Aliflammeem

# 3342

Ahasiba a **l** nnasu an yutrakoo an yaqooloo amanna wahum la yuftanoon **a**

# 3343

# 3344

Am hasiba allatheena ya'maloona a **l** ssayyiati an yasbiqoona saa ma yahkumoon **a**

# 3345

Man kana yarjoo liqaa Allahi fainna ajala Allahi laatin wahuwa a **l** ssamee'u al'aleem **u**

# 3346

Waman jahada fainnama yujahidu linafsihi inna Allaha laghaniyyun 'ani al'alameen **a**

# 3347

Wa **a** llatheena amanoo wa'amiloo a **l** ssalihati lanukaffiranna 'anhum sayyiatihim walanajziyannahum ahsana allathee kanoo ya'maloon **a**

# 3348

Wawassayna alinsana biwalidayhi husnan wain jahadaka litushrika bee ma laysa laka bihi 'ilmun fala tuti'huma ilayya marji'ukum faonabbiokum bima kuntum ta'maloon **a**

# 3349

Wa **a** llatheena amanoo wa'amiloo a **l** ssalihati lanudkhilannahum fee a **l** ssaliheen **a**

# 3350

Wamina a **l** nnasi man yaqoolu amanna bi **A** llahi faitha oothiya fee Allahi ja'ala fitnata a **l** nnasi ka'athabi Allahi walain jaa nasrun min rabbika layaqoolunna inna kunna ma'akum awalaysa Allahu bia'lama bima fee sudoori al'alameen **a**

# 3351

Walaya'lamanna Allahu allatheena amanoo walaya'lamanna almunafiqeen **a**

# 3352

Waqala allatheena kafaroo lillatheena amanoo ittabi'oo sabeelana wanahmil khatayakum wama hum bihamileena min khatayahum min shayin innahum lakathiboon **a**

# 3353

Walayahmilunna athqalahum waathqalan ma'a athqalihim walayusalunna yawma alqiyamati 'amma kanoo yaftaroon **a**

# 3354

Walaqad arsana noohan ila qawmihi falabitha feehim alfa sanatin illa khamseena 'aman faakhathahumu a **l** ttoofanu wahum _th_ alimoon **a**

# 3355

Faanjaynahu waashaba a **l** ssafeenati waja'anahaayatan lil'alameen **a**

# 3356

Waibraheema ith qala liqawmihi o'budoo Allaha wa **i** ttaqoohu thalikum khayrun lakum in kuntum ta'lamoon **a**

# 3357

Innama ta'budoona min dooni Allahi awthanan watakhluqoona ifkan inna allatheena ta'budoona min dooni Allahi la yamlikoona lakum rizqan fa **i** btaghoo 'inda Allahi a **l** rrizqa wa **o** 'budoohu wa **o** shkuroo lahu ilayhi turja'oon **a**

# 3358

Wain tukaththiboo faqad kaththaba omamun min qablikum wama 'ala a **l** rrasooli illa albalaghu almubeen **u**

# 3359

Awalam yaraw kayfa yubdio Allahu alkhalqa thumma yu'eeduhu inna thalika 'ala Allahi yaseer **un**

# 3360

Qul seeroo fee alardi fa **o** n _th_ uroo kayfa badaa alkhalqa thumma Allahu yunshio a **l** nnashata alakhirata inna Allaha 'ala kulli shayin qadeer **un**

# 3361

Yu'aththibu man yashao wayarhamu man yashao wailayhi tuqlaboon **a**

# 3362

Wama antum bimu'jizeena fee alardi wala fee a **l** ssamai wama lakum min dooni Allahi min waliyyin wala naseer **in**

# 3363

Wa **a** llatheena kafaroo biayati Allahi waliqaihi olaika yaisoo min rahmatee waolaika lahum 'athabun aleem **un**

# 3364

Fama kana jawaba qawmihi illa an qaloo oqtuloohu aw harriqoohu faanjahu Allahu mina a **l** nnari inna fee thalika laayatin liqawmin yuminoon **a**

# 3365

Waqala innama ittakhathtum min dooni Allahi awthanan mawaddata baynikum fee alhayati a **l** ddunya thumma yawma alqiyamati yakfuru ba'dukum biba'din wayal'anu ba'dukum ba'dan wamawakumu a **l** nnaru wama lakum min nasireen **a**

# 3366

Faamana lahu lootun waqala innee muhajirun ila rabbee innahu huwa al'azeezu alhakeem **u**

# 3367

Wawahabna lahu ishaqa waya'qooba waja'ana fee thurriyyatihi a **l** nnubuwwata wa **a** lkitaba waataynahu ajrahu fee a **l** ddunya wainnahu fee alakhirati lamina a **l** ssaliheen **a**

# 3368

Walootan ith qala liqawmihi innakum latatoona alfahishata ma sabaqakum biha min ahadin mina al'alameen **a**

# 3369

Ainnakum latatoona a **l** rrijala wataqta'oona a **l** ssabeela watatoona fee nadeekumu almunkara fama kana jawaba qawmihi illa an qaloo itina bi'athabi Allahi in kunta mina a **l** ssadiqeen **a**

# 3370

Qala rabbi onsurnee 'ala alqawmi almufsideen **a**

# 3371

Walamma jaat rusuluna ibraheema bi **a** lbushra qaloo inna muhlikoo ahli hathihi alqaryati inna ahlaha kanoo _th_ alimeen **a**

# 3372

Qala inna feeha lootan qaloo nahnu a'lamu biman feeha lanunajjiyannahu waahlahu illa imraatahu kanat mina alghabireen **a**

# 3373

Walamma an jaat rusuluna lootan seea bihim wadaqa bihim thar'an waqaloo la takhaf wala tahzan inna munajjooka waahlaka illa imraataka kanat mina alghabireen **a**

# 3374

Inna munziloona 'ala ahli hathihi alqaryati rijzan mina a **l** ssamai bima kanoo yafsuqoon **a**

# 3375

Walaqad tarakna minhaayatan bayyinatan liqawmin ya'qiloon **a**

# 3376

Waila madyana akhahum shu'ayban faqala ya qawmi o'budoo Allaha wa **o** rjoo alyawma alakhira wala ta'thaw fee alardi mufsideen **a**

# 3377

Fakaththaboohu faakhathathumu a **l** rrajfatu faasbahoo fee darihim jathimeen **a**

# 3378

Wa'adan wathamooda waqad tabayyana lakum min masakinihim wazayyana lahumu a **l** shshaytanu a'malahum fasaddahum 'ani a **l** ssabeeli wakanoo mustabsireen **a**

# 3379

Waqaroona wafir'awna wahamana walaqad jaahum moosa bi **a** lbayyinati fa **i** stakbaroo fee alardi wama kanoo sabiqeen **a**

# 3380

Fakullan akhathna bithanbihi faminhum man arsana 'alayhi hasiban waminhum man akhathathu a **l** ssayhatu waminhum man khasafna bihi alarda waminhum man aghraqna wama kana Allahu liya _th_ limahum walakin kanoo anfusahum ya _th_ limoon **a**

# 3381

Mathalu allatheena ittakhathoo min dooni Allahi awliyaa kamathali al'ankabooti ittakhathat baytan wainna awhana albuyooti labaytu al'ankabooti law kanoo ya'lamoon **a**

# 3382

Inna Allaha ya'lamu ma yad'oona min doonihi min shayin wahuwa al'azeezu alhakeem **u**

# 3383

Watilka alamthalu nadribuha li **l** nnasi wama ya'qiluha illa al'alimoon **a**

# 3384

Khalaqa Allahu a **l** ssamawati wa **a** larda bi **a** lhaqqi inna fee thalika laayatan lilmumineen **a**

# 3385

Otlu ma oohiya ilayka mina alkitabi waaqimi a **l** ssalata inna a **l** ssalata tanha 'ani alfahshai wa **a** lmunkari walathikru Allahi akbaru wa **A** llahu ya'lamu ma tasna'oon **a**

# 3386

Wala tujadiloo ahla alkitabi illa bi **a** llatee hiya ahsanu illa allatheena _th_ alamoo minhum waqooloo amanna bi **a** llathee onzila ilayna waonzila ilaykum wailahuna wailahukum wahidun wanahnu lahu muslimoon **a**

# 3387

Wakathalika anzana ilayka alkitaba fa **a** llatheena ataynahumu alkitaba yuminoona bihi wamin haolai man yuminu bihi wama yajhadu biayatina illa alkafiroon **a**

# 3388

Wama kunta tatloo min qablihi min kitabin wala takhuttuhu biyameenika ithan la **i** rtaba almubtiloon **a**

# 3389

Bal huwa ayatun bayyinatun fee sudoori allatheena ootoo al'ilma wama yajhadu biayatina illa a **l** _thth_ alimoon **a**

# 3390

Waqaloo lawla onzila 'alayhi ayatun min rabbihi qul innama alayatu 'inda Allahi wainnama ana natheerun mubeen **un**

# 3391

Awalam yakfihim anna anzana 'alayka alkitaba yutla 'alayhim inna fee thalika larahmatan wathikra liqawmin yuminoon **a**

# 3392

Qul kafa bi **A** llahi baynee wabaynakum shaheedan ya'lamu ma fee a **l** ssamawati wa **a** lardi wa **a** llatheena amanoo bi **a** lbatili wakafaroo bi **A** llahi olaika humu alkhasiroon **a**

# 3393

Wayasta'jiloonaka bi **a** l'athabi walawla ajalun musamman lajaahumu al'athabu walayatiyannahum baghtatan wahum la yash'uroon **a**

# 3394

Yasta'jiloonaka bi **a** l'athabi wainna jahannama lamuheetatun bi **a** lkafireen **a**

# 3395

Yawma yaghshahumu al'athabu min fawqihim wamin tahti arjulihim wayaqoolu thooqoo ma kuntum ta'maloon **a**

# 3396

Ya 'ibadiya allatheena amanoo inna ardee wasi'atun faiyyaya fa **o** 'budoon **i**

# 3397

Kullu nafsin thaiqatu almawti thumma ilayna turja'oon **a**

# 3398

Wa **a** llatheena amanoo wa'amiloo a **l** ssalihati lanubawwiannahum mina aljannati ghurafan tajree min tahtiha alanharu khalideena feeha ni'ma ajru al'amileen **a**

# 3399

Allatheena sabaroo wa'ala rabbihim yatawakkaloon **a**

# 3400

Wakaayyin min dabbatin la tahmilu rizqaha Allahu yarzuquha waiyyakum wahuwa a **l** ssamee'u al'aleem **u**

# 3401

Walain saatahum man khalaqa a **l** ssamawati wa **a** larda wasakhkhara a **l** shshamsa wa **a** lqamara layaqoolunna Allahu faanna yufakoon **a**

# 3402

Allahu yabsutu a **l** rrizqa liman yashao min 'ibadihi wayaqdiru lahu inna Allaha bikulli shayin 'aleem **un**

# 3403

Walain saatahum man nazzala mina a **l** ssamai maan faahya bihi alarda min ba'di mawtiha layaqoolunna Allahu quli alhamdu lillahi bal aktharuhum la ya'qiloon **a**

# 3404

Wama hathihi alhayatu a **l** ddunya illa lahwun wala'ibun wainna a **l** ddara alakhirata lahiya alhayawanu law kanoo ya'lamoon **a**

# 3405

# 3406

# 3407

# 3408

Waman a _th_ lamu mimmani iftara 'ala Allahi kathiban aw kaththaba bi **a** lhaqqi lamma jaahu alaysa fee jahannama mathwan lilkafireen **a**

# 3409

# 3410

# 3411

# 3412

Fee adna alardi wahum min ba'di ghalabihim sayaghliboon **a**

# 3413

# 3414

# 3415

# 3416

# 3417

# 3418

Awalam yaseeroo fee alardi fayan _th_ uroo kayfa kana 'aqibatu allatheena min qablihim kanoo ashadda minhum quwwatan waatharoo alarda wa'amarooha akthara mimma 'amarooha wajaathum rusuluhum bi **a** lbayyinati fama kana Allahu liya _th_ limahum walakin kanoo anfusahum ya _th_ limoon **a**

# 3419

# 3421

# 3422
