# 3423

Wayawma taqoomu a **l** ssa'atu yawmaithin yatafarraqoon **a**

# 3424

Faamma allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo a **l** ssalihati fahum fee rawdatin yuhbaroon **a**

# 3425

Waamma allatheena kafaroo wakaththaboo biayatina waliqai alakhirati faolaika fee al'athabi muhdaroon **a**

# 3426

Fasubhana Allahi heena tumsoona waheena tusbihoon **a**

# 3427

Walahu alhamdu fee a **l** ssamawati wa **a** lardi wa'ashiyyan waheena tu _th_ hiroon **a**

# 3428

Yukhriju alhayya mina almayyiti wayukhriju almayyita mina alhayyi wayuhyee alarda ba'da mawtiha wakathalika tukhrajoon **a**

# 3429

Wamin ayatihi an khalaqakum min turabin thumma itha antum basharun tantashiroon **a**

# 3430

Wamin ayatihi an khalaqa lakum min anfusikum azwajan litaskunoo ilayha waja'ala baynakum mawaddatan warahmatan inna fee thalika laayatin liqawmin yatafakkaroon **a**

# 3431

Wamin ayatihi khalqu a **l** ssamawati wa **a** lardi wa **i** khtilafu asinatikum waalwanikum inna fee thalika laayatin lil'alimeen **a**

# 3432

Wamin ayatihi manamukum bi **a** llayli wa **al** nnahari wa **i** btighaokum min fadlihi inna fee thalika laayatin liqawmin yasma'oon **a**

# 3433

Wamin ayatihi yureekumu albarqa khawfan watama'an wayunazzilu mina a **l** ssamai maan fayuhyee bihi alarda ba'da mawtiha inna fee thalika laayatin liqawmin ya'qiloon **a**

# 3434

Wamin ayatihi an taqooma a **l** ssamao wa **a** lardu biamrihi thumma itha da'akum da'watan mina alardi itha antum takhrujoon **a**

# 3435

Walahu man fee a **l** ssamawati wa **a** lardi kullun lahu qanitoon **a**

# 3436

Wahuwa allathee yabdao alkhalqa thumma yu'eeduhu wahuwa ahwanu 'alayhi walahu almathalu ala'la fee a **l** ssamawati wa **a** lardi wahuwa al'azeezu alhakeem **u**

# 3437

Daraba lakum mathalan min anfusikum hal lakum mi mma malakat aymanukum min shurakaa fee ma razaqnakum faantum feehi sawaon takhafoonahum kakheefatikum anfusakum kathalika nufassilu alayati liqawmin ya'qiloon **a**

# 3438

Bali ittaba'a allatheena _th_ alamoo ahwaahum bighayri 'ilmin faman yahdee man adalla Allahu wama lahum min nasireen **a**

# 3439

Faaqim wajhaka li **l** ddeeni haneefan fitrata Allahi allatee fatara a **l** nnasa 'alayha la tabdeela likhalqi Allahi thalika a **l** ddeenu alqayyimu walakinna akthara a **l** nnasi la ya'lamoon **a**

# 3440

Muneebeena ilayhi wa **i** ttaqoohu waaqeemoo a **l** ssalata wala takoonoo mina almushrikeen **a**

# 3441

Mina allatheena farraqoo deenahum wakanoo shiya'an kullu hizbin bima ladayhim farihoon **a**

# 3442

Waitha massa a **l** nnasa durrun da'aw rabbahum muneebeena ilayhi thumma itha athaqahum minhu rahmatan itha fareequn minhum birabbihim yushrikoon **a**

# 3443

Liyakfuroo bimaataynahum fatamatta'oo fasawfa ta'lamoon **a**

# 3444

Am anzana 'alayhim sultanan fahuwa yatakallamu bima kanoo bihi yushrikoon **a**

# 3445

Wa **i** tha athaqna a **l** nnasa rahmatan farihoo biha wain tusibhum sayyiatun bima qaddamat aydeehim itha hum yaqnatoon **a**

# 3446

Awalam yaraw anna Allaha yabsutu a **l** rrizqa liman yashao wayaqdiru inna fee thalika laayatin liqawmin yuminoon **a**

# 3447

Faati tha alqurbahaqqahu wa **a** lmiskeena wa **i** bna a **l** ssabeeli thalika khayrun lillatheena yureedoona wajha Allahi waolaika humu almuflihoon **a**

# 3448

Wamaataytum min riban liyarbuwa fee amwali a **l** nnasi fala yarboo 'inda Allahi wamaataytum min zakatin tureedoona wajha Allahi faolaika humu almud'ifoon **a**

# 3449

Allahu allathee khalaqakum thumma razaqakum thumma yumeetukum thumma yuhyeekum hal min shurakaikum man yaf'alu min thalikum min shayin subhanahu wata'ala 'amma yushrikoon **a**

# 3450

_Th_ ahara alfasadu fee albarri wa **a** lbahri bima kasabat aydee a **l** nnasi liyutheeqahum ba'da allathee 'amiloo la'allahum yarji'oon **a**

# 3451

Qul seeroo fee alardi fa **o** n _th_ uroo kayfa kana 'aqibatu allatheena min qablu kana aktharuhum mushrikeen **a**

# 3452

Faaqim wajhaka li **l** ddeeni alqayyimi min qabli an yatiya yawmun la maradda lahu mina Allahi yawmaithin yassadda'oon **a**

# 3453

Man kafara fa'alayhi kufruhu waman 'amila salihan falianfusihim yamhadoon **a**

# 3454

Liyajziya allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo a **l** ssalihati min fadlihi innahu la yuhibbu alkafireen **a**

# 3455

Wamin ayatihi an yursila a **l** rriyaha mubashshiratin waliyutheeqakum min rahmatihi walitajriya alfulku biamrihi walitabtaghoo min fadlihi wala'allakum tashkuroon **a**

# 3456

Walaqad arsana min qablika rusulan ila qawmihim fajaoohum bi **a** lbayyinati fa **i** ntaqamna mina allatheena ajramoo wakana haqqan 'alayna nasru almumineen **a**

# 3457

Allahu allathee yursilu a **l** rriyaha fatutheeru sahaban fayabsutuhu fee a **l** ssamai kayfa yashao wayaj'aluhu kisafan fatara alwadqa yakhruju min khilalihi faitha asaba bihi man yashao min 'ibadihi itha hum yastabshiroon **a**

# 3458

Wain kanoo min qabli an yunazzala 'alayhim min qablihi lamubliseen **a**

# 3459

Fa **o** n _th_ ur ilaathari rahmati Allahi kayfa yuhyee alarda ba'da mawtiha inna thalika lamuhyee almawta wahuwa 'ala kulli shayin qadeer **un**

# 3460

Walain arsana reehan faraawhu musfarran la _th_ alloo min ba'dihi yakfuroon **a**

# 3461

Fainnaka la tusmi'u almawta wala tusmi'u a **l** ssumma a **l** ddu'aa itha wallaw mudbireen **a**

# 3462

Wama anta bihadi al'umyi 'an dalalatihim in tusmi'u illa man yuminu biayatina fahum muslimoon **a**

# 3463

Allahu allathee khalaqakum min da'fin thumma ja'ala min ba'di da'fin quwwatan thumma ja'ala min ba'di quwwatin da'fan washaybatan yakhluqu ma yashao wahuwa al'aleemu alqadeer **u**

# 3464

Wayawma taqoomu a **l** ssa'atu yuqsimu almujrimoona ma labithoo ghayra sa'atin kathalika kanoo yufakoon **a**

# 3465

Waqala allatheena ootoo al'ilma wa **a** leemana laqad labithtum fee kitabi Allahi ila yawmi alba'thi fahatha yawmu alba'thi walakinnakum kuntum la ta'lamoon **a**

# 3466

Fayawmaithin la yanfa'u allatheena _th_ alamoo ma'thiratuhum wala hum yusta'taboon **a**

# 3467

Walaqad darabna li **l** nnasi fee hatha alqurani min kulli mathalin walain jitahum biayatin layaqoolanna allatheena kafaroo in antum illa mubtiloon **a**

# 3468

Kathalika yatba'u Allahu 'ala quloobi allatheena la ya'lamoon **a**

# 3469

Fa **i** sbir inna wa'da Allahi haqqun wala yastakhiffannaka allatheena la yooqinoon **a**

# 3470

Aliflammeem

# 3471

Tilka ayatu alkitabi alhakeem **i**

# 3472

Hudan warahmatan lilmuhsineen **a**

# 3473

Allatheena yuqeemoona a **l** ssalata wayutoona a **l** zzakata wahum bi **a** lakhirati hum yooqinoon **a**

# 3474

Olaika 'ala hudan min rabbihim waolaika humu almuflihoon **a**

# 3475

Wamina a **l** nnasi man yashtaree lahwa alhadeethi liyudilla 'an sabeeli Allahi bighayri 'ilmin wayattakhithaha huzuwan olaika lahum 'athabun muheen **un**

# 3476

Waitha tutla 'alayhi ayatuna walla mustakbiran kaan lam yasma'ha kaanna fee othunayhi waqran fabashshirhu bi'athabin aleem **in**

# 3477

Inna allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo a **l** ssalihati lahum jannatu a **l** nna'eem **i**

# 3478

Khalideena feeha wa'da Allahi haqqan wahuwa al'azeezu alhakeem **u**

# 3479

Khalaqa a **l** ssamawati bighayri 'amadin tarawnaha waalqa fee alardi rawasiya an tameeda bikum wabaththa feeha min kulli dabbatin waanzana mina a **l** ssamai maan faanbatna feeha min kulli zawjin kareem **in**

# 3480

Hatha khalqu Allahi faaroonee matha khalaqa allatheena min doonihi bali a **l** _thth_ alimoona fee dalalin mubeen **in**

# 3481

Walaqad atayna luqmana alhikmata ani oshkur lillahi waman yashkur fainnama yashkuru linafsihi waman kafara fainna Allaha ghaniyyun hameed **un**

# 3482

Waith qala luqmanu li **i** bnihi wahuwa ya'i _th_ uhu ya bunayya la tushrik bi **A** llahi inna a **l** shshirka la _th_ ulmun 'a _th_ eem **un**

# 3483

Wawassayna alinsana biwalidayhi hamalathu ommuhu wahnan 'ala wahnin wafisaluhu fee 'amayni ani oshkur lee waliwalidayka ilayya almaseer **u**

# 3484

Wain jahadaka 'ala an tushrika bee ma laysa laka bihi 'ilmun fala tuti'huma wasahibhuma fee a **l** ddunya ma'roofan wa **i** ttabi' sabeela man anaba ilayya thumma ilayya marji'ukum faonabbiokum bima kuntum ta'maloon **a**

# 3485

Ya bunayya innaha in taku mithqala habbatin min khardalin fatakun fee sakhratin aw fee a **l** ssamawati aw fee alardi yati biha Allahu inna Allaha lateefun khabeer **un**

# 3486

Ya bunayya aqimi a **l** ssalata wamur bi **a** lma'roofi wa **i** nha 'ani almunkari wa **i** sbir 'ala ma asabaka inna thalika min 'azmi alomoor **i**

# 3487

Wala tusa''ir khaddaka li **l** nnasi wala tamshi fee alardi marahan inna Allaha la yuhibbu kulla mukhtalin fakhoor **in**

# 3488

Wa **i** qsid fee mashyika wa **o** ghdud min sawtika inna ankara alaswati lasawtu alhameer **i**

# 3489

Alam taraw anna Allaha sakhkhara lakum ma fee a **l** ssamawati wama fee alardi waasbagha 'alaykum ni'amahu _th_ ahiratan wabatinatan wamina a **l** nnasi man yujadilu fee Allahi bighayri 'ilmin wala hudan wala kitabin muneer **in**

# 3490

Waitha qeela lahumu ittabi'oo ma anzala Allahu qaloo bal nattabi'u ma wajadna 'alayhi abaana awalaw kana a **l** shshaytanu yad'oohum ila 'athabi a **l** ssa'eer **i**

# 3491

Waman yuslim wajhahu ila Allahi wahuwa muhsinun faqadi istamsaka bi **a** l'urwati alwuthqa waila Allahi 'aqibatu alomoor **i**

# 3492

Waman kafara fala yahzunka kufruhu ilayna marji'uhum fanunabbiohum bima 'amiloo inna Allaha 'aleemun bithati a **l** ssudoor **i**

# 3493

Numatti'uhum qaleelan thumma nadtarruhum ila 'athabin ghalee _th_ **in**

# 3494

Walain saatahum man khalaqa a **l** ssamawati wa **a** larda layaqoolunna Allahu quli alhamdu lillahi bal aktharuhum la ya'lamoon **a**

# 3495

Lillahi ma fee a **l** ssamawati wa **a** lardi inna Allaha huwa alghaniyyu alhameed **u**

# 3496

Walaw annama fee alardi min shajaratin aqlamun wa **a** lbahru yamudduhu min ba'dihi sab'atu abhurin ma nafidat kalimatu Allahi inna Allaha 'azeezun hakeem **un**

# 3497

Ma khalqukum wala ba'thukum illa kanafsin wahidatin inna Allaha samee'un baseer **un**

# 3498

Alam tara anna Allaha yooliju allayla fee a **l** nnahari wayooliju a **l** nnahara fee allayli wasakhkhara a **l** shshamsa wa **a** lqamara kullun yajree ila ajalin musamman waanna Allaha bima ta'maloona khabeer **un**

# 3499

Thalika bianna Allaha huwa alhaqqu waanna ma yad'oona min doonihi albatilu waanna Allaha huwa al'aliyyu alkabeer **u**

# 3500

Alam tara anna alfulka tajree fee albahri bini'mati Allahi liyuriyakum min ayatihi inna fee thalika laayatin likulli sabbarin shakoor **in**

# 3501

Waitha ghashiyahum mawjun ka **al** _thth_ ulali da'awoo Allaha mukhliseena lahu a **l** ddeena falamma najjahum ila albarri faminhum muqtasidun wama yajhadu biayatina illa kullu khattarin kafoor **in**

# 3502

Ya ayyuha a **l** nnasu ittaqoo rabbakum wa **i** khshaw yawman la yajzee walidun 'an waladihi wala mawloodun huwa jazin 'an walidihi shayan inna wa'da Allahi haqqun fala taghurrannakumu alhayatu a **l** ddunya wala yaghurrannakum bi **A** llahi algharoor **u**

# 3503

Inna Allaha 'indahu 'ilmu a **l** ssa'ati wayunazzilu alghaytha waya'lamu ma fee alarhami wama tadree nafsun matha taksibu ghadan wama tadree nafsun biayyi ardin tamootu inna Allaha 'aleemun khabeer **un**

# 3504

Aliflammeem

# 3505

Tanzeelu alkitabi la rayba feehi min rabbi al'alameen **a**

# 3506

Am yaqooloona iftarahu bal huwa alhaqqu min rabbika litunthira qawman ma atahum min natheerin min qablika la'allahum yahtadoon **a**

# 3507

Allahu allathee khalaqa a **l** ssamawati wa **a** larda wama baynahuma fee sittati ayyamin thumma istawa 'ala al'arshi ma lakum min doonihi min waliyyin wala shafee'in afala tatathakkaroon **a**

# 3508

Yudabbiru alamra mina a **l** ssamai ila alardi thumma ya'ruju ilayhi fee yawmin kana miqdaruhu alfa sanatin mimma ta'uddoon **a**

# 3509

Thalika 'alimu alghaybi wa **al** shshahadati al'azeezu a **l** rraheem **u**

# 3510

Allathee ahsana kulla shayin khalaqahu wabadaa khalqa alinsani min teen **in**

# 3511

Thumma ja'ala naslahu min sulalatin min main maheen **in**

# 3512

Thumma sawwahu wanafakha feehi min roohihi waja'ala lakumu a **l** ssam'a wa **a** labsara wa **a** lafidata qaleelan ma tashkuroon **a**

# 3513

Waqaloo aithadalana fee alardi ainna lafee khalqin jadeedin bal hum biliqai rabbihim kafiroon **a**

# 3514

Qul yatawaffakum malaku almawti allathee wukkila bikum thumma ila rabbikum turja'oon **a**

# 3515

Walaw tara ithi almujrimoona nakisoo ruoosihim 'inda rabbihim rabbana absarna wasami'na faarji'na na'mal salihan inna mooqinoon **a**

# 3516

Walaw shina laatayna kulla nafsin hudaha walakin haqqa alqawlu minnee laamlaanna jahannama mina aljinnati wa **al** nnasi ajma'een **a**

# 3517

Fathooqoo bima naseetum liqaa yawmikum hatha inna naseenakum wathooqoo 'athaba alkhuldi bima kuntum ta'maloon **a**

# 3518

Innama yuminu biayatina allatheena ithathukkiroo biha kharroo sujjadan wasabbahoo bihamdi rabbihim wahum la yastakbiroon **a**

# 3519

Tatajafa junoobuhum 'ani almadaji'i yad'oona rabbahum khawfan watama'an wamimma razaqnahum yunfiqoon **a**

# 3520

Fala ta'lamu nafsun ma okhfiya lahum min qurrati a'yunin jazaan bima kanoo ya'maloon **a**

# 3521

Afaman kana muminan kaman kana fasiqan la yastawoon **a**

# 3522

Amma allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo a **l** ssalihati falahum jannatu almawa nuzulan bima kanoo ya'maloon **a**

# 3523

Waamma allatheena fasaqoo famawahumu a **l** nnaru kullama aradoo an yakhrujoo minha o'eedoo feeha waqeela lahum thooqoo 'athaba a **l** nnari allathee kuntum bihi tukaththiboon **a**

# 3524

Walanutheeqannahum mina al'athabi aladna doona al'athabi alakbari la'allahum yarji'oon **a**

# 3525

Waman a _th_ lamu mimman thukkira biayati rabbihi thumma a'rada 'anha inna mina almujrimeena muntaqimoon **a**

# 3526

Walaqad atayna moosa alkitaba fala takun fee miryatin min liqaihi waja'anahu hudan libanee israeel **a**

# 3527

Waja'ana minhum aimmatan yahdoona biamrina lammasabaroo wakanoo biayatina yooqinoon **a**

# 3528

Inna rabbaka huwa yafsilu baynahum yawma alqiyamati feema kanoo feehi yakhtalifoon **a**

# 3529

Awalam yahdi lahum kam ahlakna min qablihim mina alqurooni yamshoona fee masakinihim inna fee thalika laayatin afala yasma'oon **a**

# 3530

Awalam yaraw anna nasooqu almaa ila alardi aljuruzi fanukhriju bihi zar'an takulu minhu an'amuhum waanfusuhum afala yubsiroon **a**

# 3531

Wayaqooloona mata hatha alfathu in kuntum sadiqeen **a**

# 3532

Qul yawma alfathi la yanfa'u allatheena kafaroo eemanuhum wala hum yun _th_ aroon **a**

# 3533

Faa'rid 'anhum wa **i** nta _th_ ir innahum munta _th_ iroon **a**

# 3534

Ya ayyuha a **l** nnabiyyu ittaqi Allaha wala tuti'i alkafireena wa **a** lmunafiqeena inna Allaha kana 'aleeman hakeema **n**

# 3535

Wa **i** ttabi' ma yooha ilayka min rabbika inna Allaha kana bima ta'maloona khabeera **n**

# 3536

Watawakkal 'ala Allahi wakafa bi **A** llahi wakeela **n**

# 3537

Ma ja'ala Allahu lirajulin min qalbayni fee jawfihi wama ja'ala azwajakumu allaee tu _th_ ahiroona minhunna ommahatikum wama ja'ala ad'iyaakum abnaakum thalikum qawlukum biafwahikum wa **A** llahu yaqoolu alhaqqa wahuwa yahdee a **l** ssabeel **a**

# 3538

Od'oohum liabaihim huwa aqsatu 'inda Allahi fain lam ta'lamoo abaahum faikhwanukum fee a **l** ddeeni wamawaleekum walaysa 'alaykum junahun feema akhtatum bihi walakin ma ta'ammadat quloobukum wakana Allahu ghafooran raheema **n**

# 3539

A **l** nnabiyyu awla bi **a** lmumineena min anfusihim waazwajuhu ommahatuhum waoloo alarhami ba'duhum awla biba'din fee kitabi Allahi mina almumineena wa **a** lmuhajireena illa an taf'aloo ila awliyaikum ma'roofan kana thalika fee alkitabi mastoora **n**

# 3540

Waith akhathna mina a **l** nnabiyyeena meethaqahum waminka wamin noohin waibraheema wamoosa wa'eesa ibni maryama waakhathna minhum meethaqan ghalee _th_ a **n**

# 3541

Liyasala a **l** ssadiqeena 'an sidqihim waa'adda lilkafireena 'athaban aleema **n**

# 3542

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo othkuroo ni'mata Allahi 'alaykum ith jaatkum junoodun faarsana 'alayhim reehan wajunoodan lam tarawha wakana Allahu bima ta'maloona baseera **n**

# 3543

Ith jaookum min fawqikum wamin asfala minkum waith zaghati alabsaru wabalaghati alquloobu alhanajira wata _th_ unnoona bi **A** llahi a **l** _thth_ unoona

# 3544

Hunalika ibtuliya almuminoona wazulziloo zilzalan shadeeda **n**

# 3545

Waith yaqoolu almunafiqoona wa **a** llatheena fee quloobihim maradun ma wa'adana Allahu warasooluhu illa ghuroora **n**

# 3546

Waith qalat taifatun minhum ya ahla yathriba la muqama lakum fa **i** rji'oo wayastathinu fareequn minhumu a **l** nnabiyya yaqooloona inna buyootana 'awratun wama hiya bi'awratin in yureedoona illa firara **n**

# 3547

Walaw dukhilat 'alayhim min aqtariha thumma suiloo alfitnata laatawha wama talabbathoo biha illa yaseera **n**

# 3548

Walaqad kanoo 'ahadoo Allaha min qablu la yuwalloona aladbara wakana 'ahdu Allahi masoola **n**

# 3549

Qul lan yanfa'akumu alfiraru in farartum mina almawti awi alqatli waithan la tumatta'oona illa qaleela **n**

# 3550

Qul man tha allathee ya'simukum mina Allahi in arada bikum sooan aw arada bikum rahmatan wala yajidoona lahum min dooni Allahi waliyyan wala naseera **n**

# 3551

Qad ya'lamu Allahu almu'awwiqeena minkum wa **a** lqaileena liikhwanihim halumma ilayna wala yatoona albasa illa qaleela **n**

# 3552

Ashihhatan 'alaykum faitha jaa alkhawfu raaytahum yan _th_ uroona ilayka tadooru a'yunuhum ka **a** llathee yughsha 'alayhi mina almawti faithathahaba alkhawfu salaqookum biasinatin hidadin ashihhatan 'ala alkhayri olaika lam yuminoo faahbata Allahu a'malahum wakana thalika 'ala Allahi yaseera **n**

# 3553

Yahsaboona alahzaba lam yathhaboo wain yati alahzabu yawaddoo law annahum badoona fee ala'rabi yasaloona 'an anbaikum walaw kanoo feekum ma qataloo illa qaleela **n**

# 3554

Laqad kana lakum fee rasooli Allahi oswatun hasanatun liman kana yarjoo Allaha wa **a** lyawma alakhira wathakara Allaha katheera **n**

# 3555

Walamma raa almuminoona alahzaba qaloo hatha ma wa'adana Allahu warasooluhu wasadaqa Allahu warasooluhu wama zadahum illa eemanan watasleema **n**

# 3556

Mina almumineena rijalun sadaqoo ma 'ahadoo Allaha 'alayhi faminhum man qada nahbahu waminhum man yanta _th_ iru wama baddaloo tabdeela **n**

# 3557

Liyajziya Allahu a **l** ssadiqeena bisidqihim wayu'aththiba almunafiqeena in shaa aw yatooba 'alayhim inna Allaha kana ghafooran raheema **n**

# 3558

Waradda Allahu allatheena kafaroo bighay _th_ ihim lam yanaloo khayran wakafa Allahu almumineena alqitala wakana Allahu qawiyyan 'azeeza **n**

# 3559

Waanzala allatheena _th_ aharoohum min ahli alkitabi min sayaseehim waqathafa fee quloobihimu a **l** rru'ba fareeqan taqtuloona watasiroona fareeqa **n**

# 3560

Waawrathakum ardahum wadiyarahum waamwalahum waardan lam tataooha wakana Allahu 'ala kulli shayin qadeera **n**

# 3561

Ya ayyuha a **l** nnabiyyu qul liazwajika in kuntunna turidna alhayata a **l** ddunya wazeenataha fata'alayna omatti'kunna waosarrihkunna sarahan jameela **n**

# 3562

Wain kuntunna turidna Allaha warasoolahu wa **al** ddara alakhirata fainna Allaha a'adda lilmuhsinati minkunna ajran 'a _th_ eema **n**

# 3563

Ya nisaa a **l** nnabiyyi man yati minkunna bifahishatin mubayyinatin yuda'af laha al'athabu di'fayni wakana thalika 'ala Allahi yaseera **n**

# 3564

Waman yaqnut minkunna lillahi warasoolihi wata'mal salihan nutiha ajraha marratayni waa'tadna laha rizqan kareema **n**

# 3565

Ya nisaa a **l** nnabiyyi lastunna kaahadin mina a **l** nnisai ini ittaqaytunna fala takhda'na bi **a** lqawli fayatma'a allathee fee qalbihi maradun waqulna qawlan ma'roofa **n**

# 3566

Waqarna fee buyootikunna wala tabarrajna tabarruja aljahiliyyati aloola waaqimna a **l** ssalata waateena a **l** zzakata waati'na Allaha warasoolahu innama yureedu Allahu liyuthhiba 'ankumu a **l** rrijsa ahla albayti wayutahhirakum tatheera **n**

# 3567

Wa **o** thkurna ma yutla fee buyootikunna min ayati Allahi wa **a** lhikmati inna Allaha kana lateefan khabeera **n**

# 3568

Inna almuslimeena wa **a** lmuslimati wa **a** lmumineena wa **a** lmuminati wa **a** lqaniteena wa **a** lqanitati wa **al** ssadiqeena wa **al** ssadiqati wa **al** ssabireena wa **al** ssabirati wa **a** lkhashi'eena wa **a** lkhashi'ati wa **a** lmutasaddiqeena wa **a** lmutasaddiqati wa **al** ssaimeena wa **al** ssaimati wa **a** lhafi _th_ eena furoojahum wa **a** lhafi _th_ ati wa **al** ththakireena Allaha katheeran wa **al** ththakirati a'adda Allahu lahum maghfiratan waajran 'a _th_ eema **n**

# 3569

Wama kana limuminin wala muminatin itha qada Allahu warasooluhu amran an yakoona lahumu alkhiyaratu min amrihim waman ya'si Allaha warasoolahu faqad dalla dalalan mubeena **n**

# 3570

Waith taqoolu lillathee an'ama Allahu 'alayhi waan'amta 'alayhi amsik 'alayka zawjaka wa **i** ttaqi Allaha watukhfee fee nafsika ma Allahu mubdeehi watakhsha a **l** nnasa wa **A** llahu ahaqqu an takhshahu falamma qada zaydun minha wataran zawwajnakaha likay la yakoona 'ala almumineena harajun fee azwaji ad'iyaihim itha qadaw minhunna wataran wakana amru Allahi maf'oola **n**

# 3571

Ma kana 'ala a **l** nnabiyyi min harajin feema farada Allahu lahu sunnata Allahi fee allatheena khalaw min qablu wakana amru Allahi qadaran maqdoora **n**

# 3572

Allatheena yuballighoona risalati Allahi wayakhshawnahu wala yakhshawna ahadan illa Allaha wakafa bi **A** llahi haseeba **n**

# 3573

Ma kana muhammadun aba ahadin min rijalikum walakin rasoola Allahi wakhatama a **l** nnabiyyeena wakana Allahu bikulli shayin 'aleema **n**

# 3574

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo othkuroo Allaha thikran katheera **n**

# 3575

Wasabbihoohu bukratan waaseela **n**

# 3576

Huwa allathee yusallee 'alaykum wamalaikatuhu liyukhrijakum mina a **l** _thth_ ulumati ila a **l** nnoori wakana bi **a** lmumineena raheema **n**

# 3577

Tahiyyatuhum yawma yalqawnahu salamun waa'adda lahum ajran kareema **n**

# 3578

Ya ayyuha a **l** nnabiyyu inna arsanaka shahidan wamubashshiran wanatheera **n**

# 3579

Wada'iyan ila Allahi biithnihi wasirajan muneera **n**

# 3580

Wabashshiri almumineena bianna lahum mina Allahi fadlan kabeera **n**

# 3581

Wala tuti'i alkafireena wa **a** lmunafiqeena wada' athahum watawakkal 'ala Allahi wakafa bi **A** llahi wakeela **n**

# 3582

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo itha nakahtumu almuminati thumma tallaqtumoohunna min qabli an tamassoohunna fama lakum 'alayhinna min 'iddatin ta'taddoonaha famatti'oohunna wasarrihoohunna sarahan jameela **n**

# 3583

Ya ayyuha a **l** nnabiyyu inna ahlana laka azwajaka allatee atayta ojoorahunna wama malakat yameenuka mimma afaa Allahu 'alayka wabanati 'ammika wabanati 'ammatika wabanati khalika wabanati khalatika allatee hajarna ma'aka wa **i** mraatan muminatan in wahabat nafsaha li **l** nnabiyyi in arada a **l** nnabiyyu an yastankihaha khalisatan laka min dooni almumineena qad 'alimna ma faradna 'alayhim fee azwajihim wama malakat aymanuhum likayla yakoona 'alayka harajun wakana Allahu ghafooran raheema **n**

# 3584

Turjee man tashao minhunna watuwee ilayka man tashao wamani ibtaghayta mimman 'azata fala junaha 'alayka thalika adna an taqarra a'yunuhunna wala yahzanna wayardayna bimaataytahunna kulluhunna wa **A** llahu ya'lamu ma fee quloobikum wakana Allahu 'aleeman haleema **n**

# 3585

La yahillu laka a **l** nnisao min ba'du wala an tabaddala bihinna min azwajin walaw a'jabaka husnuhunna illa ma malakat yameenuka wakana Allahu 'ala kulli shayin raqeeba **n**

# 3586

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la tadkhuloo buyoota a **l** nnabiyyi illa an yuthana lakum ilata'amin ghayra na _th_ ireena inahu walakin itha du'eetum fa **o** dkhuloo faithata'imtum fa **i** ntashiroo wala mustaniseena lihadeethin inna thalikum kana yuthee a **l** nnabiyya fayastahyee minkum wa **A** llahu la yastahyee mina alhaqqi waitha saatumoohunna mata'an fa **i** saloohunna min warai hijabin thalikum atharu liquloobikum waquloobihinna wama kana lakum an tuthoo rasoola Allahi wala an tankihoo azwajahu min ba'dihi abadan inna thalikum kana 'inda Allahi 'a _th_ eema **n**

# 3587

In tubdoo shayan aw tukhfoohu fainna Allaha kana bikulli shayin 'aleema **n**

# 3588

La junaha 'alayhinna fee abaihinna wala abnaihinna wala ikhwanihinna wala abnai ikhwanihinna wala abnai akhawatihinna wala nisaihinna wala ma malakat aymanuhunna wa **i** ttaqeena Allaha inna Allaha kana 'ala kulli shayin shaheeda **n**

# 3589

Inna Allaha wamalaikatahu yusalloona 'ala a **l** nnabiyyi ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo salloo 'alayhi wasallimoo tasleema **n**

# 3590

Inna allatheena yuthoona Allaha warasoolahu la'anahumu Allahu fee a **l** ddunya wa **a** lakhirati waa'adda lahum 'athaban muheena **n**

# 3591

Wa **a** llatheena yuthoona almumineena wa **a** lmuminati bighayri ma iktasaboo faqadi ihtamaloo buhtanan waithman mubeena **n**

# 3592

Ya ayyuha a **l** nnabiyyu qul liazwajika wabanatika wanisai almumineena yudneena 'alayhinna min jalabeebihinna thalika adna an yu'rafna fala yuthayna wakana Allahu ghafooran raheema **n**

# 3593

Lain lam yantahi almunafiqoona wa **a** llatheena fee quloobihim maradun wa **a** lmurjifoona fee almadeenati lanughriyannaka bihim thumma la yujawiroonaka feeha illa qaleela **n**

# 3594

Mal'ooneena aynama thuqifoo okhithoo waquttiloo taqteela **n**

# 3595

Sunnata Allahi fee allatheena khalaw min qablu walan tajida lisunnati Allahi tabdeela **n**

# 3596

Yasaluka a **l** nnasu 'ani a **l** ssa'ati qul innama 'ilmuha 'inda Allahi wama yudreeka la'alla a **l** ssa'ata takoonu qareeba **n**

# 3597

Inna Allaha la'ana alkafireena waa'adda lahum sa'eera **n**

# 3598

Khalideena feeha abadan la yajidoona waliyyan wala naseera **n**

# 3599

Yawma tuqallabu wujoohuhum fee a **l** nnari yaqooloona ya laytana ata'na Allaha waata'na a **l** rrasoola

# 3600

Waqaloo rabbana inna ata'na sadatana wakubaraana faadalloona a **l** ssabeela

# 3601

Rabbanaatihim di'fayni mina al'athabi wa **i** l'anhum la'nan kabeera **n**

# 3602

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la takoonoo ka **a** llatheena athaw moosa fabarraahu Allahu mimma qaloo wakana 'inda Allahi wajeeha **n**

# 3603

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo ittaqoo Allaha waqooloo qawlan sadeeda **n**

# 3604

Yuslih lakum a'malakum wayaghfir lakum thunoobakum waman yuti'i Allaha warasoolahu faqad faza fawzan 'a _th_ eema **n**

# 3605

Inna 'aradna alamanata 'ala a **l** ssamawati wa **a** lardi wa **a** ljibali faabayna an yahmilnaha waashfaqna minha wahamalaha alinsanu innahu kana _th_ alooman jahoola **n**

# 3606

Liyu'aththiba Allahu almunafiqeena wa **a** lmunafiqati wa **a** lmushrikeena wa **a** lmushrikati wayatooba Allahu 'ala almumineena wa **a** lmuminati wakana Allahu ghafooran raheema **n**

# 3607

Alhamdu lillahi allathee lahu ma fee a **l** ssamawati wama fee alardi walahu alhamdu fee alakhirati wahuwa alhakeemu alkhabeer **u**

# 3608

Ya'lamu ma yaliju fee alardi wama yakhruju minha wama yanzilu mina a **l** ssamai wama ya'ruju feeha wahuwa a **l** rraheemu alghafoor **u**

# 3609

Waqala allatheena kafaroo la tateena a **l** ssa'atu qul bala warabbee latatiyannakum 'alimi alghaybi la ya'zubu 'anhu mithqalu tharratin fee a **l** ssamawati wala fee alardi wala asgharu min thalika wala akbaru illa fee kitabin mubeen **in**

# 3610

Liyajziya allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo a **l** ssalihati olaika lahum maghfiratun warizqun kareem **un**

# 3611

Wa **a** llatheena sa'aw fee ayatina mu'ajizeena olaika lahum 'athabun min rijzin aleem **in**

# 3612

Wayara allatheena ootoo al'ilma allathee onzila ilayka min rabbika huwa alhaqqa wayahdee ilasirati al'azeezi alhameed **i**

# 3613

Waqala allatheena kafaroo hal nadullukum 'ala rajulin yunabbiokum itha muzziqtum kulla mumazzaqin innakum lafee khalqin jadeed **in**

# 3614

Aftara 'ala Allahi kathiban am bihi jinnatun bali allatheena la yuminoona bi **a** lakhirati fee al'athabi wa **al** ddalali alba'eed **i**

# 3615

Afalam yaraw ila ma bayna aydeehim wama khalfahum mina a **l** ssamai wa **a** lardi in nasha nakhsif bihimu alarda aw nusqit 'alayhim kisafan mina a **l** ssamai inna fee thalika laayatan likulli 'abdin muneeb **in**

# 3616

Walaqad atayna dawooda minna fadlan ya jibalu awwibee ma'ahu wa **al** ttayra waalanna lahu alhadeed **a**

# 3617

Ani i'mal sabighatin waqaddir fee a **l** ssardi wa **i** 'maloo salihan innee bima ta'maloona baseer **un**

# 3618

Walisulaymana a **l** rreeha ghuduwwuha shahrun warawahuha shahrun waasana lahu 'ayna alqitri wamina aljinni man ya'malu bayna yadayhi biithni rabbihi waman yazigh minhum 'an amrina nuthiqhu min 'athabi a **l** ssa'eer **i**

# 3619

Ya'maloona lahu ma yashao min mahareeba watamatheela wajifanin ka **a** ljawabi waqudoorin rasiyatin i'maloo ala dawooda shukran waqaleelun min 'ibadiya a **l** shshakoor **u**

# 3620

Falamma qadayna 'alayhi almawta ma dallahum 'ala mawtihi illa dabbatu alardi takulu minsaatahu falamma kharra tabayyanati aljinnu an law kanoo ya'lamoona alghayba ma labithoo fee al'athabi almuheen **i**

# 3621

Laqad kana lisabain fee maskanihim ayatun jannatani 'an yameenin washimalin kuloo min rizqi rabbikum wa **o** shkuroo lahu badatun tayyibatun warabbun ghafoor **un**

# 3622

Faa'radoo faarsana 'alayhim sayla al'arimi wabaddanahum bijannatayhim jannatayni thawatay okulin khamtin waathlin washayin min sidrin qaleel **in**

# 3623

Thalika jazaynahum bima kafaroo wahal nujazee illa alkafoor **a**

# 3624

Waja'ana baynahum wabayna alqura allatee barakna feeha quran _th_ ahiratan waqaddarna feeha a **l** ssayra seeroo feeha layaliya waayyaman amineen **a**

# 3625

Faqaloo rabbana ba'id bayna asfarina wa _th_ alamoo anfusahum faja'anahum ahadeetha wamazzaqnahum kulla mumazzaqin inna fee thalika laayatin likulli sabbarin shakoor **in**

# 3626

Walaqad saddaqa 'alayhim ibleesu _th_ annahu fa **i** ttaba'oohu illa fareeqan mina almumineen **a**

# 3627

Wama kana lahu 'alayhim min sultanin illa lina'lama man yuminu bi **a** lakhirati mimman huwa minha fee shakkin warabbuka 'ala kulli shayin hafee _th_ **un**

# 3628

Quli od'oo allatheena za'amtum min dooni Allahi la yamlikoona mithqala tharratin fee a **l** ssamawati wala fee alardi wama lahum feehima min shirkin wama lahu minhum min _th_ aheer **in**

# 3629

Wala tanfa'u a **l** shshafa'atu 'indahu illa liman athina lahu hatta itha fuzzi'a 'an quloobihim qaloo matha qala rabbukum qaloo alhaqqa wahuwa al'aliyyu alkabeer **u**

# 3630

Qul man yarzuqukum mina a **l** ssamawati wa **a** lardi quli Allahu wainna aw iyyakum la'ala hudan aw fee dalalin mubeen **in**

# 3631

Qul la tusaloona 'amma ajramna wala nusalu 'amma ta'maloon **a**

# 3632

Qul yajma'u baynana rabbuna thumma yaftahu baynana bi **a** lhaqqi wahuwa alfattahu al'aleem **u**

# 3633

Qul arooniya allatheena alhaqtum bihi shurakaa kalla bal huwa Allahu al'azeezu alhakeem **u**

# 3634

Wama arsanaka illa kaffatan li **l** nnasi basheeran wanatheeran walakinna akthara a **l** nnasi la ya'lamoon **a**

# 3635

Wayaqooloona mata hatha alwa'du in kuntum sadiqeen **a**

# 3636

Qul lakum mee'adu yawmin la tastakhiroona 'anhu sa'atan wala tastaqdimoon **a**

# 3637

Waqala allatheena kafaroo lan numina bihatha alqurani wala bi **a** llathee bayna yadayhi walaw tara ithi a **l** _thth_ alimoona mawqoofoona 'inda rabbihim yarji'u ba'duhum ila ba'din alqawla yaqoolu allatheena istud'ifoo lillatheena istakbaroo lawla antum lakunna mumineen **a**

# 3638

Qala allatheena istakbaroo lillatheena istud'ifoo anahnu sadadnakum 'ani alhuda ba'da ith jaakum bal kuntum mujrimeen **a**

# 3639

Waqala allatheena istud'ifoo lillatheena istakbaroo bal makru allayli wa **al** nnahari ith tamuroonana an nakfura bi **A** llahi wanaj'ala lahu andadan waasarroo a **l** nnadamata lamma raawoo al'athaba waja'ana alaghlala fee a'naqi allatheena kafaroo hal yujzawna illa ma kanoo ya'maloon **a**

# 3640

Wama arsana fee qaryatin min natheerin illa qala mutrafooha inna bima orsiltum bihi kafiroon **a**

# 3641

Waqaloo nahnu aktharu amwalan waawladan wama nahnu bimu'aththabeen **a**

# 3642

Qul inna rabbee yabsutu a **l** rrizqa liman yashao wayaqdiru walakinna akthara a **l** nnasi la ya'lamoon **a**

# 3643

Wama amwalukum wala awladukum bi **a** llatee tuqarribukum 'indana zulfa illa man amana wa'amila salihan faolaika lahum jazao a **l** ddi'fi bima 'amiloo wahum fee alghurufati aminoon **a**

# 3644

Wa **a** llatheena yas'awna fee ayatina mu'ajizeena olaika fee al'athabi muhdaroon **a**

# 3645

Qul inna rabbee yabsutu a **l** rrizqa liman yashao min 'ibadihi wayaqdiru lahu wama anfaqtum min shayin fahuwa yukhlifuhu wahuwa khayru a **l** rraziqeen **a**

# 3646

Wayawma yahshuruhum jamee'an thumma yaqoolu lilmalaikati ahaolai iyyakum kanoo ya'budoon **a**

# 3647

Qaloo subhanaka anta waliyyuna min doonihim bal kanoo ya'budoona aljinna aktharuhum bihim muminoon **a**

# 3648

Fa **a** lyawma la yamliku ba'dukum liba'din naf'an waladarran wanaqoolu lillatheena _th_ alamoo thooqoo 'athaba a **l** nnari allatee kuntum biha tukaththiboon **a**

# 3649

Waitha tutla 'alayhim ayatuna bayyinatin qaloo ma hatha illa rajulun yureedu an yasuddakum 'amma kana ya'budu abaokum waqaloo ma hatha illa ifkun muftaran waqala allatheena kafaroo lilhaqqi lamma jaahum in hatha illa sihrun mubeen **un**

# 3650

Wamaataynahum min kutubin yadrusoonaha wama arsana ilayhim qablaka min natheer **in**

# 3651

Wakaththaba allatheena min qablihim wama balaghoo mi'shara maataynahum fakaththaboo rusulee fakayfa kana nakeer **i**

# 3652

Qul innama a'i _th_ ukum biwahidatin an taqoomoo lillahi mathna wafurada thumma tatafakkaroo ma bisahibikum min jinnatin in huwa illa natheerun lakum bayna yaday 'athabin shadeed **in**

# 3653

Qul ma saatukum min ajrin fahuwa lakum in ajriya illa 'ala Allahi wahuwa 'ala kulli shayin shaheed **un**

# 3654

Qul inna rabbee yaqthifu bi **a** lhaqqi 'allamu alghuyoob **i**

# 3655

Qul jaa alhaqqu wama yubdio albatilu wama yu'eed **u**

# 3656

Qul in dalatu fainnama adillu 'ala nafsee waini ihtadaytu fabima yoohee ilayya rabbee innahu samee'un qareeb **un**

# 3657

Walaw tara ith fazi'oo fala fawta waokhithoo min makanin qareeb **in**

# 3658

Waqaloo amanna bihi waanna lahumu a **l** ttanawushu min makanin ba'eed **in**

# 3659

Waqad kafaroo bihi min qablu wayaqthifoona bi **a** lghaybi min makanin ba'eed **in**

# 3660

Waheela baynahum wabayna ma yashtahoona kama fu'ila biashya'ihim min qablu innahum kanoo fee shakkin mureeb **in**

# 3661

Alhamdu lillahi fatiri a **l** ssamawati wa **a** lardi ja'ili almalaikati rusulan olee ajnihatin mathna wathulatha waruba'a yazeedu fee alkhalqi ma yashao inna Allaha 'ala kulli shayin qadeer **un**

# 3662

Ma yaftahi Allahu li **l** nnasi min rahmatin fala mumsika laha wama yumsik fala mursila lahu min ba'dihi wahuwa al'azeezu alhakeem **u**

# 3663

Ya ayyuha a **l** nnasu othkuroo ni'mata Allahi 'alaykum hal min khaliqin ghayru Allahi yarzuqukum mina a **l** ssamai wa **a** lardi la ilaha illa huwa faanna tufakoon **a**

# 3664

Wain yukaththibooka faqad kuththibat rusulun min qablika waila Allahi turja'u alomoor **u**

# 3665

Ya ayyuha a **l** nnasu inna wa'da Allahi haqqun fala taghurrannakumu alhayatu a **l** ddunya wala yaghurrannakum bi **A** llahi algharoor **u**

# 3666

Inna a **l** shshaytana lakum 'aduwwun fa **i** ttakhithoohu 'aduwwan innama yad'oo hizbahu liyakoonoo min ashabi a **l** ssa'eer **i**

# 3667

Allatheena kafaroo lahum 'athabun shadeedun wa **a** llatheena amanoo wa'amiloo a **l** ssalihati lahum maghfiratun waajrun kabeer **un**

# 3668

Afaman zuyyina lahu sooo 'amalihi faraahu hasanan fainna Allaha yudillu man yashao wayahdee man yashao fala tathhab nafsuka 'alayhim hasaratin inna Allaha 'aleemun bima yasna'oon **a**

# 3669

Wa **A** llahu allathee arsala a **l** rriyaha fatutheeru sahaban fasuqnahu ila baladin mayyitin faahyayna bihi alarda ba'da mawtiha kathalika a **l** nnushoor **u**

# 3670

Man kana yureedu al'izzata falillahi al'izzatu jamee'an ilayhi yas'adu alkalimu a **l** ttayyibu wa **a** l'amalu a **l** ssalihu yarfa'uhu wa **a** llatheena yamkuroona a **l** ssayyiati lahum 'athabun shadeedun wamakru olaika huwa yaboor **u**

# 3671

Wa **A** llahu khalaqakum min turabin thumma min nutfatin thumma ja'alakum azwajan wama tahmilu min ontha wala tada'u illa bi'ilmihi wama yu'ammaru min mu'ammarin wala yunqasu min 'umurihi illa fee kitabin inna thalika 'ala Allahi yaseer **un**

# 3672

Wama yastawee albahrani hatha 'athbun furatun saighun sharabuhu wahatha milhun ojajun wamin kullin takuloona lahman tariyyan watastakhrijoona hilyatan talbasoonaha watara alfulka feehi mawakhira litabtaghoo min fadlihi wala'allakum tashkuroon **a**

# 3673

Yooliju allayla fee a **l** nnahari wayooliju a **l** nnahara fee allayli wasakhkhara a **l** shshamsa wa **a** lqamara kullun yajree liajalin musamman thalikumu Allahu rabbukum lahu almulku wa **a** llatheena tad'oona min doonihi ma yamlikoona min qitmeer **in**

# 3674

In tad'oohum la yasma'oo du'aakum walaw sami'oo ma istajaboo lakum wayawma alqiyamati yakfuroona bishirkikum wala yunabbioka mithlu khabeer **in**

# 3675

Ya ayyuha a **l** nnasu antumu alfuqarao ila Allahi wa **A** llahu huwa alghaniyyu alhameed **u**

# 3676

In yasha yuthhibkum wayati bikhalqin jadeed **in**

# 3677

Wamathalika 'ala Allahi bi'azeez **in**

# 3678

Wala taziru waziratun wizra okhra wain tad'u muthqalatun ilahimliha la yuhmal minhu shayon walaw kana tha qurba innama tunthiru allatheena yakhshawna rabbahum bi **a** lghaybi waaqamoo a **l** ssalata waman tazakka fainnama yatazakka linafsihi waila Allahi almaseer **u**

# 3679

Wama yastawee ala'ma wa **a** lbaseer **u**

# 3680

Wala a **l** _thth_ ulumatu wala a **l** nnoor **u**

# 3681

Wala a **l** _thth_ illu wala alharoor **u**

# 3682

Wama yastawee alahyao wala alamwatu inna Allaha yusmi'u man yashao wama anta bimusmi'in man fee alquboor **i**

# 3683

In anta illa natheer **un**

# 3684

Inna arsanaka bi **a** lhaqqi basheeran wanatheeran wain min ommatin illa khala feeha natheer **un**

# 3685

Wain yukaththibooka faqad kaththaba allatheena min qablihim jaathum rusuluhum bi **a** lbayyinati wabi **al** zzuburi wabi **a** lkitabi almuneer **i**

# 3686

Thumma akhathtu allatheena kafaroo fakayfa kana nakeer **i**

# 3687

Alam tara anna Allaha anzala mina a **l** ssamai maan faakhrajna bihi thamaratin mukhtalifan alwanuha wamina aljibali judadun beedun wahumrun mukhtalifun alwanuha wagharabeebu sood **un**

# 3688

Wamina a **l** nnasi wa **al** ddawabbi wa **a** lan'ami mukhtalifun alwanuhu kathalika innama yakhsha Allaha min 'ibadihi al'ulamao inna Allaha 'azeezun ghafoor **un**

# 3689

Inna allatheena yatloona kitaba Allahi waaqamoo a **l** ssalata waanfaqoo mimma razaqnahum sirran wa'alaniyatan yarjoona tijaratan lan taboor **a**

# 3690

Liyuwaffiyahum ojoorahum wayazeedahum min fadlihi innahu ghafoorun shakoor **un**

# 3691

Wa **a** llathee awhayna ilayka mina alkitabi huwa alhaqqu musaddiqan lima bayna yadayhi inna Allaha bi'ibadihi lakhabeerun baseer **un**

# 3692

Thumma awrathna alkitaba allatheena istafayna min 'ibadina faminhum _th_ alimun linafsihi waminhum muqtasidun waminhum sabiqun bi **a** lkhayrati biithni Allahi thalika huwa alfadlu alkabeer **u**

# 3693

Jannatu 'adnin yadkhuloonaha yuhallawna feeha min asawira min thahabin waluluan walibasuhum feehahareer **un**

# 3694

Waqaloo alhamdu lillahi allathee athhaba 'anna alhazana inna rabbana laghafoorun shakoor **un**

# 3695

Allathee ahallana dara almuqamati min fadlihi la yamassuna feeha nasabun wala yamassuna feeha lughoob **un**

# 3696

Wa **a** llatheena kafaroo lahum naru jahannama la yuqda 'alayhim fayamootoo wala yukhaffafu 'anhum min 'athabiha kathalika najzee kulla kafoor **in**

# 3697

Wahum yastarikhoona feeha rabbana akhrijna na'mal salihan ghayra allathee kunna na'malu awalam nu'ammirkum ma yatathakkaru feehi man tathakkara wajaakumu a **l** nnatheeru fathooqoo fama li **l** _thth_ alimeena min naseer **in**

# 3698

Inna Allaha 'alimu ghaybi a **l** ssamawati wa **a** lardi innahu 'aleemun bithati a **l** ssudoor **i**

# 3699

Huwa allathee ja'alakum khalaifa fee alardi faman kafara fa'alayhi kufruhu wala yazeedu alkafireena kufruhum 'inda rabbihim illa maqtan wala yazeedu alkafireena kufruhum illa khasara **n**

# 3700

Qul araaytum shurakaakumu allatheena tad'oona min dooni Allahi aroonee matha khalaqoo mina alardi am lahum shirkun fee a **l** ssamawati am ataynahum kitaban fahum 'ala bayyinatin minhu bal in ya'idu a **l** _thth_ alimoona ba'duhum ba'dan illa ghuroora **n**

# 3701

Inna Allaha yumsiku a **l** ssamawati wa **a** larda an tazoola walain zalata in amsakahuma min ahadin min ba'dihi innahu kana haleeman ghafoora **n**

# 3702

Waaqsamoo bi **A** llahi jahda aymanihim lain jaahum natheerun layakoonunna ahda min ihda alomami falamma jaahum natheerun ma zadahum illa nufoora **n**

# 3703

Istikbaran fee alardi wamakra a **l** ssayyii wala yaheequ almakru a **l** ssayyio illa biahlihi fahal yan _th_ uroona illa sunnata alawwaleena falan tajida lisunnati Allahi tabdeelan walan tajida lisunnati Allahi tahweela **n**

# 3704

Wasalamun 'ala almursaleen **a**

# 3970

Wa **a** lhamdu lillahi rabbi al'alameen **a**

# 3971

# 3972

# 3973

# 3974

# 3975

# 3976

# 3977

# 3978

# 3979

# 3980

# 3981

# 3983

# 3984

# 3985

# 3986

# 3987

# 3988

# 3989

# 3990

# 3991

Wahal ataka nabao alkhasmi ith tasawwaroo almihrab **a**

# 3992

Ith dakhaloo 'ala dawooda fafazi'a minhum qaloo la takhaf khasmani bagha ba'duna 'ala ba'din fa **o** hkum baynana bi **a** lhaqqi wala tushtit wa **i** hdina ila sawai a **l** ssirat **i**

# 3993

Inna hatha akhee lahu tis'un watis'oona na'jatan waliya na'jatun wahidatun faqala akfilneeha wa'azzanee fee alkhitab **i**

# 3994

Qala laqad _th_ alamaka bisuali na'jatika ila ni'ajihi wainna katheeran mina alkhulatai layabghee ba'duhum 'ala ba'din illa allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo a **l** ssalihati waqaleelun ma hum wa _th_ anna dawoodu annama fatannahu fa **i** staghfara rabbahu wakharra raki'an waanab **a**

# 3995

Faghafarna lahu thalika wainna lahu 'indana lazulfa wahusna maab **in**

# 3996

Ya dawoodu inna ja'anaka khaleefatan fee alardi fa **o** hkum bayna a **l** nnasi bi **a** lhaqqi wala tattabi'i alhawa fayudillaka 'an sabeeli Allahi inna allatheena yadilloona 'an sabeeli Allahi lahum 'athabun shadeedun bima nasoo yawma alhisab **i**

# 3997

Wama khalaqna a **l** ssamaa wa **a** larda wama baynahuma batilan thalika _th_ annu allatheena kafaroo fawaylun lillatheena kafaroo mina a **l** nnar **i**

# 3998

Am naj'alu allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo a **l** ssalihati ka **a** lmufsideena fee alardi am naj'alu almuttaqeena ka **a** lfujjar **i**

# 3999

# 4000

# 4010

# 4060

# 4061

Ala lillahi a **l** ddeenu alkhalisu wa **a** llatheena ittakhathoo min doonihi awliyaa ma na'buduhum illa liyuqarriboona ila Allahi zulfa inna Allaha yahkumu baynahum fee ma hum feehi yakhtalifoona inna Allaha la yahdee man huwa kathibun kaffar **un**

# 4062

Law arada Allahu an yattakhitha waladan la **i** stafa mimma yakhluqu ma yashao subhanahu huwa Allahu alwahidu alqahhar **u**

# 4063

Khalaqa a **l** ssamawati wa **a** larda bi **a** lhaqqi yukawwiru allayla 'ala a **l** nnahari wayukawwiru a **l** nnahara 'ala allayli wasakhkhara a **l** shshamsa wa **a** lqamara kullun yajree liajalin musamman ala huwa al'azeezu alghaffar **u**

# 4064

Khalaqakum min nafsin wahidatin thumma ja'ala minha zawjaha waanzala lakum mina alan'ami thamaniyata azwajin yakhluqukum fee butooni ommahatikum khalqan min ba'di khalqin fee _th_ ulumatin thalathin thalikumu Allahu rabbukum lahu almulku la ilaha illa huwa faanna tusrafoon **a**

# 4065

In takfuroo fainna Allaha ghaniyyun 'ankum wala yarda li'ibadihi alkufra wain tashkuroo yardahu lakum wala taziru waziratun wizra okhra thumma ila rabbikum marji'ukum fayunabbiokum bima kuntum ta'maloona innahu 'aleemun bithati a **l** ssudoor **i**

# 4066

Waitha massa alinsana durrun da'a rabbahu muneeban ilayhi thumma itha khawwalahu ni'matan minhu nasiya ma kana yad'oo ilayhi min qablu waja'ala lillahi andadan liyudilla 'an sabeelihi qul tamatta' bikufrika qaleelan innaka min ashabi a **l** nnar **i**

# 4067

Amman huwa qanitun anaa allayli sajidan waqaiman yahtharu alakhirata wayarjoo rahmata rabbihi qul hal yastawee allatheena ya'lamoona wa **a** llatheena la ya'lamoona innama yatathakkaru oloo alalbab **i**

# 4068

Qul ya 'ibadi allatheena amanoo ittaqoo rabbakum lillatheena ahsanoo fee hathihi a **l** ddunyahasanatun waardu Allahi wasi'atun innama yuwaffa a **l** ssabiroona ajrahum bighayri hisab **in**

# 4074

# 4077

# 4078

# 4079

Alam tara anna Allaha anzala mina a **l** ssamai maan fasalakahu yanabee'a fee alardi thumma yukhriju bihi zar'an mukhtalifan alwanuhu thumma yaheeju fatarahu musfarran thumma yaj'aluhu hutaman inna fee thalika lathikra liolee alalbab **i**

# 4080

# 4081

Allahu nazzala ahsana alhadeethi kitaban mutashabihan mathaniya taqsha'irru minhu juloodu allatheena yakhshawna rabbahum thumma taleenu julooduhum waquloobuhum ilathikri Allahi thalika huda Allahi yahdee bihi man yashao waman yudlili Allahu fama lahu min had **in**

# 4096

# 4099

# 4100

Allahu yatawaffa alanfusa heena mawtiha wa **a** llatee lam tamut fee manamiha fayumsiku allatee qada 'alayha almawta wayursilu alokhra ila ajalin musamman inna fee thalika laayatin liqawmin yatafakkaroon **a**

# 4101

# 4102

# 4103

# 4104

Quli allahumma fatira a **l** ssamawati wa **a** lardi 'alima alghaybi wa **al** shshahadati anta tahkumu bayna 'ibadika fee ma kanoo feehi yakhtalifoon **a**

# 4105

Walaw anna lillatheena _th_ alamoo ma fee alardi jamee'an wamithlahu ma'ahu la **i** ftadaw bihi min sooi al'athabi yawma alqiyamati wabada lahum mina Allahi ma lam yakoonoo yahtasiboon **a**

# 4106

Wabada lahum sayyiatu ma kasaboo wahaqa bihim ma kanoo bihi yastahzioon **a**

# 4107

Faitha massa alinsana durrun da'ana thumma itha khawwanahu ni'matan minna qala innama ooteetuhu 'ala 'ilmin bal hiya fitnatun walakinna aktharahum la ya'lamoon **a**

# 4108

# 4109

# 4110

# 4111

Qul ya 'ibadiya allatheena asrafoo 'ala anfusihim la taqnatoo min rahmati Allahi inna Allaha yaghfiru a **l** ththunooba jamee'an innahu huwa alghafooru a **l** rraheem **u**

# 4112

# 4113

# 4114

# 4115

# 4116

# 4117

# 4118

# 4119

# 4120

# 4121

# 4122

# 4123

# 4124
