# 4125

Wama qadaroo Allaha haqqa qadrihi wa **a** lardu jamee'an qabdatuhu yawma alqiyamati wa **al** ssamawatu matwiyyatun biyameenihi subhanahu wata'ala 'amma yushrikoon **a**

# 4126

Wanufikha fee a **l** ssoori fasa'iqa man fee a **l** ssamawati waman fee alardi illa man shaa Allahu thumma nufikha feehi okhra faitha hum qiyamun yan _th_ uroon **a**

# 4127

Waashraqati alardu binoori rabbiha wawudi'a alkitabu wajeea bi **al** nnabiyyeena wa **al** shshuhadai waqudiya baynahum bi **a** lhaqqi wahum la yu _th_ lamoon **a**

# 4128

Wawuffiyat kullu nafsin ma 'amilat wahuwa a'lamu bima yaf'aloon **a**

# 4129

Waseeqa allatheena kafaroo ila jahannama zumaran hatta itha jaooha futihat abwabuha waqala lahum khazanatuha alam yatikum rusulun minkum yatloona 'alaykum ayati rabbikum wayunthiroonakum liqaa yawmikum hatha qaloo bala walakin haqqat kalimatu al'athabi 'ala alkafireen **a**

# 4130

Qeela odkhuloo abwaba jahannama khalideena feeha fabisa mathwa almutakabbireen **a**

# 4131

Waseeqa allatheena ittaqaw rabbahum ila aljannati zumaran hatta itha jaooha wafutihat abwabuha waqala lahum khazanatuha salamun 'alaykum tibtum fa **o** dkhulooha khalideen **a**

# 4132

Waqaloo alhamdu lillahi allathee sadaqana wa'dahu waawrathana alarda natabawwao mina aljannati haythu nashao fani'ma ajru al'amileen **a**

# 4133

Watara almalaikata haffeena min hawli al'arshi yusabbihoona bihamdi rabbihim waqudiya baynahum bi **a** lhaqqi waqeela alhamdu lillahi rabbi al'alameen **a**

# 4134

Hameem

# 4135

Tanzeelu alkitabi mina Allahi al'azeezi al'aleem **i**

# 4136

Ghafiri a **l** ththanbi waqabili a **l** ttawbi shadeedi al'iqabi thee a **l** ttawli la ilaha illa huwa ilayhi almaseer **u**

# 4137

Ma yujadilu fee ayati Allahi illa allatheena kafaroo fala yaghrurka taqallubuhum fee albilad **i**

# 4138

Kaththabat qablahum qawmu noohin wa **a** lahzabu min ba'dihim wahammat kullu ommatin birasoolihim liyakhuthoohu wajadaloo bi **a** lbatili liyudhidoo bihi alhaqqa faakhathtuhum fakayfa kana 'iqab **i**

# 4139

Wakathalika haqqat kalimatu rabbika 'ala allatheena kafaroo annahum ashabu a **l** nnar **i**

# 4140

Allatheena yahmiloona al'arsha waman hawlahu yusabbihoona bihamdi rabbihim wayuminoona bihi wayastaghfiroona lillatheena amanoo rabbana wasi'ta kulla shayin rahmatan wa'ilman fa **i** ghfir lillatheena taboo wa **i** ttaba'oo sabeelaka waqihim 'athaba aljaheem **i**

# 4141

Rabbana waadkhilhum jannati 'adnin allatee wa'adtahum waman salaha min abaihim waazwajihim wathurriyyatihim innaka anta al'azeezu alhakeem **u**

# 4142

Waqihimu a **l** ssayyiati waman taqi a **l** ssayyiati yawmaithin faqad rahimtahu wathalika huwa alfawzu al'a _th_ eem **u**

# 4143

Inna allatheena kafaroo yunadawna lamaqtu Allahi akbaru min maqtikum anfusakum ith tud'awna ila aleemani fatakfuroon **a**

# 4144

Qaloo rabbana amattana ithnatayni waahyaytana ithnatayni fa **i** 'tarafna bithunoobina fahal ila khuroojin min sabeel **in**

# 4145

Thalikum biannahu itha du'iya Allahu wahdahu kafartum wain yushrak bihi tuminoo fa **a** lhukmu lillahi al'aliyyi alkabeer **i**

# 4146

Huwa allathee yureekum ayatihi wayunazzilu lakum mina a **l** ssamai rizqan wama yatathakkaru illa man yuneeb **u**

# 4147

Fa **o** d'oo Allaha mukhliseena lahu a **l** ddeena walaw kariha alkafiroon **a**

# 4148

Rafee'u a **l** ddarajati thoo al'arshi yulqee a **l** rrooha min amrihi 'ala man yashao min 'ibadihi liyunthira yawma a **l** ttalaq **i**

# 4149

Yawma hum barizoona la yakhfa 'ala Allahi minhum shayon limani almulku alyawma lillahi alwahidi alqahhar **i**

# 4150

Alyawma tujza kullu nafsin bima kasabat la _th_ ulma alyawma inna Allaha saree'u alhisab **i**

# 4151

Waanthirhum yawma alazifati ithi alquloobu lada alhanajiri ka _th_ imeena ma li **l** _thth_ alimeena min hameemin wala shafee'in yuta' **u**

# 4152

Ya'lamu khainata ala'yuni wama tukhfee a **l** ssudoor **u**

# 4153

Wa **A** llahu yaqdee bi **a** lhaqqi wa **a** llatheena yad'oona min doonihi la yaqdoona bishayin inna Allaha huwa a **l** ssamee'u albaseer **u**

# 4154

Awa lam yaseeroo fee alardi fayan _th_ uroo kayfa kana 'aqibatu allatheena kanoo min qablihim kanoo hum ashadda minhum quwwatan waatharan fee alardi faakhathahumu Allahu bithunoobihim wama kana lahum mina Allahi min waq **in**

# 4155

Thalika biannahum kanat tateehim rusuluhum bi **a** lbayyinati fakafaroo faakhathahumu Allahu innahu qawiyyun shadeedu al'iqab **i**

# 4156

Walaqad arsana moosa biayatina wasultanin mubeen **in**

# 4157

Ila fir'awna wahamana waqaroona faqaloo sahirun kaththab **un**

# 4158

Falamma jaahum bi **a** lhaqqi min 'indina qaloo oqtuloo abnaa allatheena amanoo ma'ahu wa **i** stahyoo nisaahum wama kaydu alkafireena illa fee dalal **in**

# 4159

Waqala fir'awnu tharoonee aqtul moosa walyad'u rabbahu innee akhafu an yubaddila deenakum aw an yu _th_ hira fee alardi alfasad **a**

# 4160

Waqala moosa innee 'uthtu birabbee warabbikum min kulli mutakabbirin la yuminu biyawmi alhisab **i**

# 4161

Waqala rajulun muminun min ali fir'awna yaktumu eemanahu ataqtuloona rajulan an yaqoola rabbiyya Allahu waqad jaakum bi **a** lbayyinati min rabbikum wain yaku kathiban fa'alayhi kathibuhu wain yaku sadiqan yusibkum ba'du allathee ya'idukum inna Allaha la yahdee man huwa musrifun kaththab **un**

# 4162

Ya qawmi lakumu almulku alyawma _th_ ahireena fee alardi faman yansuruna min basi Allahi in jaana qala fir'awnu ma oreekum illa ma ara wama ahdeekum illa sabeela a **l** rrashad **i**

# 4163

Waqala allathee amana ya qawmi innee akhafu 'alaykum mithla yawmi alahzab **i**

# 4164

Mithla dabi qawmi noohin wa'adin wathamooda wa **a** llatheena min ba'dihim wama Allahu yureedu _th_ ulman lil'ibad **i**

# 4165

Waya qawmi innee akhafu 'alaykum yawma a **l** ttanad **i**

# 4166

Yawma tuwalloona mudbireena ma lakum mina Allahi min 'asimin waman yudlili Allahu fama lahu min had **in**

# 4167

Walaqad jaakum yoosufu min qablu bi **a** lbayyinati fama ziltum fee shakkin mimma jaakum bihi hatta itha halaka qultum lan yab'atha Allahu min ba'dihi rasoolan kathalika yudillu Allahu man huwa musrifun murtab **un**

# 4168

Allatheena yujadiloona fee ayati Allahi bighayri sultanin atahum kabura maqtan 'inda Allahi wa'inda allatheena amanoo kathalika yatba'u Allahu 'ala kulli qalbi mutakabbirin jabbar **in**

# 4169

Waqala fir'awnu ya hamanu ibni lee sarhan la'allee ablughu alasbab **a**

# 4170

Asbaba a **l** ssamawati faattali'a ila ilahi moosa wainnee laa _th_ unnuhu kathiban wakathalika zuyyina lifir'awna sooo 'amalihi wasudda 'ani a **l** ssabeeli wama kaydu fir'awna illa fee tabab **in**

# 4171

Waqala allathee amana ya qawmi ittabi'ooni ahdikum sabeela a **l** rrashad **i**

# 4172

Ya qawmi innama hathihi alhayatu a **l** ddunya mata'un wainna alakhirata hiya daru alqarar **i**

# 4173

Man 'amila sayyiatan fala yujza illa mithlaha waman 'amila salihan min thakarin aw ontha wahuwa muminun faolaika yadkhuloona aljannata yurzaqoona feeha bighayri hisab **in**

# 4174

Waya qawmi ma lee ad'ookum ila a **l** nnajati watad'oonanee ila a **l** nnar **i**

# 4175

Tad'oonanee liakfura bi **A** llahi waoshrika bihi ma laysa lee bihi 'ilmun waana ad'ookum ila al'azeezi alghaffar **i**

# 4176

La jarama annama tad'oonanee ilayhi laysa lahu da'watun fee a **l** ddunya wala fee alakhirati waanna maraddana ila Allahi waanna almusrifeena hum ashabu a **l** nnar **i**

# 4177

Fasatathkuroona ma aqoolu lakum waofawwidu amree ila Allahi inna Allaha baseerun bi **a** l'ibad **i**

# 4178

Fawaqahu Allahu sayyiati ma makaroo wahaqa biali fir'awna sooo al'athab **i**

# 4179

A **l** nnaru yu'radoona 'alayha ghuduwwan wa'ashiyyan wayawma taqoomu a **l** ssa'atu adkhiloo ala fir'awna ashadda al'athab **i**

# 4180

Waith yatahajjoona fee a **l** nnari fayaqoolu a **l** ddu'afao lillatheena istakbaroo inna kunna lakum taba'an fahal antum mughnoona 'anna naseeban mina a **l** nnar **i**

# 4181

Qala allatheena istakbaroo inna kullun feeha inna Allaha qad hakama bayna al'ibad **i**

# 4182

Waqala allatheena fee a **l** nnari likhazanati jahannama od'oo rabbakum yukhaffif 'anna yawman mina al'athab **i**

# 4183

Qaloo awalam taku tateekum rusulukum bi **a** lbayyinati qaloo bala qaloo fa **o** d'oo wama du'ao alkafireena illa fee dalal **in**

# 4184

Inna lanansuru rusulana wa **a** llatheena amanoo fee alhayati a **l** ddunya wayawma yaqoomu alashhad **u**

# 4185

Yawma la yanfa'u a **l** _thth_ alimeena ma'thiratuhum walahumu alla'natu walahum sooo a **l** ddar **i**

# 4186

Walaqad atayna moosa alhuda waawrathna banee israeela alkitab **a**

# 4187

Hudan wathikra liolee alalbab **i**

# 4188

Fa **i** sbir inna wa'da Allahi haqqun wa **i** staghfir lithanbika wasabbih bihamdi rabbika bi **a** l'ashiyyi wa **a** libkar **i**

# 4189

Inna allatheena yujadiloona fee ayati Allahi bighayri sultanin atahum in fee sudoorihim illa kibrun ma hum bibaligheehi fa **i** sta'ith bi **A** llahi innahu huwa a **l** ssamee'u albaseer **u**

# 4190

Lakhalqu a **l** ssamawati wa **a** lardi akbaru min khalqi a **l** nnasi walakinna akthara a **l** nnasi la ya'lamoon **a**

# 4191

Wama yastawee ala'ma wa **a** lbaseeru wa **a** llatheena amanoo wa'amiloo a **l** ssalihati wala almuseeo qaleelan ma tatathakkaroon **a**

# 4192

Inna a **l** ssa'ata laatiyatun la rayba feeha walakinna akthara a **l** nnasi la yuminoon **a**

# 4193

Waqala rabbukumu od'oonee astajib lakum inna allatheena yastakbiroona 'an 'ibadatee sayadkhuloona jahannama dakhireen **a**

# 4194

Allahu allathee ja'ala lakumu allayla litaskunoo feehi wa **al** nnahara mubsiran inna Allaha lathoo fadlin 'ala a **l** nnasi walakinna akthara a **l** nnasi la yashkuroon **a**

# 4195

Thalikumu Allahu rabbukum khaliqu kulli shayin la ilaha illa huwa faanna tufakoon **a**

# 4196

Kathalika yufaku allatheena kanoo biayati Allahi yajhadoon **a**

# 4197

Allahu allathee ja'ala lakumu alarda qararan wa **al** ssamaa binaan wasawwarakum faahsana suwarakum warazaqakum mina a **l** ttayyibati thalikumu Allahu rabbukum fatabaraka Allahu rabbu al'alameen **a**

# 4198

Huwa alhayyu la ilaha illa huwa fa **o** d'oohu mukhliseena lahu a **l** ddeena alhamdu lillahi rabbi al'alameen **a**

# 4199

Qul innee nuheetu an a'buda allatheena tad'oona min dooni Allahi lamma jaaniya albayyinatu min rabbee waomirtu an oslima lirabbi al'alameen **a**

# 4200

Huwa allathee khalaqakum min turabin thumma min nutfatin thumma min 'alaqatin thumma yukhrijukum tiflan thumma litablughoo ashuddakum thumma litakoonoo shuyookhan waminkum man yutawaffa min qablu walitablughoo ajalan musamman wala'allakum ta'qiloon **a**

# 4201

Huwa allathee yuhyee wayumeetu faitha qada amran fainnama yaqoolu lahu kun fayakoon **u**

# 4202

Alam tara ila allatheena yujadiloona fee ayati Allahi anna yusrafoon **a**

# 4203

Allatheena kaththaboo bi **a** lkitabi wabima arsana bihi rusulana fasawfa ya'lamoon **a**

# 4204

Ithi alaghlalu fee a'naqihim wa **al** ssalasilu yushaboon **a**

# 4205

Fee alhameemi thumma fee a **l** nnari yusjaroon **a**

# 4206

Thumma qeela lahum ayna ma kuntum tushrikoon **a**

# 4207

Min dooni Allahi qaloo dalloo 'anna bal lam nakun nad'oo min qablu shayan kathalika yudillu Allahu alkafireen **a**

# 4208

Thalikum bima kuntum tafrahoona fee alardi bighayri alhaqqi wabima kuntum tamrahoon **a**

# 4209

Odkhuloo abwaba jahannama khalideena feeha fabisa mathwa almutakabbireen **a**

# 4210

Fa **i** sbir inna wa'da Allahi haqqun faimma nuriyannaka ba'da allathee na'iduhum aw natawaffayannaka failayna yurja'oon **a**

# 4211

Walaqad arsana rusulan min qablika minhum man qasasna 'alayka waminhum man lam naqsus 'alayka wama kana lirasoolin an yatiya biayatin illa biithni Allahi faitha jaa amru Allahi qudiya bi **a** lhaqqi wakhasira hunalika almubtiloon **a**

# 4212

Allahu allathee ja'ala lakumu alan'ama litarkaboo minha waminha takuloon **a**

# 4213

Walakum feeha manafi'u walitablughoo 'alayhahajatan fee sudoorikum wa'alayha wa'ala alfulki tuhmaloon **a**

# 4214

Wayureekum ayatihi faayya ayati Allahi tunkiroon **a**

# 4215

Afalam yaseeroo fee alardi fayan _th_ uroo kayfa kana 'aqibatu allatheena min qablihim kanoo akthara minhum waashadda quwwatan waatharan fee alardi fama aghna 'anhum ma kanoo yaksiboon **a**

# 4216

Falamma jaathum rusuluhum bi **a** lbayyinati farihoo bima 'indahum mina al'ilmi wahaqa bihim ma kanoo bihi yastahzioon **a**

# 4217

Falamma raaw basana qaloo amanna bi **A** llahi wahdahu wakafarna bima kunna bihi mushrikeen **a**

# 4218

Falam yaku yanfa'uhum eemanuhum lamma raaw basana sunnata Allahi allatee qad khalat fee 'ibadihi wakhasira hunalika alkafiroon **a**

# 4219

Hameem

# 4220

Tanzeelun mina a **l** rrahmani a **l** rraheem **i**

# 4221

Kitabun fussilat ayatuhu quranan 'arabiyyan liqawmin ya'lamoon **a**

# 4222

Basheeran wanatheeran faa'rada aktharuhum fahum la yasma'oon **a**

# 4223

Waqaloo quloobuna fee akinnatin mimma tad'oona ilayhi wafee athanina waqrun wamin baynina wabaynika hijabun fa **i** 'mal innana 'amiloon **a**

# 4224

Qul innama ana basharun mithlukum yooha ilayya annama ilahukum ilahun wahidun fa **i** staqeemoo ilayhi wa **i** staghfiroohu wawaylun lilmushrikeen **a**

# 4225

Allatheena la yutoona a **l** zzakata wahum bi **a** lakhirati hum kafiroon **a**

# 4226

Inna allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo a **l** ssalihati lahum ajrun ghayru mamnoon **in**

# 4227

Qul ainnakum latakfuroona bi **a** llathee khalaqa alarda fee yawmayni wataj'aloona lahu andadan thalika rabbu al'alameen **a**

# 4228

Waja'ala feeha rawasiya min fawqiha wabaraka feeha waqaddara feeha aqwataha fee arba'ati ayyamin sawaan li **l** ssaileen **a**

# 4229

Thumma istawa ila a **l** ssamai wahiya dukhanun faqala laha walilardi itiyataw'an aw karhan qalata ataynatai'een **a**

# 4230

Faqadahunna sab'a samawatin fee yawmayni waawha fee kulli samain amraha wazayyanna a **l** ssamaa a **l** ddunya bimasabeeha wahif _th_ an thalika taqdeeru al'azeezi al'aleem **i**

# 4231

Fain a'radoo fuqul anthartukum sa'iqatan mithla sa'iqati 'adin wathamood **a**

# 4232

Ith jaathumu a **l** rrusulu min bayni aydeehim wamin khalfihim alla ta'budoo illa Allaha qaloo law shaa rabbuna laanzala malaikatan fainna bima orsiltum bihi kafiroon **a**

# 4233

Faamma 'adun fa **i** stakbaroo fee alardi bighayri alhaqqi waqaloo man ashaddu minna quwwatan awalam yaraw anna Allaha allathee khalaqahum huwa ashaddu minhum quwwatan wakanoo biayatina yajhadoon **a**

# 4234

Faarsana 'alayhim reehan sarsaran fee ayyamin nahisatin linutheeqahum 'athaba alkhizyi fee alhayati a **l** ddunya wala'athabu alakhirati akhza wahum la yunsaroon **a**

# 4235

Waamma thamoodu fahadaynahum fa **i** stahabboo al'ama 'ala alhuda faakhathathum sa'iqatu al'athabi alhooni bima kanoo yaksiboon **a**

# 4236

Wanajjayna allatheena amanoo wakanoo yattaqoon **a**

# 4237

Wayawma yuhsharu a'dao Allahi ila a **l** nnari fahum yooza'oon **a**

# 4238

Hatta itha ma jaooha shahida 'alayhim sam'uhum waabsaruhum wajulooduhum bima kanoo ya'maloon **a**

# 4239

Waqaloo lijuloodihim lima shahidtum 'alayna qaloo antaqana Allahu allathee antaqa kulla shayin wahuwa khalaqakum awwala marratin wailayhi turja'oon **a**

# 4240

Wama kuntum tastatiroona an yashhada 'alaykum sam'ukum wala absarukum wala juloodukum walakin _th_ anantum anna Allaha la ya'lamu katheeran mimma ta'maloon **a**

# 4241

Wathalikum _th_ annukumu allathee _th_ anantum birabbikum ardakum faasbahtum mina alkhasireen **a**

# 4242

Fain yasbiroo fa **al** nnaru mathwan lahum wain yasta'tiboo fama hum mina almu'tabeen **a**

# 4243

Waqayyadna lahum quranaa fazayyanoo lahum ma bayna aydeehim wama khalfahum wahaqqa 'alayhimu alqawlu fee omamin qad khalat min qablihim mina aljinni wa **a** linsi innahum kanoo khasireen **a**

# 4244

Waqala allatheena kafaroo la tasma'oo lihatha alqurani wa **i** lghaw feehi la'allakum taghliboon **a**

# 4245

Falanutheeqanna allatheena kafaroo 'athaban shadeedan walanajziyannahum aswaa allathee kanoo ya'maloon **a**

# 4246

Thalika jazao a'dai Allahi a **l** nnaru lahum feeha daru alkhuldi jazaan bima kanoo biayatina yajhadoon **a**

# 4247

Waqala allatheena kafaroo rabbana arina allathayni adallana mina aljinni wa **a** linsi naj'alhuma tahta aqdamina liyakoona mina alasfaleen **a**

# 4248

Inna allatheena qaloo rabbuna Allahu thumma istaqamoo tatanazzalu 'alayhimu almalaikatu alla takhafoo wala tahzanoo waabshiroo bi **a** ljannati allatee kuntum too'adoon **a**

# 4249

Nahnu awliyaokum fee alhayati a **l** ddunya wafee alakhirati walakum feeha ma tashtahee anfusukum walakum feeha ma tadda'oon **a**

# 4250

Nuzulan min ghafoorin raheem **in**

# 4251

Waman ahsanu qawlan mimman da'a ila Allahi wa'amila salihan waqala innanee mina almuslimeen **a**

# 4252

Wala tastawee alhasanatu wala a **l** ssayyiatu idfa' bi **a** llatee hiya ahsanu faitha allathee baynaka wabaynahu 'adawatun kaannahu waliyyun hameem **un**

# 4253

Wama yulaqqaha illa allatheena sabaroo wama yulaqqaha illathoo ha _thth_ in 'a _th_ eem **in**

# 4254

Waimma yanzaghannaka mina a **l** shshaytani nazghun fa **i** sta'ith bi **A** llahi innahu huwa a **l** ssamee'u al'aleem **u**

# 4255

Wamin ayatihi allaylu wa **al** nnaharu wa **al** shshamsu wa **a** lqamaru la tasjudoo li **l** shshamsi wala lilqamari wa **o** sjudoo lillahi alathee khalaqahunna in kuntum iyyahu ta'budoon **a**

# 4256

Faini istakbaroo fa **a** llatheena 'inda rabbika yusabbihoona lahu bi **a** llayli wa **al** nnahari wahum la yasamoon **a**

# 4257

Wamin ayatihi annaka tara alarda khashi'atan faitha anzana 'alayha almaa ihtazzat warabat inna allathee ahyaha lamuhyee almawta innahu 'ala kulli shayin qadeer **un**

# 4258

Inna allatheena yulhidoona fee ayatina la yakhfawna 'alayna afaman yulqa fee a **l** nnari khayrun am man yatee aminan yawma alqiyamati i'maloo ma shitum innahu bima ta'maloona baseer **un**

# 4259

Inna allatheena kafaroo bi **al** ththikri lamma jaahum wainnahu lakitabun 'azeez **un**

# 4260

La yateehi albatilu min bayni yadayhi wala min khalfihi tanzeelun min hakeemin hameed **in**

# 4261

Ma yuqalu laka illa ma qad qeela li **l** rrusuli min qablika inna rabbaka lathoo maghfiratin wathoo 'iqabin aleem **in**

# 4262

Walaw ja'anahu quranan a'jamiyyan laqaloo lawla fussilat ayatuhu aa'jamiyyun wa'arabiyyun qul huwa lillatheena amanoo hudan washifaon wa **a** llatheena la yuminoona fee athanihim waqrun wahuwa 'alayhim 'aman olaika yunadawna min makanin ba'eed **in**

# 4263

Walaqad atayna moosa alkitaba fa **i** khtulifa feehi walawla kalimatun sabaqat min rabbika laqudiya baynahum wainnahum lafee shakkin minhu mureeb **in**

# 4264

Man 'amila salihan falinafsihi waman asaa fa'alayha wama rabbuka bi _th_ allamin lil'abeed **i**

# 4265

Ilayhi yuraddu 'ilmu a **l** ssa'ati wama takhruju min thamaratin min akmamiha wama tahmilu min ontha wala tada'u illa bi'ilmihi wayawma yunadeehim ayna shurakaee qaloo athannaka ma minna min shaheed **in**

# 4266

Wadalla 'anhum ma kanoo yad'oona min qablu wa _th_ annoo ma lahum min mahees **in**

# 4267

La yasamu alinsanu min du'ai alkhayri wain massahu a **l** shsharru fayaoosun qanoot **un**

# 4268

Walain athaqnahu rahmatan minna min ba'di darraa massathu layaqoolanna hatha lee wama a _th_ unnu a **l** ssa'ata qaimatan walain ruji'tu ila rabbee inna lee 'indahu lalhusna falanunabbianna allatheena kafaroo bima 'amiloo walanutheeqannahum min 'athabin ghalee _th_ **in**

# 4269

Waitha an'amna 'ala alinsani a'rada wanaa bijanibihi waitha massahu a **l** shsharru fathoo du'ain 'areed **in**

# 4270

Qul araaytum in kana min 'indi Allahi thumma kafartum bihi man adallu mimman huwa fee shiqaqin ba'eed **in**

# 4271

Sanureehim ayatina fee alafaqi wafee anfusihim hatta yatabayyana lahum annahu alhaqqu awalam yakfi birabbika annahu 'ala kulli shayin shaheed **un**

# 4272

Ala innahum fee miryatin min liqai rabbihim ala innahu bikulli shayin muheet **un**

# 4273

Hameem

# 4274

'aynseenqaf

# 4275

Kathalika yoohee ilayka waila allatheena min qablika Allahu al'azeezu alhakeem **u**

# 4276

Lahu ma fee a **l** ssamawati wama fee alardi wahuwa al'aliyyu al'a _th_ eem **u**

# 4277

Takadu a **l** ssamawatu yatafattarna min fawqihinna wa **a** lmalaikatu yusabbihoona bihamdi rabbihim wayastaghfiroona liman fee alardi ala inna Allaha huwa alghafooru a **l** rraheem **u**

# 4278

Wa **a** llatheena ittakhathoo min doonihi awliyaa Allahu hafee _th_ un 'alayhim wama anta 'alayhim biwakeel **in**

# 4279

Wakathalika awhayna ilayka quranan 'arabiyyan litunthira omma alqura waman hawlaha watunthira yawma aljam'i la rayba feehi fareequn fee aljannati wafareequn fee a **l** ssa'eer **i**

# 4280

Walaw shaa Allahu laja'alahum ommatan wahidatan walakin yudkhilu man yashao fee rahmatihi wa **al** _thth_ alimoona ma lahum min waliyyin wala naseer **in**

# 4281

Ami ittakhathoo min doonihi awliyaa fa **A** llahu huwa alwaliyyu wahuwa yuhyee almawta wahuwa 'ala kulli shayin qadeer **un**

# 4282

Wama ikhtalaftum feehi min shayin fahukmuhu ila Allahi thalikumu Allahu rabbee 'alayhi tawakkatu wailayhi oneeb **u**

# 4283

Fatiru a **l** ssamawati wa **a** lardi ja'ala lakum min anfusikum azwajan wamina alan'ami azwajan yathraokum feehi laysa kamithlihi shayon wahuwa a **l** ssamee'u albaseer **u**

# 4284

Lahu maqaleedu a **l** ssamawati wa **a** lardi yabsutu a **l** rrizqa liman yashao wayaqdiru innahu bikulli shayin 'aleem **un**

# 4285

Shara'a lakum mina a **l** ddeeni ma wassa bihi noohan wa **a** llathee awhayna ilayka wama wassayna bihi ibraheema wamoosa wa'eesa an aqeemoo a **l** ddeena wala tatafarraqoo feehi kabura 'ala almushrikeena ma tad'oohum ilayhi Allahu yajtabee ilayhi man yashao wayahdee ilayhi man yuneeb **u**

# 4286

Wama tafarraqoo illa min ba'di ma jaahumu al'ilmu baghyan baynahum walawla kalimatun sabaqat min rabbika ila ajalin musamman laqudiya baynahum wainna allatheena oorithoo alkitaba min ba'dihim lafee shakkin minhu mureeb **in**

# 4287

Falithalika fa **o** d'u wa **i** staqim kama omirta wala tattabi' ahwaahum waqul amantu bima anzala Allahu min kitabin waomirtu lia'dila baynakum Allahu rabbuna warabbukum lana a'maluna walakum a'malukum lahujjata baynana wabaynakumu Allahu yajma'u baynana wailayhi almaseer **u**

# 4288

Wa **a** llatheena yuhajjoona fee Allahi min ba'di ma istujeeba lahu hujjatuhum dahidatun 'inda rabbihim wa'alayhim ghadabun walahum 'athabun shadeed **un**

# 4289

Allahu allathee anzala alkitaba bi **a** lhaqqi wa **a** lmeezani wama yudreeka la'alla a **l** ssa'ata qareeb **un**

# 4290

Yasta'jilu biha allatheena la yuminoona biha wa **a** llatheena amanoo mushfiqoona minha waya'lamoona annaha alhaqqu ala inna allatheena yumaroona fee a **l** ssa'ati lafee dalalin ba'eed **in**

# 4291

Allahu lateefun bi'ibadihi yarzuqu man yashao wahuwa alqawiyyu al'azeez **u**

# 4292

Man kana yureedu hartha alakhirati nazid lahu fee harthihi waman kana yureedu hartha a **l** ddunya nutihi minha wama lahu fee alakhirati min naseeb **in**

# 4293

Am lahum shurakao shara'oo lahum mina a **l** ddeeni ma lam yathan bihi Allahu walawla kalimatu alfasli laqudiya baynahum wainna a **l** _thth_ alimeena lahum 'athabun aleem **un**

# 4294

Tara a **l** _thth_ alimeena mushfiqeena mimma kasaboo wahuwa waqi'un bihim wa **a** llatheena amanoo wa'amiloo a **l** ssalihati fee rawdati aljannati lahum ma yashaoona 'inda rabbihim thalika huwa alfadlu alkabeer **u**

# 4295

Thalika allathee yubashshiru Allahu 'ibadahu allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo a **l** ssalihati qul la asalukum 'alayhi ajran illa almawaddata fee alqurba waman yaqtarif hasanatan nazid lahu feehahusnan inna Allaha ghafoorun shakoor **un**

# 4296

Am yaqooloona iftara 'ala Allahi kathiban fain yashai Allahu yakhtim 'ala qalbika wayamhu Allahu albatila wayuhiqqu alhaqqa bikalimatihi innahu 'aleemun bithati a **l** ssudoor **i**

# 4297

Wahuwa allathee yaqbalu a **l** ttawbata 'an 'ibadihi waya'foo 'ani a **l** ssayyiati waya'lamu ma taf'aloon **a**

# 4298

Wayastajeebu allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo a **l** ssalihati wayazeeduhum min fadlihi wa **a** lkafiroona lahum 'athabun shadeed **un**

# 4299

Walaw basata Allahu a **l** rrizqa li'ibadihi labaghaw fee alardi walakin yunazzilu biqadarin ma yashao innahu bi'ibadihi khabeerun baseer **un**

# 4300

Wahuwa allathee yunazzilu alghaytha min ba'di ma qanatoo wayanshuru rahmatahu wahuwa alwaliyyu alhameed **u**

# 4301

Wamin ayatihi khalqu a **l** ssamawati wa **a** lardi wama baththa feehima min dabbatin wahuwa 'ala jam'ihim itha yashao qadeer **un**

# 4302

Wama asabakum min museebatin fabima kasabat aydeekum waya'foo 'an katheer **in**

# 4303

Wama antum bimu'jizeena fee alardi wama lakum min dooni Allahi min waliyyin wala naseer **in**

# 4304

Wamin ayatihi aljawari fee albahri ka **a** la'lam **i**

# 4305

In yasha yuskini a **l** rreeha faya _th_ lana rawakida 'ala _th_ ahrihi inna fee thalika laayatin likulli sabbarin shakoor **in**

# 4306

Aw yoobiqhunna bima kasaboo waya'fu 'an katheer **in**

# 4307

Waya'lama allatheena yujadiloona fee ayatina ma lahum min mahees **in**

# 4308

Fama ooteetum min shayin famata'u alhayati a **l** ddunya wama 'inda Allahi khayrun waabqa lillatheena amanoo wa'ala rabbihim yatawakkaloon **a**

# 4309

Wa **a** llatheena yajtaniboona kabaira alithmi wa **a** lfawahisha waitha ma ghadiboo hum yaghfiroon **a**

# 4310

Wa **a** llatheena istajaboo lirabbihim waaqamoo a **l** ssalata waamruhum shoora baynahum wamimma razaqnahum yunfiqoon **a**

# 4311

Wa **a** llatheena itha asabahumu albaghyu hum yantasiroon **a**

# 4312

Wajazao sayyiatin sayyiatun mithluha faman 'afa waaslaha faajruhu 'ala Allahi innahu la yuhibbu a **l** _thth_ alimeen **a**

# 4313

Walamani intasara ba'da _th_ ulmihi faolaika ma 'alayhim min sabeel **in**

# 4314

Innama a **l** ssabeelu 'ala allatheena ya _th_ limoona a **l** nnasa wayabghoona fee alardi bighayri alhaqqi olaika lahum 'athabun aleem **un**

# 4315

Walaman sabara waghafara inna thalika lamin 'azmi alomoor **i**

# 4316

Waman yudlili Allahu fama lahu min waliyyin min ba'dihi watara a **l** _thth_ alimeena lamma raawoo al'athaba yaqooloona hal ila maraddin min sabeel **in**

# 4317

Watarahum yu'radoona 'alayha khashi'eena mina a **l** ththulli yan _th_ uroona min tarfin khafiyyin waqala allatheena amanoo inna alkhasireena allatheena khasiroo anfusahum waahleehim yawma alqiyamati ala inna a **l** _thth_ alimeena fee 'athabin muqeem **in**

# 4318

Wama kana lahum min awliyaa yansuroonahum min dooni Allahi waman yudlili Allahu fama lahu min sabeel **in**

# 4319

Istajeeboo lirabbikum min qabli an yatiya yawmun la maradda lahu mina Allahi ma lakum min maljain yawmaithin wama lakum min nakeer **in**

# 4320

Fain a'radoo fama arsanaka 'alayhim hafee _th_ an in 'alayka illa albalaghu wainna itha athaqna alinsana minna rahmatan fariha biha wain tusibhum sayyiatun bima qaddamat aydeehim fainna alinsana kafoor **un**

# 4321

Lillahi mulku a **l** ssamawati wa **a** lardi yakhluqu ma yashao yahabu liman yashao inathan wayahabu liman yashao a **l** ththukoor **a**

# 4322

Aw yuzawwijuhum thukranan wainathan wayaj'alu man yashao 'aqeeman innahu 'aleemun qadeer **un**

# 4323

Wama kana libasharin an yukallimahu Allahu illa wahyan aw min warai hijabin aw yursila rasoolan fayoohiya biithnihi ma yashao innahu 'aliyyun hakeem **un**

# 4324

Wakathalika awhayna ilayka roohan min amrina ma kunta tadree ma alkitabu wala aleemanu walakin ja'anahu nooran nahdee bihi man nashao min 'ibadina wainnaka latahdee ilasiratin mustaqeem **in**

# 4325

Sirati Allahi allathee lahu ma fee a **l** ssamawati wama fee alardi ala ila Allahi taseeru alomoor **u**

# 4326

Hameem

# 4327

Wa **a** lkitabi almubeen **i**

# 4328

Inna ja'anahu quranan 'arabiyyan la'allakum ta'qiloona

# 4329

Wainnahu fee ommi alkitabi ladayna la'aliyyun hakeem **un**

# 4330

Afanadribu 'ankumu a **l** ththikra safhan an kuntum qawman musrifeen **a**

# 4331

Wakam arsana min nabiyyin fee alawwaleen **a**

# 4332

Wama yateehim min nabiyyin illa kanoo bihi yastahzioon **a**

# 4333

Faahlakna ashadda minhum batshan wamada mathalu alawwaleen **a**

# 4334

Walain saatahum man khalaqa a **l** ssamawati wa **a** larda layaqoolunna khalaqahunna al'azeezu al'aleem **u**

# 4335

Allathee ja'ala lakumu alarda mahdan waja'ala lakum feeha subulan la'allakum tahtadoon **a**

# 4336

Wa **a** llathee nazzala mina a **l** ssamai maan biqadarin faansharna bihi badatan maytan kathalika tukhrajoon **a**

# 4337

Wa **a** llathee khalaqa alazwaja kullaha waja'ala lakum mina alfulki wa **a** lan'ami ma tarkaboon **a**

# 4338

Litastawoo 'ala _th_ uhoorihi thumma tathkuroo ni'mata rabbikum itha istawaytum 'alayhi wataqooloo subhana allathee sakhkhara lana hatha wama kunna lahu muqrineen **a**

# 4339

Wainna ila rabbina lamunqaliboon **a**

# 4340

Waja'aloo lahu min 'ibadihi juzan inna alinsana lakafoorun mubeen **un**

# 4341

Ami ittakhatha mimma yakhluqu banatin waasfakum bi **a** lbaneen **a**

# 4342

Waitha bushshira ahaduhum bimadaraba li **l** rrahmani mathalan _th_ alla wajhuhu muswaddan wahuwa ka _th_ eem **un**

# 4343

Awaman yunashshao fee alhilyati wahuwa fee alkhisami ghayru mubeen **in**

# 4344

Waja'aloo almalaikata allatheena hum 'ibadu a **l** rrahmani inathan ashahidoo khalqahum satuktabu shahadatuhum wayusaloon **a**

# 4345

Waqaloo law shaa a **l** rrahmanu ma 'abadnahum ma lahum bithalika min 'ilmin in hum illa yakhrusoon **a**

# 4346

Am ataynahum kitaban min qablihi fahum bihi mustamsikoon **a**

# 4347

Bal qaloo inna wajadnaabaana 'ala ommatin wainna 'alaatharihim muhtadoon **a**

# 4348

Wakathalika ma arsana min qablika fee qaryatin min natheerin illa qala mutrafooha inna wajadnaabaana 'ala ommatin wainna 'alaatharihim muqtadoon **a**

# 4349

Qala awalaw jitukum biahda mimma wajadtum 'alayhi abaakum qaloo inna bima orsiltum bihi kafiroon **a**

# 4350

Fa **i** ntaqamna minhum fa **o** n _th_ ur kayfa kana 'aqibatu almukaththibeen **a**

# 4351

Waith qala ibraheemu liabeehi waqawmihi innanee baraon mimma ta'budoon **a**

# 4352

Illa allathee fataranee fainnahu sayahdeen **i**

# 4353

Waja'alaha kalimatan baqiyatan fee 'aqibihi la'allahum yarji'oon **a**

# 4354

Bal matta'tu haolai waabaahum hatta jaahumu alhaqqu warasoolun mubeen **un**

# 4355

Walamma jaahumu alhaqqu qaloo hatha sihrun wainna bihi kafiroon **a**

# 4356

Waqaloo lawla nuzzila hatha alquranu 'ala rajulin mina alqaryatayni 'a _th_ eem **un**

# 4357

Ahum yaqsimoona rahmata rabbika nahnu qasamna baynahum ma'eeshatahum fee alhayati a **l** ddunya warafa'na ba'dahum fawqa ba'din darajatin liyattakhitha ba'duhum ba'dan sukhriyyan warahmatu rabbika khayrun mimma yajma'oon **a**

# 4358

Walawla an yakoona a **l** nnasu ommatan wahidatan laja'ana liman yakfuru bi **al** rrahmani libuyootihim suqufan min fiddatin wama'arija 'alayha ya _th_ haroon **a**

# 4359

Walibuyootihim abwaban wasururan 'alayha yattakioon **a**

# 4360

Wazukhrufan wain kullu thalika lamma mata'u alhayati a **l** ddunya wa **a** lakhiratu 'inda rabbika lilmuttaqeen **a**

# 4361

Waman ya'shu 'an thikri a **l** rrahmani nuqayyid lahu shaytanan fahuwa lahu qareen **un**

# 4362

Wainnahum layasuddoonahum 'ani a **l** ssabeeli wayahsaboona annahum muhtadoon **a**

# 4363

Hatta itha jaana qala ya layta baynee wabaynaka bu'da almashriqayni fabisa alqareen **u**

# 4364

Walan yanfa'akumu alyawma ith _th_ alamtum annakum fee al'athabi mushtarikoon **a**

# 4365

Afaanta tusmi'u a **l** ssumma aw tahdee al'umya waman kana fee dalalin mubeen **in**

# 4366

Faimma nathhabanna bika fainna minhum muntaqimoon **a**

# 4367

Aw nuriyannaka allathee wa'adnahum fainna 'alayhim muqtadiroon **a**

# 4368

Fa **i** stamsik bi **a** llathee oohiya ilayka innaka 'alasiratin mustaqeem **in**

# 4369

Wainnahu lathikrun laka waliqawmika wasawfa tusaloon **a**

# 4370

Wa **i** sal man arsana min qablika min rusulina aja'ana min dooni a **l** rrahmani alihatan yu'badoon **a**

# 4371

Walaqad arsana moosa biayatina ila fir'awna wamalaihi faqala innee rasoolu rabbi al'alameen **a**

# 4372

Falamma jaahum biayatina itha hum minha yadhakoon **a**

# 4373

Wama nureehim min ayatin illa hiya akbaru min okhtiha waakhathnahum bi **a** l'athabi la'allahum yarji'oon **a**

# 4374

Waqaloo ya ayyuha a **l** sahiru od'u lana rabbaka bima 'ahida 'indaka innana lamuhtadoon **a**

# 4375

Falamma kashafna 'anhumu al'athaba itha hum yankuthoon **a**

# 4376

Wanada fir'awnu fee qawmihi qala ya qawmi alaysa lee mulku misra wahathihi alanharu tajree min tahtee afala tubsiroon **a**

# 4377

Am ana khayrun min hatha allathee huwa maheenun wala yakadu yubeen **u**

# 4378

Falawla olqiya 'alayhi aswiratun min thahabin aw jaa ma'ahu almalaikatu muqtarineen **a**

# 4379

Fa **i** stakhaffa qawmahu faata'oohu innahum kanoo qawman fasiqeen **a**

# 4380

Falammaasafoona intaqamna minhum faaghraqnahum ajma'een **a**

# 4381

Faja'anahum salafan wamathalan lilakhireen **a**

# 4382

Walammaduriba ibnu maryama mathalan itha qawmuka minhu yasiddoon **a**

# 4383

Waqaloo aalihatuna khayrun am huwa madaraboohu laka illa jadalan bal hum qawmun khasimoon **a**

# 4384

In huwa illa 'abdun an'amna 'alayhi waja'anahu mathalan libanee israeel **a**

# 4385

Walaw nashao laja'ana minkum malaikatan fee alardi yakhlufoon **a**

# 4386

Wainnahu la'ilmun li **l** ssa'ati fala tamtarunna biha wa **i** ttabi'ooni hathasiratun mustaqeem **un**

# 4387

Wala yasuddannakumu a **l** shshaytanu innahu lakum 'aduwwun mubeen **un**

# 4388

Walamma jaa 'eesa bi **a** lbayyinati qala qad jitukum bi **a** lhikmati waliobayyina lakum ba'da allathee takhtalifoona feehi fa **i** ttaqoo Allaha waatee'oon **i**

# 4389

Inna Allaha huwa rabbee warabbukum fa **o** 'budoohu hathasiratun mustaqeem **un**

# 4390

Fa **i** khtalafa alahzabu min baynihim fawaylun lillatheena _th_ alamoo min 'athabi yawmin aleem **in**

# 4391

Hal yan _th_ uroona illa a **l** ssa'ata an tatiyahum baghtatan wahum la yash'uroon **a**

# 4392

Alakhillao yawmaithin ba'duhum liba'din 'aduwwun illa almuttaqeen **a**

# 4393

Ya 'ibadi la khawfun 'alaykumu alyawma wala antum tahzanoon **a**

# 4394

Allatheena amanoo biayatina wakanoo muslimeen **a**

# 4395

Odkhuloo aljannata antum waazwajukum tuhbaroon **a**

# 4396

Yutafu 'alayhim bisihafin min thahabin waakwabin wafeeha ma tashtaheehi alanfusu watalaththu ala'yunu waantum feeha khalidoon **a**

# 4397

Watilka aljannatu allatee oorithtumooha bima kuntum ta'maloon **a**

# 4398

Lakum feeha fakihatun katheeratun minha takuloon **a**

# 4399

Inna almujrimeena fee 'athabi jahannama khalidoon **a**

# 4400

La yufattaru 'anhum wahum feehi mublisoon **a**

# 4401

Wama _th_ alamnahum walakin kanoo humu a **l** _thth_ alimeen **a**

# 4402

Wanadaw ya maliku liyaqdi 'alayna rabbuka qala innakum makithoon **a**

# 4403

Laqad jinakum bi **a** lhaqqi walakinna aktharakum lilhaqqi karihoon **a**

# 4404

Am abramoo amran fainna mubrimoon **a**

# 4405

Am yahsaboona anna la nasma'u sirrahum wanajwahum bala warusuluna ladayhim yaktuboon **a**

# 4406

Qul in kana li **l** rrahmani waladun faana awwalu al'abideen **a**

# 4407

Subhana rabbi a **l** ssamawati wa **a** lardi rabbi al'arshi 'amma yasifoon **a**

# 4408

Fatharhum yakhoodoo wayal'aboo hatta yulaqoo yawmahumu allathee yoo'adoon **a**

# 4409

Wahuwa allathee fee a **l** ssamai ilahun wafee alardi ilahun wahuwa alhakeemu al'aleem **u**

# 4410

Watabaraka allathee lahu mulku a **l** ssamawati wa **a** lardi wama baynahuma wa'indahu 'ilmu a **l** ssa'ati wailayhi turja'oon **a**

# 4411

Wala yamliku allatheena yad'oona min doonihi a **l** shshafa'ata illa man shahida bi **a** lhaqqi wahum ya'lamoon **a**

# 4412

Walain saatahum man khalaqahum layaqoolunna Allahu faanna yufakoon **a**

# 4413

Waqeelihi yarabbi inna haolai qawmun la yuminoon **a**

# 4414

Fa **i** sfah 'anhum waqul salamun fasawfa ya'lamoon **a**

# 4416

Wa **a** lkitabi almubeen **i**

# 4417

# 4418

# 4419

# 4420

Rahmatan min rabbika innahu huwa a **l** ssamee'u al'aleem **u**

# 4421

# 4422

# 4423

# 4424

Fa **i** rtaqib yawma tatee a **l** ssamao bidukhanin mubeen **in**

# 4425

# 4426

Rabbana ikshif 'anna al'athaba inna muminoon **a**

# 4427

# 4428

# 4429

# 4430

# 4431

# 4432

# 4433

# 4434

# 4435

# 4439

# 4440

# 4441

# 4442

# 4443

# 4444

# 4445

# 4446

# 4447

# 4448

# 4449

# 4450

Fatoo biabaina in kuntum sadiqeen **a**

# 4451

Ahum khayrun am qawmu tubba'in wa **a** llatheena min qablihim ahlaknahum innahum kanoo mujrimeen **a**

# 4452

Wama khalaqna a **l** ssamawati wa **a** larda wama baynahuma la'ibeen **a**

# 4453

Ma khalaqnahuma illa bi **a** lhaqqi walakinna aktharahum la ya'lamoon **a**

# 4454

Inna yawma alfasli meeqatuhum ajma'een **a**

# 4455

Yawma la yughnee mawlan 'an mawlan shayan wala hum yunsaroon **a**

# 4456

# 4457

Inna shajarata a **l** zzaqqoom **i**

# 4458

Ta'amu alatheem **i**

# 4459

Ka **a** lmuhli yaghlee fee albutoon **i**

# 4460

Kaghalyi alhameem **i**

# 4461

Khuthoohu fa **i** 'tiloohu ila sawai aljaheem **i**

# 4462

Thumma subboo fawqa rasihi min 'athabi alhameem **i**

# 4463

Thuq innaka anta al'azeezu alkareem **u**

# 4464

Inna hatha ma kuntum bihi tamtaroon **a**

# 4465

Inna almuttaqeena fee maqamin ameen **in**

# 4466

Fee jannatin wa'uyoon **in**

# 4467

Yalbasoona min sundusin waistabraqin mutaqabileen **a**

# 4468

Kathalika wazawwajnahum bihoorin 'een **in**

# 4469

Yad'oona feeha bikulli fakihatin amineen **a**

# 4470

La yathooqoona feeha almawta illa almawtata aloola wawaqahum 'athaba aljaheem **i**

# 4471

Fadlan min rabbika thalika huwa alfawzu al'a _th_ eem **u**

# 4472

Fainnama yassarnahu bilisanika la'allahum yatathakkaroon **a**

# 4473

Fa **i** rtaqib innahum murtaqiboon **a**

# 4474

Hameem

# 4475

Tanzeelu alkitabi mina Allahi al'azeezi alhakeem **i**

# 4476

Inna fee a **l** ssamawati wa **a** lardi laayatin lilmumineen **a**

# 4477

Wafee khalqikum wama yabuththu min dabbatin ayatun liqawmin yooqinoon **a**

# 4478

Wa **i** khtilafi allayli wa **al** nnahari wama anzala Allahu mina a **l** ssamai min rizqin faahya bihi alarda ba'da mawtiha watasreefi a **l** rriyahi ayatun liqawmin ya'qiloon **a**

# 4479

Tilka ayatu Allahi natlooha 'alayka bi **a** lhaqqi fabiayyi hadeethin ba'da Allahi waayatihi yuminoon **a**

# 4480

Waylun likulli affakin atheem **in**

# 4481

Yasma'u ayati Allahi tutla 'alayhi thumma yusirru mustakbiran kaan lam yasma'ha fabashshirhu bi'athabin aleem **in**

# 4482

Waitha 'alima min ayatina shayan ittakhathaha huzuwan olaika lahum 'athabun muheen **un**

# 4483

Min waraihim jahannamu wala yughnee 'anhum ma kasaboo shayan wala ma ittakhathoo min dooni Allahi awliyaa walahum 'athabun 'a _th_ eem **un**

# 4484

Hatha hudan wa **a** llatheena kafaroo biayati rabbihim lahum 'athabun min rijzin aleem **in**

# 4485

Allahu allathee sakhkhara lakumu albahra litajriya alfulku feehi biamrihi walitabtaghoo min fadlihi wala'allakum tashkuroon **a**

# 4486

Wasakhkhara lakum ma fee a **l** ssamawati wama fee alardi jamee'an minhu inna fee thalika laayatin liqawmin yatafakkaroon **a**

# 4487

Qul lillatheena amanoo yaghfiroo lillatheena la yarjoona ayyama Allahi liyajziya qawman bima kanoo yaksiboon **a**

# 4488

Man 'amila salihan falinafsihi waman asaa fa'alayha thumma ila rabbikum turja'oon **a**

# 4489

Walaqad atayna banee israeela alkitaba wa **a** lhukma wa **al** nnubuwwata warazaqnahum mina a **l** ttayyibati wafaddanahum 'ala al'alameen **a**

# 4490

Waataynahum bayyinatin mina alamri fama ikhtalafoo illa min ba'di ma jaahumu al'ilmu baghyan baynahum inna rabbaka yaqdee baynahum yawma alqiyamati feema kanoo feehi yakhtalifoon **a**

# 4491

Thumma ja'anaka 'ala sharee'atin mina alamri fa **i** ttabi'ha wala tattabi' ahwaa allatheena la ya'lamoon **a**

# 4492

Innahum lan yughnoo 'anka mina Allahi shayan wainna a **l** _thth_ alimeena ba'duhum awliyao ba'din wa **A** llahu waliyyu almuttaqeen **a**

# 4493

Hatha basairu li **l** nnasi wahudan warahmatun liqawmin yooqinoon **a**

# 4494

Am hasiba allatheena ijtarahoo a **l** ssayyiati an naj'alahum ka **a** llatheena amanoo wa'amiloo a **l** ssalihati sawaan mahyahum wamamatuhum saa ma yahkumoon **a**

# 4495

Wakhalaqa Allahu a **l** ssamawati wa **a** larda bi **a** lhaqqi walitujza kullu nafsin bima kasabat wahum la yu _th_ lamoon **a**

# 4496

Afaraayta mani ittakhatha ilahahu hawahu waadallahu Allahu 'ala 'ilmin wakhatama 'ala sam'ihi waqalbihi waja'ala 'ala basarihi ghishawatan faman yahdeehi min ba'di Allahi afala tathakkaroon **a**

# 4497

Waqaloo ma hiya illahayatuna a **l** ddunya namootu wanahya wama yuhlikuna illa a **l** ddahru wama lahum bithalika min 'ilmin in hum illa ya _th_ unnoon **a**

# 4498

Waitha tutla 'alayhim ayatuna bayyinatin ma kana hujjatahum illa an qaloo itoo biabaina in kuntum sadiqeen **a**

# 4499

Quli Allahu yuhyeekum thumma yumeetukum thumma yajma'ukum ila yawmi alqiyamati la rayba feehi walakinna akthara a **l** nnasi la ya'lamoon **a**

# 4500

Walillahi mulku a **l** ssamawati wa **a** lardi wayawma taqoomu a **l** ssa'atu yawmaithin yakhsaru almubtiloon **a**

# 4501

Watara kulla ommatin jathiyatan kullu ommatin tud'a ila kitabiha alyawma tujzawna ma kuntum ta'maloon **a**

# 4502

Hatha kitabuna yantiqu 'alaykum bi **a** lhaqqi inna kunna nastansikhu ma kuntum ta'maloon **a**

# 4503

Faamma allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo a **l** ssalihati fayudkhiluhum rabbuhum fee rahmatihi thalika huwa alfawzu almubeen **u**

# 4504

Waamma allatheena kafaroo afalam takun ayatee tutla 'alaykum fa **i** stakbartum wakuntum qawman mujrimeen **a**

# 4505

Waitha qeela inna wa'da Allahi haqqun wa **al** ssa'atu la rayba feeha qultum ma nadree ma a **l** ssa'atu in na _th_ unnu illa _th_ annan wama nahnu bimustayqineen **a**

# 4506

Wabada lahum sayyiatu ma 'amiloo wahaqa bihim ma kanoo bihi yastahzioon **a**

# 4507

Waqeela alyawma nansakum kama naseetum liqaa yawmikum hatha wamawakumu a **l** nnaru wama lakum min nasireen **a**

# 4508

Thalikum biannakumu ittakhathtum ayati Allahi huzuwan wagharratkumu alhayatu a **l** ddunya fa **a** lyawma la yukhrajoona minha wala hum yusta'taboon **a**

# 4509

Falillahi alhamdu rabbi a **l** ssamawati warabbi alardi rabbi al'alameen **a**

# 4510

Walahu alkibriyao fee a **l** ssamawati wa **a** lardi wahuwa al'azeezu alhakeem **u**

# 4511

Hameem

# 4512

Tanzeelu alkitabi mina Allahi al'azeezi alhakeem **i**

# 4513

Ma khalaqna a **l** ssamawati wa **a** larda wama baynahuma illa bi **a** lhaqqi waajalin musamman wa **a** llatheena kafaroo 'amma onthiroo mu'ridoon **a**

# 4514

Qul araaytum ma tad'oona min dooni Allahi aroonee matha khalaqoo mina alardi am lahum shirkun fee a **l** ssamawati eetoonee bikitabin min qabli hatha aw atharatin min 'ilmin in kuntum sadiqeen **a**

# 4515

Waman adallu mimman yad'oo min dooni Allahi man la yastajeebu lahu ila yawmi alqiyamati wahum 'an du'aihim ghafiloon **a**

# 4516

Waithahushira a **l** nnasu kanoo lahum a'daan wakanoo bi'ibadatihim kafireen **a**

# 4517

Waitha tutla 'alayhim ayatuna bayyinatin qala allatheena kafaroo lilhaqqi lamma jaahum hatha sihrun mubeen **un**

# 4518

Am yaqooloona iftarahu qul ini iftaraytuhu fala tamlikoona lee mina Allahi shayan huwa a'lamu bima tufeedoona feehi kafa bihi shaheedan baynee wabaynakum wahuwa alghafooru a **l** rraheem **u**

# 4519

Qul ma kuntu bid'an mina a **l** rrusuli wama adree ma yuf'alu bee wala bikum in attabi'u illa ma yooha ilayya wama ana illa natheerun mubeen **un**

# 4520

Qul araaytum in kana min 'indi Allahi wakafartum bihi washahida shahidun min banee israeela 'ala mithlihi faamana wa **i** stakbartum inna Allaha la yahdee alqawma a **l** _thth_ alimeen **a**

# 4521

Waqala allatheena kafaroo lillatheena amanoo law kana khayran ma sabaqoona ilayhi waith lam yahtadoo bihi fasayaqooloona hatha ifkun qadeem **un**

# 4522

Wamin qablihi kitabu moosa imaman warahmatan wahatha kitabun musaddiqun lisanan 'arabiyyan liyunthira allatheena _th_ alamoo wabushra lilmuhsineen **a**

# 4523

Inna allatheena qaloo rabbuna Allahu thumma istaqamoo fala khawfun 'alayhim wala hum yahzanoon **a**

# 4524

Olaika ashabu aljannati khalideena feeha jazaan bima kanoo ya'maloon **a**

# 4525

Wawassayna alinsana biwalidayhi ihsanan hamalathu ommuhu kurhan wawada'athu kurhan wahamluhu wafisaluhu thalathoona shahran hatta itha balagha ashuddahu wabalagha arba'eena sanatan qala rabbi awzi'nee an ashkura ni'mataka allatee an'amta 'alayya wa'ala walidayya waan a'mala salihan tardahu waaslih lee fee thurriyyatee innee tubtu ilayka wainnee mina almuslimeen **a**

# 4526

Olaika allatheena nataqabbalu 'anhum ahsana ma 'amiloo wanatajawazu 'an sayyiatihim fee ashabi aljannati wa'da a **l** ssidqi allathee kanoo yoo'adoon **a**

# 4527

Wa **a** llathee qala liwalidayhi offin lakuma ata'idaninee an okhraja waqad khalati alquroonu min qablee wahuma yastagheethani Allaha waylaka amin inna wa'da Allahi haqqun fayaqoolu ma hatha illa asateeru alawwaleen **a**

# 4528

Olaika allatheena haqqa 'alayhimu alqawlu fee umamin qad khalat min qablihim mina aljinni wa **a** linsi innahum kanoo khasireen **a**

# 4529

Walikullin darajatun mimma 'amiloo waliyuwaffiyahum a'malahum wahum la yu _th_ lamoon **a**

# 4530

Wayawma yu'radu allatheena kafaroo 'ala a **l** nnari athhabtum tayyibatikum fee hayatikumu a **l** ddunya wa **i** stamta'tum biha fa **a** lyawma tujzawna 'athaba alhooni bima kuntum tastakbiroona fee alardi bighayri alhaqqi wabima kuntum tafsuqoon **a**

# 4531

Wa **o** thkur akha 'adin ith anthara qawmahu bi **a** lahqafi waqad khalati a **l** nnuthuru min bayni yadayhi wamin khalfihi alla ta'budoo illa Allaha innee akhafu 'alaykum 'athaba yawmin 'a _th_ eem **in**

# 4532

Qaloo ajitana litafikana 'an alihatina fatina bima ta'iduna in kunta mina a **l** ssadiqeen **a**

# 4533

Qala innama al'ilmu 'inda Allahi waoballighukum ma orsiltu bihi walakinnee arakum qawman tajhaloon **a**

# 4534

Falamma raawhu 'aridan mustaqbila awdiyatihim qaloo hatha 'aridun mumtiruna bal huwa ma ista'jatum bihi reehun feeha 'athabun aleem **un**

# 4535

Tudammiru kulla shayin biamri rabbiha faasbahoo la yura illa masakinuhum kathalika najzee alqawma almujrimeen **a**

# 4536

Walaqad makkannahum feema in makkannakum feehi waja'ana lahum sam'an waabsaran waafidatan fama aghna 'anhum sam'uhum wala absaruhum wala afidatuhum min shayin ith kanoo yajhadoona biayati Allahi wahaqa bihim ma kanoo bihi yastahzioon **a**

# 4537

Walaqad ahlakna mahawlakum mina alqura wasarrafna alayati la'allahum yarji'oon **a**

# 4538

Falawla nasarahumu allatheena ittakhathoo min dooni Allahi qurbanan alihatan bal dalloo 'anhum wathalika ifkuhum wama kanoo yaftaroon **a**

# 4539

Waithsarafna ilayka nafaran mina aljinni yastami'oona alqurana falammahadaroohu qaloo ansitoo falamma qudiya wallaw ila qawmihim munthireen **a**

# 4540

Qaloo ya qawmana inna sami'na kitaban onzila min ba'di moosa musaddiqan lima bayna yadayhi yahdee ila alhaqqi wailatareeqin mustaqeem **in**

# 4541

Ya qawmana ajeeboo da'iya Allahi waaminoo bihi yaghfir lakum min thunoobikum wayujirkum min 'athabin aleem **in**

# 4542

Waman la yujib da'iya Allahi falaysa bimu'jizin fee alardi walaysa lahu min doonihi awliyaa olaika fee dalalin mubeen **in**

# 4543

Awalam yaraw anna Allaha allathee khalaqa a **l** ssamawati wa **a** larda walam ya'ya bikhalqihinna biqadirin 'ala an yuhyiya almawta bala innahu 'ala kulli shayin qadeer **un**

# 4544

Wayawma yu'radu allatheena kafaroo 'ala a **l** nnari alaysa hatha bi **a** lhaqqi qaloo bala warabbina qala fathooqoo al'athaba bima kuntum takfuroon **a**

# 4545

Fa **i** sbir kamasabara oloo al'azmi mina a **l** rrusuli wala tasta'jil lahum kaannahum yawma yarawna ma yoo'adoona lam yalbathoo illa sa'atan min naharin balaghun fahal yuhlaku illa alqawmu alfasiqoon **a**

# 4546

Allatheena kafaroo wasaddoo 'an sabeeli Allahi adalla a'malahum

# 4547

Wa **a** llatheena amanoo wa'amiloo a **l** ssalihati waamanoo bima nuzzila 'ala muhammadin wahuwa alhaqqu min rabbihim kaffara 'anhum sayyiatihim waaslaha balahum

# 4548

Thalika bianna allatheena kafaroo ittaba'oo albatila waanna allatheena amanoo ittaba'oo alhaqqa min rabbihim kathalika yadribu Allahu li **l** nnasi amthalahum

# 4549

Faitha laqeetumu allatheena kafaroo fadarba a **l** rriqabi hatta itha athkhantumoohum fashuddoo alwathaqa faimma mannan ba'du waimma fidaan hatta tada'a alharbu awzarahathalika walaw yashao Allahu la **i** ntasara minhum walakin liyabluwa ba'dakum biba'din wa **a** llatheena qutiloo fee sabeeli Allahi falan yudilla a'malahum

# 4550

Sayahdeehim wayuslihu balahum

# 4551

Wayudkhiluhumu aljannata 'arrafaha lahum

# 4552

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo in tansuroo Allaha yansurkum wayuthabbit aqdamakum

# 4553

Wa **a** llatheena kafaroo fata'san lahum waadalla a'malahum

# 4554

Thalika biannahum karihoo ma anzala Allahu faahbata a'malahum

# 4555

Afalam yaseeroo fee alardi fayan _th_ uroo kayfa kana 'aqibatu allatheena min qablihim dammara Allahu 'alayhim walilkafireena amthaluha

# 4556

Thalika bianna Allaha mawla allatheena amanoo waanna alkafireena la mawla lahum

# 4557

Inna Allaha yudkhilu allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo a **l** ssalihati jannatin tajree min tahtiha alanharu wa **a** llatheena kafaroo yatamatta'oona wayakuloona kama takulu alan'amu wa **al** nnaru mathwan lahum

# 4558

Wakaayyin min qaryatin hiya ashaddu quwwatan min qaryatika allatee akhrajatka ahlaknahum fala nasira lahum

# 4559

Afaman kana 'ala bayyinatin min rabbihi kaman zuyyina lahu sooo 'amalihi wa **i** ttaba'oo ahwaahum

# 4560

Mathalu aljannati allatee wu'ida almuttaqoona feeha anharun min main ghayri asinin waanharun min labanin lam yataghayyar ta'muhu waanharun min khamrin laththatin li **l** shsharibeena waanharun min 'asalin musaffan walahum feeha min kulli a **l** ththamarati wamaghfiratun min rabbihim kaman huwa khalidun fee a **l** nnari wasuqoo maan hameeman faqatta'a am'aahum

# 4561

Waminhum man yastami'u ilayka hatta itha kharajoo min 'indika qaloo lillatheena ootoo al'ilma matha qala anifan olaika allatheena taba'a Allahu 'ala quloobihim wa **i** ttaba'oo ahwaahum

# 4562

Wa **a** llatheena ihtadaw zadahum hudan waatahum taqwahum

# 4563

Fahal yan _th_ uroona illa a **l** ssa'ata an tatiyahum baghtatan faqad jaa ashratuha faanna lahum itha jaathum thikrahum

# 4564

Fa **i** 'lam annahu la ilaha illa Allahu wa **i** staghfir lithanbika walilmumineena wa **a** lmuminati wa **A** llahu ya'lamu mutaqallabakum wamathwakum

# 4565

Wayaqoolu allatheena amanoo lawla nuzzilat sooratun faitha onzilat sooratun muhkamatun wathukira feeha alqitalu raayta allatheena fee quloobihim maradun yan _th_ uroona ilayka na _th_ ara almaghshiyyi 'alayhi mina almawti faawla lahum

# 4566

Ta'atun waqawlun ma'roofun faitha 'azama alamru falaw sadaqoo Allaha lakana khayran lahum

# 4567

Fahal 'asaytum in tawallaytum an tufsidoo fee alardi watuqatti'oo arhamakum

# 4568

Olaika allatheena la'anahumu Allahu faasammahum waa'ma absarahum

# 4569

Afala yatadabbaroona alqurana am 'ala quloobin aqfaluha

# 4570

Inna allatheena irtaddoo 'ala adbarihim min ba'di ma tabayyana lahumu alhuda a **l** shshaytanu sawwala lahum waamla lahum

# 4571

Thalika biannahum qaloo lillatheena karihoo ma nazzala Allahu sanutee'ukum fee ba'di alamri wa **A** llahu ya'lamu israrahum

# 4572

Fakayfa itha tawaffathumu almalaikatu yadriboona wujoohahum waadbarahum

# 4573

Thalika biannahumu ittaba'oo ma askhata Allaha wakarihoo ridwanahu faahbata a'malahum

# 4574

Am hasiba allatheena fee quloobihim maradun an lan yukhrija Allahu adghanahum

# 4575

Walaw nashao laaraynakahum fala'araftahum biseemahum walata'rifannahum fee lahni alqawli wa **A** llahu ya'lamu a'malakum

# 4576

Walanabluwannakum hatta na'lama almujahideena minkum wa **al** ssabireena wanabluwa akhbarakum

# 4577

Inna allatheena kafaroo wasaddoo 'an sabeeli Allahi washaqqoo a **l** rrasoola min ba'di ma tabayyana lahumu alhuda lan yaduroo Allaha shayan wasayuhbitu a'malahum

# 4578

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo atee'oo Allaha waatee'oo a **l** rrasoola wala tubtiloo a'malakum

# 4579

Inna allatheena kafaroo wasaddoo 'an sabeeli Allahi thumma matoo wahum kuffarun falan yaghfira Allahu lahum

# 4580

Fala tahinoo watad'oo ila a **l** ssalmi waantumu ala'lawna wa **A** llahu ma'akum walan yatirakum a'malakum

# 4581

Innama alhayatu a **l** ddunya la'ibun walahwun wain tuminoo watattaqoo yutikum ojoorakum wala yasalkum amwalakum

# 4582

In yasalkumooha fayuhfikum tabkhaloo wayukhrij adghanakum

# 4583

Haantum haolai tud'awna litunfiqoo fee sabeeli Allahi faminkum man yabkhalu waman yabkhal fainnama yabkhalu 'an nafsihi wa **A** llahu alghaniyyu waantumu alfuqarao wain tatawallaw yastabdil qawman ghayrakum thumma la yakoonoo amthalakum

# 4584

Inna fatahna laka fathan mubeena **n**

# 4585

Liyaghfira laka Allahu ma taqaddama min thanbika wama taakhkhara wayutimma ni'matahu 'alayka wayahdiyaka siratan mustaqeema **n**

# 4586

Wayansuraka Allahu nasran 'azeeza **n**

# 4587

Huwa allathee anzala a **l** ssakeenata fee quloobi almumineena liyazdadoo eemanan ma'a eemanihim walillahi junoodu a **l** ssamawati wa **a** lardi wakana Allahu 'aleeman hakeema **n**

# 4588

Liyudkhila almumineena wa **a** lmuminati jannatin tajree min tahtiha alanharu khalideena feeha wayukaffira 'anhum sayyiatihim wakana thalika 'inda Allahi fawzan 'a _th_ eema **n**

# 4589

Wayu'aththiba almunafiqeena wa **a** lmunafiqati wa **a** lmushrikeena wa **a** lmushrikati a **l** _thth_ anneena bi **A** llahi _th_ anna a **l** ssawi 'alayhim dairatu a **l** ssawi waghadiba Allahu 'alayhim wala'anahum waa'adda lahum jahannama wasaat maseera **n**

# 4590

Walillahi junoodu a **l** ssamawati wa **a** lardi wakana Allahu 'azeezan hakeema **n**

# 4591

Inna arsanaka shahidan wamubashshiran wanatheera **n**

# 4592

Lituminoo bi **A** llahi warasoolihi watu'azziroohu watuwaqqiroohu watusabbihoohu bukratan waaseela **n**

# 4593

Inna allatheena yubayi'oonaka innama yubayi'oona Allaha yadu Allahi fawqa aydeehim faman nakatha fainnama yankuthu 'ala nafsihi waman awfa bima 'ahada 'alayhu Allaha fasayuteehi ajran 'a _th_ eema **n**

# 4594

Sayaqoolu laka almukhallafoona mina ala'rabi shaghalatna amwaluna waahloona fa **i** staghfir lana yaqooloona biasinatihim ma laysa fee quloobihim qul faman yamliku lakum mina Allahi shayan in arada bikum darran aw arada bikum naf'an bal kana Allahu bima ta'maloona khabeera **n**

# 4595

Bal _th_ anantum an lan yanqaliba a **l** rrasoolu wa **a** lmuminoona ila ahleehim abadan wazuyyina thalika fee quloobikum wa _th_ anantum _th_ anna a **l** ssawi wakuntum qawman boora **n**

# 4596

Waman lam yumin bi **A** llahi warasoolihi fainna a'tadna lilkafireena sa'eera **n**

# 4597

Walillahi mulku a **l** ssamawati wa **a** lardi yaghfiru liman yashao wayu'aththibu man yashao wakana Allahu ghafooran raheema **n**

# 4598

Sayaqoolu almukhallafoona itha intalaqtum ila maghanima litakhuthoohatharoona nattabi'kum yureedoona an yubaddiloo kalama Allahi qul lan tattabi'oona kathalikum qala Allahu min qablu fasayaqooloona bal tahsudoonana bal kanoo la yafqahoona illa qaleela **n**

# 4599

Qul lilmukhallafeena mina ala'rabi satud'awna ila qawmin olee basin shadeedin tuqatiloonahum aw yuslimoona fain tutee'oo yutikumu Allahu ajran hasanan wain tatawallaw kama tawallaytum min qablu yu'aththibkum 'athaban aleema **n**

# 4600

Laysa 'ala ala'maharajun wala 'ala ala'raji harajun wala 'ala almareedi harajun waman yuti'i Allaha warasoolahu yudkhilhu jannatin tajree min tahtiha alanharu waman yatawalla yu'aththibhu 'athaban aleema **n**

# 4601

Laqad radiya Allahu 'ani almumineena ith yubayi'oonaka tahta a **l** shshajarati fa'alima ma fee quloobihim faanzala a **l** sakeenata 'alayhim waathabahum fathan qareeba **n**

# 4602

Wamaghanima katheeratan yakhuthoonaha wakana Allahu 'azeezan hakeema **n**

# 4603

Wa'adakumu Allahu maghanima katheeratan takhuthoonaha fa'ajjala lakum hathihi wakaffa aydiya a **l** nnasi 'ankum walitakoona ayatan lilmumineena wayahdiyakum siratan mustaqeema **n**

# 4604

Waokhra lam taqdiroo 'alayha qad ahata Allahu biha wakana Allahu 'ala kulli shayin qadeera **n**

# 4605

Walaw qatalakumu allatheena kafaroo lawallawoo aladbara thumma la yajidoona waliyyan wala naseera **n**

# 4606

Sunnata Allahi allatee qad khalat min qablu walan tajida lisunnati Allahi tabdeela **n**

# 4607

Wahuwa allathee kaffa aydiyahum 'ankum waaydiyakum 'anhum bibatni makkata min ba'di an a _th_ farakum 'alayhim wakana Allahu bima ta'maloona baseera **n**

# 4608

Humu allatheena kafaroo wasaddookum 'ani almasjidi alharami wa **a** lhadya ma'koofan an yablugha mahillahu walawla rijalun muminoona wanisaon muminatun lam ta'lamoohum an tataoohum fatuseebakum minhum ma'arratun bighayri 'ilmin liyudkhila Allahu fee rahmatihi man yashao law tazayyaloo la'aththabna allatheena kafaroo minhum 'athaban aleema **n**

# 4609

Ith ja'ala allatheena kafaroo fee quloobihimu alhamiyyata hamiyyata aljahiliyyati faanzala Allahu sakeenatahu 'ala rasoolihi wa'ala almumineena waazamahum kalimata a **l** ttaqwa wakanoo ahaqqa biha waahlaha wakana Allahu bikulli shayin 'aleema **n**

# 4610

Laqad sadaqa Allahu rasoolahu a **l** rruya bi **a** lhaqqi latadkhulunna almasjida alharama in shaa Allahu amineena muhalliqeena ruoosakum wamuqassireena la takhafoona fa'alima ma lam ta'lamoo faja'ala min dooni thalika fathan qareeba **n**

# 4611

Huwa allathee arsala rasoolahu bi **a** lhuda wadeeni alhaqqi liyu _th_ hirahu 'ala a **l** ddeeni kullihi wakafa bi **A** llahi shaheeda **n**

# 4612

Muhammadun rasoolu Allahi wa **a** llatheena ma'ahu ashiddao 'ala alkuffari ruhamao baynahum tarahum rukka'an sujjadan yabtaghoona fadlan mina Allahi waridwanan seemahum fee wujoohihim min athari a **l** ssujoodi thalika mathaluhum fee a **l** ttawrati wamathaluhum fee alinjeeli kazar'in akhraja shatahu faazarahu fa **i** staghla _th_ a fa **i** stawa 'ala sooqihi yu'jibu a **l** zzurra'a liyaghee _th_ a bihimu alkuffara wa'ada Allahu allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo a **l** ssalihati minhum maghfiratan waajran 'a _th_ eema **n**

# 4613

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la tuqaddimoo bayna yadayi Allahi warasoolihi wa **i** ttaqoo Allaha inna Allaha samee'un 'aleem **un**

# 4614

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la tarfa'oo aswatakum fawqa sawti a **l** nnabiyyi wala tajharoo lahu bi **a** lqawli kajahri ba'dikum liba'din an tahbata a'malukum waantum la tash'uroon **a**

# 4615

Inna allatheena yaghuddoona aswatahum 'inda rasooli Allahi olaika allatheena imtahana Allahu quloobahum li **l** ttaqwa lahum maghfiratun waajrun 'a _th_ eem **un**

# 4616

Inna allatheena yunadoonaka min warai alhujurati aktharuhum la ya'qiloon **a**

# 4617

Walaw annahum sabaroo hatta takhruja ilayhim lakana khayran lahum wa **A** llahu ghafoorun raheem **un**

# 4618

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo in jaakum fasiqun binabain fatabayyanoo an tuseeboo qawman bijahalatin fatusbihoo 'ala ma fa'atum nadimeen **a**

# 4619

Wa **i** 'lamoo anna feekum rasoola Allahi law yutee'ukum fee katheerin mina alamri la'anittum walakinna Allaha habbaba ilaykumu aleemana wazayyanahu fee quloobikum wakarraha ilaykumu alkufra wa **a** lfusooqa wa **a** l'isyana olaika humu a **l** rrashidoon **a**

# 4620

Fadlan mina Allahi wani'matan wa **A** llahu 'aleemun hakeem **un**

# 4621

Wain taifatani mina almumineena iqtataloo faaslihoo baynahuma fain baghat ihdahuma 'ala alokhra faqatiloo allatee tabghee hatta tafeea ila amri Allahi fain faat faaslihoo baynahuma bi **a** l'adli waaqsitoo inna Allaha yuhibbu almuqsiteen **a**

# 4622

Innama almuminoona ikhwatun faaslihoo bayna akhawaykum wa **i** ttaqoo Allaha la'allakum turhamoon **a**

# 4623

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la yaskhar qawmun min qawmin 'asa an yakoonoo khayran minhum wala nisaon min nisain 'asa an yakunna khayran minhunna wala talmizoo anfusakum wala tanabazoo bi **a** lalqabi bisa alismu alfusooqu ba'da aleemani waman lam yatub faolaika humu a **l** _thth_ alimoon **a**

# 4624

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo ijtaniboo katheeran mina a **l** _thth_ anni inna ba'da a **l** _thth_ anni ithmun wala tajassasoo wala yaghtab ba'dukum ba'dan ayuhibbu ahadukum an yakula lahma akheehi maytan fakarihtumoohu wa **i** ttaqoo Allaha inna Allaha tawwabun raheem **un**

# 4625

Ya ayyuha a **l** nnasu inna khalaqnakum min thakarin waontha waja'anakum shu'ooban waqabaila lita'arafoo inna akramakum 'inda Allahi atqakum inna Allaha 'aleemun khabeer **un**

# 4626

Qalati ala'rabu amanna qul lam tuminoo walakin qooloo aslamna walamma yadkhuli aleemanu fee quloobikum wain tutee'oo Allaha warasoolahu la yalitkum min a'malikum shayan inna Allaha ghafoorun raheem **un**

# 4627

Innama almuminoona allatheena amanoo bi **A** llahi warasoolihi thumma lam yartaboo wajahadoo biamwalihim waanfusihim fee sabeeli Allahi olaika humu a **l** ssadiqoon **a**

# 4628

Qul atu'allimoona Allaha bideenikum wa **A** llahu ya'lamu ma fee a **l** ssamawati wama fee alardi wa **A** llahu bikulli shayin 'aleem **un**

# 4629

# 4630

# 5079

Huwa allathee khalaqa a **l** ssamawati wa **a** larda fee sittati ayyamin thumma istawa 'ala al'arshi ya'lamu ma yaliju fee alardi wama yakhruju minha wama yanzilu mina a **l** ssamai wama ya'ruju feeha wahuwa ma'akum ayna ma kuntum wa **A** llahu bima ta'maloona baseer **un**

# 5082
