# 5083

Wama lakum la tuminoona bi **A** llahi wa **al** rrasoolu yad'ookum lituminoo birabbikum waqad akhatha meethaqakum in kuntum mumineen **a**

# 5084

Huwa allathee yunazzilu 'ala 'abdihi ayatin bayyinatin liyukhrijakum mina a **l** _thth_ ulumati ila a **l** nnoori wainna Allaha bikum laraoofun raheem **un**

# 5085

Wama lakum alla tunfiqoo fee sabeeli Allahi walillahi meerathu a **l** ssamawati wa **a** lardi la yastawee minkum man anfaqa min qabli alfathi waqatala olaika a' _th_ amu darajatan mina allatheena anfaqoo min ba'du waqataloo wakullan wa'ada Allahu alhusna wa **A** llahu bima ta'maloona khabeer **un**

# 5086

Man tha allathee yuqridu Allaha qardan hasanan fayuda'ifahu lahu walahu ajrun kareem **un**

# 5087

Yawma tara almumineena wa **a** lmuminati yas'a nooruhum bayna aydeehim wabiaymanihim bushrakumu alyawma jannatun tajree min tahtiha alanharu khalideena feehathalika huwa alfawzu al'a _th_ eem **u**

# 5088

Yawma yaqoolu almunafiqoona wa **a** lmunafiqatu lillatheena amanoo on _th_ uroona naqtabis min noorikum qeela irji'oo waraakum fa **i** ltamisoo nooran faduriba baynahum bisoorin lahu babun batinuhu feehi a **l** rrahmatu wa _th_ ahiruhu min qibalihi al'athab **u**

# 5089

Yunadoonahum alam nakun ma'akum qaloo bala walakinnakum fatantum anfusakum watarabbastum wa **i** rtabtum wagharratkumu alamaniyyu hatta jaa amru Allahi wagharrakum bi **A** llahi algharoor **u**

# 5090

Fa **a** lyawma la yukhathu minkum fidyatun wala mina allatheena kafaroo mawakumu a **l** nnaru hiya mawlakum wabisa almaseer **u**

# 5091

Alam yani lillatheena amanoo an takhsha'a quloobuhum lithikri Allahi wama nazala mina alhaqqi wala yakoonoo ka **a** llatheena ootoo alkitaba min qablu fatala 'alayhimu alamadu faqasat quloobuhum wakatheerun minhum fasiqoon **a**

# 5092

I'lamoo anna Allaha yuhyee alarda ba'da mawtiha qad bayyanna lakumu alayati la'allakum ta'qiloon **a**

# 5093

Inna almussaddiqeena wa **a** lmussaddiqati waaqradoo Allaha qardan hasanan yuda'afu lahum walahum ajrun kareem **un**

# 5094

Wa **a** llatheena amanoo bi **A** llahi warusulihi olaika humu a **l** ssiddeeqoona wa **al** shshuhadao 'inda rabbihim lahum ajruhum wanooruhum wa **a** llatheena kafaroo wakaththaboo biayatina olaika ashabu aljaheem **i**

# 5095

I'lamoo annama alhayatu a **l** ddunya la'ibun walahwun wazeenatun watafakhurun baynakum watakathurun fee alamwali wa **a** lawladi kamathali ghaythin a'jaba alkuffara nabatuhu thumma yaheeju fatarahu musfarran thumma yakoonu hutaman wafee alakhirati 'athabun shadeedun wamaghfiratun mina Allahi waridwanun wama alhayatu a **l** ddunya illa mata'u alghuroor **i**

# 5096

Sabiqoo ila maghfiratin min rabbikum wajannatin 'arduha ka'ardi a **l** ssamai wa **a** lardi o'iddat lillatheena amanoo bi **A** llahi warusulihi thalika fadlu Allahi yuteehi man yashao wa **A** llahu thoo alfadli al'a _th_ eem **i**

# 5097

Ma asaba min museebatin fee alardi wala fee anfusikum illa fee kitabin min qabli an nabraaha inna thalika 'ala Allahi yaseer **un**

# 5098

Likayla tasaw 'ala ma fatakum wala tafrahoo bimaatakum wa **A** llahu la yuhibbu kulla mukhtalin fakhoor **in**

# 5099

Allatheena yabkhaloona wayamuroona a **l** nnasa bi **a** lbukhli waman yatawalla fainna Allaha huwa alghaniyyu alhameed **u**

# 5100

Laqad arsana rusulana bi **a** lbayyinati waanzana ma'ahumu alkitaba wa **a** lmeezana liyaqooma a **l** nnasu bi **a** lqisti waanzana alhadeeda feehi basun shadeedun wamanafi'u li **l** nnasi waliya'lama Allahu man yansuruhu warusulahu bi **a** lghaybi inna Allaha qawiyyun 'azeez **un**

# 5101

Walaqad arsana noohan waibraheema waja'ana fee thurriyyatihima a **l** nnubuwwata wa **a** lkitaba faminhum muhtadin wakatheerun minhum fasiqoon **a**

# 5102

Thumma qaffayna 'alaatharihim birusulina waqaffayna bi'eesa ibni maryama waataynahu alinjeela waja'ana fee quloobi allatheena ittaba'oohu rafatan warahmatan warahbaniyyatan ibtada'ooha ma katabnaha 'alayhim illa ibtighaa ridwani Allahi fama ra'awhahaqqa ri'ayatiha faatayna allatheena amanoo minhum ajrahum wakatheerun minhum fasiqoon **a**

# 5103

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo ittaqoo Allaha waaminoo birasoolihi yutikum kiflayni min rahmatihi wayaj'al lakum nooran tamshoona bihi wayaghfir lakum wa **A** llahu ghafoorun raheem **un**

# 5104

Lialla ya'lama ahlu alkitabi alla yaqdiroona 'ala shayin min fadli Allahi waanna alfadla biyadi Allahi yuteehi man yashao wa **A** llahu thoo alfadli al'a _th_ eem **i**

# 5105

Qad sami'a Allahu qawla allatee tujadiluka fee zawjiha watashtakee ila Allahi wa **A** llahu yasma'u tahawurakuma inna Allaha samee'un baseer **un**

# 5106

Allatheena yu _th_ ahiroona minkum min nisaihim ma hunna ommahatihim in ommahatuhum illa allaee waladnahum wainnahum layaqooloona munkaran mina alqawli wazooran wainna Allaha la'afuwwun ghafoor **un**

# 5107

Wa **a** llatheena yu _th_ ahiroona min nisaihim thumma ya'oodoona lima qaloo fatahreeru raqabatin min qabli an yatamassathalikum too'a _th_ oona bihi wa **A** llahu bima ta'maloona khabeer **un**

# 5108

Faman lam yajid fasiyamu shahrayni mutatabi'ayni min qabli an yatamassa faman lam yastati' fait'amu sitteena miskeenan thalika lituminoo bi **A** llahi warasoolihi watilka hudoodu Allahi walilkafireena 'athabun aleem **un**

# 5109

Inna allatheena yuhaddoona Allaha warasoolahu kubitoo kama kubita allatheena min qablihim waqad anzanaayatin bayyinatin walilkafireena 'athabun muheen **un**

# 5110

Yawma yab'athuhumu Allahu jamee'an fayunabbiohum bima 'amiloo ahsahu Allahu wanasoohu wa **A** llahu 'ala kulli shayin shaheed **un**

# 5111

Alam tara anna Allaha ya'lamu ma fee a **l** ssamawati wama fee alardi ma yakoonu min najwa thalathatin illa huwa rabi'uhum wala khamsatin illa huwa sadisuhum wala adna min thalika wala akthara illa huwa ma'ahum ayna ma kanoo thumma yunabbiohum bima 'amiloo yawma alqiyamati inna Allaha bikulli shayin 'aleem **un**

# 5112

Alam tara ila allatheena nuhoo 'ani a **l** nnajwa thumma ya'oodoona lima nuhoo 'anhu wayatanajawna bi **a** lithmi wa **a** l'udwani wama'siyati a **l** rrasooli waitha jaooka hayyawka bima lam yuhayyika bihi Allahu wayaqooloona fee anfusihim lawla yu'aththibuna Allahu bima naqoolu hasbuhum jahannamu yaslawnaha fabisa almaseer **u**

# 5113

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo itha tanajaytum fala tatanajaw bi **a** lithmi wa **a** l'udwani wama'siyati a **l** rrasooli watanajaw bi **a** lbirri wa **al** ttaqwa wa **i** ttaqoo Allaha allathee ilayhi tuhsharoon **a**

# 5114

Innama a **l** nnajwa mina a **l** shshaytani liyahzuna allatheena amanoo walaysa bidarrihim shayan illa biithni Allahi wa'ala Allahi falyatawakkali almuminoon **a**

# 5115

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo itha qeela lakum tafassahoo fee almajalisi fa **i** fsahoo yafsahi Allahu lakum waitha qeela onshuzoo fa **o** nshuzoo yarfa'i Allahu allatheena amanoo minkum wa **a** llatheena ootoo al'ilma darajatin wa **A** llahu bima ta'maloona khabeer **un**

# 5116

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo itha najaytumu a **l** rrasoola faqaddimoo bayna yaday najwakum sadaqatan thalika khayrun lakum waatharu fain lam tajidoo fainna Allaha ghafoorun raheem **un**

# 5117

Aashfaqtum an tuqaddimoo bayna yaday najwakum sadaqatin faith lam taf'aloo wataba Allahu 'alaykum faaqeemoo a **l** ssalata waatoo a **l** zzakata waatee'oo Allaha warasoolahu wa **A** llahu khabeerun bima ta'maloon **a**

# 5118

Alam tara ila allatheena tawallaw qawman ghadiba Allahu 'alayhim ma hum minkum wala minhum wayahlifoona 'ala alkathibi wahum ya'lamoon **a**

# 5119

a'adda Allahu lahum 'athaban shadeedan innahum saa ma kanoo ya'maloon **a**

# 5120

Ittakhathoo aymanahum junnatan fasaddoo 'an sabeeli Allahi falahum 'athabun muheen **un**

# 5121

Lan tughniya 'anhum amwaluhum wala awladuhum mina Allahi shayan olaika ashabu a **l** nnari hum feeha khalidoon **a**

# 5122

Yawma yab'athuhumu Allahu jamee'an fayahlifoona lahu kama yahlifoona lakum wayahsaboona annahum 'ala shayin ala innahum humu alkathiboon **a**

# 5123

Istahwatha 'alayhimu a **l** shshaytanu faansahum thikra Allahi olaika hizbu a **l** shshaytani ala inna hizba a **l** shshaytani humu alkhasiroon **a**

# 5124

Inna allatheena yuhaddoona Allaha warasoolahu olaika fee alathalleen **a**

# 5125

Kataba Allahu laaghlibanna ana warusulee inna Allaha qawiyyun 'azeez **un**

# 5126

La tajidu qawman yuminoona bi **A** llahi wa **a** lyawmi alakhiri yuwaddoona man hadda Allaha warasoolahu walaw kanoo abaahum aw abnaahum aw ikhwanahum aw 'asheeratahum olaika kataba fee quloobihimu aleemana waayyadahum biroohin minhu wayudkhiluhum jannatin tajree min tahtiha alanharu khalideena feeha radiya Allahu 'anhum waradoo 'anhu olaika hizbu Allahi ala inna hizba Allahi humu almuflihoon **a**

# 5127

Sabbaha lillahi ma fee a **l** ssamawati wama fee alardi wahuwa al'azeezu alhakeem **u**

# 5128

Huwa allathee akhraja allatheena kafaroo min ahli alkitabi min diyarihim liawwali alhashri ma _th_ anantum an yakhrujoo wa _th_ annoo annahum mani'atuhum husoonuhum mina Allahi faatahumu Allahu min haythu lam yahtasiboo waqathafa fee quloobihimu a **l** rru'ba yukhriboona buyootahum biaydeehim waaydee almumineena fa **i** 'tabiroo ya olee alabsar **i**

# 5129

Walawla an kataba Allahu 'alayhimu aljalaa la'aththabahum fee a **l** ddunya walahum fee alakhirati 'athabu a **l** nnar **i**

# 5130

Thalika biannahum shaqqoo Allaha warasoolahu waman yushaqqi Allaha fainna Allaha shadeedu al'iqab **i**

# 5131

Ma qata'tum min leenatin aw taraktumooha qaimatan 'ala osooliha fabiithni Allahi waliyukhziya alfasiqeen **a**

# 5132

Wama afaa Allahu 'ala rasoolihi minhum fama awjaftum 'alayhi min khaylin wala rikabin walakinna Allaha yusallitu rusulahu 'ala man yashao wa **A** llahu 'ala kulli shayin qadeer **un**

# 5133

Ma afaa Allahu 'ala rasoolihi min ahli alqura falillahi wali **l** rrasooli walithee alqurba wa **a** lyatama wa **a** lmasakeeni wa **i** bni a **l** ssabeeli kay la yakoona doolatan bayna alaghniyai minkum wamaatakumu a **l** rrasoolu fakhuthoohu wama nahakum 'anhu fa **i** ntahoo wa **i** ttaqoo Allaha inna Allaha shadeedu al'iqab **i**

# 5134

Lilfuqarai almuhajireena allatheena okhrijoo min diyarihim waamwalihim yabtaghoona fadlan mina Allahi waridwanan wayansuroona Allaha warasoolahu olaika humu a **l** ssadiqoon **a**

# 5135

Wa **a** llatheena tabawwaoo a **l** ddara wa **a** leemana min qablihim yuhibboona man hajara ilayhim wala yajidoona fee sudoorihim hajatan mimma ootoo wayuthiroona 'ala anfusihim walaw kana bihim khasasatun waman yooqa shuhha nafsihi faolaika humu almuflihoon **a**

# 5136

Wa **a** llatheena jaoo min ba'dihim yaqooloona rabbana ighfir lana waliikhwanina allatheena sabaqoona bi **a** leemani wala taj'al fee quloobina ghillan lillatheena amanoo rabbana innaka raoofun raheem **un**

# 5137

Alam tara ila allatheena nafaqoo yaqooloona liikhwanihimu allatheena kafaroo min ahli alkitabi lain okhrijtum lanakhrujanna ma'akum wala nutee'u feekum ahadan abadan wain qootiltum lanansurannakum wa **A** llahu yashhadu innahum lakathiboon **a**

# 5138

Lain okhrijoo la yakhrujoona ma'ahum walain qootiloo la yansuroonahum walain nasaroohum layuwallunna aladbara thumma la yunsaroon **a**

# 5139

Laantum ashaddu rahbatan fee sudoorihim mina Allahi thalika biannahum qawmun la yafqahoon **a**

# 5140

La yuqatiloonakum jamee'an illa fee quran muhassanatin aw min warai judurin basuhum baynahum shadeedun tahsabuhum jamee'an waquloobuhum shattathalika biannahum qawmun la ya'qiloon **a**

# 5141

Kamathali allatheena min qablihim qareeban thaqoo wabala amrihim walahum 'athabun aleem **un**

# 5142

Kamathali a **l** shshaytani ith qala lilinsani okfur falamma kafara qala innee bareeon minka innee akhafu Allaha rabba al'alameen **a**

# 5143

Fakana 'aqibatahuma annahuma fee a **l** nnari khalidayni feeha wathalika jazao a **l** _thth_ alimeen **a**

# 5144

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo ittaqoo Allaha watan _th_ ur nafsun ma qaddamat lighadin wa **i** ttaqoo Allaha inna Allaha khabeerun bima ta'maloon **a**

# 5145

Wala takoonoo ka **a** llatheena nasoo Allaha faansahum anfusahum olaika humu alfasiqoon **a**

# 5146

La yastawee ashabu a **l** nnari waashabu aljannati ashabu aljannati humu alfaizoon **a**

# 5147

Law anzana hatha alqurana 'ala jabalin laraaytahu khashi'an mutasaddi'an min khashyati Allahi watilka alamthalu nadribuha li **l** nnasi la'allahum yatafakkaroon **a**

# 5148

Huwa Allahu allathee la ilaha illa huwa 'alimu alghaybi wa **al** shshahadati huwa a **l** rrahmanu a **l** rraheem **u**

# 5149

Huwa Allahu allathee la ilaha illa huwa almaliku alquddoosu a **l** ssalamu almuminu almuhayminu al'azeezu aljabbaru almutakabbiru subhana Allahi 'amma yushrikoon **a**

# 5150

Huwa Allahu alkhaliqu albario almusawwiru lahu alasmao alhusna yusabbihu lahu ma fee a **l** ssamawati wa **a** lardi wahuwa al'azeezu alhakeem **u**

# 5151

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la tattakhithoo 'aduwwee wa'aduwwakum awliyaa tulqoona ilayhim bi **a** lmawaddati waqad kafaroo bima jaakum mina alhaqqi yukhrijoona a **l** rrasoola waiyyakum an tuminoo bi **A** llahi rabbikum in kuntum kharajtum jihadan fee sabeelee wa **i** btighaa mardatee tusirroona ilayhim bi **a** lmawaddati waana a'lamu bima akhfaytum wama a'lantum waman yaf'alhu minkum faqad dalla sawaa a **l** ssabeel **i**

# 5152

In yathqafookum yakoonoo lakam a'daan wayabsutoo ilaykum aydiyahum waasinatahum bi **al** ssooi wawaddoo law takfuroon **a**

# 5153

Lan tanfa'akum arhamukum wala awladukum yawma alqiyamati yafsilu baynakum wa **A** llahu bima ta'maloona baseer **un**

# 5154

Qad kanat lakum oswatun hasanatun fee ibraheema wa **a** llatheena ma'ahu ith qaloo liqawmihim inna buraao minkum wamimma ta'budoona min dooni Allahi kafarna bikum wabada baynana wabaynakumu al'adawatu wa **a** lbaghdao abadan hatta tuminoo bi **A** llahi wahdahu illa qawla ibraheema liabeehi laastaghfiranna laka wama amliku laka mina Allahi min shayin rabbana 'alayka tawakkana wailayka anabna wailayka almaseer **u**

# 5155

Rabbana la taj'ana fitnatan lillatheena kafaroo wa **i** ghfir lana rabbana innaka anta al'azeezu alhakeem **u**

# 5156

Laqad kana lakum feehim oswatun hasanatun liman kana yarjoo Allaha wa **a** lyawma alakhira waman yatawalla fainna Allaha huwa alghanniyyu alhameed **u**

# 5157

'asa Allahu an yaj'ala baynakum wabayna allatheena 'adaytum minhum mawaddatan wa **A** llahu qadeerun wa **A** llahu ghafoorun raheem **un**

# 5158

La yanhakumu Allahu 'ani allatheena lam yuqatilookum fee a **l** ddeeni walam yukhrijookum min diyarikum an tabarroohum watuqsitoo ilayhim inna Allaha yuhibbu almuqsiteen **a**

# 5159

Innama yanhakumu Allahu 'ani allatheena qatalookum fee a **l** ddeeni waakhrajookum min diyarikum wa _th_ aharoo 'ala ikhrajikum an tawallawhum waman yatawallahum faolaika humu a **l** _thth_ alimoon **a**

# 5160

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo itha jaakumu almuminatu muhajiratin fa **i** mtahinoohunna Allahu a'lamu bieemanihinna fain 'alimtumoohunna muminatin fala tarji'oohunna ila alkuffari la hunna hillun lahum wala hum yahilloona lahunna waatoohum ma anfaqoo wala junaha 'alaykum an tankihoohunna ithaataytumoohunna ojoorahunna wala tumsikoo bi'isami alkawafiri wa **i** saloo ma anfaqtum walyasaloo ma anfaqoo thalikum hukmu Allahi yahkumu baynakum wa **A** llahu 'aleemun hakeem **un**

# 5161

Wain fatakum shayon min azwajikum ila alkuffari fa'aqabtum faatoo allatheena thahabat azwajuhum mithla ma anfaqoo wa **i** ttaqoo Allaha allathee antum bihi muminoon **a**

# 5162

Ya ayyuha a **l** nnabiyyu itha jaaka almuminatu yubayi'naka 'ala an la yushrikna bi **A** llahi shayan wala yasriqna wala yazneena wala yaqtulna awladahunna wala yateena bibuhtanin yaftareenahu bayna aydeehinna waarjulihinna wala ya'seenaka fee ma'roofin fabayi'hunna wa **i** staghfir lahunna Allaha inna Allaha ghafoorun raheem **un**

# 5163

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la tatawallaw qawman ghadiba Allahu 'alayhim qad yaisoo mina alakhirati kama yaisa alkuffaru min ashabi alquboor **i**

# 5164

Sabbaha lillahi ma fee a **l** ssamawati wama fee alardi wahuwa al'azeezu alhakeem **u**

# 5165

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo lima taqooloona ma la taf'aloon **a**

# 5166

Kabura maqtan 'inda Allahi an taqooloo ma la taf'aloon **a**

# 5167

Inna Allaha yuhibbu allatheena yuqatiloona fee sabeelihi saffan kaannahum bunyanun marsoos **un**

# 5168

Waith qala moosa liqawmihi ya qawmi lima tuthoonanee waqad ta'lamoona annee rasoolu Allahi ilaykum falamma zaghoo azagha Allahu quloobahum wa **A** llahu la yahdee alqawma alfasiqeen **a**

# 5169

Waith qala 'eesa ibnu maryama ya banee israeela innee rasoolu Allahi ilaykum musaddiqan lima bayna yadayya mina a **l** ttawrati wamubashshiran birasoolin yatee min ba'dee ismuhu ahmadu falamma jaahum bi **a** lbayyinati qaloo hatha sihrun mubeen **un**

# 5170

Waman a _th_ lamu mimmani iftara 'ala Allahi alkathiba wahuwa yud'a ila alislami wa **A** llahu la yahdee alqawma a **l** _thth_ alimeen **a**

# 5171

Yureedoona liyutfioo noora Allahi biafwahihim wa **A** llahu mutimmu noorihi walaw kariha alkafiroon **a**

# 5172

Huwa allathee arsala rasoolahu bi **a** lhuda wadeeni alhaqqi liyu _th_ hirahu 'ala a **l** ddeeni kullihi walaw kariha almushrikoon **a**

# 5173

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo hal adullukum 'ala tijaratin tunjeekum min 'athabin aleem **in**

# 5174

Tuminoona bi **A** llahi warasoolihi watujahidoona fee sabeeli Allahi biamwalikum waanfusikum thalikum khayrun lakum in kuntum ta'lamoon **a**

# 5175

Yaghfir lakum thunoobakum wayudkhilkum jannatin tajree min tahtiha alanharu wamasakina tayyibatan fee jannati 'adnin thalika alfawzu al'a _th_ eem **u**

# 5176

Waokhra tuhibboonaha nasrun mina Allahi wafathun qarreebun wabashshiri almumineen **a**

# 5177

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo koonoo ansara Allahi kama qala 'eesa ibnu maryama lilhawariyyeena man ansaree ila Allahi qala alhawariyyoona nahnu ansaru Allahi faamanat taifatun min banee israeela wakafarat taifatun faayyadna allatheena amanoo 'ala 'aduwwihim faasbahoo _th_ ahireen **a**

# 5178

Yusabbihu lillahi ma fee a **l** ssamawati wama fee alardi almaliki alquddoosi al'azeezi alhakeem **i**

# 5179

Huwa allathee ba'atha fee alommiyyeena rasoolan minhum yatloo 'alayhim ayatihi wayuzakkeehim wayu'allimuhumu alkitaba wa **a** lhikmata wain kanoo min qablu lafee dalalin mubeen **in**

# 5180

Waakhareena minhum lamma yalhaqoo bihim wahuwa al'azeezu alhakeem **u**

# 5181

Thalika fadlu Allahi yuteehi man yashao wa **A** llahu thoo alfadli al'a _th_ eem **i**

# 5182

Mathalu allatheena hummiloo a **l** ttawrata thumma lam yahmilooha kamathali alhimari yahmilu asfaran bisa mathalu alqawmi allatheena kaththaboo biayati Allahi wa **A** llahu la yahdee alqawma a **l** _thth_ alimeen **a**

# 5183

Qul ya ayyuha allatheena hadoo in za'amtum annakum awliyao lillahi min dooni a **l** nnasi fatamannawoo almawta in kuntum sadiqeen **a**

# 5184

Wala yatamannawnahu abadan bima qaddamat aydeehim wa **A** llahu 'aleemun bi **al** _thth_ alimeen **a**

# 5185

Qul inna almawta allathee tafirroona minhu fainnahu mulaqeekum thumma turaddoona ila 'alimi alghaybi wa **al** shshahadati fayunabbiokum bima kuntum ta'maloon **a**

# 5186

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo itha noodiya li **l** ssalati min yawmi aljumu'ati fa **i** s'aw ilathikri Allahi watharoo albay'a thalikum khayrun lakum in kuntum ta'lamoon **a**

# 5187

Faitha qudiyati a **l** ssalatu fa **i** ntashiroo fee alardi wa **i** btaghoo min fadli Allahi wa **o** thkuroo Allaha katheeran la'allakum tuflihoon **a**

# 5188

Waitha raaw tijaratan aw lahwan infaddoo ilayha watarakooka qaiman qul ma 'inda Allahi khayrun mina allahwi wamina a **l** ttijarati wa **A** llahu khayru a **l** rraziqeen **a**

# 5189

Itha jaaka almunafiqoona qaloo nashhadu innaka larasoolu Allahi wa **A** llahu ya'lamu innaka larasooluhu wa **A** llahu yashhadu inna almunafiqeena lakathiboon **a**

# 5190

Ittakhathoo aymanahum junnatan fasaddoo 'an sabeeli Allahi innahum saa ma kanoo ya'maloon **a**

# 5191

Thalika biannahum amanoo thumma kafaroo fatubi'a 'ala quloobihim fahum la yafqahoon **a**

# 5192

Waitha raaytahum tu'jibuka ajsamuhum wain yaqooloo tasma' liqawlihim kaannahum khushubun musannadatun yahsaboona kulla sayhatin 'alayhim humu al'aduwwu fa **i** htharhum qatalahumu Allahu anna yufakoon **a**

# 5193

Waitha qeela lahum ta'alaw yastaghfir lakum rasoolu Allahi lawwaw ruoosahum waraaytahum yasuddoona wahum mustakbiroon **a**

# 5194

Sawaon 'alayhim astaghfarta lahum am lam tastaghfir lahum lan yaghfira Allahu lahum inna Allaha la yahdee alqawma alfasiqeen **a**

# 5195

Humu allatheena yaqooloona la tunfiqoo 'ala man 'inda rasooli Allahi hatta yanfaddoo walillahi khazainu a **l** ssamawati wa **a** lardi walakinna almunafiqeena la yafqahoon **a**

# 5196

Yaqooloona lain raja'na ila almadeenati layukhrijanna ala'azzu minha alathalla walillahi al'izzatu walirasoolihi walilmumineena walakinna almunafiqeena la ya'lamoon **a**

# 5197

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la tulhikum amwalukum wala awladukum 'an thikri Allahi waman yaf'al thalika faolaika humu alkhasiroon **a**

# 5198

Waanfiqoo min ma razaqnakum min qabli an yatiya ahadakumu almawtu fayaqoola rabbi lawla akhkhartanee ila ajalin qareebin faassaddaqa waakun mina a **l** ssaliheen **a**

# 5199

Walan yuakhkhira Allahu nafsan itha jaa ajaluha wa **A** llahu khabeerun bima ta'maloon **a**

# 5200

Yusabbihu lillahi ma fee a **l** ssamawati wama fee alardi lahu almulku walahu alhamdu wahuwa 'ala kulli shayin qadeer **un**

# 5201

Huwa allathee khalaqakum faminkum kafirun waminkum muminun wa **A** llahu bima ta'maloona baseer **un**

# 5202

Khalaqa a **l** ssamawati wa **a** larda bi **a** lhaqqi wasawwarakum faahsana suwarakum wailayhi almaseer **u**

# 5203

Ya'lamu ma fee a **l** ssamawati wa **a** lardi waya'lamu ma tusirroona wama tu'linoona wa **A** llahu 'aleemun bithati a **l** ssudoor **i**

# 5204

Alam yatikum nabao allatheena kafaroo min qablu fathaqoo wabala amrihim walahum 'athabun aleem **un**

# 5205

Thalika biannahu kanat tateehim rusuluhum bi **a** lbayyinati faqaloo abasharun yahdoonana fakafaroo watawallaw wa **i** staghna Allahu wa **A** llahu ghaniyyun hameed **un**

# 5206

Za'ama allatheena kafaroo an lan yub'athoo qul bala warabbee latub'athunna thumma latunabbaonna bima 'amiltum wathalika 'ala Allahi yaseer **un**

# 5207

Faaminoo bi **A** llahi warasoolihi wa **al** nnoori allathee anzana wa **A** llahu bima ta'maloona khabeer **un**

# 5208

Yawma yajma'ukum liyawmi aljam'i thalika yawmu a **l** ttaghabuni waman yumin bi **A** llahi waya'mal salihan yukaffir 'anhu sayyiatihi wayudkhilhu jannatin tajree min tahtiha alanharu khalideena feeha abadan thalika alfawzu al'a _th_ eem **u**

# 5209

Wa **a** llatheena kafaroo wakaththaboo biayatina olaika ashabu a **l** nnari khalideena feeha wabisa almaseer **u**

# 5210

Ma asaba min museebatin illa biithni Allahi waman yumin bi **A** llahi yahdi qalbahu wa **A** llahu bikulli shayin 'aleem **un**

# 5211

Waatee'oo Allaha waatee'oo a **l** rrasoola fain tawallaytum fainnama 'ala rasoolina albalaghu almubeen **u**

# 5212

Allahu la ilaha illa huwa wa'ala Allahi falyatawakkali almuminoon **a**

# 5213

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo inna min azwajikum waawladikum 'aduwwan lakum fa **i** htharoohum wain ta'foo watasfahoo wataghfiroo fainna Allaha ghafoorun raheem **un**

# 5214

Innama amwalukum waawladukum fitnatun wa **A** llahu 'indahu ajrun 'a _th_ eem **un**

# 5215

Fa **i** ttaqoo Allaha ma istata'tum wa **i** sma'oo waatee'oo waanfiqoo khayran lianfusikum waman yooqa shuhha nafsihi faolaika humu almuflihoon **a**

# 5216

In tuqridoo Allaha qardan hasanan yuda'ifhu lakum wayaghfir lakum wa **A** llahu shakoorun haleem **un**

# 5217

'alimu alghaybi wa **al** shshahadati al'azeezu alhakeem **u**

# 5218

Ya ayyuha a **l** nnabiyyu ithatallaqtumu a **l** nnisaa fatalliqoohunna li'iddatihinna waahsoo al'iddata wa **i** ttaqoo Allaha rabbakum la tukhrijoohunna min buyootihinna wala yakhrujna illa an yateena bifahishatin mubayyinatin watilka hudoodu Allahi waman yata'adda hudooda Allahi faqad _th_ alama nafsahu la tadree la'alla Allaha yuhdithu ba'da thalika amra **n**

# 5219

Faitha balaghna ajalahunna faamsikoohunna bima'roofin aw fariqoohunna bima'roofin waashhidoo thaway 'adlin minkum waaqeemoo a **l** shshahadata lillahi thalikum yoo'a _th_ u bihi man kana yuminu bi **A** llahi wa **a** lyawmi alakhiri waman yattaqi Allaha yaj'al lahu makhraja **n**

# 5220

Wayarzuqhu min haythu la yahtasibu waman yatawakkal 'ala Allahi fahuwa hasbuhu inna Allaha balighu amrihi qad ja'ala Allahu likulli shayin qadra **n**

# 5221

Wa **a** llaee yaisna mina almaheedi min nisaikum ini irtabtum fa'iddatuhunna thalathatu ashhurin wa **a** llaee lam yahidna waolatu alahmali ajaluhunna an yada'na hamlahunna waman yattaqi Allaha yaj'al lahu min amrihi yusra **n**

# 5222

Thalika amru Allahi anzalahu ilaykum waman yattaqi Allaha yukaffir 'anhu sayyiatihi wayu' _th_ im lahu ajra **n**

# 5223

Askinoohunna min haythu sakantum min wujdikum wala tudarroohunna litudayyiqoo 'alayhinna wain kunna olati hamlin faanfiqoo 'alayhinna hatta yada'na hamlahunna fain arda'na lakum faatoohunna ojoorahunna watamiroo baynakum bima'roofin wain ta'asartum fasaturdi'u lahu okhra

# 5224

Liyunfiq thoo sa'atin min sa'atihi waman qudira 'alayhi rizquhu falyunfiq mimmaatahu Allahu la yukallifu Allahu nafsan illa maataha sayaj'alu Allahu ba'da 'usrin yusra **n**

# 5225

Wakaayyin min qaryatin 'atat 'an amri rabbiha warusulihi fahasabnahahisaban shadeedan wa'aththabnaha 'athaban nukra **n**

# 5226

Fathaqat wabala amriha wakana 'aqibatu amriha khusra **n**

# 5227

a'adda Allahu lahum 'athaban shadeedan fa **i** ttaqoo Allaha ya olee alalbabi allatheena amanoo qad anzala Allahu ilaykum thikra **n**

# 5228

Rasoolan yatloo 'alaykum ayati Allahi mubayyinatin liyukhrija allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo a **l** ssalihati mina a **l** _thth_ ulumati ila a **l** nnoori waman yumin bi **A** llahi waya'mal salihan yudkhilhu jannatin tajree min tahtiha alanharu khalideena feeha abadan qad ahsana Allahu lahu rizqa **n**

# 5229

Allahu allathee khalaqa sab'a samawatin wamina alardi mithlahunna yatanazzalu alamru baynahunna lita'lamoo anna Allaha 'ala kulli shayin qadeerun waanna Allaha qad ahata bikulli shayin 'ilma **n**

# 5230

Ya ayyuha a **l** nnabiyyu lima tuharrimu ma ahalla Allahu laka tabtaghee mardata azwajika wa **A** llahu ghafoorun raheem **un**

# 5231

Qad farada Allahu lakum tahillata aymanikum wa **A** llahu mawlakum wahuwa al'aleemu alhakeem **u**

# 5232

Waith asarra a **l** nnabiyyu ila ba'di azwajihi hadeethan falamma nabbaat bihi waa _th_ harahu Allahu 'alayhi 'arrafa ba'dahu waa'rada 'an ba'din falamma nabbaaha bihi qalat man anbaaka hatha qala nabbaaniya al'aleemu alkhabeer **u**

# 5233

In tatooba ila Allahi faqad saghat quloobukuma wain ta _th_ ahara 'alayhi fainna Allaha huwa mawlahu wajibreelu wasalihu almumineena wa **a** lmalaikatu ba'da thalika _th_ aheer **un**

# 5234

'asa rabbuhu in tallaqakunna an yubdilahu azwajan khayran minkunna muslimatin muminatin qanitatin taibatin 'abidatin saihatin thayyibatin waabkara **n**

# 5235

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo qoo anfusakum waahleekum naran waqooduha a **l** nnasu wa **a** lhijaratu 'alayha malaikatun ghila _th_ un shidadun la ya'soona Allaha ma amarahum wayaf'aloona ma yumaroon **a**

# 5236

Ya ayyuha allatheena kafaroo la ta'tathiroo alyawma innama tujzawna ma kuntum ta'maloon **a**

# 5237

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo tooboo ila Allahi tawbatan nasoohan 'asa rabbukum an yukaffira 'ankum sayyiatikum wayudkhilakum jannatin tajree min tahtiha alanharu yawma la yukhzee Allahu a **l** nnabiyya wa **a** llatheena amanoo ma'ahu nooruhum yas'a bayna aydeehim wabiaymanihim yaqooloona rabbana atmim lana noorana wa **i** ghfir lana innaka 'ala kulli shayin qadeer **un**

# 5238

Ya ayyuha a **l** nnabiyyu jahidi alkuffara wa **a** lmunafiqeena wa **o** ghlu _th_ 'alayhim wamawahum jahannamu wabisa almaseer **u**

# 5239

Daraba Allahu mathalan lillatheena kafaroo imraata noohin wa **i** mraata lootin kanata tahta 'abdayni min 'ibadinasalihayni fakhanatahuma falam yughniya 'anhuma mina Allahi shayan waqeela odkhula a **l** nnara ma'a a **l** ddakhileen **a**

# 5240

Wadaraba Allahu mathalan lillatheena amanoo imraata fir'awna ith qalat rabbi ibni lee 'indaka baytan fee aljannati wanajjinee min fir'awna wa'amalihi wanajjinee mina alqawmi a **l** _thth_ alimeen **a**

# 5241

Wamaryama ibnata 'imrana allatee ahsanat farjaha fanafakhna feehi min roohina wasaddaqat bikalimati rabbiha wakutubihi wakanat mina alqaniteen **a**

# 5242

Tabaraka allathee biyadihi almulku wahuwa 'ala kulli shayin qadeer **un**

# 5243

Allathee khalaqa almawta wa **a** lhayata liyabluwakum ayyukum ahsanu 'amalan wahuwa al'azeezu alghafoor **u**

# 5244

Allathee khalaqa sab'a samawatin tibaqan ma tara fee khalqi a **l** rrahmani min tafawutin fa **i** rji'i albasara hal tara min futoor **in**

# 5245

Thumma irji'i albasara karratayni yanqalib ilayka albasaru khasian wahuwa haseer **un**

# 5246

Walaqad zayyanna a **l** ssamaa a **l** ddunya bimasabeeha waja'anaha rujooman li **l** shshayateeni waa'tadna lahum 'athaba a **l** ssa'eer **i**

# 5247

Walillatheena kafaroo birabbihim 'athabu jahannama wabisa almaseer **u**

# 5248

Itha olqoo feeha sami'oo laha shaheeqan wahiya tafoor **u**

# 5249

Takadu tamayyazu mina alghay _th_ i kullama olqiya feeha fawjun saalahum khazanatuha alam yatikum natheer **un**

# 5250

Qaloo bala qad jaana natheerun fakaththabna waqulna ma nazzala Allahu min shayin in antum illa fee dalalin kabeer **in**

# 5251

Waqaloo law kunna nasma'u aw na'qilu ma kunna fee ashabi a **l** ssa'eer **i**

# 5252

Fa **i** 'tarafoo bithanbihim fasuhqan liashabi a **l** ssa'eer **i**

# 5253

Inna allatheena yakhshawna rabbahum bi **a** lghaybi lahum maghfiratun waajrun kabeer **un**

# 5254

Waasirroo qawlakum awi ijharoo bihi innahu 'aleemun bithati a **l** ssudoor **i**

# 5255

Ala ya'lamu man khalaqa wahuwa allateefu alkhabeer **u**

# 5256

Huwa allathee ja'ala lakumu alarda thaloolan fa **i** mshoo fee manakibiha wakuloo min rizqihi wailayhi a **l** nnushoor **u**

# 5257

Aamintum man fee a **l** ssamai an yakhsifa bikumu alarda faitha hiya tamoor **u**

# 5258

Am amintum man fee a **l** ssamai an yursila 'alaykum hasiban fasata'lamoona kayfa natheer **i**

# 5259

Walaqad kaththaba allatheena min qablihim fakayfa kana nakeer **i**

# 5260

Awalam yaraw ila a **l** ttayri fawqahum saffatin wayaqbidna ma yumsikuhunna illa a **l** rrahmanu innahu bikulli shayin baseer **un**

# 5261

Amman hatha allathee huwa jundun lakum yansurukum min dooni a **l** rrahmani ini alkafiroona illa fee ghuroor **in**

# 5262

Amman hatha allathee yarzuqukum in amsaka rizqahu bal lajjoo fee 'utuwwin wanufoor **in**

# 5263

Afaman yamshee mukibban 'ala wajhihi ahda amman yamshee sawiyyan 'alasiratin mustaqeem **in**

# 5264

Qul huwa allathee anshaakum waja'ala lakumu a **l** ssam'a wa **a** labsara wa **a** lafidata qaleelan ma tashkuroon **a**

# 5265

Qul huwa allathee tharaakum fee alardi wailayhi tuhsharoon **a**

# 5266

Wayaqooloona mata hatha alwa'du in kuntum sadiqeen **a**

# 5267

Qul innama al'ilmu 'inda Allahi wainnama ana natheerun mubeen **un**

# 5268

Falamma raawhu zulfatan seeat wujoohu allatheena kafaroo waqeela hatha allathee kuntum bihi tadda'oon **a**

# 5269

Qul araaytum in ahlakaniya Allahu waman ma'iya aw rahimana faman yujeeru alkafireena min 'athabin aleem **in**

# 5270

Qul huwa a **l** rrahmanu amanna bihi wa'alayhi tawakkana fasata'lamoona man huwa fee dalalin mubeen **in**

# 5271

Qul araaytum in asbaha maokum ghawran faman yateekum bimain ma'een **in**

# 5272

Noon wa **a** lqalami wama yasturoon **a**

# 5273

Ma anta bini'mati rabbika bimajnoon **in**

# 5274

Wainna laka laajran ghayra mamnoon **in**

# 5275

Wainnaka la'ala khuluqin 'a _th_ eem **in**

# 5276

Fasatubsiru wayubsiroon **a**

# 5277

Biayyikumu almaftoon **u**

# 5278

Inna rabbaka huwa a'lamu biman dalla 'an sabeelihi wahuwa a'lamu bi **a** lmuhtadeen **a**

# 5279

Fala tuti'i almukaththibeen **a**

# 5280

Waddoo law tudhinu fayudhinoon **a**

# 5281

Wala tuti' kulla hallafin maheen **in**

# 5282

Hammazin mashshain binameem **in**

# 5283

Manna'in lilkhayri mu'tadin atheem **in**

# 5284

'utullin ba'da thalika zaneem **in**

# 5285

An kana tha malin wabaneen **a**

# 5286

Itha tutla 'alayhi ayatuna qala asateeru alawwaleen **a**

# 5287

Sanasimuhu 'ala alkhurtoom **i**

# 5288

Inna balawnahum kama balawna ashaba aljannati ith aqsamoo layasrimunnaha musbiheen **a**

# 5289

Wala yastathnoon **a**

# 5290

Fatafa 'alayhataifun min rabbika wahum naimoon **a**

# 5291

Faasbahat ka **al** ssareem **i**

# 5292

Fatanadaw musbiheen **a**

# 5293

Ani ighdoo 'alaharthikum in kuntum sarimeen **a**

# 5294

Fa **i** ntalaqoo wahum yatakhafatoon **a**

# 5295

An la yadkhulannaha alyawma 'alaykum miskeen **un**

# 5296

Waghadaw 'alahardin qadireen **a**

# 5297

Falamma raawha qaloo inna ladalloon **a**

# 5298

Bal nahnu mahroomoon **a**

# 5299

Qala awsatuhum alam aqul lakum lawla tusabbihoon **a**

# 5300

Qaloo subhana rabbina inna kunna _th_ alimeen **a**

# 5301

Faaqbala ba'duhum 'ala ba'din yatalawamoon **a**

# 5302

Qaloo ya waylana inna kunnatagheen **a**

# 5303

'asa rabbuna an yubdilana khayran minha inna ila rabbina raghiboon **a**

# 5304

Kathalika al'athabu wala'athabu alakhirati akbaru law kanoo ya'lamoon **a**

# 5305

Inna lilmuttaqeena 'inda rabbihim jannati a **l** nna'eem **i**

# 5306

Afanaj'alu almuslimeena ka **a** lmujrimeen **a**

# 5307

Ma lakum kayfa tahkumoon **a**

# 5308

Am lakum kitabun feehi tadrusoon **a**

# 5309

Inna lakum feehi lama takhayyaroon **a**

# 5310

Am lakum aymanun 'alayna balighatun ila yawmi alqiyamati inna lakum lama tahkumoon **a**

# 5311

Salhum ayyuhum bithalika za'eem **un**

# 5312

Am lahum shurakao falyatoo bishurakaihim in kanoo sadiqeen **a**

# 5313

Yawma yukshafu 'an saqin wayud'awna ila a **l** ssujoodi fala yastatee'oon **a**

# 5314

Khashi'atan absaruhum tarhaquhum thillatun waqad kanoo yud'awna ila a **l** ssujoodi wahum salimoon **a**

# 5315

Fatharnee waman yukaththibu bihatha alhadeethi sanastadrijuhum min haythu la ya'lamoon **a**

# 5316

Waomlee lahum inna kaydee mateen **un**

# 5317

Am tasaluhum ajran fahum min maghramin muthqaloon **a**

# 5318

Am 'indahumu alghaybu fahum yaktuboon **a**

# 5319

Fa **i** sbir lihukmi rabbika wala takun kasahibi alhooti ith nada wahuwa mak _th_ oom **un**

# 5320

Lawla an tadarakahu ni'matun min rabbihi lanubitha bi **a** l'arai wahuwa mathmoom **un**

# 5321

Fa **i** jtabahu rabbuhu faja'alahu mina a **l** ssaliheen **a**

# 5322

Wain yakadu allatheena kafaroo layuzliqoonaka biabsarihim lamma sami'oo a **l** ththikra wayaqooloona innahu lamajnoon **un**

# 5323

Wama huwa illathikrun lil'alameen **a**

# 5324

Alhaqqa **tu**

# 5325

Ma alhaqqa **tu**

# 5326

Wama adraka ma alhaqqa **tu**

# 5327

Kaththabat thamoodu wa'adun bi **a** lqari'a **ti**

# 5328

Faamma thamoodu faohlikoo bi **al** ttaghiya **ti**

# 5329

Waamma 'adun faohlikoo bireehin sarsarin 'atiya **tin**

# 5330

Sakhkharaha 'alayhim sab'a layalin wathamaniyata ayyamin husooman fatara alqawma feehasar'a kaannahum a'jazu nakhlin khawiya **tun**

# 5331

Fahal tara lahum min baqiya **tin**

# 5332

Wajaa fir'awnu waman qablahu wa **a** lmutafikatu bi **a** lkhatia **ti**

# 5333

Fa'asaw rasoola rabbihim faakhathahum akhthatan rabiya **tan**

# 5334

Inna lammatagha almao hamanakum fee aljariya **ti**

# 5335

Linaj'alaha lakum tathkiratan wata'iyaha othunun wa'iya **tun**

# 5336

Faitha nufikha fee a **l** ssoori nafkhatun wahida **tun**

# 5337

Wahumilati alardu wa **a** ljibalu fadukkata dakkatan wahida **tan**

# 5338

Fayawmaithin waqa'ati alwaqi'a **tu**

# 5339

Wa **i** nshaqqati a **l** ssamao fahiya yawmaithin wahiya **tun**

# 5340

Wa **a** lmalaku 'ala arjaiha wayahmilu 'arsha rabbika fawqahum yawmaithin thamaniya **tun**

# 5341

Yawmaithin tu'radoona la takhfa minkum khafiya **tun**

# 5342

Faamma man ootiya kitabahu biyameenihi fayaqoolu haomu iqraoo kitabiyah

# 5343

Innee _th_ anantu annee mulaqin hisabiyah

# 5344

Fahuwa fee 'eeshatin radiya **tin**

# 5345

Fee jannatin 'aliya **tin**

# 5346

# 5347

Kuloo wa **i** shraboo haneean bima aslaftum fee alayyami alkhaliya **ti**

# 5348

Waamma man ootiya kitabahu bishimalihi fayaqoolu ya laytanee lam oota kitabiyah

# 5349

Walam adri mahisabiyah

# 5350

Ya laytaha kanati alqadiya **tu**

# 5351

Ma aghna 'annee maliyah

# 5352

Halaka 'annee sultaniyah

# 5353

# 5354

# 5355

Thumma fee silsilatin thar'uha sab'oona thira'an fa **o** slukooh **u**

# 5356

Innahu kana la yuminu bi **A** llahi al'a _th_ eem **i**

# 5357

Wala yahuddu 'alata'ami almiskeen **i**

# 5358

# 5359

# 5360

# 5362

# 5363

# 5364

# 5365

# 5366

# 5367

# 5368

Laakhathna minhu bi **a** lyameen **i**

# 5369

# 5370

Fama minkum min ahadin 'anhu hajizeen **a**

# 5371
